Chapter 1334: True Immortal You Resuscitates

Facing Li Fan's suggestion, Mo Rubin did not immediately respond. He remained silent, deep in thought for a long time.

Gazing at Li Fan, his eyes fell upon his long, streaked-with-white hair. Perhaps it was due to Li Fan's sincere words and his genuinely approaching end of lifespan, that Mo Rubin finally nodded in agreement: "There is no reason why not."

Li Fan nodded joyfully, "Excellent! With your assistance, Daoist brother, we will surely achieve twice the results with half the effort!"

"If that's the case, let us return to the Xuanhuang Realm first!"

The phantom of the wooden sword was unsheathed, and Li Fan extended his hand, inviting Mo Rubin to enter.

Initially, Mo Rubin paid it no mind, but after personally entering the phantom's range and experiencing its incredible speed, his expression finally shifted slightly. His gaze towards Li Fan changed once more.

Finally, witnessing with his own eyes how the phantom's protection allowed them to ignore the suction of the Immortal Ruins and smoothly descend into the Xuanhuang Realm, Mo Rubin could no longer contain himself and said, "It seems, Daoist friend, you are truly one of the most remarkable individuals of this era."

Li Fan gave a wry smile and shook his head, "While I can be unrivaled in one era, I cannot suppress all eras. Moreover, even with all sorts of divine abilities, lifespan will eventually reach its limit, won't it? This divine ability is simply beyond the decree of heaven."

Mo Rubin opened his mouth, but said nothing more.

At this moment, they had descended into the Xuanhuang Realm. Mo Rubin's divine sense swept across the world silently. Upon seeing the vast regions, expanded countless times, and the towering white mist barrier between heaven and earth, even this well-traveled Dharma King of the Xuan Tian Sect couldn't help but show a flicker of astonishment in his eyes.

After a long while, he sighed with emotion, "If I hadn't truly sensed the residual traces of the Star Crossing Great Array, I would never have been able to connect this magnificent world before me with the Xuanhuang Realm of ancient times."

"After ten thousand years, the changes in the world have reached this point!"

Li Fan nodded, "When the world is on the verge of destruction, the changes in all things occur hundreds or thousands of times faster than usual. Observing these changes, their speed is like lightning, their swiftness like light. This is the Dao of Heaven saving itself..."

As Li Fan spoke, he casually conjured an illusion.

Within the ball of light, the Xuanhuang Realm was plunged into chaos, yin and yang disordered; stars dimmed, mountains and rivers trembled; plants withered, birds and beasts fled. It was a scene of imminent apocalypse.

At the critical juncture of life and death, the Xuanhuang Realm indeed gave rise to various reactive changes. Ice freezing and heat dissipating, time flowing and ebbing, heavenly punishment and earthly destruction...

Mo Rubin was momentarily mesmerized.

At a crucial moment, Li Fan let out a light cough and retracted the illusionary ball of light.

Mo Rubin felt a sense of wistful loss surge within him. He faintly sensed that the scene within the ball of light seemed to genuinely contain the principles of the evolution of heaven and earth. For any cultivator, it was an unimaginable treasure. However, Li Fan had only displayed it for too short a time, and Mo Rubin couldn't comprehend much. Moreover, as a Dharma King of the Xuan Tian Sect and a revered elder awakened from ancient times in the Xuanhuang Realm, Mo Rubin did not shamelessly ask Li Fan to display it again.

"Perhaps after we successfully find Brother Xuanyuan and become more familiar, then..." Mo Rubin couldn't help but think.

"Of course, the reason the Xuanhuang Realm has become what it is today, besides the natural changes of the Dao of Heaven, is also due to the clandestine actions of the Transmitting Dharma Heavenly Venerate," Li Fan continued to speak truthfully.

"This Transmitting Dharma is likely a Venerate from the former Heavenly Law Realm. When the Heavenly Law Realm was destroyed, Transmitting Dharma sought to use the only surviving Xuanhuang Realm in the Star Sea for reincarnation..."

"This Transmitting Dharma has cultivated in the Star Sea for thousands of years, their strength unfathomable, perhaps having reached the limits of mortality. I cannot defeat him!"

"We must act cautiously and guard against this person. Transmitting Dharma will not let go of any existence that threatens his revival of the Heavenly Law Realm," Li Fan sighed, offering a kind suggestion.

"This Transmitting Dharma is actually quite decent. It's just a pity that he is destined to be on the opposite side of the Xuanhuang Realm." Mo Rubin observed the incongruous remnants of other worlds within the Xuanhuang Realm, deep within the world, and his belief in Li Fan's words grew stronger.

"What a pity..." In truth, Mo Rubin held a certain degree of goodwill towards this powerful figure who, in name, had overthrown the Ten Immortal Sects. However, upon seeing the scene of the Xuanhuang Realm being dismembered and reshaped, and hearing Li Fan's hushed narration, that already faint goodwill vanished instantly.

"Rest assured, we will act discreetly. Until we find Brother Xuanyuan, we will not confront this Transmitting Dharma Heavenly Venerate." Mo Rubin's gaze constantly swept across the heavens and earth, as if sensing for some trace.

After a long while, he frowned, "It seems the Star Crossing Great Array is indeed severely damaged. We can only sense faint residual aura, and cannot manipulate it."

"Partly due to the passage of time, and partly because during the ten thousand years ago when the Ten Immortal Sects manipulated the Star Crossing Great Array to capture other cultivation worlds, continuous battles ensued. The array was increasingly damaged, yet the cultivators of the Ten Sects were incapable of repairing it, which ultimately led to the array's complete destruction..." Li Fan said slowly.

"At the very least, according to my investigation, that's how it happened." Seeing the sharp glint flash in Mo Rubin's eyes, Li Fan shrugged, speaking with complete honesty.

"How could those useless beings from the Ten Sects possibly manipulate the Star Crossing Great Array?! Unless..." A dangerous aura suddenly emanated from Mo Rubin.

Li Fan subtly shifted his position, agreeing, "It must have been a Dharma King who betrayed the sect and revealed the manipulation method to the Ten Sects."

Mo Rubin's brow furrowed deeply, but he did not respond. After a long silence, he shook his head and said, "Not necessarily. Perhaps they were interrogated after being captured by the Ten Immortal Sects."

Li Fan was somewhat surprised by Mo Rubin's attitude upon hearing this. Because he knew that King Xuan Tian had entrusted the manipulation methods of various sub-arrays of the Star Crossing Great Array to different Dharma Kings separately, to prevent unforeseen accidents. Mo Rubin was responsible for the Spirit Gathering Ascension Array, the Sea of Darkness. As for Ji Yuzhen, she was responsible for the Horizontal Golden Chain. Perhaps sensing Li Fan's emotions, Mo Rubin began to explain his reasons for actively defending them: "Back then, Brother Xuanyuan revealed to me that Ji Yuzhen and Luo Yichen were in charge of the Star Locking Golden Chain..."

"Among the twelve of us, anyone could have betrayed us, except for those two. They would not." Mo Rubin stated with conviction.

Li Fan pondered, "In Dharma King Ji's memories, she deeply adored King Xuan Tian. As for Luo Yichen..."

Mo Rubin nodded, "Indeed, it was only after her heart was set on Brother Xuanyuan that Luo killed all her myriad consorts. From then on, she devoted herself solely to one person."

Li Fan shook his head even more vigorously, "King Xuan Tian entrusted the same task to these two women. This was a foolish decision!"

"Daoist friend thinks too much. The two of them have a very good relationship with each other." Mo Rubin chuckled dismissively.

Li Fan did not elaborate further. While chatting casually, they decided on the first location to search for King Xuan Tian's whereabouts. It was within the Sea of Darkness. Their exploration followed a similar path to Li Fan's in his previous life. After some difficulty, and with Li Fan feigning extreme surprise, they finally reached the central core of the Spirit Gathering Ascension Array. First, they were horrified by the True Immortal corpse in the depths of the Sea of Darkness and the faintly stirrings of the True Immortal's will to survive. Regaining his senses, Mo Rubin paused slightly, "Hmm? It seems someone has been here not long ago!" Li Fan's heart was startled. He hadn't expected that Mo Rubin, despite Li Fan's efforts to conceal his tracks during his previous visit, could still detect it. However, he remained calm, his face showing a hint of pleasant surprise, and quickly asked, "Is it King Xuan Tian?" Mo Rubin did not doubt the person beside him. After all, this array seal was the formidable Immortal Array 'Spirit Gathering Ascension,' and it was not easy for ordinary individuals to break through and enter. "However, there are indeed traces of predecessors who entered this place before. Although they couldn't reach the True Immortal corpse at the very core..." "The people of the Ten Immortal Sects died here. They were likely lured by someone and then killed by the True Immortal's will to survive." "Could it be Elder Cui?" Cui Zhiyuan was another Dharma King who jointly managed the Spirit Gathering Ascension Array with him. While thinking this, Mo Rubin re-examined the traces of this array's activation and still felt something was amiss. "It doesn't seem like the restrictions were directly activated, but rather a forceful breakthrough without damaging the immortal array. Using brute force to overcome ingenuity..." "Furthermore, after the fact, the array was improved to seal the True Immortal's will and prevent intrusion." Mo Rubin pondered for a long time, ultimately finding the identity of this intruder unfathomable. Li Fan, of course, saw his confusion but did not kindly reveal the events involving the Transmitting Dharma Heavenly Venerate in his previous life. Mo Rubin agonized for a while longer before finally deciding to set this matter aside for now. He began to search for King Xuan Tian's trace within the Sea of Darkness. The Spirit Gathering Ascension Array, like a circular observation deck, suddenly illuminated within the Sea of Darkness. Faint fluctuations emanated from it, spreading rapidly through the Sea of Darkness. After a full half-incense stick of time, Li Fan finally sensed these fluctuations returning. Mo Rubin's expression was impassive as he awaited the results of the complete search. It was evident that King Xuan Tian was not present in this Sea of Darkness. Li Fan saw Mo Rubin's brow furrowed deeply again and couldn't help but comfort him, "We'll head to the next location then." Mo Rubin shook his head, "I never expected to find Brother Xuanyuan so easily." "I just feel that this Sea of Darkness is somewhat... off." Li Fan's heart stirred, "What do you mean?" "The Sea of Darkness was established upon the remains of a True Immortal. Although the True Immortal has completely perished, they were, after all, True Immortals. Their methods are far beyond the imagination of us mortal cultivators." "For instance, the 'will to survive' that naturally arises upon sensing a living being's intrusion. The Dark energy accumulated here, compared to back then, seems to have undergone subtle changes," Mo Rubin's expression was rather solemn. Li Fan followed Mo Rubin's gaze and looked into the boundless darkness. Mo Rubin continued speaking in a deep voice, "When a True Immortal perishes, the Dark energy is masterless. But this power was generated utilizing the True Immortal's remains. While everything was dormant, it was fine. But precisely because a sliver of the True Immortal's will to survive was agitated..." "Perhaps under the influence of this will to survive, the Dark energy has become different." Li Fan feigned extreme shock, "The abilities of a True Immortal are so terrifying? What specific changes are you referring to regarding this Dark energy?" Mo Rubin: "It's not clear yet. But one thing is certain: it is evolving in a direction that favors the True Immortal's revival. Even if complete resurrection is impossible, the trend will surely exist." "Perhaps when this Dark energy in the Sea of Darkness encounters life forms useful for the True Immortal's revival, it will launch a similar attack, just like the corpses you saw on the way. Their life essence was completely drained, becoming nourishment for the True Immortal's revival..." "Fortunately, after the transformation by the Spirit Gathering Ascension Array, the Dark energy is far less influenced by the True Immortal's remains than the True Immortal's will. Things are not as bad as I imagined." Li Fan deeply agreed, "The energy accumulated in this Sea of Darkness is already so immense. If it were to break free, it might devour the Xuanhuang Realm in an instant... becoming nourishment for the True Immortal's revival..." Mo Rubin cast a deep look at the Sea of Darkness and nodded in agreement, "If left unchecked, there might be such a day in the future." Li Fan asked curiously, "If, I mean hypothetically, the entire Xuanhuang Realm were used as nourishment, could it truly revive an Immortal's corpse?" Mo Rubin turned to look at Li Fan, remaining silent for a long time. Li Fan's eyes held no malice, only pure curiosity about the unknown. Mo Rubin pondered for a long time, then said, "Just based on energy levels. The current Xuanhuang Realm should be sufficient. After all, it has absorbed so many merged cultivation realms, even if they are only fragmented remnants..." "The living beings of the world may be destroyed, but their origins still remain." "But even if revived, it would likely only be an empty shell, a walking corpse, without its own true consciousness..." Li Fan nodded slowly, "A True Immortal's body is still an extremely formidable existence. If one could possess it, wouldn't it be possible, in a sense, to achieve True Immortality in this era?" Mo Rubin smiled at Li Fan's whimsical thought and did not take it seriously. After failing to find King Xuan Tian in the Sea of Darkness, the two decided to head to the second location: the Eye of the Celestial Beast. "The Eye of the Celestial Beast can not only probe the Star Sea but also monitor the Xuanhuang. It exists independently of the Xuanhuang Realm, connected only by an esoteric link. If the Celestial Beast were still alive, we could reach it directly. But now that the Celestial Beast is dead, reaching it will require some effort," Mo Rubin explained. Afterward, he accompanied Li Fan to Jiushan Prefecture. Looking at the nine continuous mountain ranges standing tall between heaven and earth, a hint of sadness flashed in Mo Rubin's eyes. Then, just like in his previous life, he found the immortal artifact's white jade flagpole within the underground ruins. "This is..." "An immortal artifact?" Li Fan feigned great shock. Mo Rubin was dismissive, "The Immortal Spiritual Power is depleted, leaving only the shell of an immortal artifact." "However, using it to travel to the Eye of the Celestial Beast is not difficult." Mo Rubin used the white jade flagpole as the central core and began to prepare the formation. "During my search for King Xuan Tian, I also encountered some fragments of immortal artifacts. However, they were all like this white jade flagpole, with their Immortal Spiritual Power exhausted. Some were even shattered as if they had suffered immense calamities." "Back then, what kind of calamitous scene did King Xuan Tian witness in the Immortal Realm? It was so catastrophic that even the Immortal Realm could not escape?" Li Fan mused, inquiring as he prepared. Mo Rubin, who was preparing the flagpole, paused slightly, as if lost in memory.

Chapter 1335: The Calamity of the Immortal Realm's Dissipation

"Regarding this question, it's not just you and I. Even the ancient Xuanhuang Realm, everyone who knew that Brother Xuanyuan ascended to immortality and then returned from the Immortal Realm, was immensely curious." Mo Rubin said with deep emotion.

"However, no matter what methods they used to inquire, Brother Xuanyuan never revealed the details. He merely spoke vaguely of a terrifying calamity in the Immortal Realm."

"Even we, his Dharma King brothers, and Ji Yuzhen, whom Brother Xuanyuan trusted the most, were not told."

"It wasn't until Brother Xuanyuan achieved a breakthrough and decided to implement the 'luring the snakes out of their holes' plan that he briefly mentioned the calamity in the Immortal Realm."

"He called it the 'Dao Annihilation'. Although he didn't describe the specific scenes of the Dao Annihilation calamity to us, just these two words sent chills down our spines. All of us Dharma King brothers saw a fleeting look of fear in Brother Xuanyuan's eyes..."

"Dao Annihilation." Li Fan savored these two words, and gradually, an uncontrollable chill spread through his heart. He recalled the fragmented memories he had glimpsed within the True Immortal's flesh and blood.

Broken voices echoed from the towering figure above the True Immortal. "Qionglang Star Domain... Annihilation... Guarding..."

Li Fan mused, "This word 'annihilation' likely refers to the 'Dao Annihilation' calamity. The Qionglang Star Domain suffered a calamity, requiring True Immortals to be dispatched to guard it, or perhaps to guard other star domains to prevent future occurrences?"

Li Fan secretly speculated, "As expected, the calamity that led to the destruction of the Immortal Realm had precursors. The Immortal Realm must have attempted various self-rescue measures, but ultimately could not prevent the spread of the Dao Annihilation calamity."

New questions arose in Li Fan's mind. Did the Dao Annihilation calamity only target and appear in the Immortal Realm? After the destruction of the Immortal Realm, did the Dao Annihilation calamity disappear without a trace? Or, one day, would it reappear in the lower Star Sea? What was the relationship between the Dao Annihilation calamity and the erosion disaster Li Fan had witnessed in the Boundless Mirror and the ruins of the Yishi Sect?

The uncontrolled surge of True Immortal script power swept across the Star Sea, bringing destruction to a vast expanse. Starlight dimmed, transforming into the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. But... life had not been completely extinguished. Not to mention the still vibrant Xuanhuang Realm, even the seemingly dead Star Sea retained its consciousness. With the passage of time, its eventual revival was almost a certainty.

"The destructive calamity encountered by the Utmost Darkness Star Sea is likely on a completely different level than the Dao Annihilation calamity." The word 'annihilation' conjured in Li Fan's mind the image of everything being utterly obliterated under the calamity.

"Perhaps not even fragments of the world would remain," Li Fan felt a shudder run through him.

As Li Fan's thoughts drifted, Mo Rubin continued, "Brother Xuanyuan had instructed that knowing the details of the Immortal Realm's calamity would be more harmful than beneficial to us."

"He even advised us to avoid recalling its name as much as possible, because it might take the opportunity to manifest as a nightmare or a heart demon. Even if we haven't seen its true form, it can still exploit our vulnerabilities."

"He only told us the name 'Dao Annihilation' to instill a basic sense of prevention." Mo Rubin's expression was grave. "If we don't know its name, even if we encounter its signs for the first time, we wouldn't recognize its true nature. But if we know its name, even the first glimpse of its manifestation will trigger a premonition in our hearts."

"In fact, Brother Xuanyuan encountered this world-ending calamity as soon as he arrived in the Immortal Realm. He learned various details about the Dao Annihilation calamity later through his interactions with the Faceless Immortal."

"Enough. Let's not discuss this matter further." Mo Rubin abruptly stopped speaking.

While he was speaking, the formation of the white jade flagpole was prepared. Mo Rubin's expression became solemn as he formed hand seals. The white jade flagpole rose, emitting a halo of light that enveloped them both. "Go!" Similar to Li Fan's phantom wooden sword, the white jade flagpole aimed at the sky, adjusting its direction. Then, the flagpole body exuded specks of white light, accumulating power for a few breaths before shooting towards the sky with Li Fan and Mo Rubin. Although its speed was slightly slower than Li Fan's sword shadow divine ability, the refined, aggressive intent imbued within it, capable of breaking through all obstacles, was something Li Fan's divine ability lacked. The light column formed by the flagpole's passage was extremely thin, with no energy leakage, thus not attracting the attention of Xuanhuang Realm cultivators. Li Fan, inside the flagpole, watched the scenery of the Xuanhuang Realm rapidly recede. Even the suction of the Immortal Ruins only slightly slowed their speed. Mo Rubin, meanwhile, focused on manipulating the flagpole, occasionally dodging areas where True Immortal remnants gathered. Calculating that the white jade flagpole would not collide with that basin filled with True Immortal remnants, Li Fan patiently waited. After flying through the Star Sea for about the time it takes to burn an incense stick, the white jade flagpole suddenly halted. The light dispersed, forming a bubble-like sphere that enveloped them. Then, it violently collided with an invisible barrier layer in the void. The white light bubble perfectly acted as a buffer, dissipating the impact force. Li Fan and Mo Rubin had arrived within the Eye of the Celestial Beast.

"Ah!" A scream immediately echoed in the relatively small area. It wasn't from Li Fan or Mo Rubin, but from Han Zhong, a cultivator Li Fan had seen before who had erroneously entered the Eye of the Celestial Beast due to the teleportation array mishap in Jiushan Prefecture. Trapped for a long time, Han Zhong had already lost hope of escaping. Only the instinct for survival kept him clinging to life. Now, seeing other living people, he first let out a cry of excitement.

Before he could say anything more... Mo Rubin's expression changed slightly. He directly unleashed a black light that struck Han Zhong's body! Alas, Han Zhong's eyes were filled with disbelief as he vanished into nothingness inexplicably!

"Daoist brother you..." Li Fan feigned astonishment. Mo Rubin, however, first conducted a highly cautious inspection, ensuring that no fragments of Han Zhong remained. Only then did he explain, "Although I don't know why this cultivator appeared here, he has already been contaminated."

"It's best to be cautious and prevent infection by rashly coming into contact with him." Li Fan's expression softened slightly, still puzzled, "Contaminated?"

Mo Rubin looked around as he spoke, "It's a very troublesome ailment. Even Brother Xuanyuan found it quite difficult to resolve."

"It should be related to the calamity in the Immortal Realm..."

"However, it's generally very difficult to encounter in the Star Sea. This place is the Eye of the Celestial Beast, so the possibility of contamination is higher."

"The concentration of this ailment in the lower Star Sea is extremely low. It was like this ten thousand years ago, and after ten thousand years, I also investigated it while traveling in the Star Sea. It seems there haven't been any significant changes. But the Eye of the Celestial Beast observes vast Star Domains. When the scale is magnified to a certain limit, even if the concentration is extremely low, it will truly reveal itself." Mo Rubin said, setting up several restrictions around them. These seemed specifically designed to counter this void-borne ailment.

Li Fan pondered Mo Rubin's words. "This ailment, due to the expansion of the observation area, its infection probability has increased... Doesn't that mean that just observing it can lead to transmission?" Li Fan was startled.

Mo Rubin nodded, "Precisely. This is also why I eliminated him without a second thought. Fortunately, the probability of this ailment spreading through ordinary means is low, and I've checked just now. There's no leakage. This place is safe for now."

"Such a peculiar mode of transmission, and related to the Immortal Realm's calamity..." Li Fan appeared worried. "What happens after infection? I didn't see any anomalies in that trapped cultivator just now?"

Mo Rubin conjured several more restrictions. The 'transparent bubble' that had originally tightly encased them, barely large enough for two or three people, slowly expanded as if inflating.

"There were no anomalies because the ailment was still latent within him and hadn't erupted yet. If you came into contact, you would understand its horror. The upper limit of one's spirit and life origin would be reduced. The degree of reduction would deepen with the severity of the infection. In the end, although not dead, one would become as fragile as a piece of paper."

"Even a gentle breeze could blow away your soul. Of course, before that, you would have to endure the various agonies brought about by the reduction of your life origin's upper limit." Mo Rubin sighed with some emotion, "Imagine, others' soft whispers sound like thunder in your ears, even causing your soul to ache and tear. An ordinary touch feels like being violently struck, leaving your flesh and blood mangled..."

"The normal world becomes a doomsday where terrifying calamities unfold ceaselessly in your eyes. At that point, death might be a form of release."

"But because of this ailment, before being reduced to the absolute limit, in order to maintain its propagation, it would instead sustain the host's life. Unable to live, yet unable to die..." Mo Rubin shook his head slightly. "Speaking of which, this ailment is indeed quite troublesome."

Li Fan said this, but his mind flashed back to the scene in his previous life where the Heavenly Physician used a jade bottle to collect the black energy emanating from the deceased Han Zhong. "It would be troublesome if this spread in the Xuanhuang Realm," Li Fan remarked in an odd tone.

"Ten thousand years have passed, and this ailment has hardly spread at all. Even if it has a tendency to spread in the lower realms, the time required would certainly be extremely long," Mo Rubin said casually. His attention was focused on the Eye of the Celestial Beast.

"This transparent space is the Eye of the Celestial Beast? It seems Xuan Tian is not here either." Li Fan expressed some regret.

Mo Rubin shook his head, "This is just an observation point of the Eye of the Celestial Beast. Do you know, little insects in the world are composed of countless small eyes forming a true eye? The Celestial Beast is also like this."

Li Fan suddenly understood. As Mo Rubin continued to cast spells, the transparent bubble shook violently and shrank, as if trying to expel them both.

*Pfft!* The bubble burst, and Li Fan felt a momentary dizziness. The next moment, they were in a strange space. It was like one of countless bubbles floating on the sea. On the arc-shaped boundary, countless identical scenes of other bubbles flashed. Li Fan could even vaguely see himself and Mo Rubin in some of the bubbles outside. However, the appearances, clothing, expressions, and movements of the other 'selves' were all different from the true self. Yet, there was a strange sense of familiarity. Countless 'mes', their gazes intersecting, gave Li Fan a very peculiar feeling.

"It's just a distortion caused by the simultaneous observation of countless Eyes of the Celestial Beast."

"As long as we remain true to ourselves, we will not be deceived." Mo Rubin seemed accustomed to this strange scene. He surveyed their surroundings, seemingly searching for something among the myriad bubbles.

"Brother Xuanyuan did not pass down the method for manipulating the Eye of the Celestial Beast array. Fortunately, I've been here a few times before. I can only slowly search using this archaic method." Mo Rubin said with some helplessness.

The number of Eyes of the Celestial Beast in this place seemed infinite. They appeared to be extremely close to each other, yet also infinitely far apart. Divine sense couldn't lock onto them; one could only observe with the naked eye. Moreover, the countless bubbles were not static. Occasionally, like waves lapping at the shore, countless bubbles simultaneously underwent irregular diffusion, changing their positions. This made most of the previous observations useless. Despite the arduousness, Mo Rubin did not show any frustration, focusing intently on his observation. At the same time, he did not forget to remind Li Fan, "Within the Eye of the Celestial Beast, laws are almost self-contained. You don't need to worry about your lifespan running out. Even if you stay here for ten thousand years, you won't age and die."

"If your end of lifespan comes and you truly don't want to die, you can also hide in here. While it doesn't guarantee immortality, prolonging your life for a few thousand more years should be no problem."

Li Fan nodded. "This Celestial Beast is truly remarkable."

"It is said that its size is comparable to a prefecture of the Xuanhuang Realm. Could it be that King Xuan Tian brought it back from the Immortal Realm?" Li Fan inquired.

Mo Rubin nodded as Li Fan had expected. "Yes and no. Back then, Brother Xuanyuan thought it was merely a dead object, an ordinary jade pendant. Unexpectedly, after encountering water, it actually developed a living aura."

"After careful nurturing, it grew larger and larger, and its combat power also increased exponentially."

"I am ashamed to say, if it were a fight to the death, perhaps even I would not be its opponent." A trace of nostalgia flickered in Mo Rubin's eyes. Then, perhaps thinking of the Celestial Beast that had long since died and whose bones had turned into mountains, a strong murderous intent flashed in Mo Rubin's eyes.

Li Fan did not respond. A silence fell once more. Li Fan, like Mo Rubin, began to search for any possible clues within the countless bubbles. Although the number of bubbles here was like the stars in the sky, innumerable, and they constantly changed, Li Fan possessed the Dao Stone's enhancement. Each bubble was different from the others. Each time he observed, after deeply imprinting it in his mind, Li Fan effectively left a unique mark on it. Regardless of how the bubbles shifted, they were all clearly distinguishable in his eyes.

Time slowly passed, and the number of bubbles marked by Li Fan increased. Options were ruled out one by one, and Li Fan's gaze grew sharper. Because he discovered something quite peculiar. Compared to his own true form, in the distorted scenes on those peculiar bubbles, his body seemed to be missing a small piece. Each bubble had a different missing part. But if they were combined...

Chapter 1336: The Predecessor of Gu Ming Dao

These missing parts were all very small. If not for the Dao Stone recording each one and comparing them, Li Fan would not have so easily discovered this anomaly hidden within the myriad Eyes of the Celestial Beast.

"Mo Rubin said earlier that the difference in the scenes was due to the distortions caused by the observation of different Eyes of the Celestial Beast..." Li Fan's gaze seemed to pierce through these countless bubbles, reaching towards the very back.

"These missing pieces can actually be seen as blind spots of the Eyes of the Celestial Beast. Or rather, an invisible entity occupies a fixed position within the observation range of the Celestial Beast's vision. Even with the observation of hundreds or thousands of fields of vision, its entirety cannot be grasped. Only by stitching together the blind spots of all the Eyes of the Celestial Beast..."

Li Fan's thoughts surged, and in his mind, those small fragments slowly pieced together, eventually forming a circuitous, profoundly mysterious, and extremely complex character! To call it a character was an understatement; before Li Fan's eyes, it even resembled a distorted human figure!

This human figure character was formless and intangible, yet it fell within the observation range of the Eyes of the Celestial Beast. Any single Eye of the Celestial Beast, let alone grasping its entirety, couldn't even detect the presence of the human figure character. However, it occupied a portion of the field of vision. It was like a shadow cast by an object illuminated from different angles. Even if one couldn't perceive the object's original form by 'looking,' by combining all the shadow patterns and performing reverse calculations, the formless and intangible entity could be reconstructed!

"This character..." Li Fan suppressed the shock in his heart and did not reveal any abnormality before Mo Rubin.

This human figure character was not a True Immortal script. But its essence might be no different from a True Immortal script. The True Immortal scripts such as 'Chaos,' 'Hunger,' and 'Creation' were projections of the Dao, concrete manifestations of power. And this human figure character before him was also a projection of a certain Dao.

"The moment cultivators observe a True Immortal script, the specific power it represents naturally appears in their minds. 'Hunger,' 'Chaos,' 'Creation,' and even that mysterious character representing the distinction between Immortals and mortals, are all like this. The reason is that all True Immortal scripts are the engravings and annotations of the Dao by that 'Inscription Dao Immortal.' The Great Dao is originally formless, yet the Inscription Dao Immortal could materialize its essence into characters, making it immensely easier for mortals to perceive and understand."

"But this human figure character did not..." Li Fan slowly pondered the vast power contained within the character. "Perhaps it was naturally formed, a projection of a certain Dao's power. Or perhaps it was the attempt of another True Immortal at 'Inscribing Dao'."

"However, this one was clearly far inferior to the later Inscription Dao Immortal!" The reason for judging that this character appeared before the Inscription Dao Immortal was that the Dao of True Immortals does not tolerate others. If the Inscription Dao Immortal already existed, no other 'Inscription Dao' attempts would appear in the world.

"At the moment of action, terrifying, nameless True Immortal power would have mercilessly crushed it."

The gap between this unknown practitioner and the true Inscription Dao Immortal was like that between two painters trying to record the mountains and rivers of the world with their brushes. The Inscription Dao Immortal's painting was lifelike, making the viewer feel almost as if they were there. But that practitioner's work was like a child's doodle, an abstract combination of lines, let alone resembling the actual subject, it was incredibly difficult even to ascertain what the painting was meant to depict.

Li Fan gazed at the distorted human figure character for a long time, lost in silent contemplation. Yet, he did not feel any disdain due to this supposedly crude method of inscribing Dao. Only because the object this human figure character attempted to inscribe... was the origin Dao itself.

Having witnessed Transformation of Creation, the change between Immortals and mortals, and even the change between True and False, Li Fan's ability to discern and identify the rank of True Immortal scripts was probably unmatched even by True Immortals.

Li Fan vaguely sensed that despite the crude method of inscribing Dao, it did not affect the rank of the origin Dao that this distorted human figure character attempted to inscribe. "Perhaps it is on par with the change between Immortals and mortals, or even above Creation."

A barely perceptible glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. "The Celestial Beast was formed from a jade pendant brought back from the Immortal Realm by King Xuan Tian in the past. Yet, after encountering water, it surprisingly transformed into a living being."

"Could it be due to the character hidden within this jade pendant?"

The method of discovering this hidden human figure character was both difficult and simple. Even if King Xuan Tian did not possess the Dao Stone, Li Fan did not believe that with his Half-Immortal strength, he could not have discovered this hidden secret. Similarly, the Sea of Darkness and the Ghost Tribe were all King Xuan Tian's doing. That character representing the distinction between Immortals and mortals, it was unlikely he wouldn't have noticed it.

"Perhaps King Xuan Tian's breakthrough back then relied on the power of these two characters," Li Fan mused inwardly.

As the inscription method of this human figure character was too crude, Li Fan could not comprehend anything from it for the time being. He could only deeply engrave it in his mind for now.

As for the whereabouts of King Xuan Tian... Li Fan had observed all the Eyes of the Celestial Beast. As expected, there were no signs of King Xuan Tian having been there. However, Li Fan did not voice this, remaining silent as he began to ponder how to decipher this array.

The Star Crossing Great Array was based on ancient immortal arrays, modified by King Xuan Tian. Given that he already knew about the 'Spirit Gathering Ascension Array,' it was not impossible for Li Fan to decipher the Eye of the Celestial Beast array with the aid of the End Dissolution Disc. Especially since Mo Rubin had directly brought Li Fan into the array's interior, all the operational details of the array were laid bare.

In the silence, Li Fan's deciphering progress steadily increased. Mo Rubin completed his observation of all the Eyes of the Celestial Beast only twice as long as Li Fan. A clear look of disappointment flashed across his face, unhidden.

"Not here either?" Li Fan spoke at the opportune moment.

Mo Rubin shook his head and sighed; "He didn't even come here to seek refuge."

"Both locations I deduced where Brother Xuanyuan might be hiding have turned out to be empty," Mo Rubin's expression was rather grim.

"Then shall we proceed to the next location?" Mo Rubin, however, rejected Li Fan's suggestion. "The Eye of the Celestial Beast observes the Star Sea externally and the Xuanhuang internally. Since we are here, why abandon its use?"

Mo Rubin stared at the constantly shifting myriad Eyes of the Celestial Beast and said softly. "Didn't you say earlier that King Xuan Tian didn't pass down the method for manipulating it? Can you still utilize the power of the Eye of the Celestial Beast?" Li Fan asked in surprise.

Mo Rubin replied with a proud tone: "After all, it is a part of the Star Crossing Great Array. As the saying goes, 'ten thousand changes, all stemming from the same source.' As long as you give me some time, it's not difficult to harness some of its power."

Li Fan couldn't help but praise, "Daoist brother is truly talented. How much time do you specifically need?"

"Within three to five months, it will certainly be done," Mo Rubin said in a deep voice.

Li Fan nodded slightly. After appearing to ponder for a moment, he suggested, "It would be pointless for me to just wait here. Why don't I return to the Xuanhuang Realm first and conduct a thorough search, looking for any loopholes? Perhaps I can find other clues."

Mo Rubin sized up Li Fan and finally agreed, "Very well."

Throwing out a jade talisman, Mo Rubin said, "Take this with you. If I have any results, I will notify you immediately."

Li Fan took the jade talisman and cupped his hands, "Then please, Daoist brother, escort me out of the Eye of the Celestial Beast array first."

Mo Rubin nodded and formed a hand seal. Li Fan's vision blurred, and he suddenly felt as if he had appeared in another miniature bubble. The bubble continuously shrank, gradually transforming into a thin film that enveloped Li Fan's body. Finally, the film tore apart, and in moments, Li Fan was back within the Xuanhuang Realm, in Jiushan Prefecture.

"From now on, coming here won't be as troublesome. We can directly transfer through the Celestial Beast's body." "Although the Celestial Beast is dead, its essence remains." Mo Rubin's voice echoed in Li Fan's ears before slowly fading away.

Li Fan looked up, his gaze seeming to pierce through space and time, directly towards the Eye of the Celestial Beast outside the void. After checking and confirming that Mo Rubin had not left any marks or ulterior motives on him, Li Fan narrowed his eyes and grumbled inwardly, "He agreed quite readily." "Perhaps he was just eager to get rid of me."

Li Fan vaguely sensed that Mo Rubin had not exerted his full strength within the Eye of the Celestial Beast array, possibly holding back some undisclosed skills. Therefore, he went along with the flow, proactively suggesting his departure. After all, with the aid of the End Dissolution Disc, he should be able to decipher the Eye of the Celestial Beast array even faster than Mo Rubin.

"If he can find King Xuan Tian's trace, that would be even better." "If not, at least he can contribute to the sublimation of the Xuanhuang Realm." The Dharma King of the Xuan Tian Sect was somewhat more useful than Yin Shangren or Xu Ke. Naturally, he couldn't be wasted.

With this thought, Li Fan activated the phantom wooden sword, and the next moment, he had returned to the Great Profound Minor World. The moment he returned to the Xuanhuang Realm, he sensed that Yin Shangren, who had gone missing during the reverberating Star Power storm, had safely returned. However, as the instigator of the disturbance, Bai Hua's feelings towards him had shifted from friendly to hostile. The two were confronting each other above the Dao Platform. Bai Hua appeared solemn, clearly demanding an explanation from Yin Shangren. Yin Shangren, on the other hand, kept his eyes closed, offering no explanation, yet exuding no hostility.

Li Fan looked at Yin Shangren, and a peculiar sensation arose in his heart. Having interacted with Yin Shangren for so many lifetimes, with a total of over a century of shared time, Li Fan understood him better than anyone else in the world. Li Fan easily perceived the wondrous changes that had occurred within Yin Shangren. Yin Shangren was a 'World Soul,' a remnant residue from the Xuanhuang Realm's inability to absorb the impurities during the process of devouring and merging with other destroyed cultivation realms. Because Yin Shangren's presence was often accompanied by an aura of strangeness and deathliness. But now... wisps of unique vitality emanated from this World Soul aggregate!

Li Fan couldn't help but be astonished. He immediately revealed himself, appearing before Yin Shangren. "Congratulations, Daoist friend, you have benefited from disaster!" Li Fan observed him carefully for a moment, then said softly.

At this moment, Yin Shangren slowly opened his eyes, "Without the Saint Master's help, I might never have reached the borders of the Star Sea, let alone obtained this fortuitous encounter!" Yin Shangren expressed his sincere gratitude. And the instant Li Fan saw his eyes, he understood why, when facing Bai Hua earlier, the latter had refused to open his eyes. Both eyes were black and white. The black one exuded vigorous vitality, while the white one exuded endless deathly aura.

The moment Li Fan's gaze met the black and white eyes, he felt as if he were pulled into an boundless illusion. Countless lives were born, and then destroyed amidst various calamities. Life and death underwent reincarnation and evolution at an terrifying speed. Li Fan even sensed that his 'psychological age' bar, which had never been affected by illusions, had its numbers leap rapidly the moment he fell into the black and white vortex. Li Fan was already in such a state, and Bai Hua's appearance was even worse. Even merely glancing indirectly, her normally indestructible vitreous body flickered unstably like a candle in the wind, on the verge of extinguishing! Fortunately, Yin Shangren also sensed the changes happening to Li Fan and Bai Hua. Furthermore, he harbored no intention of harming them. With some slowness and difficulty, he closed his black and white eyes. The storm of life and death illusions gradually subsided, and Li Fan and Bai Hua returned to normal.

"You..." Bai Hua pointed at Yin Shangren with astonishment, her face unable to conceal her fright. She could hardly believe that this person, whose strength was comparable to hers just a few days ago, had undergone such earth-shattering changes in merely a few days.

Li Fan asked with great interest, "What is this vitality on you? The foot of the high wall, among the continuous Great Wall of remnant realms, should only consist of destroyed worlds. How can there be such immense vitality hidden there?"

Yin Shangren paused and slowly explained, "Precisely because I discovered the vitality within that remnant realm, I acted recklessly. In fact, at that time, I was already controlled by instinct and acted involuntarily for a short period."

Li Fan frowned upon hearing this. "Even if I absorb the vitality of the black and white dual pearls now, I still don't know its origin. However, I can show the Saint Master the source of this vitality..." Yin Shangren said word by word.

After a moment of contemplation, Li Fan nodded, "The Great Profound Minor World is still too fragile." The phantom wooden sword was unsheathed, carrying Yin Shangren and Bai Hua, and arrived in the void of the Xuanhuang Realm. Catalyzed by the boundless vitality, his partially successful 'Foundation Establishment through Self' showed signs of repair. The true Dao foundation within his body was slowly integrating with himself, causing the signature double-echoing voice of Yin Shangren to cease.

With a solemn expression, Yin Shangren turned his head, avoiding Li Fan and their positions. He opened his black and white eyes again. Then, he reached out his left hand, inserted two fingers into his eye sockets, and with a slight pull, directly removed the two eyeballs! There was no gushing blood, only two black and white spheres, constantly spinning in the void! After leaving Yin Shangren's body, these black and white spheres gradually moved closer to each other. However, Yin Shangren's palm remained between them, preventing them from adhering and merging.

"The source of vitality is these two black and white pearls?" Bai Hua asked, seeing this bizarre scene.

"Not just vitality. The source of deathly aura is also from here." With the dual pearls removed from his body, Yin Shangren's speech became somewhat difficult for some reason. The black and white pearls continuously emitted their unique energy towards their surroundings. However, due to mutual attraction and restraint, they did not explosively diffuse into the void but formed a Tai Chi-like vortex, achieving a strange balance.

Li Fan looked at the black and white dual pearls, vaguely sensing a familiar aura from them.

Chapter 1337: Tai Jia Realm Divine Ability

In his previous life, Li Fan's Saint Embryo clone followed the Profound Immortal Boat on an expedition to the Xuanhuang Realm, only to fall into Transmitting Dharma's trap. He encountered a terrifying Immortal Realm overseer who, with a single glance, stripped the Immortal Boat of one-tenth of its life force. Like a giant cauldron boiling, like an abyss flowing over, it transformed a world frozen with countless cultivators into a Yin-Yang Orb.

Within the Yin-Yang Orb, two worlds were divided. One was a boundless, desolate icy ocean. The opposite of this desolate world was a vibrant, lively sea.

Initially, when Li Fan mistakenly entered the small world within the Yin-Yang Orb, he mistook it for the Daoist sanctuary of the 'Rebirth Heavenly Venerate' of the Xuanhuang Realm. This was because the world within, with its cycles of yin and yang, life and death, and the reversal of fortune, indeed corresponded to the so-called phenomenon of reversing life and death.

However, as Li Fan's vision gradually improved and he witnessed numerous genuine immortal arrays, he began to doubt his initial judgment. The array within the Yin-Yang Orb, though extraordinarily profound, was something Li Fan could comprehend the secrets of at first glance. Clearly, it was far from reaching the category of an immortal array.

The cycle of life and death within the Yin-Yang Orb was not achieved through this Reverse Life and Death Great Array, but solely through the origin power within the Yin-Yang world, derived from the Immortal Realm overseer's power. The Reverse Life and Death Great Array acted more like a catalyst, accelerating the process of reversing life and death.

In his previous life, the Saint Emperor caused immense chaos in the Xuanhuang Realm, and subsequently, the Xuanhuang Realm was plunged into a desperate situation of world-ending peril within the Myriad Things Return to Void Great Array. Transmitting Dharma and Heavenly Physician exerted all their efforts to resist, yet throughout the entire process, the mysterious 'Rebirth Heavenly Venerate' never appeared.

This might have been due to Lan Yu choosing to venture into the Star Sea for enlightenment, and the true Rebirth Heavenly Venerate not yet succeeding in reversing the natural order. However, Li Fan believed that even if the Rebirth Heavenly Venerate were born, he would likely not intervene in his world-ending actions. There were deep connections between the Rebirth Heavenly Venerate and the overseer.

The overseer bore the mission of the Immortal Realm, and besides monitoring anomalies in the Xuanhuang Realm, he also seemed responsible for collecting all different types of humans that had appeared in the Xuanhuang Realm. As for the Rebirth Heavenly Venerate... It was as if he had shed the constraints of his Immortal Realm mission and acted solely for his own benefit.

The overseer that Li Fan and the Profound Immortal Boat encountered lacked personal consciousness, acting purely on instinct or pre-established rules, almost like a puppet. It was truly difficult for such an entity to bear the responsibility of an overseer. Therefore, Li Fan conjectured that perhaps the True Spirit of the overseer had already left its original vessel, seeking freedom from its Immortal Realm duties after the destruction of the Immortal Realm.

The backlash faced by the Great Heavenly Venerate of Xuanhuang after dereliction of duty in his previous life indicated that even after the Immortal Realm's destruction, the imposed constraints remained. No one would wish to bear a shackle forever. Theoretically speaking, it was entirely reasonable for the overseer of the Xuanhuang Realm to seek freedom.

"In my previous life, I used a fake True Immortal remnant to lure the Transmitting Dharma cultivators of the Myriad Immortals Alliance into the Yin-Yang Realm, ultimately leading to their simultaneous demise. Yet, the Myriad Immortals Alliance acted as if nothing had happened. This indicates that Transmitting Dharma, or Heavenly Physician, must also know the true nature of this Rebirth Heavenly Venerate. Perhaps even Li Fan suspects that with Heavenly Physician's assistance, the transformation from an Immortal Realm overseer to the Rebirth Heavenly Venerate occurred..."

Now, in the present, the black and white dual orbs formed by Yin Shangren after detaching his black and white eyes emitted energy fluctuations that were almost identical to the Yin-Yang Orb. However, within these black and white dual orbs, life and death were clearly distinguished. They had not yet reached the level of the Xuanhuang Realm's Yin-Yang Orb, where life and death cycled ceaselessly.

Li Fan stared at the black and white dual orbs, remaining silent for a long time. After a while, he finally spoke, "There is a similar creation in a secret realm somewhere in the Xuanhuang Realm."

"However, the black and white life and death are intertwined, and compared to your mere dual life and death orbs, it is even more wondrous. Within that Yin-Yang Orb, countless corpses were frozen. I wonder..." Li Fan's gaze was intense.

Yin Shangren displayed the black and white dual orbs and then reabsorbed them into his body, transforming back into normal eyes.

"The white orb did indeed contain frozen corpses. But that was before the world's destruction."

"When the world died, those frozen corpses gradually melted away, transforming into the purest deathly aura..."

Li Fan murmured inwardly, "This should be the difference caused by the absence of an overseer."

"Among the many cultivation realms in the lower Star Sea, the Xuanhuang Realm is clearly unique. Not only did it have an appointment from the Immortal Realm, but it also had the Great Heavenly Venerate and an overseer. Furthermore, a True Immortal once personally visited. Although the reason is unknown, this True Immortal surprisingly perished..."

"And the world where Yin Shangren obtained the black and white dual orbs was also within the monitoring range of the Immortal Realm, but its level was somewhat lower than that of the Xuanhuang Realm."

Li Fan intended to eventually interact with the Rebirth Heavenly Venerate, who was suspected of shedding its physical form and escaping like a cicada shedding its shell, but his main goal in this life was Dao Integration by merging with the Heavenly Immortal Souls of the Super Xuanhuang Realm, so he aimed to avoid unnecessary variables.

Yin Shangren continued, "I am a World Soul. Originally, I thought I could only survive in this state of insignificant remnants for the rest of my life, but the moment I sensed the vast vitality within these black and white dual orbs, a strong premonition surged in my heart..."

As he spoke, the vitality within Yin Shangren's black eye spun faster.

"Perhaps there is no absolute decay in the world. The reason for being a remnant soul is merely the cessation of vitality. As long as sufficient vitality is infused..." As he spoke, Yin Shangren's complexion became increasingly rosy, appearing more and more like a normal human cultivator.

However, Li Fan narrowed his eyes and saw that things were not that simple. As Li Fan had predicted, as if agitated by the strong vitality emanating from him, the previously calm gray eye began to spin faster. Wisps of desolate, decaying deathly aura emerged from Yin Shangren's body, soon neutralizing and suppressing the original vitality. A scent of decay slowly emanated from Yin Shangren's body.

Yin Shangren coughed a few times, and the storm within his black and white eyes gradually subsided, revealing a hint of helplessness.

Bai Hua observed this, deep in thought, a hint of schadenfreude flashing in her eyes.

Li Fan spoke directly, "Life and death appear to be opposites, but in reality, they are one. You wish to incite vitality but suppress deathly aura; this will only be counterproductive."

"The living are the root of the dead. The dead are the fruit of the living. Digging at the root will surely disturb the fruit. Taking the fruit, however, may not harm the root..."

Li Fan, perfectly embodying the role of the Saint Master, actually began to expound the Dao to Yin Shangren on the spot. Yin Shangren, already possessing extraordinary comprehension, and now holding the black and white dual pearls of life and death, encountered no obstacles in understanding Li Fan's deliberately profound statements. The calm eyes showed faster and faster circulation of black and white energies.

Bai Hua also seemed to possess a keen talent for the Dao of Life and Death, and as she listened intently, she appeared to reap considerable rewards. The lecture lasted for a full half-day, practically exhausting all of Li Fan's stored knowledge.

Finally, Li Fan waved his hand, transmitting the Reverse Life and Death Great Array into the sea of consciousness of the two. This Reverse Life and Death Great Array was a further derivation by the End Dissolution Disc based on the original array within the Yin-Yang Orb, representing the pinnacle of practical application of the Dao of Life and Death within the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

The moment they came into contact with this array, Yin Shangren's face showed undisguised astonishment and joy.

"Life and death are opposites, but you might be able to use this array to slowly transform the infinite deathly aura within the white pearl into vitality. However, you must pay attention to the balance between life and death."

Li Fan glanced at Bai Hua and continued, "The vitality derived should be consumed as quickly as possible. Besides cleansing your own decay, perhaps it can also help fellow Daoist Bai."

Bai Hua's body trembled slightly, unsure what secret of hers Li Fan had discovered.

Yin Shangren nodded slightly.

"By the way, Saint Master, when I absorbed the black and white dual pearls, I also learned some information about this destroyed world."

"Although not much, it is very interesting."

After briefly organizing the Reverse Life and Death Great Array, Yin Shangren proactively stated, "This world is called [Tai Jia]."

"Before its destruction, although its scale was not large, it was an extremely powerful cultivation world in the Star Sea."

"This is because the Tai Jia Realm was an extremely rare cultivation world that lacked a world's Dao of Heaven."

"The cultivators within practiced the [Tai Jia Divine Technique], said to allow them to bypass the non-existent Dao of Heaven and directly communicate with the consciousness of the Star Sea's origin, drawing upon the power of the Star Sea..."

Yin Shangren's eyes flashed with a flicker of astonishment. From some fragmented images he displayed, the divine abilities of the cultivators in the Tai Jia Realm were indeed terrifying. Swords flew like rivers, fists shook worlds. They could traverse the Star Sea with their bare physical bodies...

Yin Shangren's tone suddenly changed, "However, precisely because they directly communicated with the origin intent of the Star Sea, they became the first to be affected when the True Immortal script power erupted in the Star Sea."

"The Star Sea divine power they relied on lost its efficacy. The Tai Jia Realm, once renowned in the Star Sea, perished at a much faster rate than ordinary cultivation realms."

"The most laughable thing is that at the moment of Tai Jia Realm's complete destruction, some cultivators of Tai Jia chose not to fight to the death. Instead, they knelt down and continued to beg for communication with the origin of the Star Sea..." Yin Shangren shook his head, filled with disdain.

Bai Hua also said, "As cultivators, we advocate for the power to reside within ourselves. Relying on the power of the Star Sea, though it may grant temporary might, ultimately turns to dust when calamity strikes."

"In fact, the cultivators of the Xuanhuang Realm who seek longevity are also the same..." Bai Hua suddenly paused here. Because she suddenly remembered their actions, pushing for the Xuanhuang Realm's ascension and wanting to ride the trend to improve their own strength and realm, seemed to have no fundamental difference from the longevity cultivators of the Xuanhuang Realm and the cultivators of the Tai Jia Realm.

Li Fan, of course, saw the reason for Bai Hua's sudden pause. He smiled slightly, "There are still differences."

"The power fed back to us after the Xuanhuang Realm's transformation ultimately belongs to ourselves. It's a one-time transaction; even if we turn against the Xuanhuang Realm in the future, this bestowed power cannot be recalled."

"As for the cultivators of the Tai Jia Realm..." Li Fan shook his head, offering no comment.

"However, the [Tai Jia Divine Technique], which directly communicates with the origin intent of the Star Sea, does have some merit."

Li Fan had previously taken Yin Shangren and the others to see the reviving origin intent of the Star Sea.

"The Xuanhuang Realm is not completely isolated. After all, it is still within the Star Sea. If its sublimation can gain the support of the Star Sea..."

Yin Shangren also perceived the potential usefulness of the Tai Jia Divine Technique.

"However, what I obtained from the black and white dual pearls are only fragmented memories," he said with regret.

Yin Shangren then haltingly recounted the incomplete [Tai Jia] Divine Technique. It was obscure and extremely strange, completely different from ordinary cultivation methods.

Li Fan, encountering this type of technique for the first time, became quite interested.

"The key essence of this technique is to communicate with the origin intent of the Star Sea."

"Ten thousand years ago, when the Star Sea was at its strongest, even Half-Immortals were like ants in the eyes of the Star Sea, let alone ordinary cultivators. To communicate with the consciousness of the Star Sea was naturally extremely difficult," Li Fan said slowly.

Yin Shangren nodded in agreement, "Indeed, the cultivation of the Tai Jia Divine Technique is extremely difficult, with only one in ten million succeeding. But once one masters it, the energy they can stir with each move and stance far surpasses that of normal cultivators."

Li Fan smiled, "However, times have changed. The Star Sea is destroyed, and its origin intent is being reborn from ruins. Currently, it's like a reincarnated great being in its infancy..."

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes, his tone filled with confidence, "The situation has reversed. Communicating with it now would be greatly reduced in difficulty."

"Let me try first!" The phantom wooden sword was unsheathed, and Li Fan rode the sword, flying away. In an instant, he traversed half of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea and arrived at the center of the Star Sea. Here, the reviving origin intent of the Star Sea was most active.

Li Fan stood quietly in the void. He did not directly activate the incomplete [Golden Armor Divine Technique]. What he had said was indeed true. However, he had not spoken the whole truth. Even with the revival of the Star Sea's consciousness, the gap between it and cultivators remained like the gulf between heaven and earth.

Currently, only a 'Child of Destiny' like the Saint Emperor, who could potentially promote the revival of the entire Star Sea, could directly converse with the Star Sea's consciousness.

As for ordinary cultivators, to achieve the same effect as the Saint Emperor...

"Then, we must first make the Star Sea see us!" Li Fan's eyes flashed with a sharp glint. The Ascension Array was instantly set up. A 'mountain peak' rose from the center of the Star Sea. Slowly ascending.

Li Fan stood atop the mountain peak, gazing upwards. Just like the ancient emperors who ascended mountains to perform 封禅 rituals, wanting to get closer to the heavens, Li Fan sought to stand higher, increasing his 'momentum' to make himself more conspicuous in the eyes of the Star Sea's origin intent.

Sensing that the Ascension Array's ascent had reached its limit. Li Fan began to silently recite the Tai Jia Divine Technique. Although incomplete, its efficacy in communicating with the Star Sea's consciousness still existed.

A thought drifted upwards, heading directly towards the source of the Star Sea.

*Boom!* Li Fan instantly felt as if he had fallen into a brilliant river of stars.

Chapter 1338: Ten Thousand Years of Favorability

"As if my body has become the universe, my will gallops through the galaxies. Tai Jia has no limits, spirit roams; Tai Jia has no change, spirit transforms; Tai Jia has no void, spirit transcends..."

Li Fan chanted silently in his heart.

And in his field of vision, just like the previous experience of the Saint Emperor, the seemingly utterly dark and desolate Star Sea, suddenly lit up with scattered points of light.

However, this time, it was different from directly contacting the True Will of the Star Sea's origin.

With the "Tai Jia Divine Technique" acting as a "translator" between them, Li Fan felt that the Star Sea's origin's True Will naturally developed a certain degree of goodwill towards him.

Not only did the contempt for ant-like beings from the Star Sea diminish and disappear, but Li Fan even sensed that the consciousness of the Star Sea was listening.

The gap between cultivators and the vast Star Sea, how immense is it?

Yet, relying on the "Tai Jia Divine Technique," it could significantly reduce this difference! This was, of course, partly due to the Star Sea being in a new ecological state of recovery after its destruction, and Li Fan's strength already standing at the pinnacle of the mortal Star Sea.

But it had to be said, the "Tai Jia Divine Technique" was indeed an extremely profound divine ability.

"Only by reaching a very high level of understanding of the Star Sea's essence can one create such a divine ability."

"Perhaps the founder of this divine technique has already ascended to immortality too." A thought suddenly flashed through Li Fan's mind.

However, he did not forget the purpose of this communication.

Maintaining the state of casting the Tai Jia Divine Technique, Li Fan's expression was solemn. First, he praised the greatness of the Star Sea and its recovery from destruction.

Then, he elaborated on the current state of desolation in the Star Sea, and emphasized the only place where life was found: the Xuanhuang Realm.

Finally, Li Fan sincerely prayed to the Star Sea's consciousness, wishing to obtain its help in the sublimation of the Xuanhuang Realm and its escape from the Immortal Ruins.

Like an ancient emperor sacrificing and praying to the heavens.

After Li Fan finished narrating his plea, he remained silent, patiently waiting for the response from the Star Sea's origin consciousness.

As if he had presented it with a difficult problem, the Star Sea's consciousness did not reply for a long time.

However, Li Fan felt that the connection between them had not been broken, so he continued to stand and wait.

During the period of connection with the Star Sea's consciousness, various thoughts and insights about the Dao of the Star Sea poured in. It was as if he had fallen into the legendary state of "unity of heaven and humanity," and every moment felt like an epiphany.

However, what Li Fan felt was a bit regrettable was that these insights were like ripples on a vast sea. Although they rose and fell, as the waves crashed, they quickly dissolved back into the water.

"It's not my own comprehension, but a phenomenon that naturally arises after being in a special state. As for how much can be remembered in the end, it depends on one's own fortune..." Li Fan understood in his heart.

Immersed in this state of near enlightenment, time passed without anyone knowing. The Star Sea's consciousness finally gave an answer.

Afterwards, Li Fan was forcibly expelled and his connection with the Star Sea's consciousness was severed.

The "Tai Jia Divine Technique." This could not be used again for a period of time.

A peculiar summoning ritual.

These two insights appeared simultaneously in Li Fan's mind.

"It seems the principle of the Tai Jia Divine Technique is to consume the goodwill of the Star Sea's origin consciousness. And this goodwill increases slowly over time. Since the destruction of Tai Jia, no cultivator has used this Tai Jia Divine Technique for ten thousand years. Therefore, the goodwill accumulated over these years has reached an astonishing level. That's why I felt the Star Sea was listening just now..." Li Fan, having completed a communication ritual with the Star Sea, realized something.

"However, the goodwill accumulated over the years has been completely depleted with my request. At least in the remaining twenty years of this life, I can no longer make it do anything that can be exploited. But it doesn't matter, after all, I have mastered this Tai Jia Divine Technique. In the next life, there will be another ten thousand years of goodwill for me to squander."

Perhaps the goodwill accumulated over ten thousand years was truly abundant. Or perhaps the sublimation of the Xuanhuang Realm was also beneficial to the overall recovery of the Star Sea.

In any case, the Star Sea's consciousness agreed to Li Fan's request and would provide help in the matter of Xuanhuang's sublimation.

The ritual it transmitted was the method for receiving the Star Sea's assistance.

"Once the ritual is set up, the Star Sea will directly bestow its great power."

"Even a nascent Star Sea is far from comparable to the Xuanhuang Realm, which has merged myriad worlds."

"With an additional layer of assistance, the Xuanhuang sublimation plan has a greater chance of success."

A peculiar look flashed in Li Fan's eyes: "I just don't know if this ritual will still be useful in the next life?"

A moment later, Li Fan vaguely shook his head, dismissing his own thought: "This ritual is, in essence, just a signal transmitter. Whether to contribute or not is up to the Star Sea's consciousness itself. Without the prior communication foundation, the Star Sea would likely only feel disturbed and then become angry. Not only would there be no Star Sea assistance, but it might even bring down disasters as punishment."

After all the goodwill was consumed, in the eyes of the Star Sea, Li Fan became no different from any other cultivator. And the duration of the ascending array had reached its limit, so Li Fan immediately drove his wooden sword phantom and left. Letting the formation collapse.

The collapse of the towering peak stirred up some ripples in the central Star Sea. After the commotion gradually subsided, a trace of extremely faint black energy, unnoticed, appeared.

It was exactly the same as the trace of black energy that had appeared before when Li Fan used the ascending array for the sublimation experiment of a minor world, causing the minor world to fall from a great height and be annihilated.

However, this time, there was no minor world falling. The black energy was born purely because this place was close to the most active area of the Star Sea's origin consciousness.

Compared to the trace of black energy that was later eaten by the Dharma Transmitter Jiang, this trace in the center of the Star Sea seemed much weaker.

However, "weak" was undoubtedly just an illusion.

This trace of black energy steadily grew stronger as time passed. The area it enveloped caused the Star Sea, which had begun to revive its vitality, to completely fall into nothingness.

But strangely, the Star Sea's origin consciousness did not discover the existence of this worm-like black energy.

It was allowed to continuously devour the Star Sea's life force, and the consciousness was helpless.

The growth rate of the black energy was extremely slow in the initial stage. However, as it devoured more areas of the Star Sea, its expansion capability also continuously strengthened.

It was expected that this black energy of unknown origin would soon ravage the Star Sea at an extremely terrifying speed.

But at this moment, the black energy was still quietly developing.

The surviving beings in the Star Sea were all unaware of this.

And Li Fan, the instigator, was also unaware of the disaster he had casually created.

At this moment, he had already returned to the Xuanhuang Realm and recounted his experiences in the central Star Sea to Yin Shangren and the others.

Bai Hua exclaimed repeatedly, her eyes filled with joy: "The goodwill accumulated over ten thousand years in Tai Jia has now become a dowry for the Xuanhuang Realm. With the help of the Star Sea's consciousness, the sublimation of Xuanhuang is within reach!"

Yin Shangren was much calmer: "Before, I also found world fragments near the Tai Jia fragments that could serve as medicinal guides for Xuanhuang."

"However, because I rashly devoured the Tai Jia fragments, the stability of the remnant wall was affected. I'm afraid we'll have to wait a while longer, until the reverberating Star Power storm completely passes, before we can proceed with the next step."

Bai Hua was even more delighted: "Indeed, everything is going smoothly. It seems that at most half a year, we can officially start the Xuanhuang sublimation plan."

Li Fan smiled: "It's not that simple. Although we have the Star Sea's assistance, we cannot be careless. The great power of the Star Sea is like a powerful tonic. If taken correctly, it will cure the illness. But if not..."

"The body cannot withstand excessive nourishment and will be harmed instead!"

Bai Hua became solemn upon hearing this.

Using the principles of the "unity of heaven and man," Li Fan once again lectured the two, assigning them tasks.

"Xu Ke is still below the high wall, his vitality is not extinguished, and he should have had another fortunate encounter. Since you caused the reverberating Star Power storm, you should go and retrieve him!" Li Fan said to Yin Shangren.

"So it should be!" Yin Shangren nodded in agreement.

Li Fan then looked at Bai Hua: "During your trip to the Star Sea border, Yin Shangren and Xu Ke both had their gains, but although you returned safely, you did not have any fortunate encounters..."

Bai Hua gave a wry smile, and then as if thinking of something, looked at Li Fan with a hint of anticipation in her eyes.

"In the Star Sea, fortunate encounters are not only found below the high wall. Go and check this place, perhaps you will have some gains." Li Fan told her a location not far from the Xuanhuang Realm in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, his expression enigmatic.

"Remember, don't be greedy, safety first. If you have no fate with it, just return."

Bai Hua firmly remembered the location Li Fan had given her, then cupped her hands in thanks.

Watching the two disappear one after another, and calculating that the time was almost up, Li Fan lazily headed back towards the Profound Immortal Boat.

The location Li Fan had pointed out to Bai Hua was a natural "highland" outside the Xuanhuang Realm.

While flying, Li Fan passed by there several times. Although he had found nothing on the surface, he had always felt that there might be some hidden secret there.

During the brief period of communication with the Star Sea's consciousness, Li Fan was even more certain of his judgment.

Therefore, he first let Bai Hua go and investigate.

The highlands that had been confirmed in the Star Sea, the high wall, and the Utmost Darkness Sea, all posed dangers. Even though he now possessed sufficient self-preservation abilities, Li Fan still would not rush into danger himself.

Not long after, he arrived outside the Profound Immortal Boat.

He deliberately released his aura, and soon the elders of the Immortal Boat arrived.

They surrounded Li Fan.

Seeing Li Fan return as promised, they all breathed a sigh of relief first.

Then, their expressions turned solemn, and they began to discuss important matters.

"Daoist friend, what did Da Qi say...?" Seeing Dao Sheng was the first to speak.

A trace of anger flashed in Li Fan's eyes: "Those who are greedy for petty gains! Let's not mention it!"

Zhong Daogong smiled slightly, his eyes flickering: "It seems your persuasion failed?"

"Something like that," Li Fan snorted coldly. "I have already told my master about my observations below the high wall, but they still remained unconvinced."

"My master even told me that there are actually quite a few such high points in the Star Sea. However, compared to the height of the high wall, the height of these high points is like the difference between the peak of a mountain on the ground and the firmament..."

"To cross it is a fool's dream!"

Li Fan's words caused the expressions of all the elders of the Immortal Boat to change slightly.

"Without special means, simply borrowing height cannot cross the high wall," Zhong Daogong said with a half-smile.

"However... Daoist friend just said that there are many high points in the Star Sea?" Zhong Daogong suddenly changed the subject and asked, his expression somewhat serious.

Li Fan nodded: "Yes. My master even personally took me to one of them. It was indeed true. Although it was lower than the location on the remnant realm Great Wall, it could still overlook the high wall."

Zhong Daogong remained silent for a long time upon hearing this.

After some discussion with the other elders, he finally said slowly: "It seems we, the Immortal Boat, have underestimated the world. How could civilizations that have survived the great calamity be simple?"

"They are strong, but cowardly. They lack the courage to even try," Li Fan retorted coldly.

Zhong Daogong, on the other hand, took the initiative to defend Da Qi, who was not present: "Daoist friend, you are oversimplifying things."

"Even with traces left by predecessors, crossing the high wall still requires a civilization to exert all its efforts. It's not something that can be described as simply trying."

"Having survived safely in the Star Sea for tens of thousands of years, perhaps they will continue to survive. There is no need to take such risks. Of course, Daoist friend's lifespan is nearing its end, and wanting to seek the truth of the Dao before dying is understandable," Zhong Daogong spoke eloquently.

Li Fan snorted coldly again but did not argue further.

The atmosphere between them became somewhat strained for a moment.

It was Jian Dao Sheng who spoke again: "Of course, Daoist friend, rest assured. Our Immortal Boat's determination to cross the high wall has never changed. Cooperating with us is probably your only choice if you want to achieve your wish."

Li Fan then seemed to remember something, furrowed his brow, and asked, "What is the reason for your Immortal Boat's obsession? Is it only because there is another half of an Immortal Boat outside the high wall?"

Seeing Dao Sheng did not answer directly, he hinted: "Before this, the Immortal Boat's situation was similar to yours. And now, although there might be a change, we are already in a difficult position."

"Moreover, with the precedent of the Shang Immortal Boat, it is not as difficult as we imagined to recreate the feat of crossing the high wall..."

"Limited to our Profound Immortal Boat," Zhong Daogong added.

Li Fan narrowed his eyes and looked at the elders of the Immortal Boat: "It seems your Immortal Boat still has secrets."

Zhong Daogong smiled without speaking.

"Since you are so confident, why should I be timid?" Li Fan said solemnly.

"I will do my best to assist the Immortal Boat in its success. Everything I have learned from Da Qi in my life was originally not meant to be passed on. But now..."

Upon hearing this, the elders of the Immortal Boat couldn't help but show a flicker of joy in their eyes.

"To be honest, besides True Immortal scripts, I have studied the Dao of Formations the most. Furthermore, I have mastered an ancient divine ability that can communicate with the Star Sea's consciousness..." Li Fan said proudly, introducing himself to everyone.

The elders of the Immortal Boat listened, their eyes shining with excitement.

"The Da Qi's research on True Immortal scripts, was it the highest achievement compared to the 'Creation' script you showed us last time?" Zhong Daogong asked the most crucial question.

Li Fan immediately retracted his arrogant expression.

"Given my status in Da Qi, the highest True Immortal script I could access was indeed "Creation."
