"However..."

Chapter 1339: Affairs of Xuanshang in Those Years

"This 'Creation' is not the highest achievement of Da Qi's research on True Immortal scripts," Li Fan said with a look of slight melancholy and sighing.

As expected, these words instantly caused the elders of the Immortal Boat to tremble inwardly.

They had personally experienced the wonders of "Creation." Even though it was a weakened version that Li Fan had merely recounted, its power was still far superior to single True Immortal scripts like "Bliss."

From this, it could be seen that the true "Creation" script undoubtedly possessed the power to turn decay into magic.

But now, Li Fan claimed that the Da Qi civilization had comprehended True Immortal scripts even higher than "Creation"?

"This... Daoist friend, is what you say true?" Even the usually composed Zhong Daogong could no longer maintain his composure and exclaimed aloud.

The other elders of the Immortal Boat also stared intently at Li Fan.

"How could I dare to speak falsely?" Li Fan said seriously.

"That script is Da Qi's highest secret, only accessible to those at my master's level. I only overheard him mention it a few times casually while attending to my master."

"It seems... it involves the 'Transformation between Immortals and Mortals.'"

"'Transformation between Immortals and Mortals'?" Li Fan's few words caused the expressions of the Immortal Boat elders to vary, and their minds to wander.

Li Fan observed their reactions. To enhance the credibility of his words, he added, "This script is indeed extraordinary. Since my master began researching it, in his daily teachings to me, some of the structures of True Immortal scripts I used to write habitually have undergone subtle changes."

"But it is precisely these seemingly insignificant changes that have caused the overall True Immortal script to undergo a transformation..."

In front of everyone, Li Fan wrote two script structures in the air with swift, flowing strokes.

Their shapes were identical, but there were subtle differences in radians, turns, and other details.

The elders of the Immortal Boat stared blankly at these two script structures, lost in thought.

It was as if an infinite magic had completely captivated their attention.

After a full half-day, Zhong Daogong was the first to recover. Without disturbing the other elders' contemplation, he turned his head, avoiding looking at the floating scripts in the air, and tried to replicate them himself.

As he gestured, a look of enlightened joy appeared on his face.

These different script structures were precisely the True Immortal script, related to the "Transformation between Immortals and Mortals," that Li Fan had obtained from the Ghost Tribe's bloodline.

That True Immortal script seemed to contain infinite principles of heaven and earth. Although Li Fan had only glimpsed a corner of it in this life, his strength was insufficient to fully replicate it.

The memory of that mysterious script vanished along with the failure of his attempt to perceive it. Only the countless subtle structures that formed the mysterious script remained somewhat imprinted in his memory.

At this moment, Li Fan was using these script structures, derived from the "Transformation between Immortals and Mortals," to deceive the elders of the Immortal Boat.

To call it deception was not entirely accurate.

The "Transformation between Immortals and Mortals" was of extremely high status.

Even a small fragment of it was enough for the elders of the Immortal Boat to benefit immensely!

Just like at this very moment, the elders who were in a state of enlightenment finally woke up one after another, as if they had been struck by a thunderbolt of enlightenment.

"Wrong, wrong! I never thought that our methods from the first half of our lives were all wrong!"

"It can actually be written like this. Just this subtle modification has increased the efficiency of writing True Immortal scripts by more than ten percent!"

"It's not just the efficiency of writing. The True Immortal scripts written using this method seem to have a higher degree of completeness inherently."

...

The elders discussed amongst themselves, filled with joy. And Li Fan, in this way, once again proved his value.

For the next month, Li Fan officially resided in the Immortal Boat.

Zhong Daogong specially created a new courtyard for Li Fan at the top of the Immortal Boat's Divine Tree, within the Immortal Severing Tower, to demonstrate his high regard for Li Fan.

And Li Fan did not let the people of the Immortal Boat down.

Single-handedly, he almost completed the Immortal Boat's rather barren formation system.

"With a wise elder leading the way, the Immortal Boat's formation research has leaped forward a hundred years in a single night," exclaimed Meng Xiaomeng, an elder of the Immortal Boat.

He carefully engraved the formation knowledge that Li Fan had imparted onto jade slips.

Meng Xiaomeng had always opposed the Immortal Boat betting all its chips on the path of True Immortal scripts. Therefore, in addition to researching True Immortal scripts, he also dabbled in formations and alchemy, attempting to open up other potential paths of survival for the Immortal Boat. However, without the guidance of a renowned master, and relying solely on his own study of the ancient formations recorded in the Immortal Boat, Meng Xiaomeng's formation skills were truly mediocre.

After witnessing Li Fan's formation theories this month, he was immediately astounded. Seeing such a rare opportunity, he dedicated all his energy to studying formations, even setting aside his research on True Immortal scripts.

Zhong Daogong did not interfere either.

After all, there were too many elders researching True Immortal scripts in the Immortal Boat, and the absence of one Meng Xiaomeng would not make a difference. However, having a new lineage of formation inheritance was quite important.

During this period, Li Fan not only established a formation inheritance system for the Immortal Boat.

Under his leadership and assistance, all the defensive formations on the Immortal Boat were rebuilt.

With the new formations, after being tested by the elders, the Immortal Boat's resistance to attacks increased more than threefold. The defensive capabilities of critical areas like the Immortal Severing Tower, the Immortal Pivot Courtyard, and the Divine Tree were also greatly enhanced.

Speaking of which, there was also a small interlude during this period.

Initially, the elders of the Immortal Boat had some reservations about rebuilding the formations, especially entrusting such a critical matter concerning the Immortal Boat's safety to Li Fan, a newcomer. The elders had differing opinions.

However, after witnessing Li Fan dismantle the original defensive array within moments and enter and exit various restricted areas as if they were nothing, the elders of the Immortal Boat were drenched in sweat and quickly reached a unanimous consensus.

Establishing a lineage and building new defenses.

With these two accomplishments, Li Fan quickly gained the deep trust of the vast majority of the Immortal Boat members.

Furthermore, with Li Fan integrating into the Immortal Boat and displaying a gentle and refined demeanor, treating everyone with kindness. He answered any questions posed by those who came to visit him without reservation.

Soon, within the circle of Immortal Boat elders, Li Fan had earned an excellent reputation. Visitors to his courtyard were endless.

One day, Li Fan was teaching the "Tai Jia Divine Technique" to several elders who had come to visit his courtyard.

"As if my body has become the universe, my will gallops through the galaxies. Tai Jia has no limits, spirit roams; Tai Jia has no change, spirit transforms; Tai Jia has no void, spirit transcends..."

The elders were all captivated by the True Immortal scripts and were initially not very interested in this so-called divine ability. However, after listening to the complete rendition of this divine ability, they all became solemn.

"Brother Li, this divine ability seems to be only a fragment?" Elder Lu Yuzhi asked with a frown.

Li Fan had been mingling with the Immortal Boat for a while and had gained everyone's goodwill. Their appellations had also become more familiar.

"Although it is a fragment, it does not hinder communication with the Star Sea's consciousness. However, even for the Star Sea's consciousness, which is close to destruction, it is not easy for us cultivators to contact it. Whether we succeed or not depends on each of your own fortunes."

After finishing the explanation of the Tai Jia Divine Technique, Li Fan looked at everyone and said with a smile, "The communication with the Star Sea can be like the ancient state of 'unity of heaven and humanity.' Whether it's enlightenment or deduction efficiency, it cannot be compared to normal circumstances."

"It even greatly benefits our comprehension of True Immortal scripts. Heh, those old fellows who didn't come today will surely regret it when they find out! We must keep our mouths shut and never reveal it unless they pay a hefty price," Gan Jingda said jovially, having understood the mysteries of the Tai Jia Divine Technique.

"Brother Li's knowledge is truly terrifyingly profound. It's like an endless treasure trove; every time I come, I gain new insights," Elder Nangong Lie's words caused everyone present to nod in admiration.

Facing everyone's praise, Li Fan responded calmly: "My lifelong wish is to pour out all the knowledge in my mind before I perish, leaving it to the Immortal Boat."

"And then, in the final moments of my life, I will risk everything to see the scenery beyond the high wall!"

Li Fan spoke with an air of freedom and indifference.

Among the elders in the room, some felt regret, some felt heartache, and some were unable to bear it.

"Brother Li, is there really no other way?"

"The Immortal Boat's treasury seems to contain some longevity elixirs. Why not..."

Li Fan waved his hand dismissively: "After the defensive formations were rebuilt, Elder Zhong took me to try the secret treasury. My lifespan has indeed reached its limit, and no heavenly materials or earthly treasures can help. I have long accepted my fate."

"I can only say that the backlash from beyond the high wall is indeed terrifying."

"However, it has only fueled my curiosity even more. My entire life, I must see what lies beyond the high wall!" Li Fan's gaze was resolute.

The people of the Immortal Boat fell silent, sighing.

Suddenly, Li Fan seemed to remember something: "Oh, right. When I suffered the backlash before, my master told me that if it weren't for the puppet I acquired from the Immortal Boat's treasury to resist some of the force, I likely wouldn't have even twenty years left, but would have perished directly."

"What is the origin of that puppet? When I chose it, I only thought its appearance was very peculiar. I didn't expect it to have the ability to resist the power from beyond the high wall."

As Li Fan spoke, he displayed an image of the puppet, standing with its hands down, its eyebrows lowered.

When Li Fan chose the puppet in the treasury, they had all accompanied him. Li Fan's words made them recall the scene, and their expressions became strange.

"This puppet actually has such a miraculous use?"

They looked at each other, but none of them knew its origin.

"Wait, I'll go check." Lu Yuzhi stood up, his expression serious.

After all, it was a relic capable of resisting the backlash from beyond the high wall, and they couldn't afford to treat it lightly.

"Brother Li, why didn't you ask about such an important matter earlier?" Nangong Lie shook his head.

Li Fan smiled: "At that moment, I heard that my lifespan was nearing its end and my bright future was shattered. I was mentally distraught and couldn't care about so many things. However, now that I've calmed down, and having just mentioned the Immortal Boat's treasury, I remembered it again."

Li Fan's explanation made the elders of the Immortal Boat unwilling to press the matter further.

Lu Yuzhi returned in a hurry not long after.

"According to the records, this puppet originates from the destroyed cultivation world, [Carefree]." Lu Yuzhi waved his hand, displaying an image to everyone.

Upon hearing this familiar name, Li Fan's heart stirred.

"The cultivators of this world disliked conflict. As their name suggests, they were naturally unrestrained and carefree, unwilling to be bound by anything. This puppet was bought from a gambler by the Xuan Shang Immortal Boat when they passed through the Carefree Realm back then."

The image shifted, and a disheveled, shabby man appeared before everyone.

The era was too ancient, and the reconstruction of the image was unstable, with frequent jumps. The sound was also intermittent.

However, it did not prevent everyone from understanding the events of that time.

"This thing is a genuine treasure. You gaining possession of it is definitely not a loss!" the shabby man said brazenly, rubbing his crotch and then sniffing his hand.

"This puppet, it seems indeed extraordinary. But your asking price of 100,000 high-grade spirit stones is too high. It exceeds my authority." Outside the picture, a crisp voice sounded.

"This was a merchant in the Carefree Realm back then, named..."

"Jia Chu. Yes, Jia Chu. It was he who completed this transaction and strictly followed the regulations of the Immortal Boat, recording the entire process and archiving it. That's why we are fortunate enough to see the scene from ten thousand years ago." Lu Yuzhi introduced to Li Fan.

"It's a pity that this Jia Chu, during the split of the Immortal Boat that year, chose to side with the Shang Immortal Boat. I don't know where he is now." Lu Yuzhi said with some regret.

Li Fan nodded slightly and continued watching the unfolding scene.

Jia Chu got up as if to leave, without any sign of reluctance.

But the shabby man, who had been nonchalant before, suddenly became anxious. He grabbed Jia Chu and said with a fawning smile, "If the price is too high, we can still negotiate. Eighty thousand, just eighty thousand will do! For a renowned sect like your Xuan Shang Immortal Boat, eighty thousand high-grade spirit stones is merely a drop in the ocean!"

Jia Chu was indifferent to the shabby man's tightly clasped hands.

He said unhurriedly, "Although our Xuan Shang Immortal Boat is a large sect, we cannot spend eighty thousand spirit stones on a puppet of unknown origin."

"Thirty thousand spirit stones is the limit I can decide. Anything more would require reporting, which is too troublesome. It's better not to make this transaction," Jia Chu's tone was decisive.

"Thirty thousand? You're squeezing me too hard," the shabby man grumbled, very displeased.

"If you think the price is too low, you can go to the native merchant guilds in the Carefree Realm to sell it," Jia Chu said indifferently.

The shabby man scratched his head and did not reply.

"The native merchant guilds in the Carefree Realm are actually inextricably linked with our Xuan Shang Immortal Boat. It's not an exaggeration to say they are our branches in the Carefree Realm. This shabby cultivator knows this, which is why he stopped talking sullenly." Lu Yuzhi explained.

In the end, after another round of bargaining, Jia Chu finally purchased the puppet for forty-five thousand spirit stones.

Before handing over the spirit stones, Jia Chu suddenly asked, "Where did you obtain this puppet?"

The shabby man's expression immediately became alert.

Jia Chu faintly pointed to the recording light ball beside him: "It's just a routine inquiry. You don't have to say if you don't want to."

"However, if there are any problems with this puppet later on, we will still find you."

Chapter 1340: Misty Starry Sky Journey

"The Xuan Shang Immortal Boat's fleet travels across the Star Sea. If we truly want to find someone, even if they flee to the desolate lands at the edge of the Star Sea, they cannot escape," Jia Chu said in a calm tone, exuding a subtle aura of dominance and confidence.

Even the Xuan Immortal Boat elders like Lu Yuzhi, ten thousand years later, couldn't help but straighten their backs and show a proud look upon hearing this.

The shabby man in the image, upon hearing this, trembled slightly and quickly waved his hands: "No, no, no. Let's explain all these troublesome matters together. I, this person, fear trouble!" Saying this, the shabby man took out a cucumber from nowhere.

While recalling, he bit into it with relish.

"This thing was given to me by someone I saved out of kindness back then, as a token of gratitude for saving his life. He said it could 'Guard against disaster and misfortune.'"

"I don't know the exact meaning, but I guessed that perhaps it could block disasters for its owner in critical moments, so I happily accepted it." The shabby man paused while speaking, wiping the juice from the corner of his mouth.

"That's what I thought. However, a while ago, I was almost beaten to death by those debt collectors, and this thing didn't do anything at all..." The man burped, speaking with a look of misfortune.

Jia Chu chuckled upon hearing this: "It's useless, yet you sold it to our Xuan Shang Immortal Boat?"

"It's not that it's useless, it's just that it's not for saving lives," the shabby man corrected Jia Chu.

"Although this puppet is useless to me, your Immortal Boat travels the Star Sea, and you will always encounter cultivators who need it. Then, if you tenfold the price and resell it, you'll definitely make a fortune. Besides, with your Immortal Boat's connections, even if you're unlucky and can't find a buyer, you'll still run into one or two fools, right? You won't be stuck with it..." the shabby man tried his best to persuade.

And looking at Jia Chu's expression, he didn't seem to care much about the profit or loss of this transaction from beginning to end, and had already decided to buy the puppet.

Lu Yuzhi sighed with some emotion: "Jia Chu's way of doing things is truly that of a standard Immortal Boat merchant. For the ancient Xuan Shang Immortal Boat that traversed the Star Sea, spirit stones were just numbers. Even short-term profits and losses were not that important..."

"What's truly important is the abundance of the Immortal Boat's secret collection, and the increase in bargaining chips against True Immortals," Zhong Daogong's voice suddenly came from outside the small building.

Before his voice had finished, he had already appeared inside.

"Elder Zhong." Everyone bowed in greeting. Zhong Daogong returned the bow, but his gaze fell on the scene in the room.

Because of Zhong Daogong's arrival, the recording of the scene was temporarily paused.

"You're actually free to come over?" Li Fan asked with a smile. Zhong Daogong, as the chief of the Immortal Severing Tower, managed all the major and minor affairs of the Immortal Boat, and naturally didn't have as much free time as other elders to visit Li Fan's courtyard frequently.

"Just now, while Yu Zhi was reviewing the documents, I also discovered some interesting things. Let's continue watching..." The recorded image continued to play.

At the end of the transaction, besides the agreed-upon forty-five thousand spirit stones, Jia Chu also gave the shabby man an additional five thousand spirit stones.

"Brother Jia, what's the meaning of this?" While asking this verbally, the man didn't hesitate to quickly pocket the five thousand spirit stones, lest the other party go back on his word.

Jia Chu smiled peacefully: "It's just incidentally inquiring about the information of the injured person you saved back then. If this puppet can truly be sold at a high price in the future, we might continue to acquire it. Let's keep the contact information for future reference." The shabby man, having received the spirit stones, was very amenable: "It's just this? Then no problem!"

"I remember, what was that person's name. Oh, right, Sun Piaomiao! He's not a native cultivator of our Carefree Realm, but a cultivator from [Xuanhuang]. He came by traversing the Star Sea. Just as he was about to arrive, he encountered a Star Sea anomaly called [Heavenly Whale Breaching the Surface], and although he narrowly escaped death, he was heavily injured and fell from the sky."

"If I hadn't been moved by a sudden impulse of kindness and taken good care of him, he would definitely not have survived in his condition back then," the shabby man said proudly.

"Xuanhuang Realm, Sun Piaomiao..." The image ended with Jia Chu's whisper. The name Sun Piaomiao caused a stir among the elders of the Immortal Boat.

"This name sounds familiar. I seem to have heard it somewhere?"

"Sun Piaomiao, Sun Piaomiao..." In fact, the moment Li Fan heard the name, his heart also trembled.

Because Sun Piaomiao was the ancestor of the Medicine King Sect in the Xuanhuang Realm. Sun Piaomiao had once traveled across myriad realms, leaving behind a travelogue and recording information on eighteen other cultivation worlds.

Among them were Carefree and Xuan Shang. Li Fan looked at Zhong Daogong, who had suddenly appeared, and asked, "The interesting thing you mentioned, is it this Sun Piaomiao?" Zhong Daogong nodded and gently waved his hand, and phantom images of three items instantly appeared before everyone.

"According to the records left by the Immortal Boat, ten years after the puppet transaction, Sun Piaomiao visited the Xuan Shang Immortal Boat and, together with the Immortal Boat, pursued the Star Sea anomaly [Meteorite Hail]."

"Meteorite Hail was one of the extremely rare anomalies in the Star Sea at that time. Countless giant crystal-like meteorites roared forward like a torrential rain from the darkness. They shattered all obstacles in their path. The collision created dazzling sparks and ice mist, sweeping out a terrifying storm of intertwined cold and heat along its path. Even being brushed by the edge of this storm was a world-ending disaster for a cultivation world," Zhong Daogong briefly explained the Star Sea anomaly of Meteorite Hail.

"Although Meteorite Hail was extremely dangerous, in the core of countless ice meteor swarms, a peculiar substance called [Abyssal Ice Dust] was often born. It is said that just a single speck of this substance could freeze an entire ordinary-sized cultivation world. And the power unleashed when the ice bursts had the might to almost cleave the heavens and earth."

"So, were they successful in their pursuit?" Li Fan asked, engrossed in listening.

"There is no record in the Profound Immortal Boat. However, from my guess, they must have successfully found some [Abyssal Ice Dust]. Sun Piaomiao took some, and left behind three items as bargaining chips. As for the rest, it was probably taken by the Shang Immortal Boat later," Zhong Daogong's tone was full of regret.

Li Fan nodded, not surprised. After all, the Shang Immortal Boat, as the de facto victor back then, had taken almost all the near-immortal powers from the Immortal Boat.

According to Zhong Daogong's description, the explosive power of Abyssal Ice Dust was no less than that of a True Immortal, so it was normal for it to be chosen by the Shang Immortal Boat.

The key was these three items left by Sun Piaomiao.

"I don't recall seeing these items in the Hundred Wonders Immortal Record secret treasure before? Could they have also gone to the Shang Immortal Boat?" Li Fan asked with a frown.

Zhong Daogong smiled: "Not at all. These three items are still in our Profound Immortal Boat's collection. However, what you visited earlier was only the outer layer of the secret treasure. These items should be in the second layer." Li Fan did not get angry, but instead teased: "It sounds like there's a third and fourth layer."

"The deepest part is the third layer. You also know about the theft by outsiders back then, but these are just necessary preventive measures," Zhong Daogong said calmly, without the slightest embarrassment.

Li Fan did not dwell on the matter any further, his gaze falling on the three relics left by Sun Piaomiao. Their style was very similar to that of the dangling puppet.

One was a gray bird with a broken wing, its wings broken, yet it still tilted its head and chirped. The second was a three-branched tree, with its branches ending not in leaves, but in countless miniature trees.

As for the third item, it was something Li Fan was very familiar with. It was a small cauldron, which, judging by its appearance, looked almost identical to the Medicine King Cauldron of the Medicine King Sect!

"Sun Piaomiao doesn't seem like an unparalleled powerhouse. Yet, the items he gifted actually contain the power to resist the high wall..." Li Fan's tone was enigmatic.

Zhong Daogong said solemnly: "Sun Piaomiao lived in an era when the immortal path was not severed. There are even records of True Immortals descending to the mortal world. Although based on the records of Sun Piaomiao's activities with the Immortal Boat back then, his strength was only at the peak of Dao Integration, it cannot be ruled out that he concealed his strength." Li Fan nodded slightly.

He did not reveal his own speculation. Sun Piaomiao's ability to traverse the Star Sea alone and return safely was undoubtedly due to his formidable strength.

But he certainly did not ascend to immortality. In the long ancient history of the cultivation world, the records of Xuanhuang cultivators ascending to immortality had all been inexplicably erased, and no trace could be found.

This is what is meant by True Immortals having no name. Perhaps only those like Mo Rubin, who experienced the transition between the old and new eras, could remember the matter of Grand Master Miaofa of the Nine Refinements Sect ascending and perishing through oral tradition.

Firstly, the descendants of the Medicine King Sect never mentioned the ascension of their ancestor Sun Piaomiao to immortality. Even Sun Piaomiao's final fate was unclear.

Did he live out his natural lifespan, die accidentally, or disappear inexplicably? The records of Sun Piaomiao only lasted until his return from traversing the Star Sea.

After that, there was no further information. Secondly, Sun Piaomiao was not only recorded in the Medicine King Sect's records.

Many scriptures in the Xuanhuang Realm mentioned him, this peerless powerhouse who pioneered the Medicine King lineage with his benevolent healing.

His existence was not erased.

"When Sun Piaomiao traversed the Star Sea back then, he intended to travel further, but he discovered the special nature of the star field where the Xuanhuang Realm was located and eventually returned..."

"Was it unwillingness, or inability?" Just as Li Fan was deep in thought, Zhong Daogong spoke again: "Sun Piaomiao left behind these three items, similar to the dangling puppet you chose earlier. Although the Immortal Boat has carefully examined them, no specific features have been found. However, since they all originated from this Sun Piaomiao, perhaps they hide some secrets..." Li Fan did not reply. The other elders were becoming restless.

"Then hurry up and check!" Li Fan said indifferently to Zhong Daogong. Zhong Daogong smiled slightly: "With your contributions during this period, I believe no elder will object to you entering the second layer of the Hundred Wonders Immortal Record secret treasure." Not long after, Li Fan followed the elders into the second layer of the Hundred Wonders Immortal Record secret treasure.

Compared to the first layer, this space was significantly smaller. All the treasures were sealed within orbs of light.

The orbs were of various colors, floating in the air. The protective measures were not formations, nor restrictions, nor True Immortal scripts.

Li Fan squinted at the myriad orbs of light, faintly sensing a breath of life from them.

"These orbs... are alive?" Zhong Daogong nodded and praised: "Your intuition is truly sharp!"

"That's right. The guardians of the second layer of the treasure vault are a miraculous life form: the Celestial Star Light Lotus. This life form was extremely rare even when the Star Sea flourished in the past. Its dreamlike radiance enveloped half the Star Domain, weaving into the shape of a dreamlike lotus. When the flower bloomed, the Star Domain was bathed in brilliant light; when the flower fell, the Star Domain plunged into silent darkness."

"Every time a world in the Star Domain is destroyed, lotus seeds are formed within the light lotus. For billions of years, this cycle has repeated... The light clusters before you were formed in this way." As Li Fan listened to Zhong Daogong's explanation, the magnificent scene of the ancient Star Sea seemed to appear before his eyes.

"The Shang Immortal Boat took away many treasures back then. This Celestial Star Light Lotus is one of the most valuable remnants."

"Treasures are sealed within the lotus seeds and cannot be easily removed. If you want to forcibly take them..." Zhong Daogong snorted coldly: "Unless the entire Celestial Star Light Lotus is destroyed! This spiritual creature resides within the Star Sea. Having survived countless calamities, its life still persists. Destroying it would require immortal power!"

"Moreover, we have tested, and even the power of True Immortal scripts cannot damage it in a short time." The elders of the Immortal Boat were clearly very confident in the protection of this Celestial Star Light Lotus.

However, a thought flashed through Li Fan's mind: "In my previous life, under the Myriad Things Return to Void Great Array, this Celestial Star Light Lotus didn't last long either."

"Now, I don't even need to use immortal formations; the Descending Dust Finger can destroy it. However, destroying it is easy, but extracting the contents within the lotus seeds is indeed somewhat difficult." The elders of the Immortal Boat naturally did not know Li Fan's dangerous thoughts. Unitedly, they carefully opened the orb containing Sun Piaomiao's three relics.

Their gazes converged on the three treasures. Li Fan's heart stirred; he sensed a similar "Returning to True" anomaly from the three-branched tree as he had from the dangling puppet.

However, he did not voice it, and together with the elders of the Immortal Boat, he observed carefully. The broken-winged gray bird and the second Medicine King Cauldron seemed to contain no special power.

"Guard against disaster and misfortune... approximates a projection of the Dao. Sun Piaomiao is indeed not simple."

"And this ability was not passed down to the Medicine King Sect." Li Fan's eyes flickered, suppressing the impulse to "Returning to True" absorption.

"Elders, have you discovered anything?" Zhong Daogong asked after observing for a long time.

"I can't see anything strange, but indeed, these items give me a very peculiar feeling." Lu Yuzhi's statement was echoed by the other elders.

If they hadn't known about the abnormality of these three items, they wouldn't have found anything wrong upon first glance.

But if they observed them after knowing, then various inconsistencies would arise.

If only one or two people felt this way, it could be explained as an illusion. But with more than ten elders present feeling the same way... then it was definitely not just an illusion.

Chapter 1341: The Reason for World Destruction Back Then

"A superior method of concealment. Only those who deliberately search for these items and know that they might hide secrets will notice their abnormality. While in the eyes of others..."

"They are merely ordinary objects." Everyone present vaguely understood.

"If not for Brother Li's chance encounter, who saw through the secret of the puppet, even after a thousand years, our Immortal Boat might not have discovered the peculiarity of these items," Lu Yuzhi exclaimed.

"The problem now is that we know they are strange, but we cannot find a way to decipher their secrets."

"Heh heh, don't worry. If we can comprehend True Immortal scripts, can't we deal with these things? Could it be that Sun Piaomiao is even stronger than True Immortals?" The elders of the Immortal Boat were very confident in themselves.

And their talent was indeed not to be underestimated. After observing continuously for seven days, someone actually discovered the anomaly in Sun Piaomiao's relics.

"Everyone, please look at this small cauldron," said Mo Yinfeng of the Immortal Severing Tower, who was usually silent and focused solely on his research.

"Previously, the Immortal Boat's multiple inspections and identifications concluded that it was a high-grade alchemy treasure, even equipped with a Grotto-Heaven space that could generate spiritual energy and cultivate spiritual plants and crops on its own. But..." Mo Yinfeng said, then cast a 【Reveal】 script, engulfing the Medicine King Cauldron.

As if falling into a hazy mist, tangible lines, thick and thin, emerged from the mist surrounding the Medicine King Cauldron.

They tore through space and flew in different directions, disappearing from everyone's observation within moments.

"This... the Medicine King Cauldron is not unique? It's still connected to beings in the Star Sea?!" The other elders of the Immortal Boat were all shocked.

Li Fan also narrowed his eyes. Because among everyone present, only he realized that one of the lines from the Medicine King Cauldron's mist was heading towards the Xuanhuang Realm.

And the others...

"Most of them are heading towards the Remnant Realm Great Wall. But there are still two or three going to a certain place in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea!" The elders discussed amongst themselves.

"Zhong Elder's interpretation of the Tai Jia picture seems more logical."

"True Immortals play chess, and the worlds descend like pieces."

"If that's the case, what was the purpose of setting up this game? And who is the final winner?" This led to even greater doubts in everyone's minds.

"Let's not delve too deep into matters involving True Immortals for now. What we know now is that this gray chess piece is likely an artifact formed by a True Immortal who refined a world. Even without the augmentation of immortal spiritual power, it can be considered half an immortal artifact."

"And it's a complete set. Those gray chess pieces that have lost their eligibility to compete are already so miraculous. It's hard to imagine what the final black and white twin worlds on the chessboard would be like!" Lu Yuzhi said with yearning.

"Heh heh, don't forget, the Immortal Realm has long since been destroyed. Even the chess player might have perished, let alone those on the chessboard. They have likely disappeared along with the Immortal Realm. On the contrary, these gray chess pieces that left the game earlier have coincidentally survived in the form of artifacts." ... The elders of the Immortal Boat discussed spiritedly.

Finally, after half a day of discussion, they reached a preliminary consensus. Since the essence is a world, they would refine it using methods for dealing with worlds.

The elders nominated Jian Dao Sheng, Zhong Daogong, and four other elders from the Dao Proving Academy, a total of five people, to merge their minds and refine it together. Li Fan was not included among them.

To avoid causing Li Fan any displeasure, the elders of the Immortal Boat specifically explained. Although Li Fan had earned the trust of the elders, he had only joined the Immortal Boat a short time ago.

The most important reason was his "approaching end of lifespan." If he were to participate now, he would perish within twenty years. After his death, it would be necessary to re-sacrifice it.

Wait. ... Li Fan waved his hand, feigning indifference. He stared intently at the gray chess piece being refined by everyone in the center of the field.

"This item is Sun Piaomiao's hidden contingency. If there are any abnormalities during the refining process, it would mean that Sun Piaomiao is still alive in this world..." Li Fan mused inwardly.

However, he was disappointed. The refining process by the elders of the Immortal Boat was surprisingly smooth. Soon, after being refined, the gray color of the chess piece seemed to fade slightly.

But ultimately, the gray color did not completely disappear.

"Did Sun Piaomiao truly perish?" A doubt flashed through Li Fan's mind. He suppressed it for now and asked Zhong Daogong and the others about their feelings.

"Marvelous. The orderly world heavenly law seems to have been tempered by a heavy hammer and reforged. Such a technique is truly divine!"

"It's not just forging a form. It has even forged hundreds of possible futures. After refining it, we can manipulate it and transform it at will among these forms..."

"Uh, this transformation likely requires a large amount of energy. Spiritual energy is not enough to support it."

"I tried, and even the power of True Immortal scripts is insufficient," Nangong Lie's tone was filled with regret.

As if they had obtained a novel treasure, the elders of the Immortal Boat rejoiced and refined the gray chess piece, transforming it into a form most suitable for the current Immortal Boat.

Bang! Bang!

Bang! Like phantom heavy hammers striking the gray chess piece. This originally small object gradually expanded in its spatial structure.

It directly covered the outer shell of the Immortal Boat. Under Li Fan's gaze, the Immortal Boat seemed to have grown a layer of gray, hard keratin.

This layer of keratin not only provided protection but also continuously supplied spiritual energy and resources to the Immortal Boat.

"With the protective shell of a world, our Immortal Boat's defensive capability has increased by more than double. The stability has also been qualitatively improved."

"We no longer need to worry about even a single True Immortal script's original power spreading causing a devastating blow to the Immortal Boat!"

"The vitality accumulated in the gray chess piece over ten thousand years has now been transferred to the Divine Tree."

"The effect is very significant! At the very least, for the next hundred years, without special circumstances, the Divine Tree will no longer need to absorb food..." ... The elders of the Immortal Boat were all overjoyed.

At this moment, Li Fan suddenly said coldly: "Elders, with such a great harvest this time, are you not going to give up on your plan to cross the high wall?" The lively scene instantly turned cold.

The elders instinctively avoided Li Fan's gaze. Finally, Zhong Daogong stepped forward to appease him: "You don't need to worry."

"Crossing the high wall is a strategy we decided on long ago and will not change due to material abundance. You can rest assured of this."

"However..."

"The more preparations, the better. Based on the mutual sensing between these gray chess pieces, there are at least eleven other identical existences in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea."

"Even just one of them has brought about earth-shattering changes to our Immortal Boat. If we gather the complete set of chess pieces..." Zhong Daogong's gaze was sharp.

"What do you think, Daoist friend? At that time, we might not even need other assistance; just the layered outer defenses alone could directly break through the high wall!"

"Moreover, the directions indicated by the sensing are clear. Even if we were to traverse the entire Star Sea at our speed, it would take no more than three years. At the same time, we will not neglect our other preparations during the journey..." Zhong Daogong provided a reasonable explanation.

Li Fan pondered for a moment, then nodded slightly, having implicitly agreed. The previously awkward atmosphere then returned to normal.

"In that case, let's not delay any longer. Let's set off immediately."

"I am also very curious about what will happen after collecting this set of gray chess pieces," Li Fan said calmly.

The elders looked at each other, then held a simple discussion meeting. They first reached a consensus: "The Profound Immortal Boat definitely cannot be moved easily."

"Indeed, with the current strength of the hull, it is not enough to withstand the pressure below the high wall."

"Collecting the gray chess pieces does not require all of us to move. It would be a burden. It would be much more convenient for us to go alone."

"Using sensing to command from afar and guide the direction. Others can disperse to various parts of the Star Sea to collect the gray chess pieces."

"This should be more efficient."

"At least three people per group, to prevent accidents."

"There are seven or eight of them not far from our current location, seemingly near the Remnant Realm Great Wall. Let's collect those first." ... While the elders were discussing, Li Fan also said in a deep voice: "I can also contribute my humble efforts. With the amplification of my escape technique, even traversing the Star Sea would only take a day's time." This time, the elders of the Immortal Boat had no reason to refuse Li Fan's proposal.

The preliminary consensus reached was that the first task of retrieving the gray chess pieces would be undertaken by Li Fan, Nangong Lie, Lu Yuzhi, and four elders from the Dao Proving Academy named Xu Gongding.

"First, investigate the situation. If you encounter any danger, prioritize your own safety," Zhong Daogong instructed before their departure.

Chapter 1342: The True Immortal Sets Up the Game

"This [Myriad Manifestations Yin-Yang Diagram], its usage is simple. It's like a mirror that can reveal the essence of things on the blank scroll. Of course, it might not be so direct. Perhaps it requires further contemplation..."

"But no matter what, it's much easier than directly studying this gray chess piece," Zhong Daogong said, his lips moving as he slowly unrolled the blank scroll.

Like a long dragon, it floated above everyone's heads.

"Go!" The gray chess piece slowly flew towards the Myriad Manifestations Yin-Yang Diagram. The moment it approached, it vanished from everyone's sight.

And on the blank scroll, as if drops of paint had fallen, bizarre and strange scenes began to appear.

It was like a storm of paint merging, different colors interweaving, colliding, and separating.

"It can analyze objects from the Immortal Realm. Could this Myriad Manifestations Diagram also be from the Immortal Realm?" Li Fan asked casually, watching the constantly changing images on the scroll.

"No, no. This Myriad Manifestations Diagram is undoubtedly an artifact from the lower realms." Jian Dao Sheng smiled and answered Li Fan's question.

"This diagram was acquired by the Xuan Shang Immortal Boat from a fallen cultivator."

"This cultivator's ancestor was a disciple of the renowned [Star Dao Sect] in the Star Sea. In ancient times, the Star Dao Sect's influence spanned several neighboring cultivation worlds. Their sect's profound techniques were said to be able to control the Dao of the Star Sea, surpassing even the Tai Jia Divine Technique you taught us." Li Fan raised his eyebrows: "How did such a magnificent sect decline?"

"That remains an eternal mystery. Not to mention now, even back then, there were various theories, and no accurate answer. Some say they offended True Immortals from the upper realms, and the upper realms sent immortal punishment. Others say the Star Dao Sect attempted to refine and control the Heavenly Dao of the Star Sea, and were ultimately backlashed by the Star Sea..."

"In short, for some unknown reason, the high-ranking officials and pillars of the Star Dao Sect seemed to have disappeared overnight. The remaining lower-level disciples, who were unaware of what had happened, waited for a short while, and realizing that the situation was irrecoverable, scattered like birds startled from a bush. Before leaving, they didn't forget to loot all the movable objects from the sect."

"Within just a month, this once renowned great sect in the Star Sea collapsed." Jian Dao Sheng sighed with emotion.

"This Myriad Manifestations Yin-Yang Diagram was a treasure of the Star Dao Sect back then. It is said that in the Star Dao Sect's Star Communication Hall, where Star Dao cultivators connected with and perceived the Heavenly Dao of the Star Sea, such Myriad Manifestations Yin-Yang Diagrams were hung everywhere."

"Every time the Heavenly Dao of the Star Sea communicated with cultivators, it was like an invisible ink brush leaving traces on the scroll. Over time, these scrolls thus depicted the Heavenly Dao of the Star Sea within them." ... Hearing this, Li Fan couldn't help but interrupt: "Even if it's a depiction of the Heavenly Dao of the Star Sea, how could it manifest objects from the upper realms?" Although he pretended to be ignorant with his question, Li Fan actually had the answer in his heart.

Zhong Daogong smiled: "The Star Sea, the lower realms, are the foundation of all things."

"The projection of the Great Dao ultimately manifests here. Even if the Immortal Realm is high above, it is not an illusion. From bottom to top, although we cannot see its true form, we can still glimpse the shadow of the Dao." Li Fan, hearing this, seemed to be encountering this theory for the first time, his mind appearing greatly shaken, falling into deep thought.

The evolution of the Myriad Manifestations Yin-Yang Diagram continued. Like an invisible True Immortal, wielding a brush and flying dragon, splashing ink and painting a vigorous script.

Finally, the color storm settled into a picture, and calm returned. Li Fan looked at the painting above their heads, his pupils contracting.

It was not a realistic style with detailed descriptions, but rather an abstract, rough sketch presenting the outlines.

A towering figure occupied nearly half the frame, looking down from above. Its face was indistinct, and it extended long arms.

Below the figure, there seemed to be a chessboard. What was placed on the chessboard were not gray chess pieces, but individual cultivation worlds, each vastly different from the others.

Those seemed to be just clusters of merged colors, and upon attempting to probe them, countless scenes of different beings actually appeared in their minds.

They were born, aged, died, cultivated, and warred within their worlds. The stories of these beings, along with the cultivation world itself, formed a chess piece on the board.

Boom... After displaying before everyone for a few breaths, this Myriad Manifestations Yin-Yang Diagram suddenly, as if blown by a strong wind, not only did the scroll itself shake violently, but

even the pigments on the canvas were swept away by the storm. The picture gradually disintegrated. The gray chess pieces also slowly retreated from the painting.

"The decomposition of the Myriad Manifestations Diagram has reached its limit." Zhong Daogong said in a deep voice, and together with the other elders, solemnly put away the Yin-Yang Myriad Manifestations Diagram.

Afterwards, they looked at the gray chess piece quietly floating in the air, falling into an eerie silence.

"If my understanding is correct, this gray chess piece seems to be a cultivation world after the extinction of its life and the withering of all things? And that towering figure should be a True Immortal from the upper realms?" It was Li Fan who spoke first.

No one responded. After a while, Jian Dao Sheng shook his head and offered his opinion: "Although the analysis of the Myriad Manifestations Diagram points directly to the essence of the matter, it would not be so superficial."

"The Medicine King Cauldron, almost self-contained, can generate spiritual energy and cultivate herbs and spiritual plants on its own..."

"How could a world devoid of life achieve that?" Zhong Daogong agreed: "Precisely. I believe that what is depicted, or rather, the world that acts as a chess piece, does not represent death. But rather, it means it has lost its role on the chessboard and has completed its mission, becoming a discarded piece." Saying this, intersecting horizontal and vertical lines appeared, and black and white chess pieces were successively placed.

Then the black pieces surrounded and ate the white pieces. These eaten white pieces left the chessboard and had no chance to return.

They transformed into gray, no longer participating in the contest between black and white pieces.

"Elder Zhong's interpretation seems more logical." Among the elders of the Immortal Boat, their communication was less about scheming and more about speaking frankly.

Zhong Daogong's interpretation of the Myriad Manifestations Diagram's image gained the approval of the vast majority of the elders.

"True Immortals play chess, and the worlds descend like pieces."

"If that's the case, what was the purpose of setting up this game? And who is the final winner?" This led to even greater doubts in everyone's minds.

"Let's not delve too deep into matters involving True Immortals for now. What we know now is that this gray chess piece is likely an artifact formed by a True Immortal who refined a world. Even without the augmentation of immortal spiritual power, it can be considered half an immortal artifact."

"And it's a complete set. Those gray chess pieces that have lost their eligibility to compete are already so miraculous. It's hard to imagine what the final black and white twin worlds on the chessboard would be like!" Lu Yuzhi said with yearning.

"Heh heh, don't forget, the Immortal Realm has long since been destroyed. Even the chess player might have perished, let alone those on the chessboard. They have likely disappeared along with the Immortal Realm. On the contrary, these gray chess pieces that left the game earlier have coincidentally survived in the form of artifacts." ... The elders of the Immortal Boat discussed spiritedly.

Finally, after half a day of discussion, they reached a preliminary consensus. Since the essence is a world, they would refine it using methods for dealing with worlds.

The elders nominated Jian Dao Sheng, Zhong Daogong, and four other elders from the Dao Proving Academy, a total of five people, to merge their minds and refine it together. Li Fan was not included among them.

To avoid causing Li Fan any displeasure, the elders of the Immortal Boat specifically explained. Although Li Fan had earned the trust of the elders, he had only joined the Immortal Boat a short time ago.

The most important reason was his "approaching end of lifespan." If he were to participate now, he would perish within twenty years. After his death, it would be necessary to re-sacrifice it.

Wait. ... Li Fan waved his hand, feigning indifference. He stared intently at the gray chess piece being refined by everyone in the center of the field.

"This item is Sun Piaomiao's hidden contingency. If there are any abnormalities during the refining process, it would mean that Sun Piaomiao is still alive in this world..." Li Fan mused inwardly.

However, he was disappointed. The refining process by the elders of the Immortal Boat was surprisingly smooth. Soon, after being refined, the gray color of the chess piece seemed to fade slightly.

But ultimately, the gray color did not completely disappear.

"Did Sun Piaomiao truly perish?" A doubt flashed through Li Fan's mind. He suppressed it for now and asked Zhong Daogong and the others about their feelings.

"Marvelous. The orderly world heavenly law seems to have been tempered by a heavy hammer and reforged. Such a technique is truly divine!"

"It's not just forging a form. It has even forged hundreds of possible futures. After refining it, we can manipulate it and transform it at will among these forms..."

"Uh, this transformation likely requires a large amount of energy. Spiritual energy is not enough to support it."

"I tried, and even the power of True Immortal scripts is insufficient," Nangong Lie's tone was filled with regret.

As if they had obtained a novel treasure, the elders of the Immortal Boat rejoiced and refined the gray chess piece, transforming it into a form most suitable for the current Immortal Boat.

Chapter 1343: Forging Immortal Realm Fragments

The Great Wall of Remaining Realms. Li Fan urged his wooden sword phantom, carrying the three Immortal Boat elders including Nangong Lie, and moved slowly within it.

"Brother Li's escape technique is truly heaven-defying. Not only is it incredibly fast, but it also mitigates the effects of the reverberating Star Power. With this protection, our search for the gray chess pieces should be much smoother," Nangong Lie lamented.

Lu Yuzhi also chimed in, "Indeed. Otherwise, just resisting this terrifying suction would consume the majority of our strength." Xu Gongding remained silent, surveying the void outside, diligently searching for traces of the gray chess pieces.

As they belonged to the same set of artifacts, their senses could not pinpoint exact locations. They only vaguely indicated a general vicinity.

Within the Great Wall of Remaining Realms, countless world fragments were scattered. And the gray chess pieces, in the form of artifacts, were hidden within these world fragments.

To find the target among them was like searching for a needle in a haystack. Especially since their divine senses were also affected here, making the exploration process even more arduous.

Li Fan now personally experienced it and finally understood the difficulty faced by the Heavenly Physician. It took thousands of years to collect fragments of the Heavenly Law Realm and it was still not completed, which was understandable.

Fortunately, the mysterious power used by the gray chess pieces for concealment was very peculiar. Knowing that there were hidden secrets within, one could detect their abnormality at a glance.

There was no need to worry about missing them during the search. The luck of the four was indeed quite good, finding the first lost chess piece only three days later.

It lay quietly on the ruins of the earth, a rusty bronze war chariot. Five divine and handsome warhorses stood proudly in front of the chariot.

The surface of the chariot was covered with sword and knife carvings, showing signs of weathering. Instead of transforming the chariot back to its original form in the void, the four first collected and preserved it, to be handled by the Immortal Boat Elder Council after returning to the Immortal Boat.

With the success of the first attempt, the few were greatly encouraged. Over the next ten days, the wooden sword phantom continuously shuttled through the Great Wall of Remaining Realms.

They also found three more disguised chess pieces. These were a broken sword, a seemingly ordinary wine gourd, and a small wooden boat.

"I can't go on. I need to rest a bit," just as they were about to press on, Li Fan suddenly turned pale and said weakly.

Lu Yuzhi realized, "We were careless. Such a heaven-defying divine ability must consume a great deal. Brother Li has been using it continuously these past few days, it's no wonder you've reached your limit..." Nangong Lie asked with concern, "How long does Brother Li need to rest? Without your escape technique's augmentation, our search efficiency will be too slow relying on just us!" Li Fan said solemnly, guaranteeing, "Don't worry, I'll recover in three days. The depletion of spiritual energy is secondary; it's mainly the immense drain on my mind." Lu Yuzhi first praised Li Fan greatly, then took the opportunity to inquire about the principle behind this escape technique.

The elders of the Immortal Boat had long coveted Li Fan's miraculous wooden sword phantom flight technique.

However, Li Fan, who was always generous in sharing his knowledge, was extremely tight-lipped about this wooden sword divine ability. He refused to reveal any details.

The elders of the Immortal Boat had not given up, trying to inquire whenever they had the chance. And this time, Li Fan's secrecy attitude actually showed a slight loosening.

"My escape technique is condensed from two supreme Dao intents. The first is the sword. The momentum of moving forward relentlessly, brave and forward-moving."

"As for the second..." Li Fan paused, whetting the curiosity of the three. Then, he unhurriedly continued, "It is [The ends of the earth are within a咫尺]! The ends of the earth and the corners of the sea are but a咫尺 apart. Crossing the Star Sea is indeed infinitely long, but if it's just a咫尺, then one step is enough!" Next, he explained the details of these two supreme true intents to the three elders.

The three elders listened attentively, nodding repeatedly, lost in deep thought. Li Fan, meanwhile, revealed an inexplicable smile.

During the process of teaching, he did not twist or falsify. With the knowledge of the Immortal Boat elders, any fabrication would be easily seen through.

Li Fan had merely hidden the most crucial part: that the core of the escape technique divine ability was the [Transformation of True and False].

What sword Dao, what "The ends of the earth are within a咫尺." Without the core blessing of the True and False Transformation, it was impossible to achieve what Li Fan could, directly ignoring the various crises and True Immortal residual powers permeating the Star Sea during flight.

Li Fan did this precisely to use this intentionally "leaked" divine ability to interfere with the minds of the three Immortal Boat elders. And Li Fan's objective, naturally, was the four gray chess pieces that had been found.

Perhaps due to psychological trauma from the past transmission of techniques, even though the four who went out to search for chess pieces this time were theoretically impossible to betray the Immortal Boat.

The Immortal Boat still formulated the rule of four people jointly guarding them. The four each controlled a fragment of the round ball. The four fragments combined to form a sealed storage space, where the searched chess pieces were stored.

Only by working together could the four take out the sealed chess pieces. In other cases, they could only observe and supervise.

Originally, the attention of the four-person group was mostly cast on these chess pieces from time to time. But with Li Fan inadvertently and proactively revealing the mystery of his supreme escape technique, the other three elders inevitably got distracted, pondering everything Li Fan had taught.

Therefore, Li Fan had more time to study the mysteries of these gray chess pieces without being noticed by the other three.

"Transforming from the gray chess piece form again requires a large amount of energy support."

"Spiritual energy is not enough, True Immortal power is also not enough."

"But the Immortal Boat has, without a sound, transformed it into its current armored keratin form..."

"It seems there are still treasures in the second and third layers of the Immortal Boat's secret collection!" Li Fan snorted inwardly, his divine sense sweeping across the four gray chess pieces.

"Forged from the [world], perhaps they are chess pieces that have lost their value and turned gray."

"If the Heavenly Physician's 'Book of Mending the Heavens' compares the world to a person, then the existence that forged this set of chess pieces treats the world as a [tool]."

"Although people and tools are different, the fundamental principle is the same."

"The prerequisite for modification is complete control over its basic mechanism..." Sensing the four creations before him, Li Fan silently chanted the 【Book of Mending the Heavens】.

Then, the characters in it, after Li Fan's comprehension and modification, transformed into another chapter.

"However, it's like copying a gourd and drawing a picture, changing the principles of the human body to methods of forging tools."

"Although some parts were forcibly transformed and nonsensical, the vast majority..."

"Is effective!" Li Fan's eyes brightened. In his vision, the four artifacts in the sealed space also changed.

The specific forms of the broken sword, war chariot, etc., no longer existed. Instead, they were replaced by intersecting bright lines.

These lines all originated from a common starting point. Outside the lines, there were even more numerous and complex dim lines.

"The starting point of the lines is the original gray chess piece form."

"And those dim lines represent the other switchable forms of the chess pieces."

"So beautiful..." Li Fan was almost mesmerized. He had once directly faced the principles of heaven and earth of the Xuanhuang Realm.

The horizontal and vertical lines that constitute the myriad different beings and scenes in heaven and earth, intertwined and spanning between heaven and earth.

Originally, Li Fan thought the principles of heaven and earth that make up the Xuanhuang Realm were already complex enough. But compared to what was unfolding before his eyes...

"What constitutes the Xuanhuang Realm is only a small part of it."

"The rest was forged by True Immortals using the laws of the Immortal Realm, reaching beyond the world!" Li Fan's heart was inexplicably shaken.

"Observing these, perhaps one can vaguely touch upon a corner of the former Immortal Realm!" Li Fan closed his eyes, feigning rest.

In reality, it was to conceal the overwhelming waves that suddenly surged within his heart. The Immortal Realm suffered the 'Calamity of Dao Annihilation,' and had been destroyed for over ten thousand years.

Everything about the former Immortal Realm had become a thing of the past. Even the True Immortals of yesteryear had now become extremely rare existences.

They were hunted by civilizations beyond the high wall. But now, Li Fan had discovered fragments of the Immortal Realm, forged and hidden using special methods.

Or rather, to describe them as fragments was an exaggeration. It was merely that during the forging of lower realm cultivation worlds, some higher Immortal Realm law fragments were incorporated.

However, for those in the latter days after the immortal path was severed, this still held extremely extraordinary significance.

Especially for Li Fan.

"The fragments of law contained within a single chess piece are too scarce."

"But what if it's a complete set of chess pieces?"

"Sun Piaomiao founded the Medicine King Sect. Judging purely from the medical principles, his understanding of the world and the Great Dao might not be inferior to the Heavenly Physician."

"I can sense the subtleties of this chess piece, and Sun Piaomiao had no reason not to; especially since he left secrets for future generations in such a peculiar way through his travelogues."

"If the fragments of the Immortal Realm can truly be reproduced through fusion..." A flash of inspiration suddenly struck Li Fan.

"Perhaps this is a 'preserving the fire' plan in a sense?" But only for a fleeting moment did Li Fan naturally think of the use of these gray chess pieces.

"My Xuanhuang sublimation plan was already quite perfect."

"If we can add some fragments of the former Immortal Realm..."

"The laws of the Immortal Realm are like heavenly pillars, strengthening the principles of the Xuanhuang Realm's heaven and earth."

"Ascending to a true immortal domain is just around the corner!" Li Fan rapidly deduced the possibilities. The results made his heart throb with excitement.

"Moreover, if the Immortal Boat were truly to gather all these gray chess pieces, I'm afraid they would lose their ambition to cross the high wall." Li Fan, with his discerning eye, naturally saw that Zhong Daogong's previous words were merely to appease them for the moment.

"However, this matter requires someone to cooperate with my act." After deliberation, his plan was set.

Another day passed. Li Fan pretended to have barely recovered his condition. He vaguely sensed the locations of Yin Shangren and Bai Hua, then urged his wooden sword phantom and flew away.

Coincidentally, his direction of travel overlapped with the sensing area of one of the chess pieces, so he did not arouse the suspicion of the Immortal Boat elders.

"Hmm? This place in the Great Wall of Remaining Realms seems to have changed a bit?" While flying, Li Fan suddenly said with feigned surprise.

As soon as he said this, the three Immortal Boat elders who were secretly comprehending the Dao were startled awake. They carefully investigated, then all shook their heads in confusion: "Could it be that Brother Li's excessive consumption has caused a misperception?"

"We don't feel anything out of the ordinary!" Facing the three's confusion, Li Fan still maintained a solemn expression.

But he couldn't articulate any specific reason. The three Immortal Boat elders exchanged glances and couldn't help but become nervous.

Li Fan's inexplicable nervousness didn't seem like an act. Sometimes, cultivators' groundless vigilance could be even more accurate than active investigation.

The four dared not be careless, their minds highly tense, guarding against potential disasters. However, it might indeed have been Li Fan's overthinking.

A period of an incense stick passed, and nothing unusual happened. The tense three elders finally began to relax again.

"It seems Brother Li was worrying unnecessarily!" Nangong Lie said with a smile. Li Fan sighed, "Perhaps it is so!" and continued searching in the Great Wall of Remaining Realms.

Not long after calming down, Li Fan was startled again.

"No! Be careful!" In his alarm, the Immortal Boat elders' auras suddenly surged. The True Immortal script 'Seal' was still prepared.

However... Scanning their surroundings and waiting for a long time, there were still no changes. The three elders stared at Li Fan.

Li Fan said somewhat sheepishly, "I don't know why today, I've been feeling restless, as if disaster is imminent..."

"Perhaps everyone doesn't know, my spiritual intuition for premonition has always been extremely accurate. It was precisely by relying on this keen spiritual intuition that I managed to avoid multiple fatal calamities..."

"I have to believe it!" Li Fan said with a wry smile. Lu Yuzhi comforted him, "It's alright, being vigilant is good. Perhaps it's because you were exhausted from traveling before, and haven't recovered yet. Why don't you rest a bit longer?" Li Fan shook his head, "Stopping makes me feel even more uneasy. Let's continue." The three elders had no choice but to go along.

They could only continue following Li Fan. In the following time, after experiencing Li Fan's two staged alarms, the three Immortal Boat elders also became utterly exhausted.

Nangong Lie seemed hesitant to speak. Lu Yuzhi was carefully considering, about to advise Li Fan to rest properly. Unbeknownst to them, Li Fan had already found Yin Shangren and Bai Hua.

And successfully, secretly contacted them. Soon, their communication was completed. In front of the three Immortal Boat elders, Li Fan's expression changed dramatically again, "Be careful!" The Immortal Boat elders, this time not only did not guard, but instead laughed in anger, "Brother Li, you..." Before he could finish speaking, an extremely terrifying deathly aura instantly surged forth.

It was as if they had personally fallen into a scene of world destruction. All four were slightly stunned. At the same time, the vitality within them began to drain at an extremely rapid pace.

While everyone was in a daze, the sealed sphere that they jointly guarded, containing the four gray chess pieces, inexplicably lost control.

It fell out in the void.

"Not good!" Nangong Lie's expression changed drastically, and he instantly woke up. The 'Town' character of the ancient script was immediately unleashed towards the direction where the deathly aura was attacking.

However, the opponent seemed to have anticipated his actions and had already fled that area. Nangong Lie's attack missed.

Lu Yuzhi also woke up at this time. He checked the situation of his companions rapidly draining vitality, his expression greatly changed.

Chapter 1344: Li Fan's Self-Defense

The Immortal Boat elders were far from as young as they appeared. Over thousands of years, they had repeatedly reversed their own aging through ancient scripts.

Returning to youth, maintaining youth. But reversal could not be equated with eternal life. Old age still quietly accumulated within them.

Now, Lu Yuzhi and the others, having suffered Yin Shangren's deathly aura attack, had the accumulated aging from past years erupt violently.

The consequence was that the effect of the death script was far better than imagined. The three Immortal Boat members' hair instantly turned snow-white.

Deep wrinkles quickly claimed their faces. An aura of decay emerged from within their bodies.

"Ancient!" Lu Yuzhi, having regained his senses, forced himself to calm down and quickly inscribed an ancient character in the void with slightly trembling hands.

The target was not an unknown enemy, but themselves!

Under the power of the "Ancient" character, the rapid aging of their bodies was somewhat alleviated, but it was only a temporary fix.

What was emanating was not genuine True Immortal script, but a crude imitation.

The extent of the reversal of their past states was far less than the speed of their aging. And the surrounding deathly aura storm continued to intensify. If this continued, all four present would soon turn into mere white bones!

Under the combined influence of the deathly aura storm and the ancient script, Li Fan and Xu Gongding also abruptly woke up.

Their expressions were terrified, at a loss what to do.

"Leave quickly!" Lu Yuzhi desperately held on, shouting at Li Fan. Li Fan's already black and white streaked hair had completely turned snow-white.

However, he looked in the direction where the sealed sphere had disappeared, struggling: "But those gray chess pieces..."

"If life is gone, then nothing remains!" Lu Yuzhi's eyes also held reluctance, but he still roared.

With a roar like venting, the wooden sword phantom unsheathed, temporarily alleviating the onslaught of the deathly aura.

The sword light flashed, carrying the four away from the terrifying deathly aura that filled the sky. As their figures disappeared into the horizon, Bai Hua and Yin Shangren slowly revealed their true forms.

Suddenly unleashing such a large-scale deathly aura storm was not easy for Yin Shangren, who had just absorbed the Yin-Yang Orb.

As if out of control, the vortex in his black and white eyes spun faster and faster. Yin Shangren had no choice but to close his eyes to calm himself.

As for Bai Hua, following Li Fan's instructions, she emitted golden light after golden light, sealing the sphere they had just snatched.

"I wonder who those three companions of the Saint Master were?"

"The characters they struck, seem to be the same as the residual True Immortal power in the Star Sea..."

"But speaking of it, the Saint Master's acting is truly superb. If he hadn't actively transmitted a message for us to cooperate, I would have almost been deceived by him." Bai Hua's expression was subtle, and she continuously set up the sealing formation in her hand. ... Outside the Great Wall of Remaining Realms.

The Immortal Boat一行, having escaped disaster, still looked shaken. Even though they had escaped the range of the deathly aura storm, a small amount of deathly aura still remained within their bodies.

It was continuously reducing their lifespan.

"Let's return to the Immortal Boat first." Lu Yuzhi, at this moment, had become extremely frail, like an old man in his seventies or eighties in the mortal world, seemingly approaching the end of his life.

Even these short four words were spoken with all his remaining strength. The condition of the others was not much better.

Especially Li Fan, who could only shake his head slightly, indicating that he was too weak to use his escape technique divine ability anymore.

Among the four, only Nangong Lie's condition was relatively better. He helped support everyone, flying towards the Immortal Boat while releasing a distress signal.

After a cup of tea, Zhong Daogong arrived with seven Immortal Boat elders in a hurry. To prevent it from being a diversionary tactic, they did not mobilize all their forces, even though the lives of four elders were in danger.

Zhong Daogong and the others who came to support looked at the four dying individuals enveloped in an aura of decay and senescence with solemn expressions.

However, knowing that saving their lives was the priority, they did not immediately pursue the reasons for the incident but first took the four back for treatment.

Through the genuine True Immortal script "Ancient" and the efforts of many life-extending treasures, the four were finally temporarily pulled back from the brink of danger.

Three days later. Li Fan stood in the small courtyard, his expression somewhat dazed.

"Only about ten years of lifespan left."

"Just one trip out, and half of it is gone!" Lu Yuzhi smiled wryly upon hearing this, "My situation is similar to yours. Less than half a century..." Nangong Lie and Xu Gongding's expressions were also extremely grim.

With such a major incident, the Elder Council would surely investigate meticulously. They truthfully recounted their experiences.

Zhong Daogong comforted them in every possible way and tried various methods to extend their lives, but the effects were minimal.

"Hmph!" The small courtyard fell silent for a moment. Suddenly, Nangong Lie slammed the stone table in the courtyard, "We suffered a great calamity, and by extension, the four gray chess pieces were also stolen..."

"It's simply an utter humiliation! Elder Zhong should have immediately led everyone to, not to mention seeking justice, at least find out the specific details of the culprits."

"But now, so much time has passed, and he hasn't made any moves. When asked, he speaks eloquently. 'We need to plan carefully'... Bah! I think he's just scared after seeing our impending doom!" Nangong Lie vented his dissatisfaction.

Lu Yuzhi frowned, "However, Elder Zhong's words are not entirely wrong. That deathly aura storm was indeed too bizarre and terrifying. Even after pondering it continuously for the past few days, I haven't found a way to confront it directly. The four of us were severely injured, and the Immortal Boat cannot withstand another similar blow in a short period." Li Fan also nodded in agreement, "Although it's helpless, it's indeed the case. This deathly aura appeared too suddenly; it was clearly aimed at our gray chess pieces."

"Don't forget, the Immortal Boat still has one piece. Perhaps the unknown enemy will storm the gates at any time..." Li Fan's words made everyone present fall silent.

The Immortal Boat always prioritized the greater good. They could still distinguish between immediate grudges and the overall interests of the Immortal Boat.

"The enemy is aggressive!" Lu Yuzhi sighed, his eyes full of worry. To deal with this unknown formidable enemy, the Immortal Boat soon convened a joint meeting of all elders.

Li Fan, as an eyewitness to the event, also attended. Zhong Daogong first gave a summary statement: "The opponent is definitely after the gray chess pieces. Now, the gray chess piece we still hold has lost some of its connection to the other pieces, presumably due to the four pieces being abducted by the opponent."

"However, there are two points of doubt."

"First, how did they clearly pinpoint the location of Elder Lu Yuzhi's group?"

"Second, by what method did they conceal our gray chess piece's connection?"

"As for the deathly aura storm used for the attack..."

"After searching the Immortal Boat's records, we have found some possibilities." Zhong Daogong's words immediately attracted everyone's attention.

Seeing Dao Sheng clear his throat, he began to explain, "Deathly aura and vitality are opposites, yet they depend on each other. After the great destruction, the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, where most regions have fallen into silence, theoretically should not contain such a massive amount of deathly aura."

"Therefore, we speculate that the origin of this deathly aura should be from a certain cultivation world."

"And to use deathly aura as an offensive weapon in a consumable manner, the amount of deathly aura they possess... is definitely unimaginable." Seeing Dao Sheng's tone was somewhat heavy.

Upon hearing this, the Immortal Boat elders quickly raised their doubts.

"The Star Sea calamity occurred long ago, and all realms were destroyed long ago. Where could they have gathered so much deathly aura?"

"It's completely illogical!" Zhong Daogong sighed, "This is the crux of the problem. Perhaps this deathly aura was accumulated by the opponent from ancient times, before the Star Sea suffered its calamity."

"The opponent is likely a civilization that has survived to this day, just like us."

"They could predict and evade the attack of True Immortal scripts; they understood the gray chess pieces made by True Immortals very well and caught us off guard. From beginning to end, the opponent never revealed themselves..."

"Judging from all their actions, this unknown civilization is stronger than our Immortal Boat, not weaker." Zhong Daogong finished speaking, and the meeting then fell into a strange silence.

All the elders frowned, lost in thought. Li Fan broke the silence, sighing, "Unexpectedly, this seemingly dead and silent Star Sea, besides the Immortal Boat and Da Qi, actually has other brilliant civilizations." The Immortal Boat elders' gazes all converged on Li Fan.

Seeing Dao Sheng narrowing his eyes, he asked, "Fellow Daoist Li, could the unknown enemy that attacked you be your hometown, Da Qi?" This was also a question on the minds of all the Immortal Boat elders.

At this moment, seeing Dao Sheng ask, everyone stared intently at Li Fan, wanting to hear his answer.

"Da Qi?" Li Fan clearly did not expect Dao Sheng to ask this.

"How could..." He first subconsciously denied it. However, soon, as if realizing something, he frowned and fell into thought, his words suddenly stopping.

After a long while, Li Fan spoke again, saying softly, "First of all, one thing I can be sure of is that there are absolutely no surveillance methods from Da Qi on me, and I would never be an insider for Da Qi..."

"I cannot produce any evidence. But after spending so much time with you all, you must understand my character." Li Fan paused, said proudly, "To put it bluntly, if I were truly a spy from Da Qi, and my target was the gray chess pieces, I could have stolen them and escaped directly with my escape technique that traverses the Star Sea when I helped rebuild the Immortal Boat's defensive formations."

"There would be no need for all this trouble." The meeting became even quieter. No one retorted. Most people remained silent at Li Fan's words, but a few still looked at Li Fan with lingering suspicion.

Li Fan's self-defense continued, "Moreover, when we were attacked, we were planning to proceed deeper into the Great Wall of Remaining Realms to collect more. If I were truly an insider, why wait until after finding more before notifying them to capture them all?"

"After the deed was done, why would I return to the Immortal Boat?"

"At that time, the other three Immortal Boat elders were all extremely weak. If it weren't for my escape technique helping them, they would have likely perished. Wouldn't it have been better to make them disappear without a trace, doing things without anyone noticing? Why go through so much trouble?" Li Fan spoke more and more angrily.

He coldly snorted, "If it weren't for the fact that my last moments with the Immortal Boat were intertwined, making me regard the Immortal Boat as my final destination, I wouldn't be wasting words with you all."
