"If I wanted to leave, who among you could stop me?" No one among the Immortal Boat elders could refute. After all, that wooden sword phantom could ignore almost all restrictive powers, which was truly unbelievable.

Zhong Daogong hurriedly stepped forward to smooth things over at this moment. He chuckled and appeased, "Fellow Daoist Li, there's no need to be so agitated. We absolutely trust you, but we know too little about Da Qi behind you, so it's natural to be suspicious." Li Fan's anger somewhat subsided.

He pondered for a moment and answered cautiously, "Da Qi has numerous factions internally. I am only familiar with the research of my master's lineage..."

"However, I have indeed never heard of anyone in Da Qi possessing such a vast amount of deathly aura."

"Moreover, my face carries some renown in Da Qi. If the opponent were truly from Da Qi, they would never dare to attack me! Otherwise, even if I died, my master would not let him off!" Li Fan said with great certainty.

Zhong Daogong nodded slightly, temporarily stopping the interrogation.

"Regarding the origin of this attack, I have some conjectures. I will share them for everyone to discuss."

"The gray chess pieces have been lying peacefully in the Immortal Boat's secret treasury for so many years without any incident. Now, they are suddenly attacked..."

"Excluding the possibility of someone deliberately leaking information, perhaps it was the aggregation of too many chess pieces that attracted attention." Zhong Daogong said loudly, "This unknown civilization might have been searching for traces of the gray chess pieces for many years. But lacking gray chess pieces in hand, they couldn't search by sensing."

"But during our collection process, the accumulation of numbers allowed them to find traces. Thus, we were exposed and attacked..." The elders present all fell into deep thought.

Hearing this, it sounded rather bizarre, but it was the only plausible explanation at present.

"If my guess is correct, then what we need to worry about now is the attack of this unknown civilization on the Immortal Boat." Zhong Daogong's tone suddenly changed.

"The gray chess pieces can sense each other. The one that transformed into the Immortal Boat's outer keratin armor can undoubtedly always provide the opponent with the general location of the Immortal Boat..."

"This is clearly unacceptable to us." The Immortal Boat elders' expressions changed drastically.

"The urgent matter is to resolve this."

"Either, strip off the keratin armor and separate it from the Immortal Boat, and simply abandon the gray chess piece."

"Or, find a way to block the sensing between the gray chess pieces." Zhong Daogong summarized. The Immortal Boat elders looked at each other, falling into a debate for a time.

Chapter 1345: Divine Arts Can Equalize the Heavens

"A gentleman does not stand under a dangerous wall. Keeping the vital lifeline of the Immortal Boat constantly exposed to enemy surveillance is never a wise move!"

"That's right. Although these gray chess pieces are True Immortal creations, they are not worth us taking such a great risk."

"How foolish! This set of chess pieces must hide a great secret. Benefits always come with risks. How can we give it up so easily!"

"Indeed, it is too much of a shame to discard it just like that. I have a plan. Since the..."

Chapter 1346: Bearing the Burden of the Immortal Realm

Just as the Profound Immortal Boat had previously speculated.

Each gray chess piece was forged from a world.

Li Fan looked at the four spinning chess pieces before him, and scenes flashed through his mind.

These were the scenes of these four dead worlds before they were transformed: endless icy lands stretching for thousands of miles; on endless plains, dynasties established by different cultivators stood tall; a terrifying sword mark splitting the world, surrounded by sparse Sword Dao Sects of enlightenment; a vast blue ocean covering the entire world, with terrifying storms raging year-round, raising giant waves thousands of feet high, destroying everything on the sea surface. Beings could only survive underwater...

The names of the four worlds also appeared in Li Fan's mind along with these illusions.

"Crystal Extreme, Hundred Qiu, Sword Gate, Abyss Sea."

Although the scenes were different, these four worlds were all full of life. However, at a certain moment, unimaginably terrifying power descended.

Everything in the world fell into stillness.

Boom! Boom! Boom!

Amidst the impact sounds like heavy hammers striking, all life was instantly annihilated. Only the world itself could survive this destructive blow.

Like a block of iron heated and melted into liquid, after cooling and hammering, it was forged into a sword. The four disparate worlds also slowly underwent inexplicable changes in their form and essence amidst the rumbling.

The chaotic illusions disappeared. Finally, they returned to the four incessantly spinning gray chess pieces.

"Saint Master, this..." It was not only Li Fan who sensed the extraordinariness of the gray chess pieces. Yin Shangren's rapidly spinning black and white eyes also indicated his inner turmoil.

"Forging chess pieces with worlds. The power of True Immortals is truly extraordinary." Li Fan glanced faintly at Yin Shangren, then sighed softly.

"True Immortals, chess pieces?" Yin Shangren, catching the two keywords, trembled slightly. He immediately said, "Indeed, my premonition was correct. The Yin-Yang Orb I absorbed before might also be related to True Immortals!"

Li Fan looked at Yin Shangren, waiting for him to continue.

Yin Shangren paused, seemingly organizing his thoughts. Then, he said calmly, "The moment I saw these four chess pieces, I felt a sense of familiarity in my heart. Not that I had seen them before, but a familiarity of the same species. Like how I see those world ghosts..."

Li Fan's eyes flickered. After pondering for a moment, he nodded, "The immense deathly aura and vitality contained within the Yin-Yang dual orbs are likely beyond the control of us cultivators."

Yin Shangren continued, "But these... chess pieces, while I feel familiar with them, I also instinctively feel a sense of fear. As if in a strict hierarchy, they are high above!"

"I also feel that although the power of life and death no longer exists in these worlds, they still have a great attraction for me. It's as if swallowing them would bring me immense benefits! Benefits even greater than the Yin-Yang dual orbs!" Yin Shangren's tone gradually became hazy. Before the greed in his eyes could become uncontrollable, he closed his eyes in time.

After a long while, the seductive whispers of celestial demons seemed to disappear from his ears, and he gradually returned to normal. However, he dared not look at the four chess pieces again.

Li Fan naturally knew the source of the fear and temptation that the gray chess pieces brought to Yin Shangren.

"Originating from fragments of Immortal Realm laws..."

Silently circulating the mutated version of the Book of Mending the Heavens, in Li Fan's vision, the four chess pieces once again transformed into intersecting horizontal and vertical lines.

These were the principles of worlds that had been forged and transformed.

Li Fan compared the similarities and differences between them.

Tens of thousands of years have passed, the Star Sea was destroyed and then revived. But the Great Dao principles that formed the foundation of the worlds had not changed much.

Through countless reincarnations, Li Fan had gained a profound understanding of the principles of heaven and earth in cultivation worlds. After several observations and comparisons, he truly discovered the parts within these four chess pieces that did not belong to the "lower realm."

They seemed indistinguishable from the lines representing ordinary heavenly principles.

In reality, they were higher-level replacements and transformed newborn forms of lower realm laws.

Although they were merely fragments used for construction, in Li Fan's eyes, they were as brilliant as the most dazzling gems.

If the principles of heaven and earth in the lower realm were like a low mountain less than a hundred meters high. Then the parts originating from the Immortal Realm within these four chess pieces were like magnificent mountain ranges stretching for hundreds of miles. All-encompassing and full of vitality.

The two were fundamentally incomparable.

Moreover, whether by coincidence or not, the fragments of Immortal Realm laws contained within these four chess pieces were different from each other.

"The laws contained within each chess piece are like a puzzle piece. When fully integrated, perhaps it will form a complete picture."

"There are thirteen gray chess pieces in total, corresponding to the twelve Dao mark information left by Sun Piaomiao back then."

"In that case..."

"There should actually be thirteen. The Medicine King Cauldron of the Medicine King Sect, inherited since ancient times in the Xuanhuang Realm, is not within the sensing range."

Thinking of this, Li Fan couldn't help but look outside the Xuanhuang Realm.

The Medicine King Cauldron of the Medicine King Sect was still struggling near the Immortal Ruins, not yet returned to the Xuanhuang Realm.

"It's not far from its falling date, so I'll wait. There's no need to risk going to the Immortal Ruins to retrieve it."

Li Fan thought this, then reached out and took a chess piece.

As expected, a peculiar sensation surged into his heart.

In the darkness, he felt the approximate location information of the gray chess pieces in the Star Sea.

"There are four here in total."

"There's one on the Profound Immortal Boat."

"There are four more within the continuous Great Wall of Remaining Realms."

"There are three more; one of them is located in the Sea of Relic Treasures."

"The remaining two..."

A flicker of strangeness flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

Because he discovered that these two gray chess pieces were actually located within the Xuanhuang Realm!

"Their original worlds were likely used by the Heavenly Physician and Transmitting Dharma to repair the Xuanhuang Realm."

"Looking at this place, I'll be back soon." Li Fan ordered Yin Shangren and Bai Hua. Disregarding their astonishment, the wooden sword phantom flashed, and Li Fan first headed towards one of the locations indicated by the sensing.

It was the bottomless Cangwu Abyss.

The Cangwu Abyss, located in the southwest corner of the Xuanhuang Realm, was like a giant rift in the Xuanhuang Realm. Its currently explored depth had reached three hundred thousand feet.

Within it, layers of strange scenes, events, and objects were distributed.

The former perilous land, to Li Fan, who could now traverse the Star Sea, hardly posed any threat.

Following the sense, all the way down.

Li Fan looked at the scenery constantly floating upwards in his vision and suddenly felt a sense of "The various things within the Cangwu Abyss should come from different destroyed cultivation worlds. They are piled here, like a temporary storage place for the materials during the process of stitching together the Xuanhuang Realm."

"If anything is missing during the repair of the world, it can be taken from here at any time. One day, this Cangwu Abyss will be filled. However, by then, the Xuanhuang Realm will have perhaps been reborn."

Li Fan observed the strange sights within the abyss with great interest.

The closer the abyss got to the surface of the Xuanhuang Realm, the greater the influence of the Xuanhuang Realm's life aura. This fused to create various unique landscapes, such as the Forest of Spirit Language, the Puppet's Ravine, and the Lost City.

But the deeper he went, the closer the world fragments floating around were to their original appearance.

After the world's destruction, it was a scene of desolation.

There were even traces of True Immortal power remaining on some world fragments.

"It can be seen as a small-scale Great Wall of Remaining Realms."

"However, its stability is not as high as the true Great Wall of Remaining Realms. The residual True Immortal power that accumulates from time to time will still erupt..."

"No wonder this is a forbidden zone for cultivators."

When the sword shadow descended, reaching a depth of five hundred and thirty thousand feet underground, Li Fan once again sensed the existence of the 'Immortal Suppressing Power' within the abyss.

"This Immortal Suppressing Power should be the pressure exerted on cultivators who intrude into the Cangwu Abyss after the Heavenly Physician imitated the Great Wall of Remaining Realms and constructed the Cangwu Abyss."

"To be precise, the 'momentum' of the Cangwu Abyss, from top to bottom, is a stepped increase. Although the height difference is extremely limited, and the overall height does not exceed the Xuanhuang Realm by much, it is extremely obvious to the cultivators within the abyss."

"Only by reaching the corresponding cultivation level can one safely survive in the abyss layer with the corresponding 'potential height.' Otherwise, it would be like a mortal accidentally entering the Immortal Realm, arriving at a height that does not belong to oneself, only to be crushed."

Having deciphered the mystery of the Cangwu Abyss, Li Fan had also roughly located the position of the gray chess piece wandering within this area.

In a pile of scattered ruins that looked like they had been chopped by thousands of sword marks, Li Fan found the fifth gray chess piece.

It was a majestic and imposing Qilin stone statue, half-fallen on the ground, just as it was during the destruction ten thousand years ago.

The stone statue was a pair, but the other one Li Fan checked was just ordinary stone.

"It's well hidden."

Li Fan crushed the stone statue, restoring it to the form of a chess piece, and then looked around.

Based on the appearance of the surrounding ruins, Li Fan also restored the world to which it originally belonged.

"Seven Fiends Realm. Seven types of fiendish qi raged within the realm, permeating all parts of the world. They could even take form and harm people. Therefore, all buildings in this realm were equipped with large and small beasts of different types to absorb and suppress them."

"It was once a cultivation world of considerable scale. The cultivators of the Seven Fiends Realm were infected with fiendish qi from birth, and every move they made carried the characteristics of the seven fiends. Even peerless geniuses possessed all seven..."

"Unfortunately, time flows. Everything has long since turned to dust." Li Fan sighed lightly and left the place, shaking his head slightly.

The remaining gray chess piece within the Xuanhuang Realm was buried underground in Tianyun Prefecture.

There were no unusual phenomena at the location.

"It should be that with the progress of the Xuanhuang Realm's fusion, fragments originally within other world fragments have now completely entered the Xuanhuang Realm."

"Just like the fragments from the Heavenly Law Realm at the bottom of the Congyun Sea. Under normal circumstances, they would be buried deep under the Congyun Mountain as the evolution progresses."

Without alarming anyone, Li Fan smoothly obtained it.

Up to this point, Li Fan had collected six gray chess pieces.

Returning to the Great Profound Minor World's Dao Platform, he placed these six chess pieces together.

As the number approached half, the influence between these chess pieces seemed to become stronger.

They rotated around each other faster and faster.

Li Fan saw that during this high-speed rotation, the lines representing the principles of the world were attracting each other and slowly merging.

And the fragments of Immortal Realm laws slowly approached, filling in the puzzle.

Even though it was only six out of thirteen, it was enough to support a qualitative change.

The Immortal Realm law puzzle was like a void appearing in the center of the ocean.

The worlds that had fallen into stillness were like calm seawater.

The moment the void appeared, the seawater surged in uncontrollably.

The six worlds, like wet, distorted planes, were sucked into the fragments of the Immortal Realm law puzzle like liquid.

According to the template designed by the puzzle, a new world was presented.

Blue sky, white clouds, rolling green grasslands.

A seemingly ordinary scene of a mortal grassland.

Li Fan felt an unprecedented vastness between heaven and earth.

The small green grass growing vigorously on the ground also contained unimaginable vitality!

"Immortal Realm?!" Li Fan was greatly shocked upon glimpsing the scene within the merged chess pieces.

"No, it's just a fragment of a former Immortal Realm. Perhaps 'Immortal Domain' is a more appropriate description."

"And this Immortal Domain is still incomplete."

There was clearly something that should exist between the Immortal Realm grasslands and the sky.

However, because the remaining seven gray chess pieces were missing, it could not be fully presented.

Li Fan stared blankly at the scene in the eye circles, a sense of regret suddenly arising.

It was as if he had personally smashed a priceless treasure, and the urge to repair it surged uncontrollably from all parts of his mind.

If Li Fan did not have the Immortal Heart Curse protecting him, and had not experienced so many similar situations, he would have lost control at this moment and rushed to chase after the remaining chess pieces.

But now, Li Fan ignored this temptation.

As the fusion was completed, only one chess piece remained in the field. It was no longer gray, but flickered with seven-colored light from time to time. Its size even expanded by a circle.

Li Fan reached out and solemnly collected the six-in-one chess piece.

"En?"

To Li Fan's surprise, the moment he collected this chess piece into his body, he felt as if he were being crushed by countless mountains.

Caught off guard, his body plummeted a few feet.

Fortunately, he reacted in time, and the power of the Xuanhuang World Destruction Transformation revived and circulated, providing a steady stream of power. He managed to withstand it.

"This is... the weight of the Immortal Realm?"

"Even a fragmented Immortal Domain is so difficult for me to bear?"

"If all thirteen fragments are gathered and fused into a true Immortal Domain, with my current cultivation, I won't be able to bear it!"

Li Fan once again felt the terrifying difference between Immortals and mortals.

But at the same time, he was delighted rather than alarmed.

"I was just worried that after the Xuanhuang Realm ascended and reached that state, I wouldn't find an anchor to support that state."

"Now, it seems that if this Immortal Domain is integrated into the Xuanhuang Realm, it will definitely adapt and not easily fall."

"With this Immortal Domain as the core, the Xuanhuang Realm might even ascend higher!"

"Truly, heaven is helping me!" Li Fan couldn't help but feel a little excited.

But soon, instinctively, he began to doubt the origin of these Immortal Domain fragments.

Chapter 1347: The Will of the Immortal Boat

These fragments of Immortal Realm laws appeared at too coincidental a time. Just as he was about to promote the Xuanhuang Realm's ascension towards the Immortal Realm, they were conveniently discovered.

Given Li Fan's personality, it was hard not to be suspicious. Thus, he attempted to slowly untangle the logical threads within.

"The concealment of the chess pieces is truly formidable. The entire Immortal Boat, and the Heavenly Physician and Transmitting Dharma, even after tens of thousands of years and countless direct interactions, have not perceived any abnormality within them."

"The reason I discovered the peculiarity of the chess pieces so easily was entirely due to the guidance of [Returning to True]. Without Returning to True, I would have also regarded them as ordinary objects..." Thinking of this, Li Fan's heart stirred slightly.

"If we only consider this aspect, the chess pieces could indeed be bait specifically targeting [Returning to True]."

"However... there are many things that only Returning to True can sense. For example, [Eternal Remnant Will]. It is purely because the level of Returning to True is too high that all these abnormalities are completely exposed before it."

"I cannot make a hasty conclusion. But it is reasonable to be cautious." Li Fan observed the seven-colored chess piece quietly lying within his body.

The chess piece seemed completely independent of Li Fan. Spiritual energy, divine sense, and other powers flowed through the location of the chess piece without any obstruction.

It was as if it didn't exist at all. And besides the "burden" of the merged Immortal Domain fragments, this chess piece brought no other influence to Li Fan.

"Thirteen gray chess pieces were hidden by Sun Piaomiao in thirteen cultivation worlds he had traveled through. And he recorded their world Dao mark information in his travelogues, passing them down to his descendants."

"But clearly, these chess pieces were not forged by Sun Piaomiao, but by True Immortals of the upper realms. Perhaps in the context of the 'Calamity of Dao Annihilation' erupting, some pessimists prepared these, seeking the resurrection of the Immortal Realm."

"For some unknown reason, they fell into Sun Piaomiao's hands." Li Fan pondered, his thoughts surging.

"During Sun Piaomiao's era, the Immortal Realm had not yet been destroyed, and the immortal path was not severed. Most True Immortals of the Immortal Realm were actively fighting against the Calamity of Dao Annihilation. It is conceivable that against such a backdrop, True Immortals who were pessimists and forged the chess pieces would not be accepted by the mainstream, and could only act in secret. Thus, they secretly passed them down to the lower realms?"

"But for some unknown reason, these backup plans have not been activated to this day. The most likely scenario is that the True Immortal who forged the chess pieces has already perished in the Calamity of Dao Annihilation that destroyed the Immortal Realm."

"Or perhaps..." Li Fan's eyes narrowed, recalling the structure of the Immortal Boat's Myriad Manifestations Yin-Yang Diagram from before.

"The entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea cannot find any black and white chess pieces still on the chessboard. Only these 'discarded' gray chess pieces remain. Perhaps, in some unknown place, beyond this high wall, those black and white chess pieces have already completed the mission of recreating the Immortal Realm?" However, this was merely Li Fan's conjecture, with no evidence to support it at present.

"Regarding these gray chess pieces, Sun Piaomiao must have known more. Sun Piaomiao himself is missing. If there are any clues left in the Star Sea, the most likely place is the Medicine King Cauldron he left behind in the Medicine King Sect."

"Anchoring for fifteen years, 'Starfall Returns to Xuanhuang.' It's coming soon..." Although these chess pieces might hide dangers behind them.

But Li Fan would certainly not give up on the plan to sublimate the Xuanhuang Realm by integrating the Immortal Domain fragments just because of a mere "possibility" of speculation. With the fragments of the Immortal Domain as the foundation, the success rate of the Xuanhuang Realm's sublimation increased significantly.

Li Fan calmed his thoughts and looked at Yin Shangren and Bai Hua. They had also witnessed the entire process of the gray chess pieces merging.

They did not dare to speak, only watched silently. Li Fan did not explain the creation of the Immortal Domain fragments after the fusion of the chess pieces to them.

But they had guessed that these chess pieces, forged from dead worlds, probably played a crucial role in the Xuanhuang sublimation plan.

"I asked you to go to that location in the depths of the Star Sea before; did you find anything?" Since returning to Da Qi, Li Fan had been busy collecting chess pieces and only now finally had some leisure.

Li Fan stared at Bai Hua and asked, In Li Fan's estimation, it should have taken Bai Hua considerable effort to investigate that unknown "high ground." Unexpectedly, she returned not long after and rendezvoused with Yin Shangren to search for Xu Ke's whereabouts.

Bai Hua brewed for a moment and explained, "Perhaps it's my incompetence. I searched for a long time in the direction you indicated, Saint Master, but found no abnormalities. Seeing that it was a waste of time to stay any longer, I had no choice but to give up and search for Xu Ke's whereabouts with Daoist Yin."

"Perhaps that opportunity was not meant for me," Bai Hua sighed. Li Fan nodded and asked again, "Then, have you found any traces of Xu Ke?" Yin Shangren replied, "We have made some progress. We discovered that Xu Ke might have been drawn into a strange zone within the Great Wall of Remaining Realms. The Great Wall of Remaining Realms is the convergence of countless destroyed worlds at the foot of the high wall. Although there are billions of fragments, they are still subtly connected as one."

"We don't quite understand the principle of its formation yet, but perhaps it can be seen as a long rope woven from countless thin threads. And the place where Xu Ke disappeared is a 'node' formed to maintain its self-stability."

"However, just as we were about to further explore that node, we received a transmission from Saint Master." Yin Shangren said with some regret.

"Node..." Li Fan pondered for a moment and continued, "It was also a sudden occurrence, and to obtain the chess pieces, I had to ask you to help me perform a play."

"Those people you saw that day were all from the Immortal Boat civilization on the edge of the Star Sea."

"To avoid exposing the Xuanhuang Realm's existence, I previously disguised myself as a member of the non-existent [Da Qi] civilization and contacted them. The Profound Immortal Boat is extremely adept at deconstructing the power of various True Immortal scripts remaining in the Star Sea, and I also engaged in several exchanges with them using the True Immortal scripts I mastered, so we both gained something."

"During this transaction, we accidentally discovered the existence of gray chess pieces within the Immortal Boat's treasury."

"These chess pieces are too important for Xuanhuang's sublimation, and I absolutely cannot miss them. Thus, I employed a little trick..." Li Fan casually explained the cause and effect to the two.

"The Profound Immortal Boat is still somewhat useful to the Xuanhuang Realm right now, so avoid contact with them to prevent exposure. Especially since the life and death aura on you is too prominent; anyone who sees you will know you snatched the gray chess pieces," Li Fan said to Yin Shangren.

Yin Shangren and Bai Hua naturally would not side with the Profound Immortal Boat. They just smiled and didn't pay much attention to Li Fan's act of snatching the gray chess pieces.

"The Immortal Boat still has several chess pieces left in the Great Wall of Remaining Realms that have not been collected, all of which can be handed over to me. You should still prioritize searching for Xu Ke's whereabouts first."

"When I have collected all the chess pieces, it won't be far from the final stage of Xuanhuang's ascension," Li Fan instructed.

Yin Shangren's expression turned solemn, and he nodded in agreement. After giving the instructions, Li Fan first used the Great Heaven's End咫尺 Array and arrived at the edge of the Great Wall of Remaining Realms.

The wooden sword phantom shuttled continuously, and it took considerable effort to collect all the remaining four gray chess pieces from this place.

Even with a heaven-defying escape technique, the depths of the Great Wall of Remaining Realms under the high wall were truly fraught with danger.

The fluctuating Star Power, which rose and fell like surging waves, could only be barely offset by Li Fan's wooden sword phantom.

He still had to face the pervasive suction's influence. Coupled with the constant burden of the Immortal Domain, Li Fan's execution of the wooden sword phantom escape technique consumed almost two to three times more energy than before.

Therefore, after collecting the four chess pieces from here, Li Fan's mind and body had become extremely exhausted. However, he had ultimately gained a great harvest.

Li Fan gazed into his body. The four gray chess pieces and the one seven-colored chess piece that had expanded by a circle floated quietly.

They were in opposition. Perhaps because the quantity was too small, these newly acquired four chess pieces only rotated around each other and could not react with the already fused seven-colored chess piece.

"Only two remain. The Profound Immortal Boat, and the Medicine King Sect."

"Once all thirteen chess pieces are in place, if my predictions are correct, a corner of the former Immortal Realm should be recreated." Li Fan's eyes narrowed.

Then, he extended his palm and struck his chest fiercely. With a muffled grunt, his previously tired face became even paler.

Without mobilizing his spiritual energy to heal his injuries, Li Fan maintained his current appearance and slowly headed towards the Immortal Boat.

Approaching the Immortal Boat, without concealing his aura, the elders reacted. Led by Zhong Daogong, they came out to greet him.

"I have not failed in my mission." Li Fan coughed lightly, cupped his hands, and said calmly.

"Thank you for your hard work, fellow Daoist!" Zhong Daogong's expression was solemn, and he actually bowed. Li Fan frowned and dodged, flashing aside.

He coldly snorted and said, "Stop with these pleasantries. Although the ritual wasn't complicated, it took me considerable effort to conceal it from my master and all the Saint Masters."

"I don't know the exact number of people the ritual will encompass, but it should be enough." Zhong Daogong nodded with a smile, "Approximately one hundred million living beings. This is absolutely sufficient to bear the backlash of casting the 'Universal Divine Technique'."

"Since that's the case, there's no need to hide it from me anymore, right?" Li Fan swept his gaze across all the elders present.

"This is not a place to talk. Let's discuss it further after entering the Immortal Boat." The Immortal Boat elders were as cautious as ever.

Everyone entered the deepest pavilion in the Immortal Severing Tower at the top of the Divine Tree. Profound patterns were already carved on the black mysterious jade floor.

Li Fan was no stranger to these symbols. They were part of the Universal Divine Technique ritual. It seemed the Immortal Boat elders were already impatient.

The elders sat according to their respective seats. Li Fan also obtained his position here. With one hundred million living beings as a foundation offering.

Ten million humans, this was an unimaginable number in the Xuan Immortal Boat, where survival resources were scarce and life was dwindling.

Therefore, after Li Fan completed the ritual, coupled with his previous performances, he finally earned the absolute trust of everyone on the Immortal Boat.

"Fellow Daoist, please remain calm."

"Please take your seat first and try the effect of the [Universal Divine Technique]." Zhong Daogong pointed to Li Fan's seat.

Li Fan did not hesitate at all, floating into his seat. The patterns beneath him instantly emitted faint light. After sitting down, Li Fan's vision also changed under the illumination of the faint light.

The positions of the surrounding Immortal Boat elders shifted strangely in space. Originally, they were all sitting on the same plane, but now, in Li Fan's eyes, everyone was distributed in a three-dimensional cube space.

Dispersed and orderly, occupying every part of the cube. And Li Fan was at the center of the cube, the focus of everyone's attention.

Li Fan's expression remained unchanged.

"Vast heaven and earth, ancient and obscure. Originally one entity, all beings are equal..." The chanting of the Immortal Boat elders came.

Ancient and vast. With a hint of strangeness. As the chanting continued, the elders raised their arms one after another.

Using their fingers as brushes, they began to write in the void before them. What each person wrote was not a complete True Immortal script.

It was just a segment of a complex structure. In Li Fan's view, countless moving lines suddenly rose around him.

These lines surrounded him, and as they were constantly perfected, a character 'Jun' (均) slowly took shape.

Boom! Instantly, Li Fan's body trembled. His vision uncontrollably floated upward, eventually stopping at a fixed position.

And here, looking down, the spell structures written by all the elders on different planes, when combined, formed the character 'Jun' (均) on a single plane!

And his body, Li Fan, was suppressed in the center by this 'Jun'! The 'Jun' character was more complex than the 'Hunger' and 'Chaos' characters Li Fan had seen before.

Although not comparable to 'Creation,' it possessed a unique and profound mystique. Under the power of the Universal Divine Technique, Li Fan also slowly felt the changes occurring in his body.

Li Fan even checked the 'Returning to True' panel. His lifespan, which had only been about 10 years left, was actually slowly increasing!

Wisps of black appeared amongst his white hair. Streams of vitality emerged from nowhere, nourishing Li Fan's decaying body.

However, Li Fan was not overjoyed by this sudden increase in lifespan, but cautiously continued to observe [Returning to True].

Only when the incoming vitality gradually depleted and the Universal Divine Technique ritual ended did Li Fan finally relax, except for the change in his physiological age on the panel.

"As expected, a mere 'Jun' character is not enough to affect Returning to True."

"It can only affect the target locked by the Universal Divine Technique, such as the lifespan that was cast on me this time."

"As for other aspects, such as divine sense and cultivation, there were no changes." After carefully inspecting his internal condition, Li Fan drew his conclusion.

Looking at the members of the Immortal Boat Elder Council. Compared to before the ritual, they had all undoubtedly aged.

However, due to the decay of lifespan and its equal distribution among everyone, the effect was not very obvious.

"How do you feel?" Zhong Daogong, representing all the elders, asked. Li Fan heard this, pretended to awaken as if from a dream, looked at his rejuvenated body.

Then, he bowed respectfully to all the elders, expressing his gratitude for this life-saving grace. The Immortal Boat elders all returned the bow.

"From now on, we are family." Zhong Daogong said very solemnly.

Chapter 1348: The Immortal Boat Plunders the Heavens' Merit

"A life-saving kindness is beyond repayment. I would not hesitate to go through fire and water!" Li Fan cupped his hands in response.

As he spoke, Li Fan checked his attributes on the "Returning to True" panel.

His remaining lifespan had skyrocketed from a mere ten years to over five hundred years.

This was enough to demonstrate the formidable power of the "Universal Divine Technique."

"After being subjected to the divine technique, my lifespan should be similar to these Immortal Boat elders."

"Over five hundred years is not a lot, but it's not insignificant either. Most importantly..."

Li Fan meticulously examined his current physical state.

Suddenly, his eyes narrowed slightly: "This extra lifespan is unstable?"

Previously, his body had been healthy and normal, so Li Fan was acutely aware that his current body, forcibly defying fate and extending its lifespan through the Universal Divine Technique, had a noticeably abnormal and rapid aging rate. It was several times faster than normal, and sometimes, it would suddenly and inexplicably decrease.

And as Li Fan observed, the suddenly fluctuating numbers on the "Returning to True" panel undeniably confirmed his guess.

Li Fan did not conceal his change in expression.

Zhong Daogong also noticed Li Fan's confusion: "The Heavenly Dao is inconstant, its flow uncertain. Change is eternal, balance is temporary."

"Balancing the world under heaven is inherently an act against the natural order. I suspect that even a True Immortal's script, if written by a genuine immortal, might not be able to maintain the 'balanced' state indefinitely. Let alone us? So you need not doubt; falling from the 'balanced' state is entirely normal."

"There are two methods to alleviate this. First, by using an authentic True Immortal script of 'Ancient,' a brief regression can slow down the rate of decline."

"Second, you can simply cast the 'Universal Divine Technique' again when your lifespan runs out. In fact, this is precisely what the Immortal Boat Elder Council is doing."

"Sharing our lifespans to extend one individual's lifespan. Everyone helps me, and I also help everyone," Zhong Daogong said with a smile, looking at the surrounding elders.

Li Fan suddenly understood, "Since that's the case, I am relieved."

He sighed and then lamented, "Finally, I understand why the Immortal Boat elders, despite their apparent disagreements, always manage to ensure collective progress on major matters."

"This Universal Divine Technique is truly profoundly mysterious! Even in Da Qi, it would undoubtedly be considered a top-tier divine ability!"

Despite Li Fan's high praise, Zhong Daogong did not show any elation. Instead, a wry smile flickered in his eyes: "It is merely a last resort. Limited by our finite resources, the Immortal Boat's population has always been maintained at a low level. The rate of talent succession is slow. To survive in this Utmost Darkness Star Sea, we must maintain the number of council members."

"Researching True Immortal scripts is also fraught with peril. A slight misstep can lead to being affected by True Immortal power. Quite a few elders have perished this way historically. Yet, it concerns the future and very survival of the Immortal Boat, and we absolutely cannot abandon it."

"Therefore, every elder is the Immortal Boat's most precious asset..."

Li Fan remained noncommittal regarding Zhong Daogong's explanation. He was well aware of the Immortal Boat's secret technique of the "Dao Pill," which allowed them to refine talented individuals and absorb their innate talents.

"It's likely that not a few geniuses have emerged from the Immortal Boat in recent years. Unfortunately, to become a new elder, talent alone is not enough. Immortal Boat elders are, in essence, somewhat similar to mortals in the Xuanhuang Realm. Neither too many nor too few are allowed; a delicate balance must be maintained." Li Fan mused silently, not voicing his thoughts.

After undergoing the Universal Divine Technique, the elders' attitudes towards him subtly shifted.

If Li Fan had previously earned their approval solely through calculated efforts for mutual benefit, then now, the elders genuinely felt a sense of camaraderie.

They truly treated him like "family."

Thus, Li Fan inquired about the "Universal Plan," which required the sacrifice of Da Qi beings.

"Such a vast number of beings are needed to bear the backlash. Who is the true target of the Universal Divine Technique...?"

This time, Zhong Daogong and the others did not hesitate or conceal.

They directly revealed the answer: "Our planned target is precisely..."

"The Star Sea's Origin Consciousness!"

Li Fan's eyes immediately lit up upon hearing this.

"Thanks to fellow Daoist Li's prior teaching of the 'Tai Jia Divine Technique,' we were able to glimpse the vast Star Sea consciousness that is currently recovering."

"Only by personally contacting it can we understand the boundless power of the Star Sea. Its might is not diminished by the annihilation of the Star Sea, and it remains beyond the comprehension of mere mortal cultivators."

"But..." The Immortal Boat elders all wore strange expressions.

Seeing Dao Sheng wave his hand, he displayed before Li Fan a scene of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea in utter desolation.

And in the center of the Star Sea, shining with a brilliant, diamond-like radiance, was the Star Sea's Origin True Will.

"The Star Sea's consciousness is essentially the same as the Heavenly Dao of the cultivation world in the past."

"In ancient times, there were cultivators who achieved unity of heaven and humanity and could partially control the world's Heavenly Dao. Now, by jointly casting the Universal Divine Technique, perhaps we can also share the Star Sea's power!" Jian Dao Sheng said forcefully.

Zhong Daogong stroked his beard and chuckled, "If we can truly balance the Star Sea's power, then crossing the high wall might be within reach, even without the assistance of True Immortal scripts!"

Li Fan frowned, deep in thought.

After a while, he slowly nodded, "Although the high wall blocks the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, that is for beings within the Star Sea. If we were to harness the Star Sea's own power and generate immense tidal waves, perhaps the droplets within those waves could leap over the high wall!"

"Precisely! Only by reaching the height of True Immortals can one cross the high wall. But the Star Sea's power is inherently not inferior to True Immortals! In ancient times, the numerous anomalies that shone in the Star Sea forced even True Immortals to temporarily avoid their path. This shows the might of the Star Sea's power. Even after being affected by the Calamity of Immortals and falling into a state of destruction, its vitality was not extinguished..."

The elders' voices grew increasingly excited.

"It is precisely our perfect target for 'balancing'!"

"If the ritual succeeds, even if we cannot lift the Immortal Boat and leap over the high wall, controlling the Star Sea's power for a time would be enough to create an absolutely safe haven for us within this Utmost Darkness Star Sea!"

...

After Li Fan listened to the Immortal Boat elders' plan, he couldn't help but clap his hands and exclaim, "Brilliant! Brilliant!"

"This is what is called 'coveting the heavens' merits for personal gain.' However..."

Li Fan's tone suddenly shifted, and he frowned, "I have communicated with the Star Sea's consciousness using the Tai Jia Divine Technique before. As cultivators, we are truly like ants before it. And now, this group of ants dares to covet power as if to stand on equal footing..."

Li Fan's expression turned somber as he looked at everyone, "The heavens have their wrath, and the Star Sea will also have its fury. Even if it succeeds, we will likely face the Star Sea Origin Consciousness's mad retaliation. Not to mention if it fails."

"At that time, perhaps it won't be our Immortal Boat that can withstand it!"

"Failure means a glorious death... Isn't the risk a bit too great?"

Li Fan had thoroughly integrated into the scenario of having gained five hundred years of lifespan, his thoughts and actions no longer as extreme as before.

Zhong Daogong nodded, agreeing with Li Fan's viewpoint, "You are right. The Immortal Boat is not yet at a point where it must stake everything. That is why you went to Da Qi."

Zhong Daogong was full of confidence.

Li Fan expressed some confusion, "Simply relying on ten million human lives can appease the Star Sea's wrath?"

Zhong Daogong smiled, his eyes gleaming, "Not by using humans. But by using worlds!"

"If it were merely a matter of human numbers, even multiplied several times, it might not make much difference to the Star Sea's Origin Consciousness. But if, using the lives of these ten million humans as a foundation, decorating them into a world, and presenting it in the name of a world, to draw away the Star Sea's power..."

"The Star Sea's backlash will be greatly weakened!" Zhong Daogong asserted confidently.

"This is due to the Star Sea's own mechanisms. Based on the traces recorded by the Immortal Boat in the past, we are almost certain of this point."

Li Fan quieted down, contemplating Zhong Daogong's words.

"Nurturing and evolving cultivation worlds is an inherent fundamental law of the Star Sea. Even if a cultivation world becomes powerful enough to influence the Star Sea, the Star Sea will not directly destroy it."

"At most, it will manifest in various forms of Star Sea anomalies."

"Star Sea anomalies are far easier to deal with compared to the wrath of the Star Sea's origin!" Jian Dao Sheng preemptively provided the answer, not giving Li Fan a chance to ponder independently.

Zhong Daogong's eyes showed pride, "Historically, most Star Sea anomalies have been recorded by our Immortal Boat, and we have basic methods to deal with them. Now that the Star Sea is merely recovering from destruction and has not yet reached a stage of rebirth or mutation, the possibility of new Star Sea anomalies emerging..."

"Is slim."

"Even if there is a small chance of new anomalies appearing, they are likely related to the residual True Immortal power pervading the void. With True Immortal scripts in hand, overcoming such storms should be no problem."

The Immortal Boat elders were all very confident.

The atmosphere in the hall quieted for a moment.

Finally, Zhong Daogong spoke again in a deep voice, "Of course, to prevent the worst-case scenario, when we perform the Universal Divine Technique, we will leave the Profound Immortal Boat and only take some necessary supplies."

"Even if our plan fails, it will be enough to preserve the Immortal Boat. With the seeds we leave behind, the Immortal Boat can continue to exist for another hundred or thousand years."

...

As it seemed, although the Profound Immortal Boat's plan to balance the Star Sea appeared reckless, in reality, the Immortal Boat had meticulously considered all aspects.

If successful, they would 'command half the Star Sea's power,' and even with dangers lurking beyond the high wall, they would have a place to reside.

If they failed, they would not lose everything.

Compared to their previous strategy of attempting to ram the high wall with the entire Immortal Boat's strength, this was vastly superior.

And this was the change the "Tai Jia Divine Technique" taught by Li Fan had brought to the Immortal Boat.

It had to be said that the Immortal Boat elders were indeed not obstinate beings.

They were able to perfectly accept new knowledge and even apply it quickly.

"Then, when do we act?"

"Since we can balance the Star Sea's power, theoretically, the stronger the Star Sea recovers, the better, right?" Li Fan stated.

However, he quickly negated his own judgment, "No, if the Star Sea becomes stronger, the power of its future retaliation will also be stronger. If we are too greedy, we might exceed the threshold we can bear..."

Zhong Daogong agreed, "Therefore, we must choose an optimal time."

"The Immortal Boat has already established a specialized organization. Elders will take turns continuously casting the Tai Jia Divine Technique to approach and observe the Star Sea consciousness."

"According to our predictions, the optimal time should arrive within thirty years."

"During this period, the Star Sea's power and the residual True Immortal power will mutually influence and restrain each other, forming a delicate balance."

"Any longer..."

"The power of True Immortals will likely dissipate into the Star Sea." Zhong Daogong arrived at the same conclusion as in his previous life.

Li Fan was pleased, "Good. Regardless, my lifespan is now abundant, and I have enough time to wait."

"What preparations do you need me to make?"

Li Fan proactively offered his assistance.

Zhong Daogong pondered for a moment and offered some suggestions, "First, it would be best to try and see if we can increase the number of humans covered by the ritual..."

Li Fan immediately frowned.

After hesitating for a while, he finally relaxed his expression, "Although it carries some risk, if we are careful, it should be possible. However, we cannot do it multiple times. If we do it, we must do it big, to avoid future regrets."

Li Fan's words greatly pleased Zhong Daogong, "The number of ritual offerings is crucial. Every doubling of the quantity increases our chance of success by another ten percent. We will have to trouble you to focus on this aspect."

"Agreed." Li Fan accepted, his expression solemn, as if contemplating how to achieve this.

"As for the second point..." Zhong Daogong paused, "You can do it incidentally. If it works, that's great; if not, it won't have a significant impact anyway. It's just a backup plan."

Li Fan asked, "Oh? Elder Zhong, please elaborate."

"The key to the ritual's success is to fake a cultivation world within the Star Sea," Zhong Daogong explained to Li Fan using simulated projections.

"As you know, all worlds in the Star Sea have been shattered. Apart from your Da Qi..."

"However, Da Qi's strength is not inferior to our Immortal Boat. Occupying it to use as a ready-made disguise would inevitably lead to a great war. It would be unwise."

"Therefore, using the remains of destroyed worlds for disguise is a viable alternative method."

"Within the Great Wall of Remaining Realms, fragments of past worlds are all interconnected, and touching one affects all others. Taking them is not easy. However, we don't actually need world remnants; we only need to obtain some imprints left after the destruction of the Heavenly Dao..." Zhong Daogong pointed towards the distant Great Wall of Remaining Realms.

"Hmm?" Li Fan appeared somewhat confused.

"What are these 'imprints of a destroyed Heavenly Dao'?"

Zhong Daogong extended his hand and produced an object.

It resembled amber, yet also like white jade.

It was formed naturally, without any carving marks.

It was shaped like a wooden umbrella.

"This is the only remnant of a cultivation world after its destruction. Our Immortal Boat obtained it in the void after a Star Sea anomaly subsided."

"If you search carefully, you will surely find many similar objects within the Great Wall of Remaining Realms. Your escape technique is divine; searching should be much easier for you."

Zhong Daogong quickly put away the wooden umbrella and white jade.

"However, there is no need to force it. Within the Immortal Boat's secret collection, there are still some such Heavenly Dao imprints. They should be sufficient to complete the disguise."

Chapter 1349: It's Indeed a Disturbance

"Collecting more is merely an added precaution."

"The most crucial aspect is the number of offerings for the Universal Ritual..." Zhong Daogong's gaze was fervent, re-emphasizing.

"If you feel any pressure, you can also choose an elder to assist you." Li Fan pondered for a moment, then finally shook his head, "My Da Qi's World Protection Immortal Artifact supervises heaven and earth. If an outsider were to intrude, it would surely cause alarm, which would be counterproductive to the plan."

"I am sufficient on my own! The optimal time window is within thirty years..."

"It won't take that long! If everything goes smoothly, I will succeed within three to five years." Li Fan was full of confidence.

"However..." Li Fan suddenly frowned.

"Your concerns are valid. Speak freely. If you require any assistance, just ask! All the elders will fully cooperate." Zhong Daogong, having received Li Fan's guarantee, was very generous.

Li Fan nodded, "My purpose for venturing out this time is as a pretext to search for treasures in Star Sea ruins. If I return empty-handed, it might arouse suspicion. I need to select something from the Immortal Boat's secret collection to bring back. Of course, something to satisfy them, from the first layer of the secret collection, will suffice." Seeing Dao Sheng heard this, he suddenly asked, "If the items brought back are of higher value, would that be more beneficial for the subsequent ritual preparation?" Li Fan subconsciously replied, "Naturally... However, to be honest, the help is indeed limited. Da Qi's academic circles are even more entrenched than our Immortal Boat Elder Council. A few treasures alone are far from enough. It still depends on time and hard-earned seniority." The elders exchanged glances, and finally, Zhong Daogong spoke, "Even a slight increase in certainty is beneficial. You can go to the second layer of the treasury to choose. Items stored there are of extremely high value but do not affect the survival and continuation of the Immortal Boat." Li Fan did not refuse and cupped his hands, "That would be for the best." Accompanied by everyone, Li Fan returned to the second layer of the Immortal Boat's secret collection.

He surveyed the rare treasures sealed within the light spheres of the "Celestial Star Light Lotus." The Immortal Boat Elder Council agreed to let him choose two items from here, and then three from the first layer.

With five treasures in hand, it would dispel Da Qi's doubts and also facilitate the smooth progress of the Universal Ritual.

Li Fan browsed the items. In the second layer of the secret collection, he first chose a Yin-Yang Jade. It was condensed from a state of subtle balance between vast amounts of Yin and Yang energies.

Li Fan had a hunch that if he infused this Yin-Yang energy into the Xuanhuang sublimation process, it might yield unexpected results.

As for the second treasure he chose... it was naturally one of Sun Piaomiao's three遗物 (relics), the three-branched divine tree that resonated with "Returning to True"!

Regarding Sun Piaomiao's relics, the Immortal Boat elders had all used the "Reveal" script to observe them. The broken-winged gray bird and the three-branched tree, unlike the Medicine King Cauldron, did not show any apparent connection to the outside world.

Ruling them out as potential gray chess pieces, the elders of the Immortal Boat deemed them to be mere decoys left by Sun Piaomiao.

Li Fan explained, "Although this item has little practical value, it was also left by Sun Piaomiao. It originates from the same source as the hanging puppet that saved my life last time. My master would surely be very interested in it." The Immortal Boat elders hesitated for a moment, but ultimately agreed to Li Fan's request.

Afterward, Li Fan went to the first layer of the secret collection and took a piece of black star stone, a peculiar bronze mirror, and a liquid long sword.

Only then did he bid farewell to the Immortal Boat. His sword shadow flashed, and he vanished into the dark Star Sea. After Li Fan left, the elders of the Immortal Boat gathered.

"Although he guaranteed it, we cannot place all our hopes solely on him," Zhong Daogong said solemnly.

"Indeed, we must also prepare other methods to mitigate the Star Sea's backlash."

"Perhaps it is time to open the third layer of the Hundred Wonders Immortal Record..." As soon as this was said, the hall fell into silence.

It was as if the third layer of the secret collection contained something that greatly intimidated everyone. The elders' expressions varied, but for a long time, no one voiced their agreement.

"Let's wait a bit longer. Let's set a five-year deadline. Everyone think again if there are any better solutions."

"If he succeeds within this period, that would be even better."

"Otherwise..." A shadow flickered in Zhong Daogong's eyes as he looked toward the now-closed entrance to the Hundred Wonders Secret Collection.

... Far from the Immortal Boat, Li Fan did not return to the Xuanhuang Realm immediately. Instead, he headed towards the Great Wall of Remaining Realms, to where Yin Shangren and Bai Hua were located.

Along the way, Li Fan took out the three-branched tree. The anomaly of "Returning to True" appeared precisely at this moment. Li Fan suppressed the burgeoning craving in his heart temporarily and first examined the creation before him.

This three-branched tree was crafted from an unknown material, neither copper nor wood, possessing the hardness and coolness of metal, yet also the vitality and ancient aura of an ancient tree.

On each branch, instead of leaves, grew another entirely new tree. And on these secondary branches, further three-branched growths emerged.

Endlessly, as if without limit. Even with Li Fan's current divine sense constantly tracking and observing, he could not ascertain the total number of branches within a short time.

"As expected, marvelous," Li Fan nodded slightly, then ceased suppressing his desire from "Returning to True." A mysterious force enveloped the three-branched tree, and the ancient creation, bathed in a soft light, gradually vanished into the air. Li Fan stared intently at the changes on the "Returning to True" panel.

However, after a long wait, the good fortune of "Returning to True's" energy charge increasing by 400% directly, as happened previously, did not occur.

In fact... Li Fan found no tangible changes.

"Could it be that 'Returning to True' consumed it in vain?" Li Fan's thought flashed briefly. However, he quickly dismissed the idea.

Based on his understanding of "Returning to True," it was extremely picky about what it consumed. Each consumption would bring about a substantial change.

This time should be no exception. Li Fan abandoned observing the "Returning to True" panel and focused entirely on "Returning to True" itself.

He even halted his Void-Crossing Wooden Sword escape technique, standing silently in the void, as Li Fan meditated.

After half a day, Li Fan suddenly opened his eyes: "Indeed, this time, the changes in 'Returning to True' are not directly reflected on the panel."

"But..." Li Fan once again conjured a phantom of his wooden sword. To outsiders, it was indistinguishable, but only to Li Fan, the wielder of the divine ability, could he discern that this phantom escape technique was now superior to before.

In a short period, such significant progress had been made. This was entirely due to Li Fan's deepened comprehension of the "Transformation Between True and False."

"It can help me comprehend the essence of 'Returning to True's' 'Transformation Between True and False'?" Li Fan was quite shocked.

The Transformation Between True and False was currently the highest-level power Li Fan had encountered in his continuous cycles of reincarnation. None other.

Li Fan's comprehension and utilization of it were extremely difficult. It relied entirely on his connection with "Returning to True," using the scenes of worlds de-materializing and re-materializing each time "Returning to True" was activated, and slowly comprehending through personal insight.

There were no shortcuts. But now, this relic of Sun Piaomiao, the three-branched tree, could actually aid in his enlightenment!

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, carefully contemplating how this incredible event had occurred. After a long while, Li Fan vaguely sensed: "The Dao of True and False is like the ultimate principle of heaven, high above."

"Only when I activate 'Returning to True' each time, can I ascend to the heavens and closely observe its changes."

"And absorbing this three-branched tree is..." Li Fan fell silent for a moment. Then, a brilliant light flashed in his eyes: "Without my participation, 'Returning to True' initiated a 'simulation'?"

"The creation and de-materialization of true and false worlds occurred in an instant, not even affecting the current world, but existing solely within 'Returning to True'!"

"While no one in the world noticed, it achieved another transformation between true and false. Only I, through the inexplicable increase in my comprehension of the Transformation Between True and False, was fortunate enough to discover it..." Becoming the only wise person in the world, Li Fan felt no excitement.

Instead, an unprecedented weight settled upon him, to the extent that his plan to rendezvous with Yin Shangren and Bai Hua was temporarily set aside.

"'Returning to True'..." Li Fan chanted silently in his heart. The surroundings instantly darkened. It was a gloom more profound than the already pitch-black and desolate Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

"'When True is taken as False, False also becomes True'," the seven bright characters appeared as usual. The ability of "Returning to True" remained unaffected and could be activated at any time.

But for some unknown reason, Li Fan felt a persistent unease that refused to subside. In Li Fan's view, worldly matters could be divided into two categories.

One was that which the ability of "Returning to True" could cover. The other was that which could influence "Returning to True."

Everything in the Star Sea, even the high wall, True Immortals, and the cat treasure, belonged to the first category. As long as he possessed "Returning to True," Li Fan was confident he could eventually overcome them all.

But the latter... was beyond Li Fan's control. The ability to influence "Returning to True" meant that Li Fan's greatest trump card had lost its efficacy.

Although this time, it seemed to be beneficial without harm. Yet, the occurrence of an uncontrollable event was definitely a warning for Li Fan.

Could future 'abnormalities' of "Returning to True," and its desire to consume, always be satisfied? What exactly did this consumption by "Returning to True" represent?

These were questions that Li Fan had to contemplate carefully. "Returning to True," as an supreme artifact that mysteriously awakened after Li Fan's transmigration, seemed intrinsically linked to his being.

It was definitely false to say he wasn't afraid of losing it one day. But his smooth journey through countless cycles of reincarnation, and even successfully establishing a foundation in the Xuanhuang Realm using a part of "Returning to True,"

had gradually made him forget his past anxieties and fears. Now, with the changes brought about by "Returning to True" after absorbing the three-branched divine tree, Li Fan was jolted awake once more.

After a long while, Li Fan finally calmed down.

"From the current perspective, it is not a bad thing for me."

"But I must quickly figure out what exactly this three-branched tree is. Why did it cause 'Returning to True' to simulate the birth and death of a world without my participation?"

"What exactly happened in that fleeting moment of world destruction and rebirth?"

"What is special about it that caused 'Returning to True' to undergo such a change?" Numerous questions flooded Li Fan's mind.

"Sun Piaomiao..." Li Fan was now convinced that this three-branched tree must also originate from the Immortal Realm.

"It is even more valuable than the gray chess pieces."

"But even Sun Piaomiao might not have understood its underlying secrets." Li Fan pondered how to study this three-branched tree.

He could not be sure if, in his next life, "Returning to True" would still have the desire to consume upon seeing the three-branched tree.

Based on past experience, "Returning to True" would not consume something it had already consumed. But perhaps this bizarre three-branched tree would be an exception.

Then came the question: if the 'abnormality' of "Returning to True" occurred again in the next life, would Li Fan choose to let it consume again?

For the first time, the decisive Li Fan fell into prolonged hesitation. This indecisiveness persisted even after he found Yin Shangren and Bai Hua in the Great Wall of Remaining Realms.

While cautiously continuing his thoughts, Li Fan activated his wooden sword phantom escape technique and hurried towards the two, who were struggling amidst the reverberating Star Power.

The location they were currently in was a "node" within the Great Wall of Remaining Realms, which Yin Shangren had mentioned earlier, created to maintain its self-stability.

The reverberating Star Power here was like giant waves crashing against reefs, with violent energy fluctuations, rivaling even the foot of the high wall. At their current strength, exploring here was still quite challenging.

"How is it? Any clues about Xu Ke?" Li Fan asked. Yin Shangren, after regulating the somewhat chaotic life and death energies within his body, responded, "We have basically confirmed that Xu Ke was indeed drawn into this place. We discovered the last marker he left behind. Although extremely faint, it matches our pre-arranged signal perfectly." Upon hearing this, Li Fan shifted some of his attention to survey their surroundings.

His vision suddenly shifted from a normal perspective to an ascended view. Li Fan unexpectedly discovered that this "node" was not a high platform within the Great Wall of Remaining Realms.

Instead, it was a depression! The continuous, majestic Great Wall abruptly fractured here. However, this fracture did not actually affect the connection of the Great Wall of Remaining Realms.

It was as if... some unseen force within this depression was sustaining the unbroken connection of the Great Wall of Remaining Realms!

"Interesting," Li Fan's interest was finally piqued. The scope of this depression, in the actual Star Sea, was merely a small area.

Barely enough for one person to stand independently. It was exceedingly difficult to drift into this spot amidst the fierce energy fluctuations, especially without any self-protection.

"Perhaps only Xu Ke, that destined person, could possess such luck." Li Fan thought this, his wooden sword phantom like a small boat on a river, heading towards the depression.

The closer they got to the fractured section of the Great Wall of Remaining Realms, the stronger the external interference affecting the wooden sword phantom became. Light and shadow flickered erratically, as if it could shatter like a bubble at any moment.

Li Fan slightly frowned, concentrating his mind, and maintained the integrity of his escape technique. Boom! The moment the phantom left the normal region of the Great Wall of Remaining Realms and completely plunged into the fractured depression, it felt like a sudden fall from a ten-thousand-foot high cliff.

Under the intense impact, the wooden sword phantom nearly disintegrated!

Chapter 1350: Fissures Span the Starry Sea

Ever since Li Fan comprehended the Wooden Sword Phantom escape technique, this was the first time he had encountered a situation where his divine ability was so violently impacted by the external environment. He even had a premonition that if not for the fact that "Returning to True" had absorbed the three-branched tree earlier and his comprehension of the Transformation Between True and False had deepened slightly...

He would have at least suffered the consequence of his divine ability shattering and sustaining severe injuries from that sudden fall.

Fortunately, Li Fan had indeed made some progress.

It was precisely this slight improvement that allowed him to barely maintain the integrity of the wooden sword phantom and successfully enter the depression node within the Great Wall of Remaining Realms!

Unlike the depression Li Fan had encountered before, which served as a reservoir for residual True Immortal power.

Upon entering this place, one could distinctly perceive the difference compared to the outside world, caused by the violent changes in altitude.

It was like a deep, bottomless chasm suddenly opening up in the earth.

Li Fan and the others were currently falling to the bottom of the abyss, gazing up at the continuous line of the sky visible above.

However, the sky here was a deathly silent expanse of utter blackness.

And this chasm depression...

Li Fan did not retract his wooden sword phantom, continuing to use it to shield Yin Shangren and Bai Hua.

He himself flashed out of the phantom's protection.

He began to sense his surroundings.

It was still a realm of darkness.

But this "darkness" was different from the desolate void outside.

It was more akin to the arrival of a midsummer night, with vibrant life subtly woven within!

"The high wall's chasm node actually harbors such immense convergence of vitality?" Li Fan was inwardly astonished.

Upon closer examination, he confirmed that this was not his imagination.

Li Fan's observation deepened.

Within the chasm depression, besides pure vitality, there seemed to be no life yet conceived.

Moreover, the actual scale of this place was not as limited as it appeared from a normal perspective. Instead, it seemed to extend endlessly outwards, as if it had no end.

With no immediate danger, Li Fan finally retracted his divine ability.

Yin Shangren and Bai Hua looked around with expressions of astonishment.

The birth of vitality in this place clearly exceeded their cognitive abilities. Their spirits remained taut, fearing that unknown creatures might suddenly emerge from the surrounding darkness to attack them.

Li Fan noticed their reactions and then became alerted. They did not seem as composed as himself.

Perhaps it was the first time they had experienced the phenomenon of "extreme difference in altitude," causing their minds to become unsettled and anxious as they left their ingrained region.

It was akin to mortals who had lived their entire lives on plateau suddenly finding themselves at the edge of a cliff or in a deep mountain valley, without any self-protection. It was natural for their mental states to change.

He calmed them with a deep voice and then led them to slowly explore the chasm depression.

A profound silence reigned.

Pure vitality, like an underground river from the dawn of creation, flowed silently here.

The vitality ascended, yet could not escape the deep chasm.

It merely condensed and gathered in this place.

Li Fan keenly sensed that the vitality here had a significant difference from the vitality that nurtured life in the Xuanhuang Realm.

If the Xuanhuang Realm possessed such an immense quantity of vitality, it would undoubtedly trigger various unimaginable changes. Mountains would rise from the ground, and trees would grow to the sky. Countless new species and life forms would surely be born.

But here, vitality was merely vitality.

It did not conform to the conditions for the birth and evolution of life, resembling a pool of stagnant water, giving a bizarre and unsettling feeling.

"Perhaps it is due to the excessively low 'potential' of this place."

Li Fan couldn't help but think this.

After leisurely exploring for more than half a day, the surrounding scenery showed no significant changes.

Li Fan frowned, instructing Yin Shangren and Bai Hua to wait where they were.

He himself, wielding his wooden sword phantom, moved at high speed.

With his current escape speed, he could traverse the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea in less than a day.

However, Li Fan was shocked to discover that this chasm was far vaster than he had imagined!

As he continued to advance, Li Fan even found that the chasm was like a labyrinth, gradually branching out in different directions.

Initially, it was manageable, with only a few forks.

But later, each branch led to dozens, even hundreds, of different passages.

Eventually, even with his heaven-defying escape technique, Li Fan dared not venture further rashly.

This chasm labyrinth was simply too immense.

After exploring rapidly for three days, theoretically, this should have been enough time to cover the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

Yet, Li Fan still could not see the end of the chasm labyrinth.

Li Fan had no choice but to rely on his memory of the path taken to return.

After explaining the situation to Yin Shangren and Bai Hua, both were profoundly shaken.

"This peculiar chasm is definitely not just beneath the Great Wall of Remaining Realms."

"Perhaps it's like an underground waterway, connecting to various parts of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea from all directions!" Yin Shangren began to understand.

Bai Hua nodded in agreement, "I can faintly sense the source of the vitality here. Apart from the countless ruins of destroyed worlds within the Great Wall of Remaining Realms, it also originates from every corner of the dormant Star Sea!"

"Like an underground river, drawing in every bit of newly generated vitality, converging here like trickling water."

If the high wall was the supreme existence that enclosed the Star Sea.

Then, the chasm depression hidden beneath the high wall was the lowest point of the entire Star Sea.

Most of the vitality that the Star Sea had recovered from its destruction, followed the ubiquitous underground fissures beneath the Star Sea, and finally converged here.

It was precisely because of the accumulation of the vast majority of the Star Sea's vitality over tens of thousands of years that the sheer volume of vitality here could make even Li Fan feel a sense of trepidation.

"This magnificent creation is by no means something mortals could achieve..."

"Could it be another work of a True Immortal? Like the high wall, intended to completely seal off the Star Sea's vitality?" Yin Shangren's expression shifted between shades of worry and contemplation.

As for Bai Hua, she had gradually emerged from her previous fear.

"Saint Master, may I extract some vitality from here?" she asked.

Li Fan's gaze flickered. After pondering for a moment, he replied, "If you only extract a small amount, without causing the vitality river to surge violently, there should be no danger."

"But remember, do not be greedy. Take what you need and stop. Otherwise..."

Li Fan surveyed the calmly flowing vitality, his expression solemn, "The quantity is too immense. Such power, when suddenly unleashed, although it is vitality, it can also kill!"

Bai Hua nodded, "I understand this. In fact, I don't need that much. Just enough to awaken the Ice-Sealed Glazed World..."

Bai Hua's tone was wistful as she transformed into her Glazed Golden Body.

Her radiant golden form, within its core, held a miniature world resembling ice carving and jade.

Faintly, scenes of countless cultivators and sects, mountains and rivers from the past could be seen.

"Glazed... Flower blooms..."

Bai Hua softly chanted, and her golden form suddenly transformed into a thirty-two-petaled Glazed Golden Flower.

Sacred and solemn.

The Glazed Golden Flower floated into the river of vitality without causing any splashes of energy scattering.

It simply floated calmly.

Its thirty-two petals slowly unfurled.

Li Fan saw wisps of vitality being drawn by these petals and channeled into the miniature world within the flower's core.

But the immense vitality before them seemed extremely viscous, not easily extracted.

With all thirty-two golden petals working in unison, only a drop or two of vitality became visible in the central miniature world.

Yet, even this meager amount of vitality was like manna from heaven to the miniature world.

It was as if a wilted flower had been watered anew, regaining its original vibrancy.

All sorts of miraculous changes occurred within the miniature world, the Myriad Blooms Realm.

Bai Hua's face showed overwhelming joy.

Yin Shangren was also momentarily captivated by this wondrous spectacle.

Li Fan, however, noticed that due to Bai Hua's extraction of vitality, a miniature vortex of immense vitality was slowly forming around her.

The vortex was initially small, but it soon gained momentum for explosive expansion.

It was as if all the vitality in the chasm was rolling in, with a power like that of a heavenly descent, crushing and engulfing everything, commanding an awe that made even Li Fan look on with surprise.

"Enough!" Li Fan frowned and called out a reminder.

Bai Hua, being relatively clear-headed and not blinded by temporary gain,

Although reluctant, she finally retracted the thirty-two-petaled Glazed Golden Flower.

Without the outlet for extraction, the gradually roaring vitality river calmed down.

However, in the short term, the accumulated vitality did not dissipate and formed a rapid current in this area.

The surge of vitality's power caused Li Fan and the others within to feel as if their souls were about to be swept away.

Li Fan had no choice but to reinforce the protection of his wooden sword phantom.

Yin Shangren, looking at the seemingly calm yet deceptively dangerous scene, suddenly realized, "I know where that contradictory and crisis-ridden feeling comes from! It's because flowing here is not just vitality alone. On the surface of the vitality, there is a layer of unknown power that absorbs vitality!"

"It is this power that continuously draws vitality from all parts of the Star Sea and stores it here!"

Bai Hua, having returned to her normal form, nodded in agreement, "It is difficult to separate this power from pure vitality, so my absorption was so arduous. Strictly speaking, the 'vitality stripping power' itself is not of a very high caliber. Even I can separate it from vitality."

"But..." Bai Hua's face showed a hint of fear.

"Its quantity is simply too vast. Whatever vitality the chasm holds, there is that much vitality stripping power. We might be able to withstand a few waves of impact, but we absolutely cannot survive continuous scouring."

Having said this, Bai Hua couldn't help but glance at Li Fan.

She paused, "Perhaps, Saint Master, with your transcendent escape technique, you might be able to escape."

Li Fan did not respond.

Instead, he reached out his hand, touching and sensing the surging vitality current around him.

The erosion of the vitality stripping power was undeniable.

The hand that was struck instantly turned pale.

It was as if the flesh and blood had been drained, and the bones beneath were faintly visible.

Furthermore, this loss of vitality slowly began to spread to other parts of his body.

Li Fan decisively severed his arm, thus halting the further encroachment of the vitality stripping power.

The severed hand fell into the river of vitality.

Without the protection of its original body, it rapidly dissolved and vanished like a wax figure under high heat,

Becoming part of the river of vitality.

"This power..."

Regrowing his arm, Li Fan moved it slightly, recalling the details he had perceived earlier.

It was not a simple extraction of vitality.

Rather, it was an instantaneous scouring away of the very foundation upon which vitality depended.

When the skin is gone, how can the hair remain attached? Without the foundation, vitality had no support and was swept away by the current.

It was a profound and mysterious sensation.

Li Fan could not yet comprehend what the 'foundation' of vitality was.

But he could clearly feel its loss.

"Indeed, it defies imagination."

"But..."

"It seems to have some similarities with the high wall?"

Li Fan mused, "The so-called high wall is a restriction of supreme rules. There is no path forward, or rather, no 'forward'!"

"And the vitality stripping power in this chasm removes the foundation for life's sustenance."

"..."

The chasm depression, hidden beneath the normal Star Sea.

Like underground rivers, it permeated every corner of the Star Sea.

Its grand scale was evident, clearly only something that could be created by the beings who constructed the high wall.

"Perhaps, just as Yin Shangren speculated, it was created to extract and seal the Star Sea's nascent vitality?"

But Li Fan soon felt a hint of doubt.

Indeed, vitality was being extracted, but not completely.

Because the immense vitality accumulated over tens of thousands of years in the chasm still lay quietly here!

While accessing the chasm was extremely difficult. Li Fan had traversed the Great Wall of Remaining Realms countless times without noticing the minuscule node entrance.

But it was not absolutely impossible.

There were still possibilities for entering by sheer chance.

For instance, during this time, Xu Ke was caught by the surging reverberating Star Power, accidentally entering this chasm.
