"If one truly wished to sever the Star Sea's vitality, with His ability to create the high wall and excavate the chasm, He could have directly extracted this vitality outside the high wall."

"But He chose to leave it within the Star Sea instead..."

Li Fan pondered, his expression becoming peculiar, "Either the creator of the chasm and the high wall are two different entities."

"Or, it was intentional."

In Li Fan's vision, the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea appeared.

The high wall loomed around the Star Sea, sealing it off.

Beneath the Star Sea, countless fissures crisscrossed, connecting channels, drawing and preserving the Star Sea's vitality.

And at the fringe of the Star Sea.

The supreme high wall and the lowest chasm.

Converged together.

"A marvel of the Star Sea."

"For the beings within the Star Sea, these are despair-inducing existences. However..."

"Perhaps this chasm is not."

The scene in Li Fan's eyes shifted again.

"The Star Sea is reviving from its destruction. However, for life to sprout anew is not a matter of a single day."

"Especially with residual True Immortal power lingering for tens of thousands of years, it has not yet dispersed. Even if vitality re-emerges, it will only be quickly polluted by the residual True Immortal power. It's like a small amount of rain in a scorching desert during the day, quickly evaporating."

"The vitality that emerges everywhere in the Star Sea is simply wasted and cannot truly give rise to life in the Star Sea."

"But if all of it were to be gathered..."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes.

Recommended the new book by Yan Shen.

The world has been divided for over three hundred years.

The central plains are filled with music and dance, while foreign tribes sharpen their weapons. Jianghu sword immortals roam freely, and famous generals suppress the ten directions.

Five years before the world descends into chaos, twelve-year-old physician Li Guan finds himself killing someone on a rainy night.

Finally, he opens his eyes and sees this chaotic world.

White bones litter the ground beneath the horses' hooves; famous generals and beauties, Jianghu, divine weapons, and common folk.

Since ancient times, only white bones and yellow sand are seen in the fields!

Confucian scholars are trampled under iron hooves; Buddhas are swept away by long spears!

This humble Daoist Li Guan invites this world to face its death!

Chapter 1351: The Supreme Being Controls the Heavens

"It is like an underground reservoir in a desert, collecting all the seeping water over millions of years."

"When the day comes, and the opportune moment arrives, with torrential rain pouring down upon the desert, this underground reservoir will unleash the subterranean waters, sweeping across the entire desert. Coupled with the momentum of heaven and earth, it will transform the boundless sands into vast wetlands in an instant!"

"This is a method for transforming heaven and earth!" Li Fan's eyes flickered, as if trying to see through the secrets hidden beneath the tranquil river of vitality.

Unfortunately, as he had speculated earlier, the creator of the river of vitality was undoubtedly an existence beyond the mortal realm.

His arrangements, especially, were clearly not achieved through formations, and thus were beyond Li Fan's current comprehension.

As Bai Hua's extraction of vitality ceased, the surging currents gradually subsided, returning to a state of dormancy. Li Fan's observations yielded no results.

Yin Shangren and Bai Hua were similarly silent. When they truly faced this place, comparable to the high wall, and were unable to uncover its secrets despite employing various methods, the gap was almost despairing. The three stood silently on the river of vitality, speechless for a long time.

After an unknown period, Li Fan shook his head slightly, "In ancient times, there was the sigh of 'gazing at the ocean and sighing.' Today, seeing the river evokes despair."

"The secrets here are beyond our current ability to explore. If Xu Ke is lost within, we can only hope for his good fortune." What was initially intended as a casual task to find Xu Ke had unexpectedly led to the discovery of a chasm system spanning the entire Star Sea beneath the Great Wall of Remaining Realms.

Thus, the plan had to change. In reality, if Li Fan had continued exploring, relying on the recording function of the Dao Refining Stone and his wooden sword phantom escape technique, he might have eventually explored the entire Star Sea chasm.

However, the focus of this life was the sublimation of the Xuanhuang Realm. The vitality contained within the Star Sea chasm was too immense. Even if some were extracted during the Xuanhuang sublimation, the already explored regions would still be more than sufficient.

"Saint Master, I intend to stay here for now," Bai Hua said, after some hesitation.

"This vitality is of great use for reviving the Myriad Blooms Realm. Although I can only extract a small amount each time, with sustained effort, within half a year, I can restore my homeland to its former vitality!" Li Fan stared at Bai Hua, his gaze seeming to penetrate her body and reach the miniature world at its core.

"Even if it is revived, your old friends might not all be able to return to life," Li Fan frowned.

Li Fan could clearly see that the Myriad Blooms Realm and the beings within it had all been refined by Bai Hua into that golden, glazed state.

Even if the surging vitality could wash it clean and restore it from its glazed state, it was uncertain how many beings could withstand such a transformation during the process.

Bai Hua's gaze remained firm, "It is about doing one's best and leaving the rest to fate! Previously, there was simply no method to revive the world. Now that a fortunate opportunity is before us, how can I turn a blind eye?" Seeing this, Li Fan did not object.

Yin Shangren then spoke, "I, like Bai Hua, do not wish to leave in the short term." Li Fan raised his eyebrows, "Is this vitality also useful to you?" Yin Shangren shook his head, "No. It's just that near this river of vitality, I feel an immense sense of peace within my heart. Those residual world souls that occasionally surfaced in my consciousness have all fallen silent here..."

This reason left Li Fan speechless.

"However, if you are idle, please also search for Xu Ke's whereabouts. If you find him, that's best. If not, do not force it; prioritize your own safety."

"The Xuanhuang sublimation is a long-term plan. We are not in a hurry for this half-year period. You two shall remain here for now. I will return to pick you up in half a year," Li Fan instructed the two.

The two cupped their hands and bid farewell to Li Fan. Li Fan then stepped forward, his wooden sword phantom reflecting around him. Moments later, a peculiar wave appeared around him.

It was the Ascension Array! With the imposing aura of a cultivator ascending and climbing the heavenly gate, it made Yin Shangren and Bai Hua instinctively step back to avoid it.

In front of them, Li Fan's actual position had not changed, but they could truly feel Li Fan moving further and further away, and higher and higher.

Li Fan, standing within the phantom of his wooden sword, gradually became ethereal. Finally, he completely faded from their sight.

"Such a technique..." Yin Shangren exclaimed, mesmerized, "If Saint Master does not return to pick us up in half a year, then we might be trapped here forever." Bai Hua did not refute, only saying,

"However, with vitality permeating this place, there is no need to worry about being trapped to death." She then continued to stare intently at the calm river of vitality, awaiting the next opportunity to absorb.

... The Great Wall of Remaining Realms. Outside the node leading to the chasm depression. Without any warning, Li Fan's figure suddenly reappeared.

The moment he returned to the Star Sea, he deactivated the Ascension Array and used his wooden sword phantom escape technique to leave the vicinity of the node.

In just a few breaths, returning from the lowest depression to the normal altitude of the Star Sea. The rapid change in altitude from low to high in such a short period caused his body and soul to feel as if they had undergone some violent impact.

Pfft, pfft... Blood splattered, and his skin cracked. His soul felt as if it had been rolled over by thousands of massive stones, compressed and crushed.

Even with Li Fan's foundation, his face turned pale in an instant.

"The previous action was akin to half an ascension. Except, it was ascending from a lower-tiered world to the current Star Sea."

"The impact experienced was already so intense. One can only imagine the trials that true ascension would entail."

"Without the protection of immortal spiritual energy, ordinary cultivators would likely have no chance of survival." Li Fan's thoughts drifted leisurely for a few breaths, and his injuries had already completely healed.

He did not leave, instead gazing at the marvel beneath the high wall. The invisible high wall, the continuous Great Wall of Remaining Realms, and the bottomless chasm of the Star Sea.

Intertwined, creating an illusionary and mysterious scene. Even with Li Fan's power nearing the pinnacle of the Star Sea,

In his eyes, this Star Sea was still filled with mysteries. Perhaps, as he grew stronger and encountered more, the mysteries in his heart would only increase.

Until one day, when he broke through a certain limit, everything would be revealed. Li Fan took one last deep look at this Star Sea marvel, then drew his wooden sword phantom and flew towards the Xuanhuang Realm.

"Dealing with the Immortal Boat's ritual is not urgent for now. If it were completed too quickly, it might arouse suspicion."

"However, as the progress advances, it is also time to officially begin nurturing the next Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate of this life." The Xuanhuang sublimation plan required a vast amount of immortal spiritual energy, which could only be accessed by the successor who became the Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate.

The position of Great Heavenly Venerate still carried the constraints of the former Immortal Realm. The scene of Sun Tianci's untimely death in the previous life was still vivid. This clearly indicated that Li Fan would never put himself at risk.

Fortunately, in this life, there was no need to create another innate Dao-harmonizing Sun Tianci. His Dao transmission projection continuously preached in various mortal small worlds, and he had already identified a suitable candidate. Li Fan moved his figure and arrived in an unnamed mortal world.

The scale of this small world was insignificant, let alone compared to Da Qi or Da Li, it was even inferior to the Lingmu Realm.

A mountain range composed of thirteen peaks constituted the entirety of the world. It was more like a small-scale grotto-heaven than a small world.

Yet, in such a mortal small world that even a Foundation Establishment cultivator might not pay attention to, Li Fan sensed the nascent birth of a faint world Heavenly Dao consciousness.

And within it, a boy whose temperament could be described as exceptionally pure and sincere. Perhaps due to the world's small size, the chances of humans giving birth to offspring were extremely difficult.

Therefore, the total human population was always maintained at a low level. To them, the resources in the mountains were almost inexhaustible.

With so few people spread across thirteen peaks, they were all familiar with each other, thus rarely experiencing conflict. Most of their time each day was idle.

Inevitably, some humans here developed curiosity about the world beyond the mountains. But just as beings in the Star Sea were confined within the high wall.

They could never leave the boundaries of their world in their entire lives. There was a small boy who, from the day he could walk, would often climb the highest peak in this world.

Standing alone on the summit, he would gaze upon this small world. The thirteen-peak mountain range unfolded before his eyes. Afterward, he would lie on the ground and silently watch the sky.

Li Fan had observed this young boy before. During his climbs and gazes, his mind was filled with various thoughts.

But when he lay down and faced the sky, his consciousness entered a state of near absolute blankness, his thoughts completely calmed.

If Li Fan could not sense his life force, he would have almost thought he had passed away. It is known that for a living being to exist in the world and interact with its surroundings will inevitably lead to the formation of one's own thoughts.

Only a very few individuals, either by chance or extraordinary talent, could enter such a state of ignorant emptiness.

However, this state, which cultivators sought but could rarely find, was the norm for this young boy.

Even... this thirteen-peak world was too small. Yet, by chance, it had given birth to its own Heavenly Dao consciousness.

Among the extremely limited number of living beings, the boy's daily act of climbing to the summit and gazing at the sky naturally drew the attention of this world's Heavenly Dao.

However, this world's True Dao consciousness was also in an infant-like nascent state, merely approaching out of instinctual curiosity.

Thus, the boy's soul became like a blank piece of paper, slowly imprinting the approaching thirteen-peak world's Heavenly Dao.

The traces left by the world's Heavenly Dao in his soul did not affect the boy's inherent disposition. He continued his daily routine of climbing to the summit and gazing at the sky.

And without his awareness, the Heavenly Dao consciousness descended with increasing familiarity, leaving its imprint. ... Li Fan observed individuals and countless small worlds.

He had to admit that this was an unparalleled miracle.

"Like man, like heaven; heaven in reality is man. Unity of heaven and man, man surpasses heaven's marvels!"

"Observing the Dao of Heaven, carrying out the Dao of Heaven, is complete!" This nameless young boy, inadvertently, achieved the perfect state that ancient cultivators recorded as their most cherished dream.

Even though the world's scale was too small, and its Heavenly Dao's perfection was incomparable to the Xuanhuang Realm,

Undoubtedly, for Li Fan, this young boy was an absolutely perfect candidate for the Great Heavenly Venerate. The Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate was essentially a proxy for heaven.

When the Heavenly Dao operated normally, in certain critical moments, the Great Heavenly Venerate would intervene and regulate. For Li Fan, he merely needed a puppet to open the legacy of the former Great Heavenly Venerate.

The less autonomous the puppet, the better. However, if it were merely an unthinking puppet, it would be impossible to pass the succession trial.

The appearance of this young boy perfectly solved Li Fan's problem.

"In his current state, after becoming the Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate, he will not make any independent decisions. He will fully adhere to the original operation method of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, governing through non-action."

"And for the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao, a Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate who does nothing is precisely what it would welcome. His compatibility might not be inferior to Mr. Bai's..." The more Li Fan looked at this young boy, the more satisfied he became.

With a flick of his finger, a small amount of light and shadow subtly entered the boy's pure and flawless blank consciousness. It did not even disturb the approaching Heavenly Dao consciousness of this world.

This time, Li Fan did not directly implant the details of the Great Heavenly Venerate's Tribulation Realm trial. Only subtle hints and guidance for critical decision points.

The boy's thoughts were too simple. With these guides, he should be able to pass the trial through instinctive choices.

"The future Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate must have a name.

"From now on, your name will be [Nameless]." To preserve Nameless's innocence, Li Fan did not even implant his own existence into his sea of consciousness.

Entering the Tribulation Realm through the Thirteen Peaks, succeeding as the Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate, and later detonating the immortal artifact to infuse the Xuanhuang Realm with immortal spiritual energy to promote its sublimation, leading to the birth of the first Heavenly Immortal Soul... all depended on silent guidance and subtle suggestions.

This meant that Li Fan would have to cooperate with Nameless in the 'Dao Harmonization Plan.' However, Nameless's nature of 'non-action and non-governance' would minimize uncontrollability.

"For a considerable period, Nameless's existence will be almost negligible."

"However, if in this life, after I attain Dao Harmonization, the Xuanhuang Realm still exists..." Li Fan's eyes gleamed with curiosity. "With the passage of time, my body merging with the Heavenly Dao consciousness of the 'Super Xuanhuang Realm,' perhaps Nameless could achieve a level comparable to a True Immortal through this opportunity!" It was foreseeable that the Xuanhuang Realm, driven by Li Fan's methods in this life, would almost ascend to an Immortal Domain.

And to merge with the Heavenly Dao consciousness of an Immortal Domain... perhaps even former True Immortals could not achieve this! At that time, his strength would surely surpass that of the Immortal Boat's Star Sea balancing consciousness!

However, the time required would be exceedingly long. Only someone like Nameless, born under such fortuitous circumstances and possessing such purity, could achieve it.

If it were Li Fan, he would not be able to endure for long before his true consciousness would inevitably clash with the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao.

Therefore, Li Fan had abandoned the idea of replacing it from the outset.

"I just don't know, when the Xuanhuang Realm ascends to become an Immortal Domain, what changes will occur in the position of the Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate?"

"Will the restrictions left by the former Immortal Realm disappear, or will they intensify?"

Chapter 1352: The Annihilation of the Dao Arrives at the Star Sea

Nameless, guided by Li Fan's subtle hints, did not immediately leave the Thirteen Peaks world. Instead, he naturally stood up from his posture of gazing at the sky.

He drew closer to the world's Heavenly Dao. He slightly extended his arms, touching the wind, touching the sky.

The blue sky and white clouds remained unchanged. The beings of the Thirteen Peaks world were unaware. Only Li Fan could see that the entire world began to tremble slightly due to Nameless's touch.

"It seems to have sensed Nameless's intention to depart, and the integration speed between this world's Heavenly Dao and him has further increased..."

"From now on, the world's Heavenly Dao will still exist, but a 'tracing copy' will accompany Nameless to a greater world beyond."

"How similar!"

"If one has the ability, who would wish to remain a bird in a cage forever?" Li Fan murmured slightly, then his expression turned solemn, "Then I will give you another push." The phantom of the True Immortal script 'Creation' flashed across the sky of the Thirteen Peaks world.

This world was too small. The 'Creation' script had only revealed itself, yet it was enough to cause earth-shattering changes to it.

Spiritual energy began to surge within the world. The Thirteen Peaks mountains slowly rose. The plants and trees in the mountains flourished with vitality.

Nameless, standing on the summit, felt a sense of awakening from his immersion. He looked around. But ultimately, he found nothing.

Feeling the changes in the surrounding world, Nameless, though puzzled, gradually showed a happy smile on his face.

... The changes in the Thirteen Peaks world continued. Li Fan, however, left a trace of his divine sense within the world to monitor Nameless's actions.

He himself departed first. Returning to the Xuanhuang Realm, he took out a jade slip from his person. It flickered urgently.

It was the jade slip left by Mo Rubing. Mo Rubing had stayed within the Eye of the Sky Beast, wanting to use its power to search for Xuan Tianwang's whereabouts within the Xuanhuang Realm and the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

He had said it would take at most three to five months to get results. Calculating the time, it was about the right moment. Upon contacting his divine sense, Mo Rubing's voice instantly appeared in Li Fan's mind.

It seemed disrupted by some interference, intermittent and unclear.

"I've discovered... something strange..."

"Come quickly." The transmission only contained this sentence. The jade slip's light then dimmed, but Li Fan could vaguely sense that it was guiding him towards the Sky Beast's bone脉 (veins) in Jiushan Prefecture.

With a single step, Li Fan arrived in the territory of Jiushan Prefecture. The so-called Sky Beast's bone脉 referred to the nine mountain ranges that spanned heaven and earth.

According to the jade slip's guidance, Li Fan arrived at the summit of Jade Prison Mountain, one of the nine mountains. Standing at its peak, he had a panoramic view of the nine mountain ranges' layout. It was likely due to the power amplification from the Sky Beast's Eye provided by Mo Rubing's jade slip; Li Fan had previously observed the entirety of Jiushan Prefecture from high altitudes many times, but never with such clarity.

All the mountains and rivers that had evolved upon the Sky Beast's remains were eliminated. In Li Fan's eyes, only the Sky Beast's most primitive form remained.

"The Nine Mountains are: Tianchang, Tian Duan, Tian Xu, Tian Cu, Tian Jie, Tian Dai, Tian Lao, Tian Dong, Tian Xi."

"These are the Nine Manifestations of the脉 (veins)."

"This Sky Beast was transformed from a jade pendant brought back from the Immortal Realm by Xuan Tianwang, yet its internal meridians are no different from those of a human..." The guiding force from the jade slip grew stronger. Suddenly, it seemed to be enveloped by a membrane.

Li Fan did not resist this force enveloping him, allowing it to lead him. A moment later, Li Fan returned to the Eye of the Sky Beast.

The sense of danger he perceived made him reinforce his own defenses. Compared to when he left, this place seemed to have undergone some changes.

And Mo Rubing's condition also appeared to be not good. It wasn't that he had suffered any obvious injuries, but rather, he looked extremely depleted, as if his vital essence had been directly drained. This was something that, for cultivators of Mo Rubing's level, would typically only happen after suffering a fatal blow.

"Brother Mo, what happened?" Li Fan first exclaimed in a low voice. Mo Rubing waved his hand, "It's fine now. It's just what I told you about that strange incident." He didn't dawdle and got straight to the point.

"Fellow Daoist, please observe." The space within the Eye of the Sky Beast suddenly lit up. The countless circular bubbles on the curved boundary around them all displayed the same scene.

"This is not real-time observation by the Eye of the Sky Beast. It is a recording of previous sights," Mo Rubing reminded him. Numerous bubbles overlapped, and myriad images merged.

Instantly, Li Fan felt as if he were present. In the silence, a Star Sea that concealed vitality. A miniature black vortex slowly rotated ceaselessly.

It represented destruction, devouring everything black. Although slow, it resolutely expanded outwards. Residual True Immortal power, Star Sea recovery power... whatever it was, under the sweep of this black vortex, everything was engulfed and assimilated.

The scene's perspective suddenly enlarged. From a corner of the Star Sea, it expanded to encompass almost the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea. The black vortex, within the already pitch-black Utmost Darkness Star Sea, was hardly noticeable.

But after Li Fan witnessed the panoramic view of the Star Sea, his gaze remained locked onto the vortex. The sense of crisis in his heart was irrepressible.

His heart skipped several beats, a rare occurrence. Li Fan then reacted. The location of the black vortex was precisely the center of the Star Sea where he had previously gone to contact the Star Sea Origin True Will!

Moreover, the black energy constituting this black vortex... bore extreme similarity to the True Immortal flesh he had decomposed with the White Circle Falling to the Mortal Realm, and the energy contained within Han Zhong when he was trapped in the Eye of the Sky Beast.

However, the feeling Li Fan got from the three was distinctly different. They were clearly on different levels. The one within the black vortex was far more dangerous.

Li Fan couldn't help but frown slightly.

"What is this?" he asked.

"I'm not sure. But I can be certain that it is related to the 'Calamity of Dao Annihilation' from the former Immortal Realm." Mo Rubing said solemnly, delivering a shocking statement.

"?" Li Fan was startled.

"Calamity of Dao Annihilation?" Mo Rubing waved his hand, and the black vortexes on the surrounding myriad bubbles disappeared, returning to the normal observation scene of the Star Sea.

"This black vortex was something I accidentally discovered while using the Eye of the Sky Beast to search the Star Sea for Brother Xuanyuan."

"Initially, I didn't pay much attention. I thought it was just a normal anomaly evolving in the Star Sea over the years. But later..." Mo Rubing coughed, extended his ten fingers towards the bubbles of the Eye of the Sky Beast.

In the blink of an eye, millions of tendrils of ink flew from Mo Rubing's fingertips, each heading towards a different bubble. Li Fan clearly saw that at the end of each ink tendril was a miniaturized figure of Mo Rubing.

However, their expressions varied, some ferocious, some terrified, some driven to madness. As the myriad Mo Rubings surged towards the bubbles of the Eye of the Sky Beast and made contact, as if undergoing some cruel torture, they all let out piercing screams.

But their bodies continued their actions. They rigidly grasped the bubbles with their hands, then violently pulled. Like a layer of rotten, foul-smelling outer skin being peeled off, they tore a layer of sticky, black unknown substance from the Eye of the Sky Beast.

Ahhh! The small Mo Rubings wailed even louder. Their figures became more and more blurred by the black corrosive substance, as if they might disappear at any moment.

But under the control of Mo Rubing's main body, they never let go. They completely tore the black decayed skin from the Eye of the Sky Beast.

Gulp, gulp... Afterward, instead of storing these black substances, they directly opened their now indistinct mouths and began to devour them greedily.

As the thick, decayed blackness entered their bodies, the faces of each miniature Mo Rubing became indistinguishable.

"'Magic Heart Unbroken, Immortal Body Undying.'" At this moment, Mo Rubing's cold voice suddenly rang out. A mysterious power instantly enveloped and descended upon those blurred figures.

Maintaining them from dissipating completely. It was as if they were containers, not shattered. They carried the black viscous substances within them.

Mo Rubing's expression was grave. He carefully summoned his demonic heart back. Of course, it did not return to himself.

Instead, he took out a jade box and placed them all inside. After completing all this, Mo Rubing finally breathed a sigh of relief.

Li Fan noticed that Mo Rubing had become even weaker. He stared intently at him, awaiting an explanation. Mo Rubing rested for a while before weakly saying, "This is already... the fourth time I've cleaned it."

"I originally thought this black energy was just a normal phenomenon of the Star Sea, with no harm. I never expected that merely observing it a few times would cause the Eye of the Sky Beast to be eroded by it."

"Fortunately, the Eye of the Sky Beast itself originates from the Immortal Realm, its nature is higher than the lower Star Sea. And it was not direct contact, so there was still room for recovery."

"I was able to remove the attached black energy by using my previous cleaning method." Li Fan heard this and also breathed a sigh of relief, "That's truly a blessing in disguise." However, he quickly realized and asked fearfully, "The Calamity of Dao Annihilation, you mentioned earlier, was the catastrophe that once destroyed the Immortal Realm. Has it now appeared in the Star Sea? Even True Immortals couldn't resist it. Are we not facing imminent disaster?"

"Fellow Daoist need not be so tense. The situation isn't that dire," Mo Rubing shook his head. He paused, carefully selecting his words, and then slowly said, "Back then, Brother Xuanyuan also worried about the Calamity of Dao Annihilation in the Immortal Realm spreading to the lower realms."

"Although he never explicitly stated it, I could discern it."

"I also mentioned to you before that the Calamity of Dao Annihilation, if its name is unknown, even if you see it face-to-face, you won't know its origins. If you know its name, even if it's the first time you encounter its signs, you will instinctively feel something. You already know the name, [Dao Annihilation]. When you saw this black energy, did you feel anything specific?" Mo Rubing asked.

Li Fan recalled what he had just seen, "I didn't feel anything."

"That's why." Mo Rubing said gravely,

"I speculate that this black energy is not the 'Calamity of Dao Annihilation' itself, but rather a sign of the approaching Calamity of Dao Annihilation!"

"And..." Mo Rubing's expression grew even more serious.

"It's not just a sign. As you saw before, the black energy seems capable of devouring everything that approaches it in the Star Sea. So if we don't take precautions and let it spread, perhaps the scale of the black energy will cause the Calamity of Dao Annihilation to arrive even faster." Li Fan frowned upon hearing this, his expression equally grave.

He seemed to be processing the information Mo Rubing had conveyed, remaining silent for a long time.

"How could this be?" After a long pause, Li Fan could only utter this sentence, his tone carrying a hint of panic.

Mo Rubing could only respond with silence.

"The ways of the world are unpredictable. Or perhaps, everything was already destined from the day the Immortal Realm was destroyed." After a long while, Mo Rubing sighed.

"Is there no way to stop the spread of this black vortex?" Li Fan asked, unwilling to accept fate.

"Even if there is, it is beyond our knowledge. Brother Xuanyuan might know a method." Li Fan's eyes lit up, as if finding a lifeline, and he quickly asked, "By the way, Brother Mo, did you find any trace of Xuan Tianwang while searching the Xuanhuang Realm and the Star Sea with the Eye of the Sky Beast?" Mo Rubing chuckled self-mockingly, "If I had found him, I wouldn't have needed to go to such lengths to clean this Dao Annihilation black energy myself."

"However..."

"It's not a complete loss." Li Fan's gaze immediately locked onto Mo Rubing.

"Back then, when Brother Xuanyuan mysteriously disappeared, at the last moment, he sent out several warning messages."

"Among them, we, his Dharma King brothers, should have all received them."

"There was also one message, transmitted outwards from the Xuanhuang Realm, even beyond the Star Sea."

"This message was extremely secretive. Originally, I shouldn't have been able to perceive it. But thanks to the Eye of the Sky Beast, I was able to sense a trace of it." Mo Rubing whispered.

Li Fan narrowed his eyes upon hearing this, "Beyond the Star Sea? Could it be..." He was startled.

"There is only one possibility. Brother Xuanyuan's recipient must have been the Faceless Immortal." Mo Rubing stated directly.

"I recall you saying that when Xuan Tianwang disappeared back then, the statue and head of the Faceless Immortal inexplicably broke..." Mo Rubing nodded, "So I speculate that Brother Xuanyuan encountered danger, and the Faceless Immortal protected him. However, he couldn't preserve the transmission medium, and the stone statue was severed."

"At the critical moment, Xuan Tianwang discovered something, and thus used the Sky Beast's Eye of the 'Great Floating Star Sea Array' to send a message out of the Star Sea, towards the location of the Faceless Immortal."

"Hoping to convey his findings to that Faceless True Immortal." Li Fan listened intently and then said, "Can we use the traces left in the Eye of the Sky Beast to ascertain what message Xuan Tianwang sent back then?"

"Unfortunately, that is impossible," Mo Rubing also said regretfully.

"Let alone the fact that Brother Xuanyuan would have undoubtedly encrypted it back then."

"Moreover, Brother did not tell us, his Dharma King brothers, about the hidden secret within the message. He chose to notify the Faceless Immortal instead, clearly implying that even if he told us, we would be unable to handle it. Just like the true form of the Calamity of Dao Annihilation, knowing it would only bring more trouble."

Chapter 1353: A Line Breaks Through the High Wall

"Xuan Tianwang's transmission..." Li Fan feigned thought and mused, then sighed after a moment, "It must be a secret that only True Immortals could touch."

Mo Rubing shook his head, "Speculation without basis is meaningless. Although we can't know Xuan Yuan's specific transmission content from back then, this transmission through the Sky Beast's Eye might be able to point us in a direction." So saying, Mo Rubing manipulated the Sky Beast's Eye again.

The countless bubble-like scenes around them froze. Then, they rapidly rewound. It was as if the Sky Beast's Eye was traveling straight forward in the Star Sea.

"This is the trajectory of Xuan Yuan's transmission through the Star Sea back then."

"The High Wall traps the living beings of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. Perhaps this transmission was the only one to escape the Star Sea in ten thousand years."

"I can calculate the exact location where the transmission broke through the High Wall. Then, I can personally go to the site and investigate." Mo Rubing explained slowly.

Li Fan frowned, "At most, it would just leave some traces on the High Wall. Could it possibly punch a hole in the High Wall?" Mo Rubing smiled mysteriously and asked slowly, "Do you know what the High Wall is?" Seeing Li Fan's slightly astonished expression, Mo Rubing asked seriously, "It's called the High Wall, but it's actually the end of the Star Sea, with no path forward. However, this end was created out of thin air, blocking the original path forward. It's like a High Wall that descended from the heavens, sealing off the Star Sea."

"That's right. The High Wall is not a creation, but a rule. Since Xuan Yuan's transmission to the Faceless Immortal back then likely broke through the High Wall and was transmitted to the outside of the starry sky, it means..."

"The rule has been broken." A sharp glint flashed in Mo Rubing's eyes. Li Fan also understood at this moment.

"If that broken rule within the High Wall has not been repaired in ten thousand years, perhaps it's a gap leading outside the High Wall!"

"But... is that possible?"

"After all, so much time has passed. Will the gap in the High Wall still exist?" Li Fan was skeptical.

Mo Rubing smiled, "That depends on our luck. The phenomenon of Dao Annihilation is about to engulf the Star Sea. If we still can't find a way to cross the High Wall..."

"Then I'm afraid there's only a dead end." His smile was filled with coldness. Hearing this, Li Fan's face also became extremely heavy.

Mo Rubing cupped his hands, "The journey to the edge of the Star Sea is long. Previously, I saw that Fellow Daoist's escape technique was unparalleled, so I wish to ask for your assistance." Li Fan responded solemnly, "It's nothing." A viscous membrane enveloped the two of them.

A moment later, they had already left the Sky Beast's Eye and arrived in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. The wooden sword phantom was quietly unsheathed, covering Li Fan and Mo Rubing.

Mo Rubing chanted incantations and cast spells. Suddenly, his forehead split open, and an oval, brownish-yellow eye emerged.

This eye gave Li Fan the same feeling as the Sky Beast's Eye he had been in before.

"This is one of the auxiliary formations of the Sky Beast's Eye, which can attach an observation point to one's body and point the way for navigation in the Star Sea." Mo Rubing explained while manipulating the brown eye to emit a light beam.

It did not illuminate the dark starry sky; perhaps only Li Fan and the two could see it, pointing straight towards the depths of the starry sky to guide their direction.

"Fellow Daoist just needs to follow forward."

"If there are dangerous areas where True Immortal residual power converges along the way, the Sky Beast's guidance will avoid them." As if to confirm Mo Rubing's words, the originally straight light beam suddenly curved.

It seemed to avoid some obstacle and then continued deeper into the Star Sea. Li Fan waved his hand, "No need for such trouble." The wooden sword phantom suddenly accelerated, not dodging or yielding, but directly charging towards the dangerous area marked by the Sky Beast's Eye.

Mo Rubing's expression suddenly changed. However, before he could speak, he was astonished to find that in just an instant, they had traveled a great distance in the Star Sea.

And that dangerous area blocking their path had no impact whatsoever, even when the wooden sword phantom passed through it.

Thus, a somewhat comical scene appeared: the guiding light of the Sky Beast's Eye kept twisting and bending ahead.

The wooden sword phantom, however, only moved forward without detour. The light had to constantly cooperate, changing its indicated direction.

And the flying speed of the wooden sword phantom was so fast that the guidance of the Sky Beast's Eye sometimes disappeared for a period.

Li Fan had no choice but to stop and wait for it to reappear. In this way, the two rushed towards the edge of the Star Sea at high speed.

"I originally thought Fellow Daoist's escape technique was already very strong. I didn't expect it to be even stronger than anticipated! You can actually ignore the True Immortal residual power accumulated in the Star Sea?" After a long period of astonishment, Mo Rubing, who had finally reacted, sighed with admiration.

"It's just that I've made some gains during this time. My lifespan, which was nearing its end, has actually increased somewhat because of this." Li Fan said calmly.

Mo Rubing's gaze swept back and forth across Li Fan's face, but ultimately said nothing more. Protected by Li Fan's escape technique, the arduous journey across the Star Sea directly turned into a clear and safe path.

Less than a day later, they had already passed through the Sea of Relic Treasures and the Great Wall of Remaining Realms, arriving at the edge of the Star Sea.

The guiding light of the Sky Beast's Eye also gradually became blurry. Li Fan slowed down accordingly.

Even though the core of the wooden sword phantom was the Transformation Between True and False, existing between illusion and reality, at such high speeds, crashing headfirst into the High Wall... it would likely shatter the divine ability on the spot and sustain severe injuries.

Mo Rubing used the Sky Beast's attached eye to observe their surroundings. As the saying goes, a millimeter deviation at the start can lead to a thousand-mile error at the end. It was too far from the Xuanhuang Realm. Even if there were no errors in calculation at the starting point, when they reached the edge of the Star Sea, the final destination's position would inevitably have some slight deviation.

"It should be nearby." Before Mo Rubing could finish speaking, the wooden sword phantom controlled by Li Fan suddenly stopped.

"No path forward, the High Wall has arrived." These eight characters made Mo Rubing's expression instantly solemn.

"Please, Fellow Daoist, walk along the boundary. If you observe any traces of the transmission from back then, I will immediately remind you." Li Fan nodded, indicating he understood.

It wasn't that he was deliberately acting aloof, but that the True Immortal residual power gathered beneath the High Wall was on a completely different level from the normal Star Sea.

Moreover, without the resistance and attenuation of the Great Wall of Remaining Realms, relying solely on oneself to withstand this immense power, even Li Fan, who now possessed the supreme escape technique, had to deal with it with all his might.

He moved with great difficulty, exploring along the wall. After an unknown amount of time, Mo Rubing still hadn't found his target.

However, Li Fan began to feel a faint sense of dizziness. A strange sense of dread welled up in his heart, urging him to leave.

Yet, his instincts did not warn him of any danger, only an inexplicable feeling in his heart. Li Fan endured and tried to understand the reason for the changes in his heart.

After a while, he seemed to gain some insight, "This is because I stayed too long beneath the High Wall, and developed an illusion of the High Wall collapsing and pressing down. It's because my own momentum is too disparate from the High Wall." Understanding this, Li Fan felt a slight sense of relief.

Since there was no actual danger, he simply ignored these internal anomalies and continued to explore the High Wall.

However, Li Fan had clearly underestimated the oppressive power of the High Wall's momentum. After another quarter of an hour, the sense of dread in Li Fan's heart intensified.

The Immortal Heart Curse was completely ineffective, and it even affected the flow of spiritual energy within his body and the movement of his thoughts.

Li Fan was even more horrified to discover that his physical size and height had imperceptibly shortened under the pressure of the High Wall's momentum.

Upon further detailed investigation, Li Fan found that it wasn't just that. His soul, and even his cultivation and strength, had also been compressed and reduced.

It felt as if the High Wall had truly descended upon him! Li Fan no longer forced himself. He retreated temporarily, moving away from the High Wall.

"This is the first time I've stayed so close to the High Wall for so long." Only after his body returned to normal did Li Fan breathe a sigh of relief.

He looked at Mo Rubing. His condition was even worse than Li Fan's. Perhaps it was due to observing the High Wall for an extended period, but the Sky Beast's attached eye on Mo Rubing's forehead seemed to be squeezed shut by a hand, closing by nearly half compared to before. And Mo Rubing's body trembled uncontrollably, as if he had encountered something terrifying. Seeing this, a flicker of doubt crossed Li Fan's mind. With Mo Rubing's disposition, even if he saw the High Wall with his own eyes, he shouldn't have been so terrified.

Finally, Mo Rubing spoke, explaining the reason.

"Myriad demonic hearts, all gazing upon the High Wall. Emotions thus multiplied a thousandfold and were imposed upon me..."

"Fellow Daoist, you mock me." Mo Rubing slowly recovered and said, "It's nothing. Even though you are an existence beyond the mortal realm, it's still hard to see such a sight."

"But have you found any trace of Xuan Tianwang's transmission?" Li Fan asked, concerned. To Li Fan's surprise, Mo Rubing nodded, "I compared the section of the boundary we passed through. Indeed, I found one spot that was different from other places."

"But the observation sample is too small; we cannot be sure yet. Next, we need to examine the entire range locked onto by the Sky Beast's Eye."

"That's fine too." After resting for a while and waiting for both of them to return to their peak condition, they set off again. Standing beneath the High Wall again, Li Fan's expression suddenly changed drastically.

Because he discovered that without any prelude, the oppressive feeling he had experienced before had reappeared!

The previous rest had not dispelled the pressure from the High Wall's momentum. When they returned to the foot of the High Wall, Li Fan and the others directly inherited the previous sensations, once again enduring the immense power of the High Wall!

Mo Rubing's body trembled violently. The fearful expression on his face indicated he was in the same situation as Li Fan.

"Since returning is useless, we can only persevere again," Mo Rubing said with intermittent, trembling words.

Li Fan closed his eyes, forcibly suppressing the discomfort in his heart. Following the guidance of the Sky Beast's attached eye, they arduvously explored along the wall.

Walking step by step, Li Fan felt himself becoming smaller and smaller. The High Wall became grander and grander, instilling even greater fear in his heart.

Fortunately, the area that needed to be investigated was not particularly vast.

"As expected, the place we encountered before was different from other parts of the High Wall. Quick!" The Sky Beast's eye, almost completely closed, cast a faint light, indicating the direction for Li Fan.

Under the oppressive force of the High Wall, as their strength was continuously weakened, the effectiveness of Li Fan's wooden sword phantom escape technique also continued to diminish.

Li Fan had a premonition that if he stayed any longer, he might not be able to maintain the wooden sword phantom state.

At that time, without the aid of the escape technique, he would be unable to escape from the foot of the High Wall. And the High Wall's pressure would only increase, potentially crushing him into oblivion.

He would only be able to rely on [Returning to True] to save his life. Fortunately, before that happened, Li Fan had finally brought Mo Rubing to the target location.

It was indeed just a single point. In the vast Utmost Darkness Star Sea, at an endless end, within it, was one spot. Without special guidance, trying to find its exact location under the pressure of the High Wall would be like a fool's dream. But with Xuan Tianwang's transmission from back then, the impossible had become possible.

Originally, Li Fan had planned to escape with his escape technique before his strength was completely depleted. But when he stepped onto this spot, the pressure of the High Wall was still present. However... it no longer accumulated. It was as if they had returned to the state they were in when they first approached the High Wall.

Li Fan and Mo Rubing exchanged glances, seeing the ecstasy in each other's eyes.

"As expected, my guess was correct! Xuan Yuan's transmission has pierced the rules of the High Wall!" Li Fan chimed in, "This place is like a weakness, a flaw in the High Wall. First of all, at least we can stay here and study the secrets of the High Wall."

"Otherwise, forget studying. Even approaching it for a long time is a luxury." Mo Rubing narrowed his eyes, his face completely dazed.

He gazed as if he saw hope of escaping the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. A demonic heart flew out from his body.

His expression was the same as Mo Rubing's main body, trying to reach out and touch the end of this spacetime.

A moment, two moments, three moments... Mo Rubing's expression gradually froze. Because he felt nothing.

That's right, all the effort to come to the location where Xuan Tianwang broke through the wall, yet facing a flawed High Wall, Mo Rubing still felt nothing.

Even a flawed High Wall was not something beings below True Immortal realm could touch. Understanding this, a trace of dispiritedness flashed across Mo Rubing's face.

Not only Mo Rubing, but even Li Fan couldn't gain any insight from this so-called loophole. Ahead lay only nothingness.

Unfathomable, unknowable. Whether there was a flaw or not, they couldn't distinguish. They could only perceive it through the specific effects the High Wall had on them.

Li Fan naturally refused to give up. He immediately had the urge to use the Ascension Array to increase his own momentum, reduce the distance to the High Wall, and try to get a closer look.

However, he then thought that Mo Rubing was by his side, and using the Ascension Array would surely attract the other party's attention. Thus, he temporarily suppressed the idea.

"I'll talk about it next time, when I come alone." With no choice but to sigh at the wall, the two fell silent for a moment.

And the High Wall's pressure did not lessen in the slightest because of their silence. Soon, it reached a point they could no longer bear.

With no other choice, Li Fan had to bring Mo Rubing back to a safe zone.

Chapter 1354: All Beings Comprehend the Principles of Immortality

Mo Rubing looked back at the boundary of the High Wall, a hint of unwillingness on his face.

However, as an unparalleled prodigy of the ancient immortal cultivation world, his mood quickly calmed down after a short while. He exhaled a turbid breath and slowly said, "In the past, I was only one step away from ascending to immortality."

"Brother Xuanyuan, a half-immortal, rarely revealed his true strength in front of us; we mostly interacted as companions."

"This gave me an illusion that the chasm between Immortals and mortals was not that deep."

"At least for me, it was by no means an insurmountable precipice. But now, hehehe..." Mo Rubing's tone was filled with sighs.

"Without climbing the peak, one does not know the height of the mountain; without facing the abyss, one does not know the depth of the water. Even if one has been close to the Immortal Ruins and truly felt the power of True Immortals, how can it compare to truly reaching out and touching it now? To be honest, the might of a True Immortal is truly beyond my imagination," Li Fan also lamented.

"Fellow Daoist, what do you plan to do next? Will you continue to stay here and study the secrets of the High Wall, or will you leave for now and continue searching for Xuan Tianwang?" After sighing, Li Fan turned to ask.

After hesitating for a moment, Mo Rubing looked back at the boundary of the High Wall again. "To leave directly like this, I am still somewhat unwilling. I plan to... look again."

"Thirty days as a deadline. If within these thirty days, there is still no harvest, I will immediately turn and leave, and never face the High Wall again in this life." Mo Rubing was somewhat conflicted and also somewhat bewildered.

Li Fan could quite understand Mo Rubing's current feelings. "To hear the Dao, one can die." The secrets of True Immortals were right before his eyes. Even if they could not be seen or touched, who could leave decisively after just a glance? Especially since the secrets of the High Wall involved hope for escaping the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

Li Fan said in a deep voice, "Since that is the case, then I will leave behind a Wooden Sword phantom to lend fellow Daoist a hand!" With that, Li Fan separated a small sword phantom, enveloping Mo Rubing within it.

"You actually chose to leave and stop studying?" Mo Rubing was immediately taken aback.

"Heh, I am different from fellow Daoist. Fellow Daoist was once someone with the hope of ascension," Li Fan said nonchalantly, first offering some praise, then sighing, "I know deeply that with my aptitude, even if I look tens of millions of times, there will be no substantial change. I am fundamentally unable to comprehend the secrets of the High Wall." Mo Rubing was speechless upon hearing this. However, glancing at the Wooden Sword phantom circling him, he was about to speak again.

But he then heard Li Fan's tone suddenly become impassioned: "However, my temporary departure does not mean I will give up!"

"Since I, this lowly person, cannot achieve it, then why not let everyone in the world try!"

"Hmm?" Mo Rubing's eyes widened abruptly, as if he thought he had misheard.

"You want to bring everyone in the world here, to comprehend the Dao at the foot of the High Wall?" He felt a sense of absurdity.

"With our strength, survival is already so difficult at the foot of the High Wall. For those with lower cultivation, they would surely be crushed by the might of the High Wall, let alone comprehend anything?"

Li Fan smiled freely, "My eyes are like the eyes of all people in the world; my hands are like the hands of all people in the world. My ultimate attainment is like all people in the world personally experiencing it..."

"Using my body as a vessel, I invite all beings in the world to comprehend the principles of the High Wall together." Amidst the words, like chanting scriptures, another phantom flew out from Li Fan's body. It shared ninety percent of the aura of the Wooden Sword phantom, but it was subtly Li Fan's appearance.

It was Li Fan separating a wisp of his divine soul and merging it with the phantom escape technique. Then, aided by formations, his divine soul's perception was amplified thousands of times.

"Let this phantom of mine stay here to accompany fellow Daoist in comprehending the Dao. As for me, I will return to the Xuanhuang Realm and share the phantom's perceptions with everyone in the world," Li Fan smiled.

Mo Rubing wanted to speak but stopped. Li Fan continued, "Don't worry, I will not directly announce the existence of the High Wall to the world, nor will I explain to them that what they are sensing is the flaw in the High Wall."

"But rather, I will simply synchronize the perceptions of my Dao comprehending phantom with them."

"Tens of millions of people, tens of millions of thoughts. Each person's answer will be different, and even if there is no correct answer among them, it will at least give us some inspiration," Li Fan said with an air of complete understanding.

"...Indeed, it is a method," Mo Rubing replied after a long silence, "Indeed, it is a method."

"I'm going now!" Before Li Fan's words had even finished, his figure had already followed the Wooden Sword that pierced the Star Sea, disappearing from Mo Rubing's sight.

Mo Rubing shook his head slightly, temporarily putting Li Fan aside. After resting for a moment, he once again activated the Wooden Sword phantom and approached to explore the flaw in the High Wall.

At the same time, even though Li Fan had not yet returned to the Xuanhuang Realm.

On the Daoscript Platforms located in various small worlds of the Xuanhuang Realm, a drastic change had already occurred. The phantom of the Holy Master, who had been lecturing day and night, suddenly stopped teaching.

Gazing at the sky, he appeared lost in thought. Then, a massive rumbling sound emanated from the Daoscript Platform.

The beings of the small worlds did not understand what had happened and were in an uproar, discussing it with uncertainty.

Suddenly, beams of dark light descended from outside the sky. Following the celestial canopy, they eroded and stained it. In just the time it takes to brew a cup of tea, the originally azure sky was completely dyed ink-black. The world thus fell into complete darkness. No matter how the great sun hanging high in the sky unleashed its brilliance, it could not illuminate this vast world.

In the small world, it was as if the Utmost Darkness Star Sea at this moment, shrouded in darkness. Only the Dao comprehending phantom, eternally standing on the Daoscript Platform, emitted a faint light, bringing the world's only remaining light.

How could the mortals of the small world have ever witnessed such a terrifying scene of light being devoured? They all believed the end of the world was nigh, instantly falling into fear and despair. If not for the light emitted by the Dao comprehending phantom, preventing the small world from falling into complete darkness, it was likely that within this short period, many beings would have committed suicide out of despair. Thus, the Dao comprehending phantom, emitting a light of salvation, became their only lifeline.

Originally, only mortals with aspirations for cultivation would go to the Daoscript Platform to listen. But now, for survival, almost all beings, instinctively like moths to a flame, rushed towards the Daoscript Platform in the center of the small world. The beings beneath the Daoscript Platform grew more numerous. The Daoscript Platform also expanded accordingly, inflating by a million times compared to its original range, almost encompassing the entire small world.

The people knelt, begging the Holy Master phantom above for salvation. The Holy Master phantom stood silently, unmoving. The people pleaded desperately, and they dared not rise until the Holy Master responded.

Finally, a sigh, tinged with sorrow for the world, echoed throughout the heavens and earth. The dark sky, with this sigh, began to change. The Holy Master phantom flew towards the sky, erupting with incomparable radiance, temporarily illuminating the dark heavens and earth. The Holy Master's figure transformed into a long rainbow, filling the sky, covering the entire sky, and slightly blocking the external darkness. It was as if a layer of light cloth had been draped over it, making the world slightly brighter.

This gave the world's beings hope to continue living. They cheered and loudly praised the Holy Master's great name. However, not long after, their cheers abruptly stopped. It seemed that rolling darkness was descending again from beyond the heavens, like a High Wall crushing down upon the sky. The light brought by the Holy Master was further extinguished by more than half. The people fell into panic once more, and cries of despair echoed through the mountains and plains. On the glowing celestial cloth, the Holy Master's resolute face was revealed. He seemed to have gathered his last ounce of strength and charged towards the dark wall outside the world, attempting to shatter the darkness that was destroying the world.

The collision between the Holy Master and the darkness occurred silently. In the end, the Holy Master disappeared completely. But the rolling dark wall outside the world... seemed to have changed somewhat. The people stared intently at the point where the Holy Master's face had finally impacted the dark wall. In their ears, they seemed to hear the Holy Master's last words to them: "The path to salvation lies within."

The people wept bitterly. Faced with the crisis of world destruction, some people gave up all hope of survival and resigned themselves to their fate. But the vast majority were doing their best to ponder the Holy Master's last words. Clearly, the method to break through the dark wall and save the world lay in that invisible but real small point created by the Holy Master's desperate blow.

Just as the beings on the ground were about to try and sense the specific details of that small point. The inconceivable happened. The Daoscript Platform left by the Holy Master emitted a faint glow, scattering onto them. In an instant, they felt as if they had crossed the distance between earth and sky, personally arriving above the celestial canopy. As if experiencing it firsthand, they felt the existence of that small point. Thus, the people understood that this was the Holy Master's last salvation for them, a method to save the world and themselves.

To save themselves, the beings on the ground unleashed astonishing potential. One by one, they quickly established a connection with the Daoscript Platform, and with mortal bodies, began to comprehend that small point within the dark wall.

... This scene occurred in all the small worlds where Daoscript Platforms were erected. And the cause of all this was naturally Li Fan. At this moment, Li Fan's true body had already returned to the Xuanhuang Realm. Using formations, he had conjured endless darkness, sealing the sky canopies of various small worlds. He felt the resistance from the Heavenly Dao of these small worlds. Although the power of a single world was negligible to Li Fan now, with the combined might of multiple worlds, Li Fan found processing it somewhat strenuous. However... it was only strenuous. After considerable effort, Li Fan suppressed them all. In any case, according to the plan, these small worlds would eventually return to the Xuanhuang Realm as nourishment for the sublimation of the Super Xuanhuang Realm. The Heavenly Dao consciousness of these small worlds would also eventually be consumed. Using formations to connect these nourishing small worlds. Li Fan observed the situation within these worlds. "Based on my experience, beings only erupt with their greatest potential when they face a fatal crisis. If I merely ask them to help comprehend, without this sense of impending crisis forcing them, their efficiency will surely decrease."

"This is very good now..." Feeling the countless thoughts of comprehension from all beings being synchronized by the Daoscript Platform, Li Fan nodded with satisfaction. The gap between mortals and cultivators was already like heaven and earth. Let alone the gap between mortals and True Immortals. But precisely because True Immortals were too high and mighty. In the eyes of True Immortals, mortals and ordinary cultivators were essentially indistinguishable. Therefore, for comprehending the flaw within the High Wall, cultivators and mortals were essentially the same.

"The advantage lies in the sheer number of mortals. The sample size is sufficiently detailed."

"Moreover, during this period, under the subtle influence of the Daoscript Platform's coverage, the small worlds have evolved towards immortal cultivation worlds. Quite a few cultivators have emerged from this group of people." Li Fan analyzed the comprehension of all beings, finding almost all of it useless. However, he was not discouraged; it had only just begun. He differentiated a formation to simulate a personality, specifically to categorize and process these thoughts of comprehension from all beings. It filtered out most of the invalid information, retaining and transmitting only what was worth Li Fan's personal inspection.

"This is also part of the plan."

"It's not that I truly expect to uncover the secrets of the High Wall relying on the masses of beings."

"Ultimately, perhaps it still depends on myself." Li Fan sensed the perceptions being synchronized from the Dao comprehending phantom far away in the Star Sea.

"The High Wall, a creation of True Immortals. Researching it alone is truly difficult."

"Besides the masses, perhaps the immortal artifacts can also help."

"It's a pity that the Immeasurable Mirror has already been fed to the Xuanhuang Realm. If I don't gain anything in this lifetime, I might consider trying it in the next." In fact, discovering the flaw in the High Wall through Mo Rubing was an unexpected joy. Li Fan's current main focus was still on the Dao integration of Heaven and Earth Immortal Souls. As for crossing the High Wall, it was not urgent for now. "Even if I truly decipher the secrets of the High Wall, I will never risk my own life!"

"The dangers outside the High Wall are truly too great!" The scene of the cat treasure devouring Immortals in his previous life, and the collapse of the High Wall, reappeared in his mind. Without fear, he snorted coldly and suppressed these stray thoughts. With a single step, he arrived at the Xuanhuang Realm. Looking up at the firmament. Having received the promises of the Star Sea, Li Fan could now almost effortlessly establish contact with the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao. Moreover, the Heavenly Dao was no longer indifferent as before. Instead, it was clearly showing a hint of obsequiousness.

"This Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao..." Li Fan snorted coldly, feeling a mix of amusement and exasperation. Temporarily setting aside these matters, Li Fan, through communication with Heaven and Earth, began to understand the various changes occurring within the Xuanhuang Realm in more detail. It was like a detailed examination before a major surgery for a critically ill patient. Although Li Fan could investigate on his own, it was always less convenient and accurate than asking the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao consciousness directly. While communicating, Li Fan also continuously imparted some of his insights gained from the Star Sea Origin True Will and the foot of the High Wall in this life to the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao. He was completely giving, with no intention of taking anything in return. This step was to strengthen the intimacy and bond with the Xuanhuang Realm. Just as it is easiest to cultivate goodwill during childhood, Li Fan also wanted to solidify their connection before the Xuanhuang Realm's sublimation. This would make it easier to swallow the Heaven and Earth Immortal Souls in the future.

Chapter 1355: Ascending the World's Heavenly Grid

Under the Xuanhuang sky, wind and clouds changed drastically. Whether it was the power of the Star Sea's recovery or the sight from overlooking after ascension,

For the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao, these were originally unfathomable secrets. It instinctively and continuously absorbed them.

Corresponding changes also quietly occurred in heaven and earth. However, this was destined to be a long process, just like the Star Sea's recovery.

At this moment, it had just begun, in its embryonic stage. Hardly anyone in the Xuanhuang Realm could perceive this change.

Li Fan, as the source of this change, especially now that he was connected with the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao,

Naturally, he could clearly see the changes in heaven and earth. This was a power of evolution directly contrary to Xuanhuang's World Destruction Transformation.

But it was equally vast and surging, stirring the heart. Li Fan also felt the rapidly increasing favorability from the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao.

With the might of the Star Sea Origin, plus the tangible benefits of generously imparting knowledge, under the dual pressure of benevolence and might, the rate of increase in favorability even far surpassed that of the Sacred Emperor in his previous life!

Only when the increase in favorability gradually slowed down did Li Fan temporarily stop this "lesson." The Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao was reluctant to part. However, Li Fan resolutely bid farewell and returned directly to the small world of Da Qi, severing the connection with the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao.

As Li Fan's birthplace and the first place of preaching in this life, the sky of Da Qi was not shrouded in darkness like other small worlds.

However, the preaching platforms stood tall, and their scale almost covered all human habitats. While the beings listened to the Sacred Master's preaching, their thoughts and insights were also simultaneously recorded on the preaching platforms.

Perceived by Li Fan. It was as if billions of beings were helping Li Fan comprehend the Dao at the same time. The content of their comprehension was all-encompassing and inexhaustible.

However, besides the Da Qi preaching platform, the thoughts and insights of beings in other small worlds were all directed towards the flaw in the High Wall.

This was also the reason why Li Fan chose to maintain the original state of Da Qi: to ensure the diversity of thoughts and insights. Within the Da Qi preaching platform, the simulated heavenly grace, like a silver eye, appeared to be still.

In reality, it rotated more than a billion times every moment, looking at the beings of Da Qi's enlightenment, the mountains and trees of the small world, the flowing water and white clouds of the small world.

Compared to when this simulated heavenly grace was first created, the silver eye had become much more lifelike.

It no longer looked like a cultivator's creation, but like a living being.

"What exactly is the Heavenly Dao of a world?" To fear the powerful and rely on the strong. The nature of the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao, similar to a pet dog, was still vivid in his memory.

Li Fan couldn't help but ponder this question. Opening his left hand, in a circular cage-like space of golden light, floated wisps of invisible intent.

These were all the Heavenly Dao consciousnesses of the small worlds that Li Fan had extracted and imprisoned here when he had callously erected the dark High Wall in various small worlds. He then used the simulated heavenly grace to replace them, maintaining the normal operation of each small world.

"What I extracted was not the complete Heavenly Dao of the world. It should only be the [Heavenly Grace] that these small worlds generated over long years, possessing various temperaments. After being extracted, the small worlds returned to their original state and operated by instinct. If I hadn't filled in my simulated heavenly grace..."

"The temperament of the Heavenly Grace should be related to the size of the world, its resource conditions, and other factors."

"For example, this one originated from a small world full of calamities. Therefore, it gave me a feeling of extreme caution and alertness towards the outside world. And this one came from a mortal world similar in size to Da Qi. This world had everything, with a rather upright aura. If we don't consider the scale, it's even more like a 'legitimate successor' than the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao..." Li Fan distinguished the various world Heavenly Graces in the cage.

Then, he slowly fed each of them to the silver eye before him. Although he still didn't know how the Heavenly Grace of a world was born or what conditions needed to be met.

Li Fan was certain that the nurturing of the Heavenly Grace itself represented a form of power. Almost visibly, as the silver eye slowly devoured these small world Heavenly Graces.

It became more and more lifelike. The feeling Li Fan got was that it was becoming...

"Livelier." Although it had seemed like a living being before, it was far from it. Now, it was almost like a pet with a soul.

Before devouring the world's Heavenly Grace, the silver eye only faithfully executed Li Fan's commands, monitoring and perceiving the thoughts of the beings in Da Qi's small world.

But now, this silver eye would occasionally secretly observe Li Fan. Its divine eye clearly conveyed a meaning of seeking favor. Li Fan met its gaze, and it seemed encouraged. Its eyeballs rolled, acting coquilshly and performing.

"Interesting." Li Fan saw a desire for more world Heavenly Graces in its eyes.

Li Fan remained indifferent and gently beckoned. The silver eye actively floated closer, bringing its body closer to Li Fan's outstretched hand.

Instantly, countless thoughts from Da Qi's small world, present and past, appeared around Li Fan, categorized.

Moreover, the silver eye perfectly organized the categories for Li Fan, making it convenient for Li Fan to view.

When Li Fan had a thought, the silver eye could quickly perceive it and then organize and present what Li Fan needed, one by one.

"Compared to before, it is undoubtedly much smarter and more useful."

"No wonder in the ancient immortal cultivation era, they always refined a world into a magical artifact at every turn. This world Heavenly Grace is almost the ultimate version of a spirit!" Li Fan mused as he looked at the silver eye before him.

"It's a pity that even after devouring so many world Heavenly Graces, this silver eye still feels far inferior to the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao."

"It seems unrealistic to replace it with this."

"What exactly is the factor that has caused its qualitative change?" If Li Fan could replace the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao consciousness with his own creation, it would undoubtedly be a matter of great significance to him.

Only by completely turning the Xuanhuang Realm into his own solid stronghold could it serve as a bridgehead for exploring beyond the High Wall.

Li Fan pondered as he perceived the thoughts of all beings conveyed by the silver eye. Suddenly, a piece of information that was heavily marked by the silver eye popped out.

Li Fan's gaze narrowed. It was the experiences of Sun Erlang, Wang Xuanba, and Yue Zhenwei, synchronized and perceived.

Previously, under Li Fan's subtle guidance, they had gone to the territory of the Five Elders Society, hoping to find the Nascent Soul Cave-Heaven.

But after a series of setbacks, they accidentally entered the Land of Joyful Peace, trapped in a dream world full of man-eating demons. They barely found a way to break free from the world and successfully escaped.

However, they did not leave the Land of Joyful Peace. In order to unravel the secrets of the Land of Joyful Peace, they had no choice but to continue to the remaining two dream boundaries.

"So much time has passed; they should have found something by now."

"The Land of Joyful Peace..." With a thought, countless lights and shadows surged towards Li Fan. The encounters of Sun Erlang and the others during this period instantly appeared.

After gaining experience from completing the first dream world, Sun Erlang and his group initially thought that the subsequent two worlds would be easier.

But the facts proved that they had vastly underestimated the risks of the Land of Joyful Peace. The second dream world they entered was a terrifying doomsday they had never heard of.

In the vast Star Sea, civilization was decaying, and life force was dim. A terrifying swarm of alien insects had become the true rulers of the Star Sea.

Wherever the insect swarms passed, all life on the ground was devoured, leaving only hard stones that were difficult to digest.

When Sun Erlang and the others descended, they saw a desolate land of deathly silence. And their mission was to survive for half a year under the siege of the insect swarms on the surface that had not yet evacuated.

The second dream world was completely different from the first. There were no puzzles. The moment they entered, task prompts and methods of leaving the world automatically appeared in their minds.

There were even task rewards. Initially, Sun Erlang and the others did not think the mission was too difficult. But when they truly clashed with the overwhelming insect swarms, they knew they were wrong.

Even with the combat divine abilities mastered from the Sacred Master phantom, facing the absolutely overwhelming numbers of the insect swarms, they experienced powerlessness for the first time.

The insect swarms were endless. No matter how many were annihilated by divine abilities, they would soon emerge from somewhere underground, filling the void.

After suffering hardships, the trio quickly changed their strategy. They fought while retreating. However, the insect swarms were almost everywhere in the world. No matter where they fled, there were always endless insect swarms chasing them.

In less than seven days, the trio was almost driven to a desperate situation. Wang Xuanba even cursed loudly, believing that this mission was impossible to complete.

Fortunately, in the previous dream world, Sun Erlang had learned the Spirit Devouring Art from the Pig Demon statue. In the midst of intense battle, he finally achieved basic mastery.

Then, using the corpses of the insect swarms as food and fighting to sustain their fight, with infinite resources for replenishment and no fear of attrition, the trio's situation immediately improved.

Sun Erlang held the line. Then, Wang Xuanba, through sheer luck, found a powerful magic artifact within the belly of an alien insect.

It could summon a mechanical puppet as tall as thirty feet. Initially, when this puppet was summoned, it remained still.

But after some research, Wang Xuanba discovered its true usage. His body transformed into ethereal light and merged with the puppet's massive form and consciousness. Using the puppet's immense power, he annihilated the insect swarms. Although the situation seemed to improve, facing the endless sea of alien insects still made Sun Erlang and the others feel despair.

They persevered in this manner for nearly three months. Their bodies and wills had almost reached their limit. Thinking that they wouldn't truly die in a dream anyway, they almost all had thoughts of giving up.

At the critical moment, it was the meticulous Yue Zhenwei who discovered that although the insect swarms seemed to act on instinct.

Their movement patterns actually followed a certain pattern, as if something was secretly directing them.

This discovery invigorated the trio. After confirming that Yue Zhenwei's discovery was highly likely, they decided to take a gamble.

They used themselves as bait, eventually luring out the master behind the insect swarms. They had initially thought that this master would be a high-ranking figure among the alien insects.

However, when that master appeared, it still surprised Sun Erlang and the others immensely. Because they were commanding the insect swarms, it appeared to be a creation of a cultivator.

A purple-gold gourd, engraved with unknown talismans. And above the gourd stood a wooden puppet boy.

He pointed his finger at Sun Erlang and the trio, who were surrounded by insect swarms. Below, the purple-gold gourd emitted various strange lights.

Countless alien insects suddenly went berserk and surged towards Sun Erlang and the trio, disregarding their lives. The trio knew that as long as they defeated the wooden puppet boy and gained control of the purple-gold gourd, they could control the insect swarms.

Completing the mission of surviving for half a year would then be easy. Thus, they fought desperately. Wang Xuanba transformed into the mechanical puppet, attracting the attention of the insect swarms.

Sun Erlang, like a sharp arrow, disregarded his own safety and charged directly towards the wooden puppet boy. And in secret, the weakest Yue Zhenwei launched the final blow.

In the end, the wooden puppet was shattered. At the end of the great battle, the trio were all on the verge of death, trapped in an endless tide of insects. But as Yue Zhenwei held the purple-gold gourd in his hand.

Those ferocious alien insects all became frozen in stillness. Subsequently, the mission of survival was no longer in doubt.

Two more months later. The second dream world was completed. After leaving the dream, the trio not only recovered from their injuries but also...

Yue Zhenwei had brought out the purple-gold gourd. Inside the gourd were a staggering ninety-nine trillion, nine hundred ninety-nine billion, nine hundred ninety-nine million, nine hundred ninety-nine thousand, nine hundred ninety-nine [Star Swallowing Insects]!

Of course, Yue Zhenwei, at the Golden Core stage, could not fully unleash the power of this magical artifact. He could only summon nine hundred million Star Swallowing Insects.

As his cultivation level increased, the number and strength of the Star Swallowing Insects he could summon would continuously improve. Although they obtained a supreme treasure, the trio did not seem overjoyed.

Instead, endless doubt and fear welled up in their hearts. Nine trillion Star Swallowing Insects, even in the real Xuanhuang Realm, possessed destructive power comparable to that of heaven and earth.

And now, this power was controlled by a mere Golden Core cultivator. Although it was only in a dream, and it was uncertain if it could be brought back to reality.

It still made Yue Zhenwei and the others feel incredibly absurd. They had only been in the dream world for such a short time and already had such gains.

It was difficult to imagine what kind of accumulation those who had been in the dream world for a long time might have. With trepidation, after resting for a while.

They headed towards the third dream world. With a treasure like the purple-gold gourd, and with the assistance of nine hundred million Star Swallowing Insects, the third world should be easily passable, right?

But upon entering the third dream world, reality dealt them another heavy blow. The moment they entered the dream world, they all transformed into immobile, speechless straw figures.
