Their spiritual energy and treasures all vanished. They could only communicate through the power of the dream itself, with simple exchanges.

This time, there were no demonic beasts or insect swarms attacking. There were also no task prompts from the dream. It was just three straw figures lying quietly on black stones that resembled mountain peaks.

Subjected to wind, rain, lightning, and thunder. Unable to move, the trio initially spent their days pondering what the condition for completing the task would be.

But as time passed day by day, their spirits began to break.

Chapter 1356: First Understanding of the Paradise Mystery

Initially, the three would occasionally exchange insights on completing tasks. But they gradually discovered that all their speculations and deductions were meaningless.

The three straw figures were like islands separate from the world. Only the wind, rain, and thunder from the heavens could interact with them.

Beyond that, everything in the mortal realm seemed to be oblivious to their existence. Birds, beasts, and insects flew past them without pause.

Even the fine dust of the world did not settle upon them. Thus, the three gradually fell silent. Lying motionlessly, they watched the world transform.

Sun rose and set, years passed. It was as if the speed had been fast-forwarded, days turning into weeks. The mountain peaks where the three were located, eroded by rain and wind, gradually became slender and sharp.

The once majestic and full mountain bodies slowly transformed into sharp, solitary peaks. Standing abruptly between heaven and earth.

The surrounding terrain of the mountain peaks also changed from continuous green mountains to magnificent canyons with countless ravines. The transformation of seas into mulberry fields occurred, yet only the black stones where Sun Erlang and the others lay remained eternally unchanged.

Under the scouring of wind and rain, the intentions of the three were also eroded by the power of time, becoming somewhat decayed and blurry.

They even began to lose their reactions to external events. If this continued, their consciousness might eventually dissipate completely.

Just as they were about to sink entirely, a majestic and sacred figure suddenly erupted with ten thousand rays of light, appearing in their minds.

It seemed taller than heaven and earth, blocking all the invading wind and rain.

"Saint Master..." Although their memories were blurry. These two words seemed etched into their souls, emerging instinctively.

"Saint Master, Saint Master, Saint Master." The three repetitively uttered these words like automatons. As if from a spring welling up, past memories resurfaced in their parched minds.

"Ah!!" The three awoke as if from a terrible nightmare. They knew that the Saint Master had saved their lives from afar.

But if they could not find a way out, they would likely still face the same fate of sinking. Thus, seizing this rare moment of clarity, the three began to discuss incessantly.

During their exchange, the three were somewhat surprised to discover that it seemed they had indeed endured tens of millions of years of time's grind.

The temperaments of the three had become much steadier. Even in the face of crisis, they no longer panicked as before.

"Dream trials are definitely not a dead end. When the mountain peak beneath us is finally broken by rain and wind erosion, and the black stone falls, perhaps liberation will come. As long as we hold on until that moment, we can complete the mission." The three finally reached this conclusion.

And with this as their final belief, they gritted their teeth and persevered. Countless more years passed, and the figure of the Saint Master in their minds had become almost invisible.

Only the constant repetition of their obsession became the reason for their persistence. This day.

The mountain, eroded to its extreme, supported only by a thin column of rock. Could no longer bear the weight of the black stone above.

After a gust of breeze, it collapsed with a roar. The three straw figures, falling from the peak into the mortal world, saw the world as if plunged into stillness in their eyes.

The clear sky suddenly turned gloomy. It was as if a black film had been cast over it. A colossal black bird's beak pierced the sky, coming from beyond the firmament.

Merely half of its bird's head was almost larger than the entire world. Its two sharp bird eyes, scanning slightly, locked onto the three falling straw figures.

Sun Erlang and the other two saw a look of satisfaction in the eyes of this indescribably giant fierce bird. With a terrifying bird cry, the world began to disintegrate inch by inch.

Within the three straw figures, three light clusters flew out from their brows, hearts, and abdomens respectively.

Slowly rising, they flew towards the fierce bird. Sun Erlang and the others, their consciousness still within the straw figures, vaguely saw the flow of time and the changes of mountains and rivers within these three light clusters.

Boom! Immediately after, the world plunged into endless darkness. Even the simulated Heavenly Dao monitoring it could not determine how much true time had passed.

Sun Erlang and the other two's consciousnesses gradually recovered. They had successfully escaped the dream. Not only were they unharmed, but they had also gained a divine ability called [Observation of Mountains and Rivers Through Time].

The self was transformed into that straw figure on the mountain peak, and time flowed as if it were stationary in itself. Then, observing the changes of the world, time flowed like a river.

It was somewhat similar to when Li Fan transformed into the Vast Ocean Pearl and observed the transformations of heaven and earth through the passage of eons. However, the powerful aspect of [Observation of Mountains and Rivers Through Time] was that after activating the divine ability, one's lifespan was almost frozen.

Even if ten million years passed in the outside world, the impact on oneself would be almost negligible. Of course, this was merely a dream prompt, a theoretical explanation.

As for whether this divine ability was truly effective... Sun Erlang and the others had no intention of trying it yet. After completing the three, and all, dream boundaries, their environment finally changed again.

They were still in the Qiu Stream Prefecture within the Five Elders' Society. However, unlike the sparsely populated situation before, the Qiu Stream Prefecture here was bustling with activity.

Not only were the cities filled with cultivators, but even the originally desolate wilderness suddenly had countless buildings appearing.

Moreover, it seemed that cultivators resided within these buildings. The changes were not only external. They also occurred within Sun Erlang and the others themselves.

"Sun Erlang, Golden Core Perfection, Number of Deaths: 1."

"Joyful Land Experience Level: 2."

"Current Unlockable Dream World Level: 3."

"Worry-Free Coins: 2000."... These were the personal information that Sun Erlang and the others could all see. When the pink progress bar finally filled up, the so-called Joyful Land Experience Level finally advanced to level 2.

An option to unlock dream worlds was added. In addition to this, there were some other more detailed information introductions.

And when their intentions focused on those texts, details would finally appear in their minds, no longer requiring them to guess.

Sun Erlang carefully read every item, so as not to miss any crucial information.

"So, local cultivators of the Five Elders' Society entering the Worry-Free Joyful Land, although they also have to undergo trials of three dream worlds, their experiences will never be as difficult as ours. In the language of the Joyful Land, the world difficulty level has reached level 3."

"The reason our encounters were so special is that we are not members of the Five Elders' Society, but unauthorized trespassers who entered without the permission of the Worry-Free Heavenly Venerable!"

"But the Heavenly Venerable is merciful and will not directly expel us. Instead, they will impose dream trials. If we can successfully pass, we can officially join the Dream Joyful Land. If we fail the trial, we will be eternally banished from the Joyful Land. And as a penalty for consuming the power used to construct the dream, a large portion of our soul power will be absorbed..." Sun Erlang's expression turned somewhat grim.

He exchanged glances with Wang Xuanba and Yue Zhenwei, and continued to check.

"The place we encountered when we first entered the dream was the transit point leading to the trial dream worlds. All cultivators entering the Joyful Land for the first time will appear there."

"Within the Dream Joyful Land, cultivators can harm each other. If this rule is ignored and combat is initiated forcefully, the attacked party will be transferred to a safe zone. And depending on the severity of the situation, the attacker will be deducted Worry-Free Coins."

"Worry-Free Coins, also known as Joyful Land Coins, are obtained by cultivators through exploration and activities within the Dream Joyful Land. They can be used in the Heavenly Venerable's Treasury to exchange for various resources and strengthen oneself."

"The Heavenly Venerable's Treasury contains everything, is all-encompassing..." Sun Erlang looked at the two thousand Joyful Land Coins he carried, and his heart stirred. He opened the details page of the Heavenly Venerable's Treasury.

Instantly, Sun Erlang was stunned. Even with his current Joyful Land Experience Level 2 authority, the number of items he could see was limited.

But the details of the Heavenly Venerable's Treasury were still unbelievable to him. Not to mention the most basic heavenly materials and earthly treasures, elixirs, and magic artifacts.

Even cultivation techniques were merely ordinary items in the Heavenly Venerable's Treasury. And unlike the cultivation techniques popular in the Xuanhuang Realm, these techniques could be cultivated to the Nascent Soul stage at the very least.

Moreover, according to the Joyful Land's explanation, there was no need to worry about being unable to cultivate profound techniques. As long as one exchanged for them, one could instantly gain an initial understanding.

Consuming Joyful Land Coins could accelerate the progress of cultivation techniques.

"Once exchanged for oneself, it cannot be shared with others. But it can be gifted before learning."

"In this way, although the Joyful Land does not have the restriction of 'no immortal techniques can be cultivated together,' it is almost the same. To cultivate, one still needs to exchange and pay."

"One's cultivation and techniques in the present world are only synchronized once upon initial entry into the Joyful Land, becoming the starting point for oneself in the Joyful Land."

"But future progress in the Joyful Land generally cannot be brought back to reality, that is, the Xuanhuang Realm." Sun Erlang's brow furrowed upon seeing this.

However, after a moment's thought, he was soon relieved. After all, the aspects of the Joyful Land were too heaven-defying. If every item could be synchronized to reality, then the scale of the Joyful Land would absolutely not be on the same level as the Xuanhuang Realm.

"As the name suggests, the Joyful Land is guided by the power of the great Worry-Free Heavenly Venerable, and is constructed from various dream worlds."

"The blueprints for constructing dream worlds may originate from historical fragments that once occurred in the Xuanhuang Realm, or from the dreams of living beings, or from even deeper, great intentions. Therefore, it is not eternally safe, but filled with all sorts of dangers."

"To facilitate exploration, there are distinctions between Dream Experience levels and Dream World levels." Sun Erlang nodded slightly.

With their Golden Core Perfection strength, exploring Level 3 dream worlds was already their limit. Any further, and they would surely die without a doubt.

With a general judgment of the danger level, explorers would not be sent to die in vain.

"In the Joyful Land, one can die."

"The number of deaths a cultivator can experience is not infinite."

"The number of deaths is a very important indicator for judging a cultivator's identity in the dream, second only to the Dream Experience Level."

"Cultivators with similar numbers of deaths are roughly in the same world layer in the Joyful Land. The general divisions are 1-3 deaths, 3-5 deaths, 5-10 deaths, 10-15 deaths."

"The death limit should be 15 deaths. If one dies again at that point..."

"It's truly death."

"And in reality, too." Sun Erlang's heart trembled.

"An increase in the number of deaths not only means a change in the surrounding personnel but also signifies the decay of one's spiritual nature."

"Spiritual nature is a hidden stat, not displayed, but it truly exists in the Joyful Land and can affect the actual efficiency of combat and cultivation."

"The more one dies, the lower the spiritual nature, and the more difficult it becomes to progress."

"It seems this spiritual nature has other effects..." Sun Erlang pondered silently.

"The number of deaths can also be eliminated through certain methods. Besides using Joyful Land Coins to exchange in the Heavenly Venerable's Treasury, one can also use items obtained from dreams."

"Of course, the value is not cheap."

"Judging by this, the Worry-Free Joyful Land is fraught with danger. But it is why the entire Five Elders' Society yearns for it, because this dream realm is truly worthy of the name [Worry-Free]."

"Every cultivator, just by paying a certain amount of Joyful Land Coins, can generate a dream world unique to them."

"Whether it's an absolute emperor who commands all, or an immortal emperor who controls everything, it can be realized in a dream."

"In the dream, it is almost indistinguishable from reality. And the more Joyful Land Coins paid, the richer the details..."

"However, besides the initial cost of forging the dream, maintaining the dream's existence also requires Joyful Land Coins."

"This is also the driving force for cultivators to explore dream worlds."

"The higher the Dream World level, although the risk is greater, the corresponding gains will also be more numerous."

"Exploring dreams can be done alone, or in groups."

"Every period of time, there will be free dream worlds available for exploration. Of course, one can also spend Joyful Land Coins to unlock them in advance."... Sun Erlang gradually gained a detailed understanding of the various aspects of the [Worry-Free Joyful Land].

What truly captured his attention were the last pieces of information he learned.

"Under normal circumstances, nothing in the dream can be brought back to reality."

"But there are exceptions."

"One is protected by the Worry-Free Heavenly Venerable's power. It can be achieved with almost no cost, but this has rarely happened in the entire history of the Joyful Land."

"Second are critical items. By submitting them, one can choose a portion of one's dream power to bring back to reality."

"Third, deep exploration of unknown dream worlds."

"Fourth... submitting a large amount of Joyful Land Coins." Sun Erlang and the others exchanged glances again, communicating with each other.

"This Joyful Land is truly beyond our expectations."

"Even the Saint Master might not fully understand it. The strength of the one who created such a magnificent land is truly unimaginable."

"However, dreams are dreams after all, and they are ultimately illusions. We must eventually return to reality."

"It's just that, from the looks of it now, it seems somewhat difficult. There are millions of beings in the Joyful Land, and only a handful can return to reality each year." Yue Zhenwei pondered.

"Actually, I think even if we can't go back, staying in this Joyful Land is not bad. Look at this treasury, there are still many dream world templates. Any one of them is extremely wonderful." Wang Xuanba stared at the various items in the Heavenly Venerable's Treasury and couldn't help but say so.

Sun Erlang remained silent.

Chapter 1357: Secret of the Primordial Yellow

In the beginning, the trio would still occasionally discuss their thoughts on completing the task. But they gradually discovered that all their guesses and deductions were meaningless.

The three straw figures seemed independent of the world. Only the wind, rain, and lightning from the heavens could come into contact with them.

Apart from that, everything in the mortal world seemed to be oblivious to their existence. Birds and beasts, insects and worms flew past them without stopping.

Even the dust of the world did not settle upon them. Thus, the trio slowly fell silent. Lying there powerlessly, watching the world change.

Sun rose and set, time passed. It was as if the fast-forward button had been pressed; days passed. The mountain peaks where the trio were located, eroded by rain and wind-blown sand, gradually became slender and sharp.

The originally majestic and towering full mountain bodies slowly became sharp lone peaks standing solitary between heaven and earth. And the terrain around the mountain peaks, from continuous green mountains, transformed into magnificent canyons with thousands of ravines. The changes of sea and mulberry fields, only the black stones on which Sun Erlang and the others lay remained eternally unchanged.

In the wind and rain, the trio's consciousness was also scoured by the power of time, becoming somewhat decayed and blurred.

They even began to lose their reaction to external events. If things continued like this, the trio's consciousness might eventually dissipate completely.

Just as they were about to completely sink into oblivion, a majestic, divine figure suddenly appeared in their minds, emitting myriad rays of divine light.

It seemed taller than heaven and earth, blocking all the invading wind and rain.

"Sacred Master..." Although their memories were already blurred, these two words seemed engraved in their souls and naturally emerged.

"Sacred Master, Sacred Master, Sacred Master." The trio repeatedly uttered these two words as if bewitched, as if a spring had gushed forth from dry ground, and past memories resurfaced in their dried-up minds.

"Ah!!" The trio abruptly woke up as if from a nightmare. They knew that the Sacred Master had saved their lives in the mystical realm.

But if they couldn't find a way to escape, they would probably still face the same fate of sinking into oblivion. Thus, they seized this rare moment of clarity and began to discuss incessantly.

During their communication, the trio was somewhat surprised to find that it seemed they had truly endured tens of millions of years of time's tempering.

The temperaments of the three had become much calmer. Even in the face of current danger, they were no longer as panicked as before.

"The dream trials will absolutely not be a dead end. When the mountain peak beneath us is finally broken by the erosion of rain and wind-blown sand, and the black stone falls, perhaps liberation will come. As long as we hold on until that moment, we can complete the mission." The three finally reached this conclusion.

And with this as their ultimate belief, they grit their teeth and persevered. After countless more years passed, the figure of the Sacred Master in their minds had become almost invisible.

Only the constantly repeated obsession became the reason for their perseverance. On this day. The mountain, which had become extremely "thin," supported only by a slender pillar of stone, could no longer bear the weight of the black stone above.

After a gentle breeze, it collapsed with a roar. The three straw figures, falling from the mountain peak into the mortal world, saw the world seem to fall into a state of stillness within their eyes.

The clear sky suddenly turned gloomy, as if covered by a layer of black film. A giant black bird's beak pierced the sky, coming from outside the celestial dome.

Just half of the bird's head was almost larger than the entire world. Its two sharp bird eyes, as they rotated slightly, locked onto the three straw figures falling below.

Sun Erlang and the trio saw a look of satisfaction in the eyes of this indescribably giant ferocious bird. With a terrifying bird cry, the world began to crumble inch by inch.

From the three straw figures, three spheres of light flew out from the center of their brows, hearts, and abdomens respectively.

They slowly ascended towards the ferocious bird. Sun Erlang and the others, their consciousness still within the straw figures, vaguely saw scenes of time flowing and mountains and rivers changing from these three spheres of light.

Boom! Following that, the world plunged into endless darkness. Even the monitoring simulated heavenly grace was uncertain how much time had truly passed.

Sun Erlang and the trio's consciousnesses finally recovered. They had successfully escaped from the dream. Not only were they unharmed, but they had even gained a divine ability called [Mountain River Time View].

Their bodies transformed into the straw figures on the mountain peaks, and time seemed to flow in a state of stillness for them. Then, observing the changes of the world through the passage of time. Similar to when Li Fan transformed into the Azure Pearl and observed the changes of the world from sea to mulberry fields. However, the powerful aspect of the [Mountain River Time View] was that after activating the divine ability, one's own lifespan was almost frozen.

Even if millions of years passed in the outside world, the impact on oneself was negligible. Of course, this was just the dream's prompt and theoretical explanation.

As for whether this divine ability was truly effective... Sun Erlang and the others had not yet planned to test it. After completing the three, and thus all, dream boundaries, their environment finally changed again.

They were still in Qiuxi Prefecture within the Five Elders Society's territory. However, unlike the sparsely populated situation before, Qiuxi Prefecture here was bustling with activity.

Not only were there cultivators everywhere in the city, but even in the originally desolate wilderness, countless buildings suddenly appeared.

And these buildings seemed to have cultivators residing within them. The changes were not limited to the outside world. They also occurred within Sun Erlang and the others themselves.

"Sun Erlang, Golden Core Consummation, Number of Deaths: 1."

"Joyful Peace Experience Level: 2."

"Current Unlockable Dream World Level: 3."

"Joyful Coins: 2000."... This was the personal information that Sun Erlang and the others could all see. When the pink progress bar was finally full, the so-called Joyful Peace Experience Level finally advanced to level 2.

An option to unlock dream worlds was added. In addition, there were some other more detailed information introductions.

And when their consciousness focused on those words, they could finally see detailed explanations in their minds, rather than having to guess everything themselves.

Sun Erlang carefully read each item to avoid missing any crucial information.

"So, native cultivators of the Five Elders Society who enter the Land of Joyful Peace must also undergo three dream world trials. However, they will never experience hardships like ours. In the words of the Land of Joyful Peace, the world difficulty level has reached level 3."

"The reason our encounters were so special is that we are not members of the Five Elders Society, but outsiders who trespassed without the permission of the Joyful Peace Heavenly Venerate!"

"But the Heavenly Venerate is merciful and will not directly expel us. Instead, He will bestow dream trials. If successful, we can officially join the Dream Land of Joyful Peace. If the trial fails, we will be forever banished from the Land of Joyful Peace. As a punishment for consuming power to construct the dream, a large portion of our soul power will be drained..." Sun Erlang's expression was somewhat grim.

He exchanged glances with Wang Xuanba and Yue Zhenwei and continued to browse.

"The place we first encountered in the dream is the transit hub leading to the trial dream worlds. All cultivators entering the Land of Joyful Peace for the first time will appear there."

"In the Land of Joyful Peace, cultivators can harm each other. If this rule is ignored and fighting occurs, the attacked party will be transferred to a safe zone. Furthermore, depending on the severity of the situation, the attacker's Joyful Coins will be deducted."

"Joyful Coins, also known as Land of Joyful Coins, are obtained by cultivators exploring and engaging in activities within the Land of Joyful Peace. They can be used in the Heavenly Venerate's Treasury to exchange for various materials to strengthen oneself."

"In the Heavenly Venerate's Treasury, there is everything, encompassing all things..." Sun Erlang looked at the 2000 Joyful Coins he carried, a thought arose in his heart, and he opened the details page of the Heavenly Venerate's Treasury.

An instant later, Sun Erlang was dumbfounded. Even with his current level 2 permission in the Land of Joyful Peace, he could only see a limited number of items.

But the item list in the Heavenly Venerate's Treasury was still unbelievable to him. Not to mention the most basic heavenly materials, earthly treasures, elixirs, and magic artifacts.

Even cultivation techniques were ordinary items in the Heavenly Venerate's Treasury. And unlike the cultivation techniques prevalent in the Xuanhuang Realm, the techniques here could at least be cultivated to the Nascent Soul stage.

Moreover, according to the Land of Joyful Peace's explanation, there was no need to worry about not being able to cultivate due to overly profound techniques. Upon completing the exchange, one could instantly achieve initial mastery.

Consuming Joyful Coins could advance the cultivation technique.

"Once redeemed, one cannot share it with others. However, it can be gifted before learning."

"Thus, although there are no restrictions on cultivating multiple techniques in the Land of Joyful Peace, it is still very similar. To cultivate, one still needs to expend resources through redemption."

"The cultivation base and techniques in the real world are only synchronized once upon entering the Land of Joyful Peace, serving as one's starting point in the Land of Joyful Peace."

"However, progress made in the Land of Joyful Peace generally cannot be brought back to reality, that is, the Xuanhuang Realm." Sun Erlang frowned upon seeing this.

However, after a moment of thought, he quickly felt relieved. After all, the things within the Land of Joyful Peace were truly too heaven-defying. If every item could be synchronized back to reality... then the scale of the Land of Joyful Peace would absolutely not be on the same level as the Xuanhuang Realm.

"As the name suggests, the Land of Joyful Peace is led by the power of the great Joyless Heavenly Venerate, constructed from various different dream worlds."

"The blueprints for constructing dream worlds may originate from historical fragments of the Xuanhuang Realm, or from the dreams of living beings, or from deeper, more profound great intents. Therefore, it is not eternally safe, but full of all sorts of dangers."

"To facilitate exploration, there are distinctions between dream experience levels and dream world levels." Sun Erlang nodded slightly.

With their Golden Core Consummation strength, exploring dream worlds of level 3 was already their limit. Any further step would undoubtedly lead to death.

With a general estimate of the danger level, it prevented dream explorers from dying in vain.

"One can die in the Land of Joyful Peace."

"The number of times a cultivator can die is not infinite."

"The number of deaths is a very important indicator for judging a cultivator's identity in the dream world, second only to the dream experience level."

"Cultivators with similar numbers of deaths are generally in the same world layer in the Land of Joyful Peace. The rough divisions are 1-3 deaths, 3-5 deaths, 5-10 deaths, and 10-15 deaths."

"The death limit should be 15 deaths. If one dies again by then..."

"It's truly death."

"The same is true in reality." Sun Erlang's heart tensed.

"An increase in the number of deaths not only means a change in the people one comes into contact with but also implies the decline of one's own spiritual essence."

"Spiritual essence is a hidden value, not displayed, but it truly exists within the Land of Joyful Peace and can affect the actual efficiency of combat and cultivation."

"The more one dies, the lower the spiritual essence, and the more difficult it becomes to make progress."

"It seems that this spiritual essence also has other influences..." Sun Erlang muttered to himself.

"The number of deaths can also be eliminated through certain methods. Besides redeeming them in the Heavenly Venerate's Treasury with Joyful Coins, one can also use some items obtained in dreams."

"Of course, they are all quite expensive."

"Looking at it this way, the Land of Joyful Peace is full of crises. But the reason it attracts the entire Five Elders Society is that this dream truly lives up to the name 'Joyful Peace'."

"Every cultivator, just by paying a certain amount of Joyful Coins, can generate a dream world exclusively for themselves."

"Whether it's an absolute emperor with absolute authority or an immortal emperor who controls everything, it can be realized in the dream."

"In dreams, it is almost indistinguishable from reality. Moreover, the more Joyful Coins paid, the richer the details..."

"However, besides the initial cost of creating the dream, maintaining the dream's existence also requires Joyful Coins."

"This is also the driving force for cultivators to explore dream worlds."

"The higher the level of the dream world, although the risk is greater, the corresponding rewards will also be greater."

"Dream exploration can be done alone, or with companions."

"Every so often, there will be free dream worlds available for exploration. Of course, one can also spend Joyful Coins to unlock them in advance."... Sun Erlang gradually gained a detailed understanding of all aspects of the "Land of Joyful Peace."

What truly caught his attention were some pieces of information he learned at the end.

"Normally, nothing in the dream can be brought back to reality."

"But there are exceptions."

"First, it is protected by the power of the Joyless Heavenly Venerate. It can be achieved with almost no cost, but this has rarely happened in the history of the Land of Joyful Peace."

"Second, key magical items. If handed over, one can choose a part of their dream power to bring back to reality."

"Third, explore deeper into unknown dream worlds."

"Fourth... pay a large amount of Joyful Coins." Sun Erlang and the others exchanged glances again, communicating with each other.

"This Land of Joyful Peace is truly beyond our expectations."

"Even the Sacred Master may not fully understand it. To be able to create such a magnificent land of joy, the power of that Joyless Heavenly Venerate is truly unfathomable."

"However, a dream is a dream, it is illusory. We must eventually return to reality."

"It's just that, looking at it now, it seems somewhat difficult. There are billions of beings in the Land of Joyful Peace, and only a handful can return to reality each year." Yue Zhenwei pondered.

"Actually, I think even if we can't go back, staying in this Land of Joyful Peace isn't bad. Look, in this treasure vault, there are still many dream world templates. Any one of them is extremely wonderful." Wang Xuanba stared at the various items in the Heavenly Venerate's Treasury and couldn't help but say so.

Sun Erlang remained silent.

Chapter 1358: Incarnated Puppet Finally Born

The sudden burst of light was so dazzling that Li Fan instinctively narrowed his eyes.

Li Fan could feel more than just the brilliance of the light itself. There was a mysterious rhythm that had inexplicably descended upon this place and converged upon the silver eye.

Li Fan had encountered similar rhythms during his cycles of reincarnation.

It was exactly the same as those that appeared from the vortex outside the heavens when a small world ascended.

However, the rhythm now appearing on the silver eye was more powerful and unfathomable.

Even with Li Fan's current cultivation and understanding of the Great Dao, he could not fathom its origin.

Under the shroud of this rhythm, it was as if a paintbrush was rapidly sketching and adding countless details to the silver eye.

Although the eye remained unchanged, to Li Fan, the observer, it appeared increasingly "vibrant."

Eventually, even Li Fan, the creator of the eye, felt a sense of unfamiliarity with his own creation.

When "vibrancy" reached its peak in the silver eye's evolution, it began to spread to the small world of Da Qi.

Like a spring breeze brushing the earth, accompanied by light thunder and gentle rain, it nourished every inch of Da Qi's land, silently and imperceptibly.

Even though Li Fan had already used the True Immortal script of 'Creation' and other powers to drive the world's transformation, this new force could still cause it to sublimate further.

"This is the power of true creation. It is not driven by the True Immortal script of 'Creation,' but rather a phenomenon that occurs naturally as the Great Dao flows and circulates."

"It is the rule described by the True Immortal script of 'Creation,' itself."

"Or rather, it is only a part of it… and it will be of great use in promoting the sublimation of the Xuanhuang Realm in this life!"

Li Fan stared intently at everything happening in the small world of Da Qi, trying to engrave every detail into his memory.

The rhythm of creation, from its descent to its disappearance, lasted for less than ten breaths.

Within the small world, only Li Fan could perceive this celestial anomaly.

When the surging rhythm subsided, the changes it brought continued, unfolding in succession within the world, completely unnoticed by all living beings.

Li Fan was immersed in the scene he had just witnessed, savoring it endlessly.

After calming down, he looked at the transformed silver eye, the counterfeited Heavenly Dao, and immediately noticed the changes.

Unlike before, when it would occasionally look at him fawningly.

Most of the time, the eye was closed. It would only open occasionally, and its gaze was no longer directed at Li Fan, but at the various aspects of the Da Qi small world below.

It seemed that Li Fan, its creator, was no longer as important to it.

"Interesting…"

Such "unruliness" instead piqued Li Fan's interest. After a careful inspection, Li Fan confirmed that this simulated Heavenly Dao was still completely under his control.

It was just that, perhaps due to its consumption of the Heavenly Daos of many small worlds, the eye had acquired a sense of "mission."

The mission to maintain the normal operation of the small world.

The priority of fulfilling this mission was only second to Li Fan's control.

Therefore, when Li Fan did not issue any commands, the silver eye instinctively operated in the mode of a "world's Heavenly Dao."

This was closer to a genuine world's Heavenly Dao than the previous "counterfeited Heavenly Dao."

Or rather, the silver eye was now truly the Heavenly Dao of the small world.

It had completed the transformation from "counterfeited" to "true."

Moreover, the energy level of the Heavenly Dao now belonging to the silver eye even surpassed that of ordinary small worlds, thus causing changes in the world itself.

"If my previous promotion of the world using the Creation script and immortal spiritual energy was an external, forceful transformation of the world."

"Then the changes happening within the silver eye now are an internal, silent, and gradual evolution of the world."

"Both methods achieve the same goal, but the latter is clearly more advanced."

Li Fan's eyes showed a contemplative look.

While comprehending the entire process, he also deduced and improved the sublimation plan for this life.

"World sublimation can generally be seen as a process of reaching a higher realm."

"From the outside in, it is like being forcibly dragged by external forces. Once the external force disappears, there is a risk of sudden collapse. Without anchoring means, the entire world would be shattered to pieces."

"From the inside out, it is like slowly pushing forward with one's own foundation, step by step, without the risk of falling. But the downside is that the entire process is too slow! It takes millions of years, and I cannot wait!"

A flash of enlightenment passed through Li Fan's eyes: "However, perhaps I can use both methods."

His divine sense delved into the silver eye, and the entire process of the counterfeited Heavenly Dao's transformation appeared in Li Fan's mind.

It confirmed his external observations. In a short period, he gained considerable insight.

"It seems that the optimal solution for promoting the Xuanhuang Realm's sublimation is to create a Heavenly Dao and replace it."

"But with my current means, I can still create a small world's Heavenly Dao. However, to create the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao…"

Li Fan shook his head slightly.

This was not only because the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao had devoured countless other cultivation worlds over the millennia.

But also because the Transmission of Dao Inversion New Law had bound cultivators of the Longevity Realm to the Xuanhuang Realm.

To eliminate the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao and replace it with a counterfeited Heavenly Dao, one would have to eliminate all these Longevity Realm cultivators as well.

Let alone the Transmission of Dao. The Joyless Heavenly Venerate, who governed the Land of Joyful Peace, had survived the World-Ending Immortal Array.

Killing him was beyond Li Fan's current capabilities.

"However, in reality, over the millennia, the Heavenly Physician and the Transmission of Dao have used the corpses of other worlds to mend the Xuanhuang Realm, employing the second method, from the inside out."

"Feeding the Xuanhuang Realm with other worlds."

"As expected, what the Heavenly Physician sought was not merely to revive the Heavenly Law Realm by borrowing corpses, but to go a step further and directly promote the resurrected Heavenly Law Realm towards the Immortal Domain."

"This is what was mentioned in the 'Record of Mending the Heavens,' 'breaking the cocoon and being reborn, ascending to transcendence'!"

"Unfortunately…"

A cold glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes: "All of this is destined to be a wedding dress for me!"

His consciousness instantly locked onto the fragment of the Immortal Domain hidden within his body, formed by the fusion of six chess pieces.

"In terms of devouring, perhaps the countless realms in the lower world cannot compare to a complete Immortal Domain."

"As soon as the last chess piece returns from beyond the heavens, it should be able to be perfectly assembled. Then, when the Xuanhuang Realm sublimates, it can be merged…"

"I will be the one to lead it!"

Thoughts surged, deducing all possible interference factors at that time.

"The preparations are actually almost complete."

"Next, I need to consider how to prevent the sublimation process from being interrupted."

"The Heavenly Physician and Transmission of Dao will inevitably return from the Star Sea. That True Immortal from the Immortal Ruins might also be awakened."

"And…"

"The Grand Master of Heaven's Capital, the Faceless Immortal…"

These individuals, each of whom could have forced Li Fan to act immediately in his previous life,

Now, Li Fan was able to plan how to resist them.

…

Half a month later.

An anomaly originating from the Xuanhuang Realm jolted Li Fan from his planning.

It was the reaction of the mark he had left near the Heavenly Yang puppet body.

In this life, due to his covert promotion of the Xuanhuang Realm's sublimation,

As the heavens and earth broadened, certain things hidden within the Xuanhuang Realm were also quietly transforming along with the Xuanhuang Realm.

For example, the ancient mutated Celestial-Miasma hidden in the underground cavity of Qiling Prefecture.

And the Heavenly Yang, quenched by the Earth-Fire Reunion Array, buried deep beneath the Earth's core in Congyun Sea.

The power of Earth-Fire was far more surging than in the previous life.

This caused Heavenly Yang to show signs of premature awakening.

Li Fan flashed his figure and arrived at the bottom of Congyun Sea.

Gazing at the puppet body buried deep underground, his mind recalled the scene in his previous life where the Heavenly Yang puppet had single-handedly resisted the Transmission of Dao Heavenly Venerate.

Although it had basically no power to fight back, it had always firmly blocked the Transmission of Dao.

He muttered to himself: "Heavenly Yang is indeed a good helper."

"It was beaten too badly in the previous life…"

"In this life, I will help you get your revenge!"

Li Fan's divine sense instantly pierced through the scorching Earth-Fire and touched the Heavenly Yang puppet body buried deep underground.

Due to its slow awakening from a state of perfection, the residual will of Heavenly Yang was not as irritable as when it was disturbed.

There was no "Heavenly Yang lived his life without being weaker than anyone else."

Only a sense of confusion from traversing thousands of years to a new era.

"Even after absorbing the power of Earth-Fire for ten thousand years, this body is still too weak."

"At most, it will reach the peak of Nascent Soul…"

"Does it deserve the title of 'not weaker than anyone else'?"

Li Fan's words instantly surfaced in Heavenly Yang's sea of consciousness.

Heavenly Yang, gradually awakening from his slumber, was instantly ignited by these words.

The earth rumbled, and the Earth-Fire surged.

The massive puppet body was about to leap from the seabed.

"Heavenly Yang lived his life…"

Heavenly Yang's guttural voice roared, low and deep, expressing his eternal belief that transcended ten thousand years and would forever shine unchanged.

However, the fervent emotion, like a volcano on the verge of eruption, instantly subsided upon hearing Li Fan's casual utterance of "Junior Brother."

This address instinctively evoked a sense of familiarity, sorrow, and guilt.

Anger vanished, replaced by a desire to confirm the identity of the speaker.

"Senior Brother will help you!"

Li Fan's blurry figure suddenly appeared.

"Nine Heavens…"

"Descending Dust Finger!"

As Li Fan whispered, the entire Congyun Sea seemed to instantly calm down. It was like a perfect mirror, without the slightest ripple of waves.

A single finger, descending slowly from the heavens.

Though merely a single finger, it possessed a majestic aura that could blot out the sun and moon.

It precisely landed upon the massive puppet body of Heavenly Yang, pressing down.

The Heavenly Yang puppet body, forged by ten thousand years of Earth-Fire,

Had already transcended the category of searching for heavenly treasures.

Yet, at this moment, under Li Fan's single finger, all the components of the puppet were easily ground into dust!

Heavenly Yang was stunned.

His unyielding will froze, and then he was about to completely dissipate into heaven and earth.

Just then, as if his master Guangyangzi's voice, slowly echoed within Heavenly Yang's fading consciousness.

"Transforming the body into matter, traversing through epochs!"

Accompanying this figure, there was also a body heavily bound by golden chains.

Heavenly Yang looked at that body, as if seeing his former self.

"Go, Heavenly Yang."

"Achieve the strongest in this world!"

His master Guangyangzi's aged voice echoed continuously.

Heavenly Yang's remaining will instinctively drifted towards that body.

Simultaneously, he activated the skill engraved deep within his instincts, [Body Transformation into Other Freedom].

With almost no obstacles, Heavenly Yang successfully attached himself to that body.

At the same time, Heavenly Yang also discovered that the body contained a thought that was of the same origin as his own, yet lacked self-awareness.

Without needing to manipulate it, that thought actively nourished his almost extinguished consciousness.

In a daze, Heavenly Yang seemed to have witnessed everything that happened during the transformation into Dao.

Sealed memories surged to the surface.

A nameless fire rekindled from the ashes.

Heavenly Yang roared that sentence once more.

"Heavenly Yang lived his life!"

"Never weaker than anyone else!"

With his mind and heart united, Heavenly Yang's residual will finally settled completely within this flesh-and-blood puppet.

Heavenly Yang discovered that this body was more like a puppet than a physical body,

A puppet formed by a combination of strange metal and flesh imbued with terrifying, unknown energy.

"Master was right. This puppet body is far more powerful than the one I forged with Earth-Fire."

"Master, I am truly so useless."

Guilt flashed by, and Heavenly Yang's last trace of will peacefully merged into this flesh-and-blood puppet.

…

The moment Heavenly Yang's consciousness was transferred to the flesh-and-blood puppet, Li Fan had already transferred them both to the small world of Da Qi.

The sublimated counterfeited Heavenly Dao, along with the meticulously laid immortal formations,

Sealed this flesh-and-blood puppet.

The aura surging from the puppet forced Li Fan to temporarily evade its power.

It was the terrifying power of True Immortal flesh, far beyond the mortal realm!

This puppet was exactly what Li Fan had previously forged using the bronze immortal crane as bones, attached with True Immortal flesh, and then infused with Heavenly Yang's eternal will.

It was empty flesh and blood, without life or soul, waiting for Heavenly Yang to awaken.

Before handing it over to Heavenly Yang this time, Li Fan had also mixed in a large amount of black star stone powder.

Indeed, solely in terms of the puppet's hardness, it was likely sufficient to withstand the terrifying suction of the Immortal Ruins and walk on the surface of the Immortal Ruins!

Heavenly Yang's will slowly merged with the True Immortal flesh puppet.

Li Fan observed the puppet's constantly changing expressions from a distance.

"With the eternal residual will assisting, it should be able to withstand the power contained within the True Immortal flesh without being completely corrupted."

"However, it is still merely a mortal. The willpower that can remain after confronting immortal power will not be much."

"Like the original Heavenly Yang puppet, acting instinctively in a daze…"

"Using my previous disguise as Guangyangzi, it was enough to make him obedient."

"But this puppet is far stronger than the original Heavenly Yang puppet."

Li Fan was quite satisfied as he carefully observed the changes occurring on the immortal puppet.

The bronze immortal crane, originating from the Immortal Boat's secret collection, was said to be forged from fragments of immortal artifacts.

The True Immortal flesh, Li Fan generated it by tracing back from the True Immortal's bones using the ancient character technique.

The black star stone powder, fragments of worlds, the smallest particles after being cut by the world-ending immortal array.

All three were existences capable of resisting immortal power.

Then, combined with the fusion of Heavenly Yang's eternal residual will…

The puppet before him could truly be called an "Immortal Puppet."

The True Immortal flesh, originally merely attached to the bronze bones.

After integrating Heavenly Yang's will, it was as if it had found its backbone, even growing dense roots that pierced into the bronze bones.

Bones and flesh completely merged into one.

Heavenly Yang's eternal residual will, like a brilliant, inextinguishable diamond, shone in the sea of consciousness.

The puppet's appearance became increasingly vivid and clear.

The surging aura slowly calmed down, and the newly born Heavenly Yang stood quietly.

His eyes were tightly closed.

Without retreating from the immortal formation's protection,

Li Fan attempted to issue a command to Heavenly Yang in the guise of Guangyangzi.

Heavenly Yang was indeed very obedient.

Only, as Li Fan had predicted, during the process of merging with and resisting the True Immortal flesh, Heavenly Yang's autonomous will had been severely eroded.

The remaining instinctive willpower was even less than anticipated.

"What a pity."

"However, with the experience from this life, in the next life, before completing the fusion, I can appropriately increase the intensity of Heavenly Yang's will."

Taking the Immortal Puppet of Heavenly Yang with him, Li Fan headed towards the depths of the Star Sea.

Li Fan began to test the strength of this Immortal Puppet body.

First, he unleashed a Great Five Elements Annihilation Sword.

This was a divine ability Li Fan had comprehended himself, but he hadn't used it for a long time, having gradually come into contact with near-immortal power.

The black light that originally seemed capable of annihilating everything left not even a shallow mark on the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet!

Li Fan raised his eyebrows, and then countless black sword lights rained down.

They surrounded the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet.

However, this seemingly fierce and imposing attack couldn't even trigger Heavenly Yang's instinctive self-defense.

Heavenly Yang stood still, allowing the black sword light to strike him.

After a long while, Li Fan nodded with satisfaction and stopped using the Five Elements Annihilation Sword.

"The Immortal Puppet body has indeed achieved immunity to all mortal powers."

"But…"

"This does not mean my Great Five Elements Annihilation Sword will be useless in the future."

"The rotation of the five elements, moving forward relentlessly, annihilating everything. The intent of this divine ability is not inferior. It's just that when facing an immortal-level existence, relying solely on the core of the five elements to exert annihilation power is too weak." Li Fan mused.

"But if it could be integrated with the 'Transformation Between True and False'…"

Li Fan flicked his finger, intending to unleash a sword strike towards the distant starry sky.

But he hesitated and couldn't bring himself to strike.

"My comprehension is still too shallow. Being able to integrate it into the escape technique is already the limit."

"To use it for combat…"

"Perhaps it will take two or three more cycles of reincarnation. Or perhaps, with the help of that miraculous item that can directly simulate reincarnation by Returning to True."

Li Fan shook his head slightly, calmed his mind, and slowly withdrew his finger.

He continued to test the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet.

Next were the powers of various True Immortal scripts.

Using essence of origin energy as ink, Li Fan unleashed all his learned skills.

The immortal formations sealed the surroundings, preventing the energy fluctuations from leaking out.

Layer upon layer of True Immortal power descended upon the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet.

Facing destructive power of pseudo-immortal level, the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet finally showed a reaction.

The True Immortal flesh seemed to inflate like a bellows, emitting a force field.

It blocked all the effects brought by the True Immortal scripts.

This was not an order from Li Fan, but Heavenly Yang's instinctive reaction.

Li Fan sensed this invisible force field, his pupils contracting sharply.

But he did not stop channeling the True Immortal scripts in his hand.

One by one, the powers of True Immortal rules were absorbed and neutralized upon approaching the force field.

The storm of True Immortal scripts was like a strong gust of wind.

It only caused the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet's clothes to flutter.

It did not inflict the slightest damage.

"Is this the power of True Immortals?"

"And this is merely the self-defense of True Immortal flesh…"

Li Fan's eyes gleamed, wanting to comprehend and study this invisible True Immortal force field.

But to his disappointment, this force field, like the flaw in the High Wall,

Although it was right before his eyes and clearly existed.

He still couldn't touch it; it was invisible and unknowable.

Suddenly, a scene appeared before Li Fan's eyes.

An eagle in the sky looked down at its prey on the ground. Then, with sharp talons extending, it swooped down.

Just as it was about to capture its prey, it slammed headfirst into a piece of transparent protective glass.

The eagle felt dizzy and, after struggling to regain its balance.

It beat against the glass before it, unable to comprehend why its prey was so close yet it could not advance an inch.

It could not comprehend the existence of the glass.

Just like Li Fan currently, unable to comprehend the existence of the High Wall and the force field.

"The power of True Immortals is not something I can touch yet."

"But a gentleman is not born extraordinary; he borrows from the extraordinary. Being able to temporarily wield it through the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet is enough."

"This way, even if I face the Immortal Boat, I will have the capital to overturn the table."

Li Fan stopped making futile efforts.

He began his final attempt.

With a solemn expression, he chanted in a low voice: "Nine Heavens Ascending Cloud Intent, True Immortal Descending to the Mortal Realm!"

He once again unleashed the Nine Heavens Descending Dust Finger.

However, this time it was with his full strength.

Burning a cluster of True Immortal flesh and empowered by the ascension array, Li Fan's vision rapidly ascended.

In an instant, it was as if he had reached the peak of the Star Sea, with the High Wall in view.

And the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet before him, though bearing the word "Immortal,"

Was merely flesh and blood, lacking immortal spiritual energy.

Therefore, it remained below the mortal realm.

In Li Fan's elevated perspective, the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet had become as small as an ant.

The seriousness and caution he had felt when facing it before completely vanished.

Li Fan suddenly felt a sense of True Immortals sitting high above, looking down upon the myriad beings below.

Locking onto the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet, with an arrogant expression, he pressed down with a finger.

Boom!

Within the sealed immortal formation, a fierce storm erupted.

The cloud-piercing intent that annihilated all beings, mixed with the momentum of falling from the heavens, manifested as a colossal finger that transformed from bean-sized to the size of a falling sky.

As if the heavens were collapsing, it pressed down fiercely!

Facing such a powerful divine ability, the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet instinctively felt a sense of danger.

A trace of bloody light flashed in its eyes, and the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet raised its hand, propping up the sky!

Li Fan grunted, his finger feeling as if it were pressing against a hard, giant rock.

Trembling, it could advance no further!

Fortunately, the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet only defended instinctively and did not counterattack.

Otherwise, Li Fan would have definitely suffered severe injuries from this blow!

Li Fan was not doing well, but the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet, after enduring Li Fan's strongest divine ability, was also not faring any better.

After all, it was not a true immortal puppet, but a fusion of several near-immortal artifacts.

This descent from a high position directly caused parts of its flesh and blood to crumble.

The bronze bones emitted a sizzling sound, clearly having suffered immense impact.

The purpose was only to test the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet's actual combat power, not to destroy it.

Seeing that it had reached its limit, Li Fan finally withdrew his divine ability.

He removed the ascension array and slowly descended from the peak of the Star Sea back to the mortal realm.

He slowly regulated his breathing, eliminating the abnormalities within his body.

Looking at the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet, Li Fan frowned slightly: "After all, it is just a puppet, not a true life form, and it lacks self-repair capabilities."

"The True Immortal flesh that was damaged during combat cannot be replenished on its own…"

Just as Li Fan was thinking this, as if Heavenly Yang had sensed his thoughts.

Driven by the core of its eternal residual will, the True Immortal flesh attached to the bronze bones suddenly surged again.

As if generating from one to two, two to three, and three to all things.

The wounds on the immortal puppet during the test were instantly erased.

The scarred immortal puppet had once again returned to its peak state.

Li Fan was astonished by this sight.

His mind suddenly recalled the scene from before when he had used the ancient character technique to stimulate the True Immortal flesh, causing it to proliferate out of thin air.

He remained silent for a long time.

After a while, he sighed from the bottom of his heart: "The power of True Immortals is indeed profound and unfathomable, not to be underestimated."

He frowned: "If it weren't for Heavenly Yang's eternal residual will serving as the core, suppressing this True Immortal flesh, this immortal puppet might have lost control at any moment."

At the same time, Li Fan understood that it was not that the immortal puppet lacked repair capabilities.

But rather, the immortal puppet's autonomy was too poor, lacking the will to actively repair.

Only when Li Fan prompted it and controlled it would it perform this action.

"It is because the invested Heavenly Yang will has been eroded too severely."

"While its resistance to damage is sufficient, if it is to be used to contain Transmission of Dao, Heavenly Physician, or even True Immortals of the Immortal Ruins, it would be somewhat strenuous."

"It seems that to maximize its combat effectiveness, its subjective performance needs to be enhanced."

Li Fan's eyes narrowed: "I recall that Master Qiao Gong seemed to have preserved the combat experience of the Immortal Puppet [Ancestor] from the Heavenly Mechanism Realm…"

"However, this guy, like Xu Ke, seems to have been swept into that deep rift in the Star Sea."

Li Fan turned his head and looked towards the edge of the Star Sea, remotely sensing the mark he had left on Master Qiao Gong.

As before, Master Qiao Gong's aura was very stable, unlike Xu Ke's fluctuating presence.

Moreover, compared to before, he seemed to be closer.

"Interesting."

"It seems I don't need to go looking for him; he will return on his own."

"That's good too!"

Li Fan's gaze swept across his surroundings, and the sealing immortal array suddenly shifted, transforming into the Myriad Things Returning to Void Array, whipping up a howling storm.

It erased all traces of combat.

"The downgraded immortal array is indeed useful."

After finishing this, Li Fan did not leave in a hurry.

Instead, he stood quietly, as if waiting for something.

The Star Sea was an eternity of darkness and silence.

Li Fan waited patiently for more than half a month.

Yet, he never received what he was waiting for.

"It seems my guess was correct. Ordinary falls after ascending do not trigger the black energy."

"Only when the weight of an entire realm, or when the fall occurs in a special region like the center of the Star Sea, will it trigger the black energy."

"These are observed phenomena. Then, what is the reason for these phenomena?"

"Calamity of Dao Annihilation…"

Li Fan muttered to himself, and together with the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet, returned to the Xuanhuang Realm.

Although the eagle could not comprehend the existence of the glass at first.

When it began to try to touch and study the properties of the glass, changes eventually occurred.

Chapter 1359: Starlight Disease, Life and Death

In a small world of Da Xuan, upon the Dao Platform.

The Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet stood behind, eyes closed, motionless.

Li Fan sat, examining the insights regarding the flaw in the High Wall, meticulously selected and refined from the sentiments of countless beings from myriad small worlds.

"Is it before us? No, it is indeed high! Like a river dam, leaping into the sky! Severing our life force, cutting off our path forward!"

"The might of the dark High Wall is immeasurable. Without divine, sacred, or immortal power, how can it be destroyed? Yet, a thousand-mile dike can be breached by an ant's nest!"

"The body of one person, the souls of ten thousand, the intentions of a hundred million. A blazing fire, illuminating the deep darkness."

...

It had to be said that in the face of a crisis of life and death, beings could indeed unleash unimaginable potential.

Among these mortals, whose cultivation barely reached the Golden Core stage, a few had, remarkably, touched upon the truth. Some of their insights and thoughts even subtly inspired Li Fan himself.

However, their level was still too distant from the High Wall.

Even with the immense quantity of hundreds of millions of thoughts, accumulating and transforming to unravel the secrets of the High Wall was by no means an easy task.

At the very least, Li Fan saw no sign of their success in the short term.

But Li Fan was not in a hurry.

He temporarily paused his examination, flicked his finger, and sent out a sword shadow, packaging all these useful thoughts and sending them to Mo Rubing.

"I hope this peerless prodigy of the ancient immortal cultivation world can truly gain something," Li Fan gazed at the starry sky, his expression unfathomable.

Although he had forged the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet in this life, according to Li Fan's deductions, relying solely on Heavenly Yang would not be enough to protect him and successfully achieve Dao integration with the Super Xuanhuang Realm's Heaven and Earth Immortal Souls.

"Besides those encountered in previous reincarnations, I must also consider what lies beyond the High Wall..."

In Li Fan's vision, the scene from the end of his previous life reappeared: the Cat Treasure's descent, the collapse of the High Wall, and even the flickering and instability of the "Returning to True" ability.

"When the Xuanhuang Immortal Domain is born, will the High Wall still be able to seal and isolate the outside and inside? If unknown forces from beyond the High Wall can sense and descend, then the time left for me is truly not much."

Based on his previous life's experiences, Li Fan calculated the buffer time.

"Before victory, plan for defeat. Although it may not happen, one must guard against it."

"My strength, with [Returning to True] as the foundation. Secondly, my array cultivation, which rivals the Star Sea. Thirdly, the 'One Finger Descending from Nine Heavens'."

"Furthermore, there are the various True Immortal scripts."

In Li Fan's sea of consciousness, the Ultimate Dissolution Disc, having completed the task of deriving the downgraded immortal array, was not resting for a moment.

It was deriving an array that could be called earth-shattering. This array was the culmination of all Li Fan's current array knowledge.

Using mortal power to perform the path of True Immortals!

Listing the arrays Li Fan currently possessed.

Derived from the [Profound Origin Spirit Great Array]: [Xuanji, Myriad Spirits Returning to Numbers], [Desolate Fall, Void Chamber Blooming Flowers], [Boundless, Primordial Square Appearance].

Inspired by the ancient Xuanhuang World-Protecting Great Array, Li Fan independently derived the arrays [Simulated, Myriad Forms of Life] and [Immortal Descent, All Things Returning to Void]. These, with their power of creation and destruction, were not inferior to orthodox immortal arrays.

And now, Li Fan intended to combine all these immortal arrays, with the [Infinite Law] as the core concept, to create an ultimate defensive immortal array!

Li Fan vividly remembered how, in his previous life, the Sacred Emperor used the [Bright Moon Starlight Great Array] to besiege the central regions of the Myriad Immortal Alliance, trapping all within, regardless of cultivation level. Upon entering, they were like falling into an endless Star Sea, trapped and unable to escape.

In this life, he intended to do the same.

However, the target Li Fan planned to enclose was the Xuanhuang Realm itself!

Outside the Xuanhuang Realm, he would build another layer of the array's High Wall!

"If I can delay all unstable factors for a period of time... that would be victory!"

The Dissolution Disc flashed, and countless array fragments generated, combined, and evolved within it.

With the foundation of the downgraded immortal array, the original barrier between immortal and mortal was broken.

The derivation direction of the immortal array proceeded as Li Fan anticipated.

"The Primordial Square Appearance Great Array can guide and analyze those who enter."

"With Void Chamber Blooming Flowers and Myriad Forms of Life, create infinite worlds that are nearly indistinguishable from reality."

"[Xuanji, Myriad Spirits Returning to Numbers] can instantly adjust the array world at will..."

"Any form of energy, any form of life, has its suitable and unsuitable environments. Combining the essence of various immortal arrays, create an infinitely changing, tailor-made inverse world!"

"To trap people with a world, to kill people with a world!"

It was as if Li Fan himself, possessing a heaven-defying treasure like [Returning to True], was still trapped within the Xuanhuang Realm and the Star Sea.

A hundred lifetimes had passed, and visible progress required even more time to transcend.

The array being derived by the Dissolution Disc was one that, for every intruder, would custom-create their own unique Xuanhuang Realm!

In terms of mechanism, the fundamental principle of this array was similar to the infinite illusory realms Li Fan experienced in the Immortal Absolute Array when he left Da Xuan in his previous life.

However, it was evident that the reality and detail of the worlds constituting this immortal array far surpassed ordinary illusions.

"Based on the blueprint of facing a Xuanhuang Realm with nightmare difficulty, creating infinite variations of the Xuanhuang Realm..."

"This array can be named [Bewildering, Xuanhuang Sentient Beings]!"

Its name was set, its intention solidified, and the array was formed.

In the Ultimate Dissolution Disc, the flashing lights suddenly stilled.

Then, they erupted outwards.

Forming a perfect sphere of light, composed of seemingly billions of fragments. In each fragment, a world scene, similar yet dissimilar to the Xuanhuang Realm, was unfolding.

In the center of these billions of fragmented worlds, the Xuanhuang Realm, enclosed by the High Wall, lay quietly in the heart of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

Emitting a faint glow, it shone upon all the surrounding world fragments.

Even Li Fan, the creator of this array, was momentarily stunned by this magnificent spectacle.

In a fleeting glimpse, Li Fan caught sight of the worlds constructed by the Dissolution Disc.

Even though he had struggled in the Xuanhuang Realm for many years, he now broke out in a cold sweat, somewhat shocked by his own creation.

"If I were to get lost in it by accident, I might be suppressed for hundreds of lifetimes."

"Below True Immortal, even if one perceives the composition of the world, they would lack the power to break through it..."

"In a sense, this [Bewildering, Xuanhuang Sentient Beings] array is absolutely the High Wall of arrays!"

Lost in thought, Li Fan watched as the light spheres outside the Dissolution Disc slowly collapsed inwards.

Finally, they converged at the core of the Ultimate Dissolution Disc.

Currently, the Dissolution Disc had only derived the core part of the [Xuanhuang Sentient Beings] array. There was still a long way to go to perfect the overall details.

However, even with just the core of the array, it was enough for Li Fan to prepare in advance.

"To complete this Xuanhuang Sentient Beings array enveloping the Xuanhuang Realm, the amount of Origin Pure Essence required is terrifyingly large."

After a rough calculation, Li Fan frowned deeply.

With the current number of You Clan members, even with their utmost efforts, they absolutely could not satisfy Li Fan's needs.

"It seems I need to think of other methods."

"Either, still resort to the method of breeding them like factory products with alien beast flesh and blood. Or, find an alternative energy source equivalent in value to Origin Pure Essence."

As Li Fan pondered this, he divided a wisp of his divine sense and descended beneath the Great Xuan.

Here, the You Clan members, since being captured and raised by Li Fan, had tripled in number.

Their daily lives revolved around eating, drinking, sleeping, and praying to the great Sacred Master.

Strangely, not only had they not weakened due to the lack of activity, but they were generally much healthier than when they were hiding and evading the pursuit of the Myriad Immortal Alliance.

This phenomenon was different from Li Fan's previous experiences.

In the past, after being exploited, the You Clan members had become extremely weak. Their lifespans shortened, and their reproductive capabilities plummeted. If not cared for properly, they faced the threat of extinction.

But judging from the current situation, the You Clan seemed to have broken free from their cursed fate.

Li Fan recalled and compared the differences between this life and past lives.

"The method of reproduction is not significantly different. Although I have not excessively oppressed them and have given them sufficient rest, Sacred Emperor in the previous life also did the same."

"The You Clan members in Da Qi also had short lifespans..."

"Could it be?"

Li Fan remembered that in this life, he had once used the Dao Pill method to possess a You Clan member, attempting to explore the True Immortal inscription hidden within their first-generation Great Heavenly Venerate bloodline.

"Is it related to this inscription that involves the transformation between immortal and mortal?" Li Fan couldn't help but speculate.

"The You Clan, the work of Xuan Tianwang of the past. Their bloodline, not only the source of generating Origin Pure Essence, but also the root of their original sin."

"Now, their curse has been lessened..."

Li Fan gradually began to understand.

"Xuan Tianwang's character, in his actions, might not have been absolute. While punishing the You Clan, perhaps he left a sliver of hope. If some You Clan members could awaken and discover the secrets within their bloodline, the shackles binding them would be weakened."

To verify his conjecture, Li Fan immediately took action.

The Sacred Master phantom, worshipped by the You Clan, silently emitted a few dark rays of light.

These randomly shone into the bodies of several You Clan members below.

As if receiving a divine revelation, these You Clan members suddenly stiffened.

In their sea of consciousness, countless scenes spontaneously surged forth.

They were overcome with excitement, first kowtowing to the Sacred Master phantom in gratitude, and then immersing themselves in the Sacred Master's enlightenment.

The prayers and murmurs grew louder and faster.

Like the You Clan member Li Fan had possessed, their bodies rapidly aged.

Some even turned white-haired in an instant, turning into withered bones.

This terrifying sight did not frighten the praying You Clan members. Instead, they felt incredibly envious, and their devout faith became even more fervent.

Finally, amidst the chanting, all the You Clan members who had received Li Fan's divine revelation burned their lives in their enlightenment, turning into flying ashes.

At the cost of this, Li Fan keenly sensed that perhaps due to the further weakening of the shackles on their bodies,

The remaining You Clan members had indeed grown stronger.

Not only in physique, but also in spirit and comprehension, they had strengthened comprehensively.

It was as if...

They were slowly reverting to what the first-generation Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate bloodline should have been.

"To be chosen by a True Immortal from the Upper Realm to become the first-generation Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate, how could such an existence be weak?"

"How could his bloodline be so inadequate?"

Li Fan's eyes narrowed, and he continued to use the Sacred Master phantom to bestow divine revelations.

With the current overall population of the You Clan, this kind of life-burning promotion could still be borne.

"However, I need to be careful about the degree of weakening the shackles."

"I don't want to face a revived Great Heavenly Venerate suddenly appearing at a critical moment in this life..."

Having suffered a setback before, Li Fan was naturally extremely cautious in this regard.

Subsequently, the gradually returning You Clan members, reverting to their original state, displayed their incredible vitality and reproductive capacity.

Their birth rate was not much slower than the creatures produced by the "flesh and blood factory" of the past.

And there were no defective products.

All offspring born were incredibly strong in physique.

They were less like humans and more like a race of demonic beasts!

As the seals on the You Clan gradually lifted, the amount of Origin Pure Essence generated by each person's prayers also increased exponentially.

This somewhat alleviated Li Fan's immediate urgency.

However, looking at the You Clan population, which had doubled again in a short period, Li Fan felt a rare chill in his heart.

"Even under severe shackles, they possessed such capabilities. If they were in their prime..."

"Their reproductive ability would likely not be much weaker than the rumored Zerg, and what's more, these You Clan members are all so physically powerful. It completely defies logic."

Thinking this, Li Fan silently and appropriately trimmed and controlled the slightly inflated You Clan population.

Only when it looked pleasing did he stop.

"It seems I need to keep an eye on them to feel at ease."

Li Fan divided a wisp of his divine sense and secretly implanted it into the Sacred Master phantom that the You Clan members worshipped.

He also set up a newly derived Xuanhuang Sentient Beings Array in the area where the You Clan lived, ensuring their complete isolation. Only then did he cease his actions.

"It seems I can't let down my guard at all."

Controlling the You Clan population growth rhythmically and linearly.

Using the Origin Pure Essence they produced to construct the [Bewildering, Xuanhuang Sentient Beings] Array.

Time thus passed swiftly.

Until one day...

Li Fan suddenly looked up at the firmament.

The Medicine King Cauldron had finally escaped the Immortal Ruins and was descending towards the Xuanhuang Realm from its periphery.

The six chess pieces fused into an Immortal Domain fragment within his body began to resonate more strongly. It seemed to urge him to hasten forward and receive it.

A sword light flashed, and Li Fan had already left the Xuanhuang Realm.

He arrived outside the world and looked at the gradually enlarging, swaying Medicine King Cauldron in his vision.

With a wave of his hand, he directly took it in.

He returned gracefully, his actions seamless.

From beginning to end, he did not alert anyone within the Xuanhuang Realm.

As if sensing Li Fan's suppression from the outside, the Medicine King Cauldron continuously emitted subtle energy fluctuations, attempting to escape Li Fan's control.

But it was merely a futile struggle.

The outer layer, the Xuanhuang Sentient Beings Array, and the inner layer, the Myriad Ages Returning to Void Array.

Under the pressure of the immortal arrays, the Medicine King Cauldron immediately became docile.

It stood still.

Li Fan divided a wisp of his divine sense, penetrated into the cauldron, and headed towards the core control center.

Familiar with the path, he ventured forward, arriving at the core control center of the Medicine King Cauldron.

Looking at the empty space within the control center, Li Fan let out a slight cold laugh.

He reached out his right hand and clenched it.

The entire space seemed to twist under this grasp.

A blurry figure was directly pulled out by Li Fan!

"Senior, spare me!"

This figure was naturally Liu Ruchen, the sect leader of the Medicine King Sect, who had been in hiding.

Drag onto the light by Li Fan, he completely lost the demeanor of a sect leader and frantically shouted!

It wasn't that Liu Ruchen was incompetent, but rather that the methods Li Fan now displayed were incomprehensible.

He had traveled all the way without triggering any of the restrictions within the Medicine King Cauldron, heading directly for the core center.

And he had seen through his hiding method with a single glance...

Liu Ruchen's thoughts raced, trying to figure out which expert from the Ten Sects was before him.

However, Li Fan appeared as ordinary as a mortal, with no aura leaking out.

This made Liu Ruchen unable to discern his identity.

Only the calm expression and a slight glance from Li Fan sent his spiritual sense into a frenzy, warning him to flee while his hands and feet turned cold.

Just as he was about to speak, Li Fan directly pressed a finger against his forehead.

An immensely powerful force, like a surging tide, rushed into his divine soul.

Originally in a severely injured and barely surviving state, Liu Ruchen was hit by this heavy blow and became on the verge of death, with only a wisp of his remnant soul remaining.

Normally, Li Fan did not resort to soul-searching techniques.

But given the clues about immortal realm fragments secretly left by Sun Piaomiao, the ancestor of the Medicine King Sect, Li Fan could not afford to be careless.

Countless scenes and memories of Liu Ruchen flooded towards Li Fan.

Li Fan examined everything in detail, scrutinizing every piece of information.

Especially any information regarding Sun Piaomiao, which he treated with utmost importance.

In Liu Ruchen's era, the name Sun Piaomiao existed only in ancient legends.

Even after succeeding to the position of Medicine King Sect leader, Liu Ruchen's knowledge of Sun Piaomiao was mostly derived from a travelogue left by his ancestor.

Previously, Li Fan had only heard about the wonders of this travelogue from the mouths of Medicine King Sect disciples.

Now, reading it word for word from Liu Ruchen's memories.

With the answer already known, revisiting some details in the travelogue. Li Fan indeed noticed some peculiarities.

The travelogue began after Sun Piaomiao established the Medicine King Sect.

Without any warning, Sun Piaomiao, as the Sect Master of the Medicine King Sect, decided to leave the Xuanhuang Realm and travel through various realms.

One had to consider that at that time, the Medicine King Sect had just been founded, its foundation was unstable, and there were too many complicated matters awaiting the Sect Master Sun Piaomiao to handle.

Yet, Sun Piaomiao simply packed up and left, leaving behind a mess, and departed without explanation.

If not for his disciples being relatively reliable, and the Medicine King Sect's core principles of healing and saving lives, generally not engaging in conflict with other sects. The Medicine King Sect might not have survived until Sun Piaomiao's return.
