Sun Piaomiao's sudden departure, while it could be explained by his free-spirited and unconventional nature.

In Li Fan's view, it was more likely that he had received some mission and was forced to leave.

One must know that with Sun Piaomiao's strength at that time, the starry sky was not a smooth path for him.

As evidenced by his encounter with anomalies in the Star Sea, nearly perishing, and falling injured into the Carefree Realm.

With this foresight, Li Fan reread Sun Piaomiao's travelogue records with greater scrutiny.

Logically, since it was a travelogue, it should record the unforgettable parts of the entire journey. However, Sun Piaomiao mentioned nothing of his own experiences, not even his near-fatal injury. All his writings were dedicated to describing the characteristics of the immortal cultivation realms he visited.

It was as if he were a recording camera without emotions,

Fearing that later generations, wanting to revisit these immortal cultivation realms, might not be able to find them.

"Most importantly, what was the purpose of the chess pieces he left behind?"

"Since he left such obvious clues for future generations, he should not have said nothing."

Li Fan carefully searched the travelogue but did not find what he was looking for, a slight frown appearing on his face.

To ensure he missed nothing, he searched again.

Still finding nothing, Li Fan searched through Liu Ruchen's other memories.

Fortune favored him. In an anecdote Liu Ruchen had heard from his master in his youth, he found a possible clue.

This anecdote was merely mentioned by Liu Ruchen's master occasionally.

Even Liu Ruchen himself had forgotten it.

"Back then, a heavily injured guest sought refuge at the Medicine King Sect."

"The injuries were too severe; everyone in the sect was unable to help. Even the ancestor's examination yielded the same conclusion."

"Logically, there is no panacea in this world. Our Medicine King Sect did its best to save him. Who knew that this guest, in despair, actually cursed our Medicine King Sect? He even used his remaining strength to frantically attack the disciples of the Medicine King Sect. Our Medicine King Sect, in its quest to save lives, is not foolish. Naturally, we also have our tempers."

"The disciples immediately took action, intending to kill him. But the ancestor stopped everyone and went to the dying guest's side, pointed to the sky, and said something."

"The guest's body trembled slightly, his murderous intent vanished. He stopped attacking, looked up at the sky, and his ferocious expression turned into two lines of tears. Then, as if relieved, he passed away."

"The ancestor sighed lightly and ordered us to bury him with respect."

Young Liu Ruchen, like everyone who heard this anecdote, naturally asked curiously: "Ancestor, what exactly did you say to him that so easily dispelled his frenzied murderous intent?" Liu Ruchen's master replied with a faint tone: "Birth, aging, sickness, and death. This is the eternal principle of the Great Dao, inescapable even by this starry sky. What about you?" "That's what the ancestor said back then."

Young Liu Ruchen, not yet able to grasp the gravity of these words, simply nodded innocently and agreed: "Yes! Dying is dying, why get angry? He deserved it!"

But returning to the present, Li Fan could taste a different flavor in Sun Piaomiao's words from back then.

"Back then, the immortal path was not yet severed, and everyone aimed to ascend to immortality. Sun Piaomiao's words do not sound like something a Medicine King who heals and saves lives would say."

"It aligns more with my previous conjecture of a pessimist in the Immortal Realm."

Li Fan mused silently, then tried to find more clues in Liu Ruchen's memories.

As expected, misfortunes rarely come alone.

Li Fan found another seemingly suspicious past event.

Normally, immortal cultivation sects would establish statues for their founding ancestors for later generations to worship.

However, the Medicine King Sect had no statues of Sun Piaomiao.

"Master, Master, what did our ancestor look like! Why isn't there even a portrait?"

"Heh, our ancestor once said, rather than worshiping him, it is better to worship the Medicine King Cauldron of our sect. We refine medicine, save lives, and succor the world, all thanks to this cauldron! Without the cauldron, there is no Medicine King, and thus no future."

...

"Medicine King Cauldron, the future."

Li Fan exhaled a long breath, withdrawing his divine sense from Liu Ruchen's memories and standing quietly in thought.

Liu Ruchen's remnant soul trembled by the side, not daring to disturb him.

"Perhaps it is merely my speculation, but in my opinion, the hints left by Sun Piaomiao are already quite obvious."

"However, the prerequisite is knowing that the Medicine King Cauldron is highly likely to be a fragment of the Immortal Realm."

"If my guess is correct, Sun Piaomiao must have hinted at the specificity of the Medicine King Cauldron elsewhere. But it was not noticed by his disciples, and the information was lost in the river of history."

"If it were not for my fortuitous discovery of the anomaly in Sun Piaomiao's遺物 (relics) on the Immortal Boat, this secret might have been buried forever."

Li Fan looked at the Medicine King Cauldron.

He activated the True and False Transformation, channeling a wisp of power from the [Art of Healing and Longevity] within his body.

Li Fan had cultivated this technique before, and coupled with his current strength, far exceeding that of ordinary Dao Integration cultivators, it was effortless to replicate, indistinguishable from the genuine Art of Healing and Longevity at this point.

Under Liu Ruchen's immensely shocked gaze, Li Fan easily broke through the restrictions of the Medicine King Cauldron and, in doing so, gained control of it.

"The disciples of the Medicine King Sect have degenerated to this extent!"

"In critical times, they do not help. Instead, they flee for their own safety..."

"Scoundrels!"

Li Fan's cold snort of anger fell upon Liu Ruchen's ears like thunder.

He knew everything about the Medicine King Sect like the back of his hand, and his tone was like that of an elder...

In an instant, a bold speculation surfaced in Liu Ruchen's mind.

"Senior is..."

Li Fan ignored him, but grabbed Liu Ruchen and flashed out of the Medicine King Cauldron.

At the same time, with a single thought, he deactivated the "Great Dream Spring and Autumn Formation" within the Cauldron.

Then, like a sieve, all the Medicine King Sect disciples who were slumbering within were shaken and tossed out.

Instantly, Medicine King Sect cultivators rained down from the sky.

Fortunately, they had already woken up and sensed something was wrong, hastily stabilizing themselves.

The Medicine King Sect disciples, just awakened from a great dream, were bewildered.

In their exchanges, their gazes gradually fixed upon Li Fan, the only stranger.

Especially Liu Ruchen's figure in Li Fan's hand, becoming increasingly blurry and on the verge of disappearing.

"Sect Master?!"

"Master?!"

The disciples, elders, and Liu San all cried out in alarm, glaring at Li Fan with rage.

Li Fan, however, remained indifferent to their hostile gazes, continuing to shake the Medicine King Cauldron.

Only when all the valuable materials hidden within the Medicine King Cauldron, as well as precious spiritual plants and herbs, flew out as clusters of light did Li Fan stop.

He reached out, and the Myriad Things Returning to Void Array manifested from his palm.

Covering the Medicine King Cauldron.

Silently, within the Immortal Ruins, the Medicine King Cauldron, which could withstand pressure for a moment, was reduced to dust inch by inch.

"Medicine King Cauldron!"

Witnessing their sect's supreme treasure being destroyed by Li Fan, the Medicine King Sect members were filled with righteous fury.

They still intended to seek revenge and retaliate against Li Fan.

But the aura of the downgraded immortal array, emanating from Li Fan's fingertips, sent them all into an abyss of ice, freezing them on the spot.

Chapter 1360: The Celestial Cauldron Transforms into a Chess Piece

Without resentment or unwillingness.

Regardless of whether they were at Dao Integration, Nascent Soul, or Yuan Ying stage.

Under the [Immortal Descent, Myriad Things Returning to Void] Great Array, the reaction of all members of the Medicine King Sect was the same.

Fear, only boundless fear filled their hearts.

Only when Li Fan withdrew the power of the world-ending immortal array did the Medicine King Sect members slowly emerge from their extreme emotions.

However, with Li Fan remaining silent, they dared not move an inch.

The power of the immortal array flowed, and though withdrawn, it did not dissipate. It formed a space of its own, enveloping the entire Medicine King Sect.

While deterring the cultivators, it also shielded them from the Xuanhuang Realm's rule of "law cannot be cultivated together," preventing the newly awakened Medicine King Sect cultivators from slaughtering each other.

Afterward, Li Fan ignored them, focusing on the smallest particles of the Medicine King True Cauldron. As expected by him, they finally coalesced into the shape of a chess piece.

However, this chess piece was not covered in a layer of gray, unlike the ones Li Fan had collected before.

Instead, it was distinctly…

White.

Even the edges of the white piece had a ring of color, very similar to the fused chess pieces.

Li Fan reached out and took the white chess piece. Gazing at it closely, this small piece seemed to contain boundless life.

And the other chess pieces he had subdued within his body, including the fused Immortal Domain fragment, all trembled slightly.

As if they had welcomed their leader, they erupted in bursts of joyous acclaim.

The urgent summons from the chess pieces within his body were several times stronger than before.

It was as if they couldn't wait to fuse with this white chess piece.

This summons even gradually transformed into Li Fan's own desire.

The craving was so intense that even circulating the Immortal Heart Curse was difficult to resist.

But Li Fan, with his extraordinary willpower,

With great perseverance, he finally suppressed the restless movements of the chess pieces within his body.

Calming his mind, he was able to re-examine the white chess piece in his hand and compare it with the six chess pieces sealed within his body.

Within Li Fan's body, there was one large and five small. The large one was seven-colored, formed by the fusion of six ordinary gray chess pieces. The five small ones revolved around the colored chess piece.

The white chess piece before him, although a single piece, gave Li Fan a feeling similar to the fused seven-colored chess piece.

"It seems that what Sun Piaomiao left in the Xuanhuang Realm must be the most crucial one."

"A complete Immortal Domain…"

"The only remaining one is the one in the Xuan Immortal Boat."

Upon thinking of meeting a corner of the shattered Immortal Realm again in the future, even Li Fan, who was as calm as ever, couldn't help but feel a surge of excitement.

"Does the fused Immortal Domain contain immortal spiritual energy?"

"Can I use this to ascend to immortality?"

"Are there any relics left by the True Immortals who forged these chess pieces within the Immortal Domain?"

"Perhaps, is there a True Immortal within the Immortal Domain who wants to be reborn along with this Immortal Domain?"

Numerous questions surged into Li Fan's mind like a tide.

If it were an ordinary cultivator, even with the Immortal Domain in hand, facing the completely unknown elements within and the immense risks, they would undoubtedly hesitate and fear to activate it.

But Li Fan, with [Returning to True] in hand, had no such worries.

Especially since Li Fan, having mastered immortal formations in this life, and his Returning to True's energy shield having doubled, he now possessed sufficient protective means.

…

The white chess piece, transformed from the Medicine King True Cauldron, seemed to possess an infinite demonic power, drawing the gaze of all cultivators present.

They could vaguely sense that a great secret was hidden behind this chess piece. However, intimidated by Li Fan's display of power just now, they only dared to watch from afar.

Finally, Liu Ruchen, having recovered, bravely spoke, "May I ask, Senior, is this chess piece a relic left by Ancestor Sun Piaomiao?"

Liu Ruchen dared to speak because Li Fan had released the Medicine King Sect cultivators from the cauldron before destroying it, showing considerable goodwill.

Li Fan stored the white chess piece within his body, separating it from the other chess pieces, and then coldly sneered, "Sun Piaomiao left this item with your descendants for so long, even leaving numerous hints, both obvious and subtle, and you still couldn't discern its true nature…"

"Truly a bunch of imbeciles!"

Li Fan's reprimand was relentless, yet it indirectly answered Liu Ruchen's question.

Most of the Medicine King Sect disciples showed a trace of shame on their faces.

Liu Ruchen smiled awkwardly and was about to inquire further when Li Fan cut him off, "This matter is beyond your involvement."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, observing Liu Ruchen, and remarked, "Although you violated the tenets of the Medicine King Sect, leading the entire sect to escape the Xuanhuang Realm was inadvertently a good deed!"

With a flick of his finger, countless images flashed in the center of the field.

These were the dramatic changes that had occurred in the Xuanhuang Realm and the Star Sea over the ten thousand years the Medicine King True Cauldron was absorbed by the Immortal Ruins.

The Medicine King Sect members were all in an uproar.

When Li Fan slightly relaxed the immortal formation's protection, they felt an immense wave of killing intent suddenly surge from their hearts towards their relatives, friends, mentors, and brothers.

Finally, they confirmed that Li Fan was not lying, and their faces turned pale with shock and despair.

Li Fan ignored them and summoned seven Dao Integration cultivators from the Medicine King Sect, including Liu Ruchen.

"Do you know what this chess piece, transformed from the Medicine King True Cauldron, is?"

"It is a fragment of the Immortal Realm left by Sun Piaomiao!"

Li Fan's words stunned the Dao Integration cultivators of the Medicine King Sect, leaving them in a state of utter disbelief.

Then, he controlled them, slightly releasing the aura emanating from the seven-colored chess piece sealed within his body.

Fragments of Immortal Realm laws, even an iota of their essence, were enough to leave the Dao Integration cultivators of the Medicine King Sect entranced and lost.

"The Immortal Realm suffered a calamity, with signs appearing long ago. Back then, Sun Piaomiao received the immortal decree and left behind a contingency plan to revive the Immortal Realm…"

Li Fan spoke eloquently, narrating the "facts" he had conjectured.

"Now Sun Piaomiao is missing, and you are his disciples. You should assist me in completing the great cause of restoring the Immortal Realm!" Li Fan arrogantly declared, as if it were a foregone conclusion.

Liu Ruchen and the others, who were still immersed in the wonder of the Immortal Realm laws,

Were suddenly stunned by Li Fan's words.

They all looked at Li Fan, their faces filled with disbelief: "Restoring the Immortal Realm? Us?"

"The Immortal Realm fragments have all been collected by me. I am only waiting for an opportunity."

"At that time, you only need to assist from the sidelines." Li Fan said calmly.

Faced with the request of Li Fan, who was suspected to be a True Immortal powerhouse, how could the Dao Integration cultivators of the Medicine King Sect refuse?

However, they were drumming their hearts, wondering why such a powerful being, who could destroy their entire sect with a wave of his hand, would need their help.

But Li Fan did not explain, and they dared not ask.

Were the people of the Medicine King Sect useful?

To Li Fan, they were certainly useful.

However, not for the purpose of rebuilding the Immortal Realm. Rather, to act as catalysts for the fusion of various powers during the sublimation of the Xuanhuang Realm.

Chapter 1361: Immortal Puppets Stealthily Enter the Boat

Up to this point, the process of finding and fusing the Immortal Domain chess pieces had been too smooth.

So smooth that Li Fan couldn't help but become suspicious, wondering if he would encounter difficulties during the final fusion of the Immortal Domain's law fragments.

If Sun Piaomiao had indeed left behind any restrictive measures, then the Medicine King Sect, as Sun Piaomiao's descendants, should be able to bypass such constraints to some extent.

This was only the first aspect.

Li Fan's gaze swept across the seven Dao Integration cultivators of the Medicine King Sect present.

"Your cultivation levels, which might have been considered top-tier among cultivators in the past, are now somewhat weak after ten thousand years of change. You're even barely enough to help me."

"Therefore, I need to help you increase your strength in a short period."

Liu Ruchen heard this and cautiously asked, "What does Senior mean by increasing our strength?"

"Now, cultivators practice by devouring the heavens and earth. Because they transform the power of heaven and earth into their own use, wielding the might of heaven and earth with every move, they can manipulate spiritual energy on a scale far exceeding ancient cultivators." Li Fan's words revealed the cultivation methods of the Reverse Heavenly Dao principles to them all.

The expressions of the Medicine King Sect's Dao Integration cultivators were not very good.

"No wonder the calamity of 'law cannot be cultivated together' descended from the heavens. Such cultivation methods are simply heretical…" Liu San muttered softly.

Li Fan snorted coldly, "What is evil? What is righteous? In the cultivation world, there is only the distinction between strong and weak! If the strong assert that the new method is justice, then the new method is justice!"

Although the Medicine King Sect members were unconvinced by this argument, under Li Fan's might, they dared not refute.

Li Fan shook his head slightly, "Alas, perhaps only when you experience the wonders of the new method firsthand will you be able to change your views."

With a gentle wave of his hand, detailed information about various Heavenly Spiritual Essences appeared before them all.

"Each of you, pick one. I will help you harmonize with the Dao again using the new method."

The seven individuals suddenly trembled.

"I choose this one, Scarlet Serpent." Jiang Yushan spoke first.

As a former guardian of the Boundless Prison, Jiang Yushan had killed countless people and had no qualms about morality. As long as it could increase her strength, she was willing to try.

"Good! You have a discerning eye! The power of this Scarlet Serpent is balanced and harmonious. It can pacify the lingering effects of the rampant killing intent within you." Li Fan nodded in praise.

With a leader, the remaining Dao Integration cultivators of the Medicine King Sect exchanged glances and no longer held back. They began to choose their desired Heavenly Spiritual Essences.

Soon, the division of Heavenly Spiritual Essences was complete.

"Without further ado, next I will take you hunting."

The phantom of the wooden sword was unsheathed, enveloping the cultivators present.

Then, in an instant, they had arrived within the Xuanhuang Realm.

Even through the sword phantom's protection, Liu Ruchen and the others could still sense the faint influence of the "law cannot be cultivated together" principle of heaven and earth.

"I cannot protect you forever. The World-Saving Longevity Scripture only needs Liu Ruchen to cultivate it. The others can switch to other Dao Integration cultivation techniques." As Li Fan spoke, he displayed information on thousands of Dao Integration True Techniques.

Each technique's power was not inferior to the World-Saving Longevity Scripture, leaving them almost dazzled.

"We'll talk about it after you return and achieve Dao Integration."

"For now, straighten your backs and focus."

Li Fan's figure floated above them.

He looked up at the sky and casually unleashed a decree.

Dark clouds churned, and wind and thunder roared.

A massive vortex immediately formed in the sky.

Like a rift in the heavens, countless bolts of lightning flashed within.

Li Fan muttered in a voice only he could hear: "Reverse the principles of heaven and earth!"

With five true words, spoken backwards to the heavens.

Li Fan was borrowing the power of heaven's will. Shortly after, seven blurry figures simultaneously responded to the call, appearing within the vortex.

These were the Heavenly Spiritual Essences that the Medicine King Sect members had each carefully chosen!

With the appearance of the seven Heavenly Spiritual Essences, the eyes of the Medicine King Sect members instantly turned red.

Each figure was like an elixir of longevity to cultivators, and now with seven gathered together…

If not for Li Fan's power suppressing them, they would have likely rushed out in a frenzy, disregarding their own lives.

Facing such overwhelming temptation, Li Fan's expression remained unchanged.

Simultaneously with the appearance of the Heavenly Spiritual Essences, the immortal formation had already silently sealed the area.

The Heavenly Spiritual Essences were highly perceptive.

Sensing the severance of their connection with the origin of heaven and earth, they immediately awoke from their daze.

But before they could make any moves,

Li Fan's five fingers, forming clouds, covered them from above.

With a casual palm press,

The seven Heavenly Spiritual Essences seemed to feel the weight of the entire world bearing down on them!

Instantly, they were immobilized!

Moreover, the invisible shackles and binding force on them grew stronger and stronger.

Li Fan's five fingers slightly curled, turning his palm into a claw.

Bang! Bang! Bang!

The sound of the Heavenly Spiritual Essences' law bodies exploding into pieces continued to be heard!

Under the terrifying force, their bodies were forced to contort.

At the moment of life and death, the law power within their bodies tried to make a final struggle, boiling and surging, attempting to escape Li Fan's control.

But like waves constantly crashing, they were ultimately unable to shake the unyielding dam.

All the struggles of the Heavenly Spiritual Essences were destined to be in vain.

The desperate burst not only failed to shake off their shackles but instead accelerated their demise.

Even amidst the greed that had clouded their minds, the scene of Li Fan suppressing the seven Heavenly Spiritual Essences with a single palm deeply shocked the Dao Integration cultivators of the Medicine King Sect.

Only when Li Fan's reprimand came did they recover from their shock: "What are you still standing there for?"

Liu Ruchen and the others felt the restraining force on them disappear, and they no longer suppressed their inner greed.

They immediately rushed towards their designated targets.

Using their ultimate moves against the Heavenly Spiritual Essences suppressed by Li Fan.

Only when they truly fought against the Heavenly Spiritual Essences did the Dao Integration cultivators of the Medicine King Sect truly experience the power of heaven and earth.

Even though the Heavenly Spiritual Essences could not fight back and could only be outputted by them.

Even though the Heavenly Spiritual Essences had already been severely injured by Li Fan's palm.

The group had almost exhausted all the spiritual energy within their bodies just to barely kill these Heavenly Spiritual Essences.

"Even among all the Heavenly Spiritual Essences, these ones you chose for me were definitely top-tier." This thought couldn't help but surface in their minds.

"And even such powerful Heavenly Spiritual Essences had no power to resist in front of Senior."

The Medicine King Sect members once again gained a concrete quantitative understanding of Li Fan's strength.

As one Heavenly Spiritual Essence after another was killed, Li Fan also released the seal of the immortal formation.

Inheriting the power of the Heavenly Spiritual Essences, the origin power of the Xuanhuang Realm's laws, descended from the massive vortex above the heavens.

Like clouds pouring from the sky, it landed on the Medicine King Sect members.

The aura on their bodies increased exponentially.

Seven newly ascended Dao Integration Immortal Venerables descended upon the Xuanhuang Realm!

At the same time, phenomena also occurred between heaven and earth.

The fall of one Heavenly Spiritual Essence could cause heaven and earth to tremble. Seven falling simultaneously…

Similar to the phenomena upon a cultivator's death, heavenly anomalies illuminated the sky.

The Medicine King Sect members felt an omnipresent, almost tangible, terrifying malice from heaven and earth!

And Li Fan, although he did not personally act, had reversed the principles of heaven and earth, suppressing the Heavenly Spiritual Essences.

He was also the culprit behind the fall of the Heavenly Spiritual Essences!

The heavenly malice he faced was hundreds of thousands of times greater than that of the Medicine King Sect's Dao Integration cultivators combined!

The previous favorability was gone, as if facing an enemy of irreconcilable hatred.

Battling against heaven and earth, malice surrounded them like a tangible entity, transforming into hideous whispers.

This made the Medicine King Sect members, who had always upheld the belief of helping the world and saving people, feel somewhat unaccustomed.

But if they were asked to return the power they had already obtained to the heavens…

That was impossible.

They would rather fight against heaven and earth!

Under such circumstances, Li Fan was neither hurried nor flustered, having prepared long ago, and stood before the Medicine King Sect's Dao Integration cultivators.

Facing the heavens, he stated the reason for his actions.

The process of Xuanhuang's sublimation would be aided by several forces.

For example, the power of the Star Sea's recovery, and the residual power of other cultivation realms sealed away.

And the immortal spiritual energy of the Great Heavenly Venerate's inheritance.

Such a multitude of complex and immense powers were like potent medicines.

The Xuanhuang Realm's current dilapidated and weak body might not be able to withstand them.

Therefore, it required medicinal agents as buffers.

The Medicine King Sect's Dao Integration cultivators, who had now devoured the Heavenly Spiritual Essences of the Xuanhuang Realm, were these medicinal agents!

Next, Li Fan would first pour the power of Xuanhuang's recovery into their bodies through various means.

Not by handing over the power to them.

But by using them as intermediary, buffer containers.

When the Xuanhuang Realm officially sublimates, the Dao Integration Immortal Venerables will fall, and all forces will return to heaven in one fell swoop!

External application, internal utilization, both proceeding simultaneously!

The medicine cures the illness, and sublimation is in sight!

…

Li Fan's confident explanation could be roughly summarized in a few words: "I'm doing this for your own good!"

However, the reasons were not fabricated by Li Fan.

They were indeed based on facts.

This was something even the Xuanhuang Realm's Heavenly Dao could sense.

The current Xuanhuang Realm was too far from its goal of sublimation.

The sum of the forces it intended to devour even slightly exceeded the Xuanhuang Realm's own capacity.

There was indeed a possibility of it being unable to handle the nourishment.

The rapidly increasing heavenly malice suddenly stopped. The Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao seemed to be contemplating.

After a brief stalemate, the malice slowly receded.

From the perspective of the Medicine King Sect members,

It appeared as if Li Fan had single-handedly faced the Xuanhuang heaven and earth, and then, through unknown methods, the heavenly malice had completely dissipated.

Such means were truly unheard of.

The Medicine King Sect members' reverence for Li Fan deepened even further.

Having successfully achieved Dao Integration with the new method, their strength had soared by leaps and bounds.

Especially Liu Ruchen, not only had his injuries completely healed, but he had also gained insights during the Dao Integration process.

Currently, Liu Ruchen, back in the Great Xuan small world, was reporting his insights to Li Fan.

"According to Senior's previous teachings, to further advance in new method Dao Integration is to reverse the principles of heaven and earth."

"However, during our Dao Integration process, we have already devoured the Heavenly Spiritual Essences. What are the Heavenly Spiritual Essences? They are the embodiment of Heavenly Laws, the continuation of Heavenly Principles."

"Therefore, the easiest entry point to reverse the principles is to follow the clues, catch the shadow, and find the person. To find the origin of the principles behind the Heavenly Spiritual Essences we devoured."

Liu Ruchen spoke eloquently: "For example, the [Red Silk] Heavenly Spiritual Essence I devoured is actually the continuation of the principle of life."

"With a clear direction, Heavenly Principles are no longer an ethereal concept. Through continuous cultivation and comprehension, one can find the origin of Heavenly Principles. However, to reverse these Heavenly Principles is almost unimaginably difficult."

"…It is like grabbing one's own hair and lifting oneself up. Without external forces, it is almost an impossible feat."

…

Li Fan listened quietly to Liu Ruchen's explanation.

It had to be said that Liu Ruchen, being able to succeed the sect leader, had truly remarkable comprehension.

The other new Dao Integration cultivators of the Medicine King Sect listened attentively, their expressions showing thoughtfulness.

Finally, after Liu Ruchen had nothing more to say, they all looked at Li Fan.

"To gain so much insight in your first day of new method Dao Integration, you are very good."

Li Fan's faint praise made Liu Ruchen feel extremely flattered.

"However, you are still thinking too simply. Over the past thousands of years in the Xuanhuang Realm, only a handful of people have been able to reverse the principles and achieve Longevity."

"And there have been no new Longevity cultivators for a long time. Do you know why?"

"Think about it carefully."

Li Fan's hints stopped abruptly, leaving the Medicine King Sect members with changed expressions and their minds racing.

Following this, the lives of the seven Dao Integration cultivators of the Medicine King Sect became very fulfilling.

They switched to new Dao Integration cultivation techniques and consolidated their newly acquired foundations.

From time to time, they would listen to the Sacred Master phantom preach beneath the preaching platform.

They would also spar with a mysterious and unfathomable senior who spoke little.

Even if this senior stood still, the Dao Integration cultivators of the Medicine King Sect, even with their full effort, could not harm him in the slightest.

Therefore, they could unleash their skills to their hearts' content and test their learning.

As for the other disciples of the Medicine King Sect…

Li Fan looked at a smaller pink eye beside the silver eye, separated by a formation.

Tens of thousands of threads converged to form a thick bridge, connecting the silver and pink eyes.

"The power of forgetting worries is pervasive throughout the Xuanhuang Realm, not just within the territory of the Five Elders Society."

"Therefore, there is no need to go to the Five Elders Society to enter the Land of Joyful Peace. It's just that previously, they couldn't find a way."

"But now, I have dispatched a total of nine thousand six hundred and thirty-two vanguard soldiers…"

"The counterfeited Heavenly Dao completely synchronizes their perceptions, which is enough to pinpoint the location of the Land of Joyful Peace through their thoughts."

The ten thousand threads acting as a bridge were Li Fan's dispatched cultivators who had entered the Land of Joyful Peace first.

And within the pink eye, slumbering were a large number of disciples of the Medicine King Sect below the Dao Integration stage!

Their physical bodies were under Li Fan's control, and with the sect leader's command, these Medicine King Sect disciples could act in accordance with orders within the Land of Joyful Peace.

Moreover, belonging to the same Medicine King Sect, they had an extraordinary tacit understanding and bond among themselves.

Their actions and explorations within the Land of Joyful Peace would therefore be more efficient.

In addition to the Medicine King Sect disciples, there were also a large number of cultivators from Great Xuan within the pink eye.

They were densely packed, charging into and exploring the Land of Joyful Peace in succession.

The pink eye did not actually break the secrets of the Land of Joyful Peace.

It merely used the cultivators who had entered the Land of Joyful Peace first to establish an entrance to the Land of Joyful Peace within the small world of Great Xuan.

The moment the pink eye manifested, Li Fan had anticipated the arrival of the Joyless Heavenly Venerate's power.

Unfortunately, it seemed that the Joyless Heavenly Venerate did not care about such trivial matters.

Li Fan was truly disappointed that he did not get to witness the Joyless Heavenly Venerate's arrival.

"I hope these people can give me some surprises," Li Fan thought.

Li Fan had a persistent premonition that the secrets hidden within the Land of Joyful Peace might be even more important than he had imagined.

Chapter 1362: The Immortal Realm Ignites the Tribulation of the Dao

Although the Profound Immortal Boat carried a civilization that had endured for ten thousand years, its internal space was not very large. Otherwise, the boat's inhabitants would not have been so constantly plagued by scarce resources.

As Li Fan had anticipated, the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet was dragged by the boat's elders, all the way into the boat's secret treasury.

The first level, the second level…

The Heavenly Star Light Lotuses bloomed across the celestial canopy. Countless lights flickered, and luminous spheres appeared one after another, weaving into a gateway. The elders jointly cast their spells, and the gateway boomed open. Within the passage, a chilling, dark green light emanated. All sorts of ominous energies, accompanied by the green light, sought to spread and corrode the surroundings. The Heavenly Star Light Lotuses were provoked, dividing into star-lit lotuses that blocked the gateway. The sea of lotuses was boundless. Even as the lotuses withered wherever the green light passed, the blockade of the lotus sea could not be breached.

"Quick!" Zhong Daogong urged, seemingly terrified of the green light breaking through. The elders also understood the gravity of the situation and slowly moved the slumbering giant puppet into the third level of the secret treasury. However, only Jian Dao Sheng among the elders followed it in. He was clad in star-light armor, a seven-colored bowl atop his head, and stood on a small boat. Although it looked somewhat comical, it was enough to illustrate Jian Dao Sheng's seriousness.

The gateway slowly closed, leaving only a beam of light extending from Jian Dao Sheng's star-light armor, maintaining a connection with the outside. It was not completely sealed.

Through Jian Dao Sheng's perspective, the appearance of the third level of the Immortal Boat's secret treasury was slowly revealed to everyone. In a spherical, vast cavity, countless green, viscous tissues writhed incessantly, emitting bone-chilling sounds. They grew and adhered to the walls. A colossal gray statue stood within the cavity. The green tissues, which covered the cavity, seemed to originate from the gray statue, following their growth trajectory. The sea of green submerged more than half of the statue's body. Thousands of green tendrils extended from the statue's head. Each tendril originated from a hollow eye socket within the head. This gray statue depicted some bizarre creature; it had a human body, but its head was devoid of facial features, merely covered in eyes.

The moment the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet entered this third level of the secret treasury, even though it exuded no aura, it immediately attracted the attention of the green substance in the cavity. Like tentacles, they surged through the air from all directions towards the Heavenly Yang. Jian Dao Sheng, seizing the opportunity, hid himself within one of the hollow eye sockets of the gray statue's head. The green tentacles were blocked by the invisible force field around the Heavenly Yang. However, perhaps due to its proximity and sensing the scent of True Immortal flesh, the green tendrils became even more agitated. The entire cavity's verdant growth was activated, surging towards the Heavenly Yang in a frenzy. In an instant, the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet was engulfed by endless green, submerged in a sea of green light, with sounds like a silkworm gnawing all around.

Li Fan's wisp of divine sense, while observing the Heavenly Yang's sensations, felt a pang of surprise. "Hmm? I can't see these green entities at all!" The information conveyed by the Heavenly Yang baffled Li Fan. "It's like rain hitting the wind…" Li Fan mused, then withdrew his divine sense from external observation. Instead, he isolated his senses and, relying solely on the Heavenly Yang, "saw" the surroundings. The surroundings instantly became quiet, as if he had arrived in a vast field, atop a high mountain, or in a deep canyon. The flowing water was as sharp as a knife, day and night, carving stones and splitting mountains. The howling wind and the pattering rain were like axes, ceaselessly hacking and transforming the terrain. And the Heavenly Yang was like this mountain, this land, this valley, being ruthlessly corroded by the invisible force of the passage of time, slowly but resolutely. The Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet instinctively defended itself. But according to the intentions conveyed by the Heavenly Yang, under the erosion of this green substance, he could only last for half a year at most without actively counterattacking. Li Fan did not act rashly for the time being.

From the Heavenly Yang's perspective, this vast cavity did not contain any writhing green tissues, allowing it to see the third level of the Immortal Boat's secret treasury completely. The strange gray statue with a thousand eyes on its human-like body sent a tremor through Li Fan's heart. And the treasure light faintly flashing from the thousand eye sockets on the statue's head made Li Fan suddenly understand. "The last chess piece's aura." "It seems these eye sockets are the Immortal Boat's treasure vaults." "They are not completely full, with less than a handful appearing." "There must be some unknown protective measures, not just exposed like this." "Jian Dao Sheng… where did he go?" "Hmm, this gray statue seems to have changed slightly from before." Li Fan quickly analyzed the current situation. The third level of the Immortal Boat's secret treasury was indeed not simple, even concealing power capable of harming the Immortal Puppet. But now, in addition to the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet's own strength, there was the power of an immortal formation pre-prepared by Li Fan. Even if it was not enough to defeat the enemy, escaping was definitely possible. Therefore, Li Fan had no intention of acting rashly and chose to observe further.

After Jian Dao Sheng merged with the gray statue through some method, the erosion speed of the green substance seemed to suddenly accelerate. In the Heavenly Yang's perception, it was like a raging wind and pouring rain. Amidst the wind and rain, the various powers comprising itself were being stripped away and diluted. "Interesting." Although Li Fan had never seen this green substance before, he detected a faint sense of familiarity from it. Especially the fact that Li Fan and the Heavenly Yang, with their different perspectives, saw completely different scenes—this further led Li Fan to associate it with something. The sound of wind and rain grew louder. Facing the erosion and encirclement by the strange substance and a dangerous situation, Li Fan felt no panic. He calmly contemplated. After an unknown period… like a lightning strike illuminating the night sky, Li Fan's thoughts snapped back. "Erosion of the Wind Tribulation?" This did not refer to the erosion of the Wind Tribulation itself, but rather that the aura of the two was almost identical. Only, the Wind Tribulation sensed by Li Fan within the Immeasurable Mirror was several times more potent than the encroaching green substance before him. It was as if the wind and rain in his perception had been amplified to the extreme. Thinking of this, Li Fan couldn't help but shift his gaze to the gray statue in the vast cavity. "The eroding green substance is used to erode the power of the Immortal level." "Judging by this, this statue…" The voices of the Immortal Boat elders, echoing in the vast cavity, validated Li Fan's guess. Through the star-light cloth left by Jian Dao Sheng outside the gateway, the Immortal Boat elders inside and outside the secret treasury could communicate with each other. However, their voices were not very clear, as if isolated from another world. "Old Jian cannot stay in the Desolate God for too long." "Although the Desolate God is already dead, and even its will has been completely obliterated. But after all, it is an existence beyond the mortal realm…" As if a routine reminder, every so often, a different elder would say it, reminding Jian Dao Sheng, who was merging with the Desolate God. After all the elders had finished their reminders, Jian Dao Sheng reappeared. In this short period of absence, his appearance had somehow changed. Li Fan was certain it was not his imagination. It was the influence of the Desolate God statue on Jian Dao Sheng! "Desolate God…" Li Fan's thoughts spun rapidly. In the ancient Profound Yellow Realm, there was a powerful sect called the Desolate God Sect. They wielded the Desolate God Seal, capable of summoning twelve Desolate Gods from the upper realm to descend and exterminate all enemies. In the eyes of the Desolate Gods, cultivators were like ants. Therefore, the Desolate God Sect was invincible in its era, almost crushing all opposition. But later, for some reason, the Desolate Gods gradually ceased responding to mortals and no longer descended to the lower realms. With their greatest reliance gone, the Desolate God Sect eventually perished. "Is this Desolate God the same one?" "Desolate Gods are not Immortals. Otherwise, they would not serve mortals, even if mortals sacrificed and invited them." "But they possess the power of Immortals…" "Servants of Immortals?" A bold guess surfaced in Li Fan's mind, and his emotions towards the statue changed. After separating from the Desolate God statue, Jian Dao Sheng still hid in one of the eye sockets. He responded to the Immortal Boat elders outside. First, he spoke a string of strange sounds, like a secret code, and then said, "This Immortal Puppet's quality is definitely not low. It can endure the corrosive power of the Desolate God for so long without showing signs of collapse." "Should I increase the guidance?" Zhong Daogong quickly stopped him, "Forget it, let's take it slow. Otherwise, once the corrosive substance accumulates, the Heavenly Star Light Lotuses might not be able to contain it." "Besides, you might not be able to handle it either." Jian Dao Sheng nodded with apparent regret. "Are there any signs of the Immortal Puppet awakening?" Zhong Daogong asked again. "No. It seems it is indeed a puppet that has lost its control core. Otherwise, facing such a dire crisis, it would never be so quiet." "That's good. We just need to wait." "Once the erosion reaches halfway, immediately pull the Immortal Puppet out again." Amidst the discussions of the Immortal Boat elders, the fate of the slumbering Immortal Puppet seemed to have been decided. Meanwhile, the corroding green substance in the vicinity, which was eroding the Heavenly Yang, suddenly sent a reminder to Li Fan. "The True Immortal flesh can be temporarily retracted into the Immortal Bronze Bones." "When facing this corrosive substance, the damage to those residual Immortal Artifact fragments will be greatly weakened." Li Fan pondered and temporarily stopped the Heavenly Yang's actions. He even allowed the Heavenly Yang to voluntarily withdraw its force field, using its flesh to experience the erosion of the corrosive green substance. "Don't worry, the True Immortal flesh can be reborn. I can even help you reforge the Immortal Bones. As long as the core is not damaged, it's a minor matter." Only the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet, having lost most of its subjective initiative, would endure the mortal crisis and obey Li Fan's instructions. The force field was voluntarily withdrawn by the Heavenly Yang. The green substance instantly came into direct contact with the True Immortal flesh. The corrosion speed was far faster than Li Fan had imagined. It was like a pile of dry grass being rapidly ignited. Except, it was not fire that ignited the True Immortal flesh, but the corrosive green substance. The green light spread vigorously, and after burning out, it left behind piles of ashes. The vibrant flesh turned into stone-like carvings. The instantaneous transformation sent a shiver down Li Fan's spine, the observer. Even more shocking to Li Fan was the sensation conveyed by the Heavenly Yang when its flesh's life force was depleted. It was not like normal aging or the natural loss of vitality. Instead, the life force that constituted the elements of life was instantly ignited and disappeared. Words could not accurately describe the feeling. Only by personally experiencing it could one understand the horror of a component of life being directly extracted. It was like the sorrow of the rabbit for the fox, the concern for its own kind. The moment the life force was extracted, the remaining elements of life also began to disintegrate. In terror, they scattered! Li Fan seemed to see the crisscrossing lines of the Great Dao that constituted the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet. After one thread was pulled out, the rest crumbled! In an instant, the powerful Immortal Puppet turned to dust! With a rapid shift of his mind, Li Fan manipulated the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet to retract a small portion of its flesh into its Immortal Bones in the final moment. The corrosive green substance, when encountering the Immortal Bones forged from residual Immortal Artifact fragments, stopped its rampant advance as if hitting a wall. And Li Fan saw clearly. The most crucial factor preventing the green erosion was that the Immortal Bones did not contain the Dao of life! "If it were the Wind Tribulation of Annihilation from the Immortal Realm's calamity, the outcome would be different. Perhaps this so-called Immortal Bone would turn to dust in an instant!" "So, are the different calamities of the Immortal Realm derived from different Great Dao principles? Do they target specific Daos?" "Dao Annihilation Tribulation…" Li Fan fell into deep thought. Meanwhile, in the vast cavity, Jian Dao Sheng, seeing the Immortal Puppet's defensive power instantly disappear and nearly completely eroded, exclaimed in surprise. "Why so fast?" Instinctively, he merged with the Desolate God statue again, intending to control the corrosive green substance and slow down the erosion. Li Fan had not forgotten the purpose of his visit. With a thought, the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet, which had been asleep, finally opened its eyes. The force field reappeared, pushing back the green substance clinging to its body. The True Immortal flesh re-emerged from the Immortal Bones, transforming the skeleton back into a puppet form. Only its body was no longer as large as before. In a flash, it had already arrived at the location of the gray statue's head. Facing the puppet's sudden resurgence, Jian Dao Sheng seemed to have anticipated it. Dozens of the thousand eyes on the head suddenly aimed at the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet, shooting out intense beams of scorching light. These beams not only possessed immense destructive power, causing the Immortal Puppet's force field to vibrate violently but also acted like ropes, binding the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet. Within the vast cavity, light after light flashed. One by one, the Immortal Boat elders appeared. Zhong Daogong's voice echoed: "Originally, it was just to prevent accidents, but we never expected it to be right! Did you really think we, the Immortal Boat, are a bunch of fools? Sending him here so directly, did you expect us to fall for it?" "Heh, we, the Immortal Boat, have been in seclusion for ten thousand years. The only thing that might have external contact, attracting covetousness, is that gray chess piece left by Sun Piaomiao. We've been waiting for you to come, but we didn't expect you to use such a foolish method!" A series of mocking voices echoed, and then the Immortal Boat elders sequentially flew into the Desolate God's eye sockets. Once occupied by the Immortal Boat elders, the originally dim eye sockets were re-energized, shooting out brilliant white light. As the light beams increased, the shackles binding the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet grew heavier. The Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet tried to move but found the binding force from the Desolate God to be unexpectedly powerful, making every step a struggle! "So this is not the third level of the Hundred Heard Immortal Record." "It's a trap." It uttered a low voice, looking at the Desolate God in front of it, which seemed to have regained its vitality by merging with the Immortal Boat elders. The gray color faded from its body, and the corrosive green substance receded below its knees. The ancient Desolate God, with its thousand eyes, fixed on the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet. After all, the Heavenly Yang was pieced together by Li Fan with all his immortal power. It was not a puppet truly crafted by a True Immortal. Facing the reviving Desolate God, it gradually fell into a disadvantage during their struggle, being slowly suppressed. Seeing victory within reach, the Immortal Boat elders finally responded triumphantly, "Not bad! Such a dormant Immortal Puppet, if we didn't awaken it, how could we possibly keep it in the Immortal Boat's sacred ground?" "We originally thought it would take more effort to lure you out. We didn't expect you to be so impatient!" "A mere Immortal Puppet, trying to barge into the Immortal Boat alone to steal treasures? You're underestimating us!" Cold and sarcastic voices echoed. But the binding force from the Desolate God did not lessen; it only intensified. Moreover, Li Fan sensed that as life force gradually revived, a peculiar aura also began to emerge from the Desolate God's body. *Creak… creak…* Besides the thousand light beams, an invisible pressure instantly pressed down on the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet. In a trance, Li Fan seemed to truly see an ancient Desolate God before him. Its face was ferocious, and all thousand eyes glared at the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet. "I was careless." "I just didn't expect your Immortal Boat to be willing to use that chess piece as bait? The aura originating from the Immortal Realm fragments cannot be faked." "Aren't you afraid of making a mistake and the chess piece falling into my hands?" The Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet's low voice first admitted its oversight, then asked with some surprise. "Anyway, we only have this last one left. If we can't form a complete set, this single piece is useless!" "Hmph, you can't catch a wolf without sacrificing your child. If we didn't lure you out, we wouldn't easily activate this Desolate God…" "Heh heh, not only is the chess piece real, but the other treasures are also real! If we're going to put on a show, we'll make it convincing!" "Stop talking nonsense with him, take him down first!" *Buzz buzz buzz…* Amidst the rising voices of the Immortal Boat elders, the ancient Desolate God actually raised its right hand. It seemed to reach out its palm to capture the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet. The giant palm was about to descend. All around, it was locked by dense beams of light. The Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet seemed to face imminent death, yet for some reason, it showed no despair. "Your plan…" "Is quite good." "But unfortunately, it all ends here." The Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet looked at the ancient Desolate God in the vast cavity. "Today, I will teach you a lesson." "In the cultivation world, the strong are respected! All schemes, in the face of absolute strength, are merely a joke!" A faint light suddenly flashed at the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet's forehead. A gust of wind arose in the vast cavity. "Not good! Stop him quickly!" The Immortal Boat elders instantly sensed something was wrong. The Desolate God's thousand eyes erupted with unprecedented brilliance. Its life force grew even denser, and the Desolate God's movements became several times faster. But it was too late. Immortal Descent, Myriad Things Returning to Void! A world-destroying gust of wind erupted from the faint light on the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet's forehead, then swept outwards. To Li Fan's surprise, the corrosive green substance, which had been suppressed by the Desolate God's life force, not only was unaffected by the void-destroying immortal array but instead, as if in its natural element, utilized the power of the world-destroying immortal array to further erode the Desolate God's body. Void Returning Immortal Array, corrosive green substance. Under the superposition of double crises, the Desolate God's lower half was completely submerged by the destructive force, leaving only a thousand-eyed head. "God of the Ancients, command Immortals!" "Tribulation!" "Condense!" With the simultaneous shouts of the Immortal Boat elders, the light flashes within the eyes of the head quickly moved and then merged into one in an instant! A giant, hollow eye instantly appeared in the center of the ancient Desolate God's face! Sacred power manifested, repelling the approaching destructive force below. Seeing this, the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet advanced instead of retreating. Wielding the power of the world-destroying immortal array, it charged directly towards the single-eyed Desolate God. Behind it, countless green substances surged like dragons, snakes, and pythons, forming a tide that followed closely. The two forces from the Immortal Realm collided. Facing the Desolate God's single eye directly, the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet's remaining True Immortal flesh dissolved like melting snow. But its Immortal Bones remained, its momentum undiminished. With the residual power of the immortal array, under the gaze of the Desolate God's single eye, it pressed forward unimpeded. It successfully reached the side of the head, where the other hollow eye sockets were located. The frenzied voices of the Immortal Boat elders rang out. The Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet locked onto the last chess piece. Reaching out, it intended to retrieve it. It sensed a binding force, similar to the scorching light beams shot from the Desolate God's eyes, but even more robust. It was enough to block the prying eyes of most cultivators in the world, yet insignificant compared to the Immortal Puppet's strength. With a slight exertion, it retrieved the last gray chess piece into its palm. Li Fan soon turned his attention to the nearest target. After retrieving one more item, sensing the Immortal Array's storm weakening and the Desolate God about to react, Li Fan no longer hesitated and activated the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet to flee rapidly. "Close the entrance!" Nan Gonglie's somewhat frenzied voice could be vaguely heard. "Are you crazy? Do you want us to be buried with the Desolate God?" The elders who maintained their reason were the majority; the exit of the Heavenly Star Light Lotuses remained open. Li Fan passed through, sweeping his gaze across the treasures in the second level of the secret treasury. He tried to take some, but found that these treasures were encased in light lotuses. Without special means to open the lotuses, they could only be destroyed entirely. After all, Li Fan's main body had not personally arrived, and the power of the immortal formation he left behind had been depleted. The Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet no longer lingered, transforming into a streak of light and fleeing. Ignoring all protective restrictions within the Immortal Boat, it departed. Before leaving, Li Fan seemed to see scenes of surging green substance, like tides, engulfing the Desolate God's head, through the gateway. Moments later, the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet did not immediately return to Great Xuan to deliver the chess piece to Li Fan's main body. Instead, it stood silently in the void, looking at the Immortal Boat not far away. The Immortal Boat trembled slightly, but in the end, it calmed down again. "As expected, it has some capabilities." "It could even block the corrosive green substance agitated by the world-ending immortal array." "Desolate God…" Li Fan's heart grew heavy. Judging from the brief confrontation just now, the Desolate God hidden within the Profound Immortal Boat, even if its strength was not fully unleashed, was comparable to the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet. Its strength in its prime was indeed astounding. "It's merely a servant of a True Immortal." "And the Profound Immortal Boat can actually control this ancient Desolate God…" "Truly pushing the art of borrowing external forces to the extreme," Li Fan praised slightly. "In my previous life, under the world-ending immortal array, this Desolate God was nowhere to be seen." "It seems that vast cavity was not inside the Immortal Boat itself, but rather a passage opened by the Heavenly Star Light Lotuses when they approached." While Li Fan was contemplating, he saw the formerly calm Immortal Boat stir again. It was not pursuing the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet, but changing its hidden position in the Star Sea. "From the Immortal Boat's perspective, it has lost a chess piece, and its enemy has lost the method to locate the Immortal Boat. As long as it re-hides, it should regain peace." "As for the loss of another immortal treasure…" Li Fan scanned the other item in the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet's hand besides the gray chess piece. It was an ancient bronze coin. The patterns on both sides were different, but no matter how Li Fan tried, he could not discern what was engraved upon them. *Wuwuwu… cco* Shifting his attention away from the bronze coin for now, Li Fan took one last look at the Profound Immortal Boat. "These losses are, for the financially well-off Profound Immortal Boat, arguably acceptable." "Perhaps the true trouble for the Immortal Boat will lie with the Desolate God." "After all, the power of a True Immortal is not easily borrowed." Li Fan smiled and manipulated the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet towards the Teleportation Array at the ends of the earth. Not long after, he returned to the Great Xuan small world. Li Fan's main body had already prepared new True Immortal flesh to re-arm the puppet. The Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet handed over the two obtained treasures to Li Fan and began to adapt to its new body. During the battle with the thousand-eyed Desolate God, the Heavenly Yang had instinctively gained some insights. After a period of silence, it slowly entered seclusion. Seeing this, Li Fan did not disturb it. He first examined the bronze coin. With his main body and a sufficiently strong divine soul, he could finally vaguely discern the patterns on the coin. One side was engraved with magnificent, continuous palaces. The other side showed countless shifting scenes superimposed upon each other. "No wonder my divine sense couldn't see clearly just now." "The speed of this change…" Li Fan's expression shifted slightly. Grasping the bronze coin, Li Fan narrowed his eyes and tried to discern each fleeting scene. Simultaneously, the Dao Transformation Stone in his mind emitted a faint glow, recording all the images one by one, then reassembling them. Thus, after sixteen days had passed, Li Fan finally completely recorded all the scenes depicted on this seemingly small bronze coin. "This bronze coin records the scenery of a certain star field in the Immortal Realm of the upper realm?" A magnificent scroll, reassembled before Li Fan, slowly unfurled. "There are no True Immortals depicted, only natural landscapes and scattered structures." Li Fan carefully observed this depiction of the Immortal Realm. The moment he fully comprehended this Immortal Domain scenery, a name naturally appeared in Li Fan's mind. "Bei Lin." "The palaces on the side of the bronze coin should be the domain of the Northern Lin ruler." Recalling the memories he had seen within the True Immortal flesh, Li Fan mused. "I wonder, what was the structure of the Immortal Realm in ancient times?" "Judging by this, could there be immortal emperors?" "If so, what would be the status of the Nameless True Immortal?" Li Fan's expression turned somewhat strange, his thoughts drifting.

Chapter 1363: Celestial Formation Traps Heavenly Doctor

Li Fan collected his thoughts, his hand tightly clutching the Northern Lin Immortal Coin, attempting to decipher its function.

"It couldn't possibly just be simple currency, right?" Li Fan always felt this Immortal Coin harbored other secrets.

He first tried infusing it with Origin Pure Essence, attempting to activate it. However, Origin Pure Essence, while the closest energy form to Immortal Spiritual Power in the lower realms, could not equate to True Immortal Spiritual Power. When facing the Northern Lin Immortal Coin, a genuine creation from the Immortal Realm, it naturally lost its efficacy. Streams of Origin Pure Essence flowed like a tide, only to strike the surface of the Immortal Coin, unable to penetrate it.

Li Fan withdrew the Origin Pure Essence, pondered for a moment, and then ascended to the void outside the Xuanhuang Realm. He initiated the Ascension Formation, attempting to observe it from a higher dimensional perspective. As expected, the view differed from his usual observation. As his "momentum" continuously escalated, the constantly changing patterns on the Immortal Coin began to transform at a slower pace, and simultaneously, more panoramic views were perceived. Moreover… on the celestial canopy depicting the entirety of the Northern Lin Immortal Domain, a vague shadow faintly appeared! Li Fan could not discern its features, but after merely a glance, the spiritual energy within his body surged uncontrollably. In an instant, he could no longer maintain his elevated posture and plummeted back to his original mortal realm. However, the boiling of his spiritual energy did not cease.

Li Fan frowned, intending to use greater power to forcibly suppress this strange turbulence. But this decision was like trying to save a burning cart by adding firewood. It was as if he was ignited by an unknown fire, burning fiercely and unceasingly, until all his spiritual energy and even his physical body were consumed. Only then did it finally end. After some time, with a strange fluctuation, Li Fan's body reappeared in the void. With a breath, his stamina and spiritual energy were replenished.

"Not only my spiritual energy and body, but even my soul was nearly affected," Li Fan stated, examining his new body's condition with a solemn expression. "Just by glimpsing that figure… is this the punishment for mortals attempting to gaze upon a True Immortal's countenance?" "If my survival capabilities were not so formidable, any Harmonious Dao cultivator in the current Xuanhuang Realm would likely not survive such a punishment." "That figure was definitely not an ordinary True Immortal… a nameless realm…" Li Fan mused thoughtfully.

Li Fan temporarily sealed the Northern Lin Immortal Coin, not rushing to fuse the Immortal Realm fragments. Instead, he suppressed it in the Da Qi small world and leisurely headed towards the Profound Immortal Boat. While en route, he ceased the arrangement of the Jun Tian Formation, lest he arouse suspicion from the Profound Immortal Boat. During his journey, Li Fan perceived the changes that had occurred within his body recently. Although the changes were minute, Li Fan's control over himself had reached a point of perfect clarity, and he naturally noticed them. He touched his face, "It's actually deforming towards the appearance of that Thousand-Eyed Desolate God… is this the price of using the Desolate God's power?" "I didn't personally participate, only being influenced by the previous Jun Tian ritual." A flicker of interest crossed Li Fan's face. Li Fan, who was committed to playing the part, first returned to the Profound Immortal Boat's original location. Finding no trace of the Profound Immortal Boat, he remained stunned for a moment. Only then did he, utilizing the mutual sensing between the Jun Tian ritual components, locate the Immortal Boat's new hiding place. The Immortal Boat's portal was tightly shut, and no elders came out to greet him. Li Fan feigned an anxious expression, directly activating his aura as a reminder. After waiting for a while longer and seeing no response from the Immortal Boat, he prepared to force his way in.

It was then that Zhong Daogong's somewhat weak voice finally transmitted, "No need to worry, we are unharmed." "It's just temporarily inconvenient to meet…" Li Fan first breathed a sigh of relief, then, hearing Zhong Daogong's words, his expression turned somewhat indignant, "After the Jun Tian ritual, we are already bound together; do you still not trust me?" Zhong Daogong sighed and explained, "No, no. Have you not noticed the changes within yourself?" Li Fan appeared greatly astonished, examining himself and then his body trembled violently, "What exactly happened?" Zhong Daogong then slowly recounted the entire incident of their encounter with the Immortal Puppet. Li Fan's expression shifted continuously, as if wanting to speak but stopping. "Fortunately, that puppet was also severely injured. In the end, it only managed to snatch the last chess piece and an Immortal Realm copper coin, failing to inflict greater damage on the Immortal Boat. Otherwise, I would truly be deserving of a thousand deaths." "The main thing is that we underestimated the power that puppet could unleash. Who would have thought that the current Star Sea still harbors existences capable of contending with a Desolate God," Zhong Daogong coughed lightly. After a long period of silence, Li Fan finally spoke, "Even if I were present, I would likely have fallen for the trap. After all, it's an Immortal Puppet, immune to True Immortal incantations, and possesses genuine True Immortal flesh…" "Could it be that the Star Sea harbors a civilization that completely surpasses the Profound Immortal Boat and Da Qi?" Li Fan feigned shock. "It's likely that this is the case," Zhong Daogong said, then changed the subject, "Now that that civilization has gathered all the chess pieces, they will likely focus all their energy on recreating the Immortal Domain of the past. They won't bother us for the time being." "They didn't leave any tracking methods? It's truly disheartening to lose such a supreme treasure just like that." "Even if we can't defeat them, tracing them to scout their strength and cause a disturbance would be good. At least let them know that we, the Profound Immortal Boat, are not to be trifled with," Li Fan scoffed. Zhong Daogong did not refute Li Fan, his expression remaining as usual, "It's simply a matter of inferior skill. The Profound Immortal Boat has always prioritized survival and does not engage in disputes based on pride. Moreover, among us, no one has yet been able to comprehend your astonishing escape technique." Li Fan was left speechless. "This Thousand-Eyed Desolate God is one of the Profound Immortal Boat's ultimate trump cards. Although it can unleash Immortal-level power, it requires extensive preparation and faces backlash afterward…" "The reason I couldn't meet you temporarily is that you, as part of the Jun Tian ritual, were not affected by the Thousand-Eyed Desolate God. You acted like an anchor, delaying our gradual transformation process," Zhong Daogong explained briefly to Li Fan. "Your being outside is actually beneficial for our recovery." Li Fan nodded, accepting this explanation. "Do you need any help? I recall a Dao Venerable from Da Qi who once researched the subject of transformations after being influenced by True Immortal power…" Zhong Daogong paused, appearing hesitant. Finally, he refused Li Fan's offer, "No need to worry. After all, we have been dealing with True Immortal incantation power for many years; we are quite experienced." Li Fan expressed some regret, "Alright. I was also worried about the Immortal Boat's safety, which is why I risked such great danger to come here. After all, the ritual is being carried out in secret…" "Currently, the ritual has already encompassed thirty million people. If all goes smoothly, it can be expanded three to fivefold," Li Fan reported his achievements. Zhong Daogong's tone finally held a hint of joy, "That's good. With this, we can surely minimize the backlash from the Star Sea." "It's just a minor hiccup; it won't have a significant impact. We must prioritize the bigger picture. The ritual cannot have any mistakes. You should return as soon as possible!" As he spoke, he was clearly issuing a polite dismissal. "It seems they still harbor doubts about me. In their extremely weakened state, they dare not let me stay. However, due to the Jun Tian ritual requiring me to find sacrifices, they cannot openly turn against me." Li Fan understood and was about to bow in farewell.

*BOOM!*

A shockwave like a monstrous wave erupted from the distant High Wall, arriving in an instant. Its speed of propagation was too fast. Coupled with Li Fan's need to conceal his strength before the Profound Immortal Boat, he feigned a lack of reaction. Swept away by this impact, he was dragged for several thousand miles in the Star Sea before he could stabilize himself. The Profound Immortal Boat, in its hidden state, was directly tossed out of its original form by this strange and powerful impact, bobbing uncontrollably like a small boat in turbulent waves.

"What happened?" Li Fan returned to the vicinity of the Profound Immortal Boat with a somewhat disheveled appearance, looking towards the source of the impact on the High Wall with an expression of surprise and uncertainty. The Profound Immortal Boat members were also perplexed. "In our recorded history, such an anomaly has only occurred three times…" "We have no clue as to its origin." "It's a pity; if we weren't in a weakened state of recovery, we would definitely pursue its source." Amidst this anomaly, the other elders of the Profound Immortal Boat emerged one by one. They all appeared somewhat weak and short of breath. Li Fan sensed the receding energy fluctuation, observing that its power dissipated significantly as it propagated through the Star Sea. It seemed that the residual True Immortal energies scattered throughout the Star Sea acted as an impediment to its passage. "I'll go take a look!" Li Fan cupped his hands towards the Profound Immortal Boat, volunteering. "Don't worry, if I can't find the source, I'll return immediately!" Without waiting for a response from the Profound Immortal Boat members, Li Fan manipulated the phantom of his wooden sword and sped towards the direction of the anomaly. Swiftly traversing the Great Wall of Remaining Realms, following the residual energy fluctuations in the Star Sea, he was about to reach the source. Li Fan's expression, however, became solemn. He discovered that this terrifying anomaly seemed to be emanating from the very crack in the High Wall. This discovery made Li Fan's heart leap. He accelerated his flight speed.

A few breaths later, when Li Fan arrived at the crack in the High Wall, he found that Mo Rubing, who should have been contemplating the secrets of the High Wall, was now only a severed head, lying unconscious. The wooden sword and enlightenment phantom he had left behind were still present, seemingly unaffected by the recent surge. "No wonder I didn't detect anything…" "What happened? Did the High Wall retaliate and injure him? Could it be that Mo Rubing truly comprehended something?" Li Fan's thoughts raced. After some investigation, he found that Mo Rubing was severely injured but not dead, which somewhat eased his mind. Just as he was about to examine the crack in the High Wall again, his expression suddenly changed. He faintly sensed a familiar aura rapidly approaching. "Sky Physician?!" "Did he also detect that anomaly and come here?" Li Fan pondered for a moment, then quickly made a decision. It was not yet necessary to have a direct conflict with the Sky Physician. If he were to discover Li Fan's secret plan to sublimate the Xuanhuang Realm, it would undoubtedly introduce complications. The phantom of the wooden sword flashed, swiftly carrying Mo Rubing's severed head and fleeing the scene. "Strange, the Profound Immortal Boat said they had observed such inexplicable fluctuations several times before." "If this fluctuation was caused by Mo Rubing comprehending the crack in the High Wall, doesn't that mean someone else had already done this before?" Recalling the Sky Physician who had arrived quickly this time, Li Fan implicitly understood. "The Sky Physician also discovered the crack in the High Wall long ago?" "And not only has he comprehended it, but he has also gained something?" "Indeed, he is not to be underestimated. Even with my immortal formations now, it is still the case," Li Fan trembled inwardly. He flew past the Great Wall of Remaining Realms and into the empty wilderness of the Star Sea. Li Fan then began to heal Mo Rubing's injuries. With a large amount of spiritual energy and soul power, Mo Rubing gradually awoke from his severe coma. Flesh and blood slowly regenerated on his body. "Uh…" Mo Rubing opened his eyes in confusion, seeing Li Fan's concerned expression, he was slightly stunned for a moment. Then he abruptly turned his head, looking around. "Hmm? Wasn't I under the High Wall?" "You were severely injured, and fortunately I found you in time," Li Fan explained briefly. As if recalling a lost memory, Mo Rubing's body trembled as if electrocuted. "What exactly happened? You looked so tragic just now. To injure you to such an extent…" Li Fan stared intently at Mo Rubing. Mo Rubing opened his mouth, but could not speak. "While you were unconscious, a peculiar fluctuation swept through the Star Sea." "And this peculiar fluctuation has been recorded three times before…" "Do you know what this signifies?" Li Fan's words caused Mo Rubing to show an expression of disbelief. After pondering for a long time, he slowly spoke, "Actually… I'm not entirely sure of the specifics." "I only remember that at the time, I was contemplating the secrets of the High Wall, and it seemed like I suddenly understood something." "I cannot describe precisely what I comprehended." "I only felt that in that instant, like a fish leaping out of the sea, or a bird breaking through the sky, I seemed to witness scenery completely different from before…" Mo Rubing's tone was somewhat ethereal. He frowned, trying to recall the feeling from back then. "Then, I lost consciousness and passed out." Li Fan could not help but ask, "You didn't even have a chance to resist?" Mo Rubing shook his head. "That strange fluctuation attenuates rapidly during its propagation in the Star Sea. The intensity I encountered near the Profound Immortal Boat was already terrifying. One can imagine the earth-shattering power at the High Wall's point of origin. If, as Mo Rubing said, it is a self-defense mechanism of the High Wall triggered by enlightenment?" Li Fan mused inwardly. At this moment, Mo Rubing also reacted, "You brought me away… does this mean someone has gone to investigate the crack in the High Wall?" "Yes. And that person's strength is immense, likely surpassing both of us," Li Fan replied with a heavy tone. Mo Rubing's expression kept changing. "No, I must return to the crack in the High Wall immediately. I have a premonition that my previous enlightenment is rapidly fading. If I cannot retain it by borrowing the aura of the High Wall again, all my previous efforts will be in vain!" he declared resolutely. Saying so, he did not wait for Li Fan's reaction and dashed directly towards his destination. To act in this manner, knowing a powerful, unknown enemy lay ahead, was completely contrary to Mo Rubing's usual demeanor. This demonstrated the immense allure of the High Wall's secrets, to the extent that it could influence one's mindset.

Li Fan pondered for a moment, then decided to follow. The phantom of the wooden sword enveloped them both, while Origin Pure Essence formed an immortal formation, concealing their presence. "Actually, returning now is also a good opportunity. The opponent just checked and found no one, so they should instinctively try to track for a while. They certainly wouldn't expect us to return…" As he spoke, the two had already returned to the crack in the High Wall. Indeed, the Sky Physician's figure was nowhere to be seen. Mo Rubing was about to step forward when Li Fan suddenly stopped him with outstretched hand. After careful observation, they discovered fine threads adhering to the void like a spiderweb, obscuring the location of the crack in the High Wall. This scene caused both Li Fan and Mo Rubing to take a sharp breath. "This…" Both of them had personally experienced the transcendent nature of the High Wall. Especially Mo Rubing, who had been contemplating under the High Wall for months on end. He knew very well that with his strength, merely staying under the High Wall for an extended period was already incredibly difficult. Let alone leaving one's energy or traces on the High Wall. "The Star Sea has produced such a person?" Li Fan, after his initial shock, quickly regained his composure, "It's just a temporary measure. Those golden threads are naturally dissipating." "We just need to wait." Mo Rubing said solemnly, "The key is, we cannot wait." "I imagine the person who set this up had similar enlightenment experiences to mine. They knew that they only needed to stall me for this period…" "And… Mo Rubing looked around, "…perhaps that person hasn't gone far either, and is waiting to ensnare us nearby." Despite saying this, Mo Rubing couldn't help but move closer to the golden threads surrounding the crack in the High Wall. The aura he was suppressing gradually became uncontrollable, indicating that his reason was being overwhelmed by desire. Frowning, Li Fan pondered for a long time, and finally sighed, "Fine. Then I'll accompany you, old friend." "I will stall the opponent!" "You must act quickly; I may not be able to hold them off for long!"
