Before his words had even finished, strands of golden threads flew out from Li Fan's body. In the void, they wove into an exquisitely beautiful and profound pattern. "Let the Sky Physician experience the quality of my [Bewildering, Xuanhuang Sentient Beings] Great Array!" Li Fan coldly snorted in his heart. While he did not wish to clash with the Sky Physician prematurely, he was certainly not afraid of him. Especially with the combined advantages of his escape technique and immortal formations, Li Fan was confident he could suppress the Sky Physician for a short period! Receiving Li Fan's assurance, Mo Rubing no longer suppressed himself. "Demonic Heart, Immortal Intent!" he roared. Instantly, thousands of faces, like vast dark clouds before a coming storm, emerged from Mo Rubing's body. They displayed various expressions. Like moths flying into a flame, they surged towards the golden threads left by the Sky Physician. Under the cover of the myriad demonic souls, Mo Rubing's true body quietly approached the High Wall. "Buzz…" A sound like vibrating strings suddenly resonated through the Star Sea. Before the demonic soul army could even approach the Sky Physician's golden threads, a large number of demonic souls were instantly vaporized, like snow under direct sunlight. However, they did not completely disappear, merely leaving behind faint shadowy figures. Upon closer inspection, these figures all bore a thin golden thread mark. The golden threads connected these figures, and they instantly turned rebellious, clashing with the demonic souls manipulated by Mo Rubing. "A mere mortal art, daring to contend with Immortal Arts?" Mo Rubing growled. His eyes instantly fell into a strange darkness. An invisible mirror quietly appeared in the center of the scene, reflecting all the demonic souls controlled by the Sky Physician's golden threads. The mirror erupted with a black light, transitioning from illusory to substantial. Then, the demonic souls within the mirror reappeared with Mo Rubing's own face! Even though they were still manipulated by golden threads within their bodies, they were forced to be possessed by Mo Rubing! Thus, relying on the cover of the immortal demonic souls, Mo Rubing successfully breached the outer defense left by the Sky Physician. As the crack in the High Wall was within reach, Mo Rubing suddenly found himself unable to move. Transparent, fine needles had unknowingly pierced his body. Initially, there was only one. Then it split into two, then four. As if possessing self-awareness, they proliferated rapidly, soon filling all of Mo Rubing's acupuncture points. The somewhat contorted expression on Mo Rubing's face gradually froze. Li Fan, who was observing the situation while setting up the formation, witnessing this scene and contemplating whether to intervene, discovered that he had underestimated Mo Rubing, the former Dharma King of the Profound Heaven Sect. The moment he froze, all the invisible fine needles were covered in a faint blackness. Like muddy swamps, they continuously eroded upwards. Upon magnification, that blackness was precisely the manifestation of Mo Rubing's demonic soul! However, compared to the demonic souls Mo Rubing had released earlier, these were even more devoid of reason, their eyes only filled with frenzied destruction, relentlessly gnawing at the sealing needles. Once a needle was devoured by the demonic souls, it was consequently pulled out of the body. They then flew towards other needles, assisting in the erosion. Thus, the sealing needles rapidly disintegrated. In just a few breaths, they were all broken by Mo Rubing. "The Myriad Kalpas Indestructible Demonic Heart Immortal Art, worthy of being an Immortal Realm cultivation technique personally chosen by King Xuan Tian for Mo Rubing. It is indeed extraordinary!" Li Fan couldn't help but praise as he witnessed Mo Rubing's charge through the formation. Having repelled the sealing needles, the last remaining defense left by the Sky Physician stood before Mo Rubing. And Li Fan, having successfully completed his formation, had already sensed the Sky Physician's aura not far away. "No matter how strong you are in the Star Sea, you must pass through my [Bewildering, Xuanhuang Sentient Beings] Great Array!" Fierce light erupted in Li Fan's eyes. Looking at the white-haired figure not far away, Li Fan seemed to recall the scene when he first encountered this peerless powerhouse from the Heavenly Law Realm. Origin Pure Essence was continuously extracted, and the Ultimate Dissolution Disc operated at its peak. During the hundred reincarnations, all knowledge gathered about the Heavenly Law Realm flashed through his mind. "Let you taste the wonderful world, tailor-made for you!" "Formation, activate!" With Li Fan's roar, an invisible wave instantly enveloped the fleeing Sky Physician. A flicker of surprise crossed his face. Then, the Sky Physician's vision went black, and he lost consciousness. When he awoke again, he was momentarily disoriented. Then, a voice of pure innocence awakened him. "Venerable! Venerable!" The Sky Physician looked towards the source of the voice. It was an adorable young girl, appearing no more than ten years old, yet already at the Nascent Soul cultivation stage. "Su Xiaomei." Information about this girl instantly appeared in the Sky Physician's mind. "Two worlds have merged, and two Heavenly Dao consciousnesses are attached to the mother and daughter respectively." "She possesses exceptional talent, naturally free from the Immortal-Mortal Barrier, a perfect constitution that countless beings dream of." "Immortal-Mortal Barrier?" The Sky Physician suddenly felt a sense of dissonance. However, after a brief dizziness, he remembered what had happened over the past ten thousand years. In the great battle for survival between the Heavenly Law Realm and the Xuanhuang Realm back then, the Heavenly Law Realm had fortunately emerged victorious. The Heavenly Law Realm successfully devoured the Xuanhuang Realm, obtaining the resources of an entire cultivation world, thus temporarily distancing itself from the Immortal Ruins. However, the cost was immense. The Venerables of the Heavenly Law Realm, except for him, Tianjue, Tianyin, Tianyu, and others, had all perished. The cultivators of the Xuanhuang Realm, in their final moments of despair, used the Xuanhuang Realm itself as a sacrifice, launching a fatal blow. The Immortal-Mortal Barrier, the impossibility of cultivating both Law and Immortal techniques simultaneously, and other Heavenly laws, were quietly implanted into the Xuanhuang Realm like poisons. Even the fundamental principles of cultivation for cultivators had subtly changed. And he, having been severely injured and fallen unconscious, failed to notice in time. By the time he awoke from his slumber, the Heavenly Law Realm had undergone earth-shattering changes. Because of the inability to cultivate both Law and Immortal techniques simultaneously, cultivators began to kill each other. After the great war, the already depleted Heavenly Law Realm was on the verge of losing its inheritance. Fortunately, after a period of turmoil, the surviving cultivators eventually had enough cultivation techniques to practice. The killing stopped, but the cultivators lost their trust in each other, surviving guardedly and isolated on a wasteland. Meanwhile, the surviving cultivators in the Star Sea discovered this remnant haven of the Heavenly Law Realm. Their original homes had been destroyed in the Star Sea calamity, so they settled here. Over the past ten thousand years, the Star Sea itself had been in flux. The suction of the Immortal Ruins was constantly drawing everything in the Star Sea. The Heavenly Law Realm, which had miraculously escaped back then, now served as the last sanctuary in the Star Sea, inevitably approaching the edge of the Immortal Ruins, teetering on the brink of complete destruction. When the Sky Physician awoke, he saw such a scene. Though profoundly shocked, he immediately took remedial measures. Through various methods, he finally persuaded several Longevity Realm powerhouses on the Heavenly Law Realm to temporarily form a loose alliance. They gathered the cultivators of the Heavenly Law Realm and supported mortal cultivation. The Heavenly Law Realm slowly regained vitality, but these Longevity Realm powerhouses each had their own ambitions. Facing the impending disaster of the Heavenly Law Realm, they were all contemplating escape. And it was the Sky Physician who was tasked with saving such a Heavenly Law Realm.

Chapter 1364: Great Venerable of All Laws

Under normal circumstances, rashly implanting fragments of other worlds, even if they were already destroyed, into the Heavenly Law Realm would inevitably cause the Heavenly Law Realm's Heavenly Dao to resist and reject the foreign object.

This was known as a rejection reaction.

However, now, the world fragment that the Heavenly Physician was stitching had already absorbed the remnants of the five Integration stage cultivators. The power of the World's Essence within these Integration stage cultivators originated from the Heavenly Law Realm itself.

Therefore, the degree of rejection during the fusion process was extremely low.

The Heavenly Law Realm smoothly completed the assimilation of the fragment.

Sensing a trace of life force slowly flowing from this world fragment into the Heavenly Law Realm, the Heavenly Physician couldn't help but let out a sigh of relief.

"It was worth the arduous journey."

After observing quietly for a period, perhaps because the Heavenly Law Realm had been in a state of hunger for a long time without sustenance, this fragment seemed to be particularly effective.

It not only replenished the energy but also stimulated the life force of the Heavenly Law Realm, which had been suppressed by the cultivators' endless greed.

"In the future, if I need to feed it again, I won't need to go through such trouble. I can directly connect to the residual power of this first fragment."

"However, it will take about two years for the Heavenly Law Realm to fully digest this world fragment..."

Thinking of this, the Heavenly Physician frowned slightly.

Although he possessed the power to travel rapidly through the Star Sea and largely disregard all dangers along the way,

The Star Sea was too vast. A round trip would take more than a year.

And according to his estimates, it would take about two years for the Heavenly Law Realm to digest this world fragment.

"At this rate, there's no extra time for other matters. I have too much on my plate..."

The Heavenly Physician sighed slightly, feeling a sense of being stretched too thin.

Although he had nurtured some promising individuals over the years, they were still far from being able to handle major responsibilities.

This made him miss his old comrades who had fought alongside him.

One figure after another flashed through the Heavenly Physician's mind, and suddenly, he paused abruptly at one of them.

"Heavenly Demon..." The Heavenly Physician's expression also became somewhat subtle.

Before the great battle between the two realms, the Heavenly Demon had already wandered beyond the heavens. Even during the most intense and brutal phase of the battle, the Heavenly Demon had not returned.

However, the Heavenly Physician could vaguely sense that the Heavenly Demon had not perished.

Instead, it still existed somewhere in the Star Sea.

Originally, the Heavenly Physician had not intended to contact this most unique existence among the Heavenly Law Realm's Venerables.

The Venerables were born from the sentient beings of the Heavenly Law Realm, resonating with and comprehending the Heavenly Law's constant principles.

The Heavenly Demon was the sole exception.

Like a dissonant note in a grand symphony, the Heavenly Demon was independently formed from the Heavenly Law Realm's Heavenly Law related to "Inner Demons." It was the very embodiment of Inner Demon Heavenly Dao.

He had communicated with other Venerables, but not much.

Born from the Heavenly Law Realm, but from the moment of its birth, it had effectively separated itself from its maternal source, the Heavenly Law Realm.

He was not concerned with the various matters of the Heavenly Law Realm.

He only sought to advance further, pursuing the illusory realm of "Supreme."

Remaining in the Heavenly Law Realm would inevitably prevent him from transcending the mortal realm, so the Heavenly Demon had resolutely departed.

Even when the Heavenly Law Realm was on the verge of destruction, the Heavenly Demon did not appear to help. It could be said that he had no remaining ties to the Heavenly Law Realm.

"I wonder if the Heavenly Demon has touched the threshold of the Supreme realm yet."

The Heavenly Physician's expression became listless. After pondering for a long time, he finally decided to search for the Heavenly Demon's whereabouts in the Star Sea.

Looking up at the sky, his figure transformed into a wisp of breeze, merging into the world of the Heavenly Law.

The constant principles roared, and the laws operated like an incredibly precise machine, running day and night.

Although the Heavenly Demon had severed its connection with the Heavenly Law's constant principles, it was still born from this world.

The Heavenly Physician, as the Great Venerable of All Laws, currently replacing the Heavenly Dao, was sensing the distant Star Sea.

After half a day, he finally detected the approximate location of the Heavenly Demon.

It turned out to be at the edge of the Star Sea, near the continuous Great Wall of Remaining Realms!

The Heavenly Physician's mind trembled, pondering the reason for the Heavenly Demon's presence there.

Without rushing to depart, before setting off, the Heavenly Physician invited the current six Longevity Heavenly Venerables of the Heavenly Law Realm.

To discuss the future of the Heavenly Law Realm.

Although they were all mere projections and not their true selves, this did not hinder their communication.

"We will all follow the Great Venerable's lead. After all, the Heavenly Law Realm is our shared home. If it truly falls into the Immortal Ruins... there will be no place for us in this vast Star Sea." The first to speak was a scholarly-looking middle-aged man.

He achieved his Dao at the end of the cultivation wasteland. Sensing that cultivators in the world were suspicious and afraid to trust anyone after years of mutual killing, he reversed the principles of heaven and earth, causing lies to cease to exist in the world. People revered him as the "True Speech Heavenly Venerable."

"Hehehe..." Before the True Speech Heavenly Venerable could finish speaking, a sinister laugh was heard.

"What does the survival of the Heavenly Law Realm have to do with me? I wish it would fall into the Immortal Ruins sooner!"

The Heavenly Physician looked at the figure hidden beneath the black hood of the opponent, and a killing intent flashed undisguisedly in his eyes.

If there was any Venerable whom the Heavenly Physician wished to eliminate, it would be this "Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable."

This person was initially a cultivator who had achieved great success in medicine. He comprehended the process of the Heavenly Law devouring the Xuanhuang Realm and used this as a mechanism for reversal.

This caused the Heavenly Law Realm's Great Dao to spontaneously generate resistance during the devouring of other worlds.

The Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable, therefore, achieved the Longevity fruit.

If not for this person's obstruction through reversal, the Heavenly Law Realm would have long ago completely devoured and assimilated the Xuanhuang Realm.

And now, even implanting world fragments into the Heavenly Law Realm would not take so much time.

The Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable, however, was not afraid of the Heavenly Physician and continued to speak sarcastically, "When the Heavenly Law falls into the Immortal Ruins, it will undoubtedly be torn to shreds. At that time, it will be the moment for my Great Dao to achieve consummation! Of course, I welcome this!"

All the Heavenly Venerables cast sideways glances at him.

Only the "Unified Heart Heavenly Venerable," Zhao Ruoxi, spoke with a hint of grievance and infatuation: "It seems Brother Li dislikes me and wishes to escape from my side."

As she spoke, it seemed as if shimmering tears dripped from her face.

The Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable's voice abruptly stopped, and he instinctively moved slightly away from the Unified Heart Heavenly Venerable, filled with apprehension.

The Heavenly Physician snorted coldly and solemnly stated: "I will not force any of you to contribute. But if anyone obstructs this..."

"Even if it means damaging the Heavenly Law's constant principles, I will surely root them out!"

"Do not say you were not warned!"

The words of the Heavenly Physician, the Great Venerable of All Laws, carried considerable power.

Under this warning, even the previously arrogant Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable dared not openly object and could only nod in agreement.

The Reverse Law Heavenly Venerable, while reversing the principles of heaven and earth, also became a part of the Heavenly Law's constant principles.

As long as heaven and earth exist, the Heavenly Venerable will not die.

Thus, the name "Longevity."

But longevity did not mean immortality.

As long as one forcibly extracted and destroyed the principles represented by the Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable from the Heavenly Law Realm.

One could achieve the killing of a Longevity Heavenly Venerable.

However, to do this required an extremely profound understanding and mastery of the principles of heaven and earth, like the Heavenly Physician, the Great Venerable of All Laws.

Secondly...

Even if it were possible, during the process of extracting the principles of heaven and earth, it would inevitably cause some impact on other constant principles of heaven and earth.

The Heavenly Law Realm, already extremely weak, could no longer withstand such a setback.

This was the reason why the Heavenly Physician had hesitated to act until now.

"However, after I complete several rounds of feeding and strengthen the Heavenly Law Realm's vitality, I should be able to deal with these parasites." The Heavenly Physician looked at the Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable, suppressing his killing intent for the time being.

"The other day, I ventured out of the Heavenly Law Realm to explore the Immortal Ruins. Vaguely, I saw a seated figure within..."

Just as the situation in the field was quiet and at a stalemate, a voice suddenly rang out, shocking everyone.

It was the "Achieved Dao Heavenly Venerable," Su Bai.

This person felt that all mortals were afflicted by the Immortal-Mortal miasma and should not easily cultivate or achieve Dao.

Therefore, he reversed this principle, bearing the suffering of the Immortal-Mortal miasma in place of all sentient beings. Mortals only needed to chant the name of the Achieved Dao Heavenly Venerable day and night, and with sincere devotion, the Immortal-Mortal miasma would dissipate.

Su Bai smiled slightly and continued, "I also glimpsed a character from the Immortal Ruins."

Using his finger as a brush, Su Bai instantly wrote the character "Hunger" in the air.

"I only saw it dimly, and could only restore it to this point," Su Bai shook his head, somewhat regretfully.

Even with Su Bai's statement, the fluctuations of power emanating from the character in the air demonstrated the terrifying nature of that True Immortal incantation.

"I believe this character is the culprit behind the fall of all things into the Immortal Ruins."

"True Immortal power naturally requires a True Immortal to wield it."

"There are quite a few remnants of True Immortal power in the Star Sea. My suggestion is to study these powers and deduce their original True Immortal incantations, then counter True Immortal incantations with True Immortal incantations." Su Bai said earnestly.

This suggestion immediately caused all the Heavenly Venerables present to ponder seriously.

Even the Heavenly Physician frowned, considering the feasibility of this.

Su Bai added another explosive piece of information: "To be honest, over the years, I have secretly researched and made some progress. Your talents are even greater than mine. If we work together to research..."

"To control the Immortal Ruins with True Immortal incantations will be within reach!"

As he said this, Su Bai wrote another character.

However, compared to the one he saw in the Immortal Ruins, this one he comprehended himself was clearly weaker.

The Heavenly Physician looked at the other Venerables, who clearly showed signs of interest. He couldn't help but feel a sense of worry.

He was already aware of the power of True Immortal incantations.

These individuals were already difficult to deal with, and if they were to master True Immortal incantations...

Then, even if a conflict arose, the Heavenly Law Realm would be affected and reduced to ruins!

Thinking of this, the Heavenly Physician's mood became even more urgent.

Following the discussion, everyone reached a consensus.

The actions were divided into three factions.

First, to assist the Heavenly Physician in nourishing and feeding the Heavenly Law Realm, thereby strengthening its power.

Second, to comprehend True Immortal incantations and resist the Immortal Ruins with external forces.

Third, to remain uninvolved and stand aloof.

After dismissing everyone, the Heavenly Physician, as the Great Venerable of the Heavenly Law Realm, couldn't help but feel somewhat weary.

With the six Longevity Heavenly Venerables holding down the fort, the Heavenly Law Realm would be safe for the time being.

Thus, the Heavenly Physician invigorated himself and immediately set off towards the Heavenly Demon's perceived location.

"If I can gain the Heavenly Demon's assistance, I can secretly possess these Longevity Heavenly Venerables without anyone knowing."

"This will minimize unnecessary casualties..."

With this thought, the Heavenly Physician's desire to find the Heavenly Demon intensified.

Traveling through the Star Sea, day after day.

Finally, he arrived at the edge of the Star Sea again.

Within his range of perception, after searching for a long time, the Heavenly Physician finally found the Heavenly Demon's location.

It was indeed alive.

However, it was frozen within a peculiar crystal!

"Crystal Wind?"

The Heavenly Physician did not approach to retrieve the Heavenly Demon directly, but merely observed from afar.

He recognized the peculiar power that had caused the Heavenly Demon to be frozen.

"Star Sea anomalies rarely appear anymore."

"It seems the Heavenly Demon encountered misfortune not long after leaving the Heavenly Law Realm..."

"Perhaps I misunderstood him, not that he refused to help, but that he was unable to."

Seeing his old friend frozen for ten thousand years in such a tragic state, the Heavenly Physician felt a surge of pity.

"It is said that when the Crystal Wind appears, it can freeze vast stretches of the Star Sea, making it one of the most terrifying Star Sea anomalies."

"Even a being of the Heavenly Demon's strength was unable to resist in the face of such immense power."

The Heavenly Physician's expression was grave: "After such a long time, the freezing power does not seem to have diminished much."

"The bone-chilling cold seems capable of freezing even the power of approaching True Immortals..."

But the Heavenly Physician was indeed worthy of his name.

After pondering on the spot for a long time, he finally found a solution.

Using hundreds of thousands of golden threads, he wrapped around the ice crystal.

Then, dragging it, he sped towards the invisible High Wall.

As he approached, he suddenly threw it out.

The ice crystal, which was flying at high speed, suddenly stopped in mid-air.

As if subjected to a violent impact, it trembled uncontrollably.

The Heavenly Physician's eyes suddenly lit up. He keenly sensed that a portion of the freezing power had been weakened by this impact.

"Only the High Wall can perhaps shake this desolate freezing power."

The Heavenly Physician lamented, and the golden threads shot out again.

The Heavenly Physician pulled the ice crystal, drawing a distance away from the High Wall.

Then, he repeated the process.

*Boom! Boom! Boom!*

With repeated collisions, the ice crystal became smaller and smaller.

When only a thin layer remained, the Heavenly Physician couldn't help but reduce the intensity of the impact.

After all, theoretically speaking, the Heavenly Demon was practically immortal.

But the High Wall was ultimately an unfathomable existence.

He had to be careful.

Otherwise, if this old friend did not die in the Star Sea catastrophe but died by his own hand...

The Heavenly Physician would surely feel extremely guilty.

Of course, the most important thing was losing a crucial ally.

The Heavenly Physician's control over power was almost meticulous.

Ultimately, through this somewhat peculiar method, he managed to awaken the Heavenly Demon.

A transparent, blurry figure stared intently at the Heavenly Physician.

It remained silent.

"Heavenly Demon..." The Heavenly Physician knew that even while frozen, the Demon had some awareness of the outside world, and he spoke first somewhat awkwardly.

The Heavenly Demon's figure suddenly disappeared.

A moment later, it had already appeared within the Heavenly Physician's sea of consciousness!

Chapter 1365: The Heavenly Demon Finally Resurrects

"Supreme Realm..."

"Is this the realm the Heavenly Physician now claims?"

Li Fan's thoughts raced, and he again set up formations around the Heavenly Physician to delay him, while looking towards Mo Rubing not far away.

His performance was almost identical to the Heavenly Physician's when he touched the High Wall within the [Xuanhuang Beings] Great Array.

There were no special auras emanating from him, but Mo Rubing seemed to have truly witnessed the scenes outside the High Wall, as if he had achieved enlightenment in an instant, tears streaming down his face.

Fortunately, Mo Rubing was gradually emerging from his state of enlightenment, and his eyes were regaining clarity.

"Let's go!"

With a flick of his hand, several golden threads flew out, instantly wrapping around Mo Rubing.

This divine ability was astonishingly similar to the one the Heavenly Physician had used within the Immortal Formation!

Pulling Mo Rubing to his side, the wooden sword phantom was unsheathed.

A moment later, the two had already left the range that the Heavenly Physician could sense.

Mo Rubing seemed to be still immersed in the afterglow of his enlightenment, his mind distantly adrift.

Li Fan did not disturb him for the time being, as he continued his journey back to the Xuanhuang Realm, while organizing the harvest he had gained from trapping the Heavenly Physician with the [Xuanhuang Beings] Great Array.

As the creator of this unprecedented immortal formation, Li Fan was not merely an observer.

The [Ephemeral, Xuanhuang Beings] Great Array was like an illusion, and its foundation as an immortal formation, infused with a trace of Li Fan's [Transformation Between True and False] profound meaning, made it less like a mere illusion experienced by the Heavenly Physician. Rather, it was more like a possibility that had truly existed in the past – a possibility of the Heavenly Law Realm defeating the Xuanhuang Realm.

However, this possibility only existed under the premise of the Immortal Formation's maintenance.

Once the Immortal Formation was broken by the Heavenly Physician, everything would vanish.

All beings within the Great Array, except for the Heavenly Physician, merged into a trace of Li Fan's will.

This included Su Bai, Reverse Fusion, and so on.

Even the so-called Heavenly Law Realm, Heavenly Demon, and High Wall were all composed of Li Fan's mixed intent.

Therefore, Li Fan could experience the Heavenly Physician's various methods from an extremely close perspective.

He could even sense the Heavenly Physician's thoughts and emotional fluctuations.

This was the terrifying power of Immortal Formations!

It was important to note that the Heavenly Physician had taught Li Fan the [Heavenly Physician Immortal Scripture] and the [Record of Mending Heaven], and could be considered Li Fan's semi-teacher.

Li Fan was well aware of all the experiences the Heavenly Physician had gone through.

Whether it was theoretical foundations or the materialization of divine abilities, after fully analyzing them, it was not difficult to replicate them.

For the current Li Fan.

It was not difficult!

Even more so, with the integration of the transcendent [Transformation Between True and False], the myriad golden threads wielded by Li Fan were even more impressive than the original.

He saw the myriad golden threads that seemed to bind Mo Rubing gradually disappear.

In reality, they had been subtly implanted into Mo Rubing's body.

However, they were currently in the "false" state, hidden, reserved for future use.

Not only Mo Rubing was unaware of this, but perhaps no one in the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea could detect this seemingly insignificant yet extraordinary technique of Li Fan.

When Li Fan needed it, the "false becoming true" transformation would be suddenly activated, and the myriad golden threads would transform from incorporeal to corporeal, erupting within Mo Rubing's body in an instant.

"These golden threads, although externally appearing as golden threads, are in reality insights into the principles of heaven and earth, and the principles of the Great Dao."

"Although my current strength is still slightly inferior to the Heavenly Physician's, in terms of comprehension in this area, I am by no means inferior to the Heavenly Physician!"

In addition to this golden thread divine ability, Li Fan also learned the Heavenly Physician's method of sealing the Heavenly Demon.

The eighty-one golden needles, although the technique differed from the [Soul Sealing and Realm Replacement] previously displayed by the Heavenly Physician, were of the same origin.

Li Fan had already learned most of it.

With further study, it would not be difficult to decipher it.

Beyond these two, the Heavenly Physician's actions in saving the Heavenly Law Realm, as the Great Venerable of All Laws, also provided Li Fan with much inspiration.

Especially the final move, condensing all constant principles of law and freezing the world's operational power.

This gave Li Fan a nascent idea regarding the Heavenly Dao essence that would be harmonized in this lifetime.

"The Heavenly Physician is indeed an inexhaustible treasure trove. It's a pity that the same immortal formation can probably no longer trap him."

"I can still try again in the next life."

"Using the [Xuanhuang Beings] as eyes, extracting all of the Heavenly Physician's knowledge and foundation."

...

As they neared the Xuanhuang Realm, Mo Rubing finally completely regained consciousness.

He was initially stunned for a moment, then upon realizing his current situation, he immediately wanted to return to the High Wall.

Li Fan frowned and restrained him with myriad golden threads.

Mo Rubing instinctively tried to break free but failed, his expression changing. He hadn't expected Li Fan to have such a trump card.

"Brother Mo, calm down."

"You have already achieved enlightenment of the High Wall twice. If you still cannot escape its temptation, you will likely be unable to escape it forever and will be perpetually lost within it!"

Li Fan's icy words finally brought Mo Rubing back to his senses.

His struggling movements slowly ceased.

However, Li Fan did not remove the golden thread restraints.

"Do you still feel the 'loss forever'?" Li Fan asked sternly.

With Li Fan's comprehension, he had yet to gain any insight from that "flaw" in the High Wall. His current words were entirely based on the Heavenly Physician's enlightenment of the High Wall's flaw within the Immortal Formation.

Mo Rubing's expression became somewhat subtle: "Loss forever. That phrase is truly fitting."

He cupped his hands, expressing his gratitude for Li Fan's previous intervention, then sighed deeply: "Thanks to Daoist brother, I can now fully glimpse the secret of the High Wall's flaw."

"However, all that I have comprehended..."

Mo Rubing paused for a long time before slowly saying, "Is not something that I, at my current level, can see."

"Hmm?" Li Fan raised his eyebrows.

"I know it sounds convoluted and even somewhat incredible, but that is precisely the truth."

"That is an enlightenment that does not exist within the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. Only by using the High Wall as a medium can we know and perceive it."

"And after leaving the High Wall, even if I have 'remembered' and 'comprehended,' I ultimately cannot manifest this non-existent thing..." Mo Rubing's expression was somewhat dazed, and he explained to Li Fan what he had encountered, word by word, with great difficulty.

Li Fan could somewhat understand Mo Rubing's explanation.

It was like if Li Fan tried to explain the [Transformation Between True and False] to Mo Rubing. Without possessing [Returning to True], no matter how hard Mo Rubing tried, he could not grasp or comprehend even a fraction of it.

He would simply regard Li Fan as a nonsensical liar.

Because, in Mo Rubing's perception, the so-called [Transformation Between True and False] simply did not exist.

"Touching the High Wall allows me to recall this enlightenment, but after leaving the High Wall, all the enlightenment is lost..."

"This is not like the moon in the mirror or the flower in the water, completely useless. It's even worse, as at least the flower and moon can be seen." Li Fan deliberately expressed extreme disappointment.

Mo Rubing pondered for a moment and then slightly shook his head: "That's not entirely true. Even if I cannot retain the enlightenment, these two times of meditation have allowed me to translate the form of the High Wall's existence into something I can understand."

As he spoke, Mo Rubing lightly tapped his index finger, drawing a circle in the air before Li Fan.

It enveloped Li Fan.

In Li Fan's field of vision, Mo Rubing suddenly disappeared. Even the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea vanished from his observation range.

Furthermore, his divine sense and the golden needle traces he had left behind all became ineffective!

It was as if walls had been erected on all four sides of him, surrounding him completely, blocking his sight and senses.

"Interesting."

"A miniature High Wall."

However, Mo Rubing's wall was clearly incomparable to the High Wall that encircled the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

Without even needing to use the [Nine Heavens Descending Dust Finger].

With a slight ascent and elevation, Li Fan casually took a step and crossed this obstacle!

Mo Rubing remained in his original position, not surprised that Li Fan had escaped so easily.

"My level of enlightenment is still insufficient."

"If you give me more time, I'm afraid it wouldn't be so easy for you to escape." Mo Rubing said slowly.

Li Fan frowned and said, "Brother Mo, your divine ability seems to be missing some crucial elements compared to the invisible High Wall..."

"Precisely because of this lack, your divine ability's power is greatly reduced. If you could analyze this missing element, you could probably achieve the effect of 'drawing a cage and trapping yourself' at will!"

Upon hearing this, a hint of unwillingness and longing flashed in Mo Rubing's eyes.

Being so easily stirred emotionally was almost impossible for Mo Rubing, who cultivated the [Myriad Tribulations Indestructible Demonic Heart Immortal Art]. The current situation could only mean that the secret of the High Wall's flaw had thoroughly shaken his mental foundation.

"I possess [Returning to True], so I have no need to worry about the 'loss forever' characteristic. However, I still haven't gained anything from that unfathomable entity. Is the gap in comprehension really that large? It seems I will have to return and continue using the myriad beings of the small world to help me comprehend the Dao. Although there may not be much time left in this life." Li Fan mused inwardly.

Next, Li Fan inquired about Mo Rubing's future plans.

"Are you still going to search for King Xuan Tian's whereabouts in the remaining areas of the Star Sea Crossing Formation?"

"During the time you were enlightening yourself at the High Wall, I have searched the Xuanhuang Realm once more. Unlike the Sky Beast's Eye and Spirit Gathering Ascension, the other parts of the Star Sea Crossing Formation appear to be severely damaged. There are likely no conditions for King Xuan Tian to conceal himself..." Li Fan said slowly.

Mo Rubing looked at the Xuanhuang Realm, not far away.

When King Xuan Tian was mentioned again, the wavering expression on his face gradually faded, returning to that of the inscrutable Twelve Law Kings of the Xuan Tian Sect.

Perhaps it was due to Li Fan's selfless obstruction earlier that trust was built.

Mo Rubing hesitated for a moment, then slowly said, "I still want to go to one last place."

"However, ten thousand years have passed, and the Xuanhuang Realm has undergone earth-shattering changes. It's difficult to distinguish the location immediately..."

"That's easy."

In an instant, a comparative map of the Xuanhuang Realm's past and present appeared before Mo Rubing.

"Here."

Mo Rubing carefully identified the location and finally chose a spot.

Li Fan's expression immediately became somewhat subtle.

"What's wrong?" Mo Rubing naturally noticed the change in Li Fan's expression.

Li Fan shook his head slightly: "You'll know when you go."

With a flash of the wooden sword phantom, Li Fan brought Mo Rubing to their destination.

It was precisely the small mountain where the fishing pond was located, and the Taoist temple!

In this lifetime, Li Fan had not utilized the fishing pond.

He had only forcibly relocated Zhong Shen Tong and the disciple Liu Li from the temple.

"This place was Brother Xuanyuan's homeland."

"It was also his final place of ascension."

"I didn't expect it to become so desolate now."

Mo Rubing slowly walked into the Taoist temple, observing carefully, and lamented.

"It's actually the last ascension site in the Xuanhuang Realm?" Li Fan was slightly surprised.

"Yes. Brother Xuanyuan was extremely sentimental about this place back then. Whenever he couldn't be found elsewhere, he could always be found here. I don't know what remarkable things happened here or what he experienced." Mo Rubing walked slowly, as if searching for King Xuan Tian's aura.

He walked all the way to the back courtyard of the Taoist temple.

And saw that ordinary small pond, Mo Rubing's pupils suddenly contracted sharply.

Then he rushed forward rapidly.

"This..."

"After ten thousand years, this place hasn't changed at all?!" Mo Rubing was shocked but also keenly sensed the extraordinary nature of this place.

"You looked strange just now, that's why? Is it this place?"

Mo Rubing suddenly turned his head and asked.

Li Fan nodded slightly: "This small pond, I was unable to destroy it. Hence, I realized the peculiarity of this place."

"However, I searched it thoroughly but could never find anything strange..."

Mo Rubing heard this and looked at the fishing pond again.

"The surrounding mountains have all changed drastically, yet only this pond water remains unchanged. There must be something hidden here..."

"Strange, but Brother Xuanyuan never mentioned any secrets here back then."

Having found the only clue, Mo Rubing was unwilling to let it go.

He tried all sorts of methods, even personally diving into the water.

But in the end, he gained nothing.

It was as if this was truly just an ordinary small pond.

The secret was right before his eyes, yet he could not perceive it.

Mo Rubing's expression became somewhat gloomy.

"This is King Xuan Tian's homeland? What kind of person was King Xuan Tian before his ascension?" Li Fan seized the opportunity to ask.

"Brother Xuanyuan's early life was truly ordinary. So ordinary that he passed before me many times, and I never even lowered my head to look at him."

"Back then, I was a direct descendant of the Nine Refinements Temple, while he was merely a cultivator at the Qi Refining stage."

"However, no one knew that hidden beneath Brother Xuanyuan's unassuming appearance was an extraordinary talent. He rose to prominence overnight, not relying on sect resources, but solely on himself, becoming the foremost ascension expert of the Xuanhuang Realm at that time, and the last one..."

Mo Rubing's expression was filled with infinite nostalgia.

And Li Fan, listening to these words, fell into deep thought.

Li Fan was certainly aware of the existence of the fishing pond.

But he had no idea when the fishing pond had existed in the Xuanhuang Realm.

After all, the fishing pond was implicitly a creation of an anonymous True Immortal, completely transcending the Xuanhuang Realm.

Even in the historical records documenting the Xuanhuang Realm's history, there was no mention of the fishing pond.

All along, Li Fan had subconsciously believed that the fishing pond suddenly appeared in the Xuanhuang Realm after the Star Sea catastrophe and the destruction of various realms.

But now it seemed...

"Could it be that King Xuan Tian's meteoric rise was due to this supreme treasure, the fishing pond?"

A thought couldn't help but arise in Li Fan's mind.

Chapter 1366: The Heavenly Doctor's Secret Heart

The Heavenly Physician, with his pale beard and hair, moved as if uninfluenced by any breeze. His wrinkled face, etched with countless lines, flickered through a myriad of different human visages. For reasons unknown, the Heavenly Demon, frozen for ten thousand years, sought to possess the Heavenly Physician the moment it was freed.

However, as the Great Venerable of All Laws, the Heavenly Physician's current form was beyond the capabilities of the weakened Heavenly Demon. With his left hand, a long golden needle was inserted straight into the crown of his head. The shifting faces on his countenance instantly returned to normal, and the ethereal figure of the Heavenly Demon was forced out.

Simultaneously, countless golden threads intricately wove an interconnected net, constructing a world akin to reality. The Heavenly Demon, just expelled from the Heavenly Physician's body, found itself unable to control its form, and was slowly drawn into this golden web. The Heavenly Demon let out waves of low roars, finally completely subdued by the Heavenly Physician.

Yet, the Heavenly Physician showed no joy on his face. "Completely unable to communicate? Has it lost all sentience after being frozen for so long?" After a thorough investigation, his tightly furrowed brows relaxed. "That's for the best. The Heavenly Demon's essence of corrupting the human heart still remains, which will make it more convenient for me to act."

He let out a sigh, lamenting the passing of an old acquaintance. Subsequently, the Heavenly Physician quickly returned to his task, dragging the sealed Heavenly Demon and another suitable world fragment back to the Heavenly Law Realm. Naturally, he did not waste the over a year of travel time. While propelling himself forward at great speed, countless tentacle-like golden threads danced around his body, clearly sensing the remnants of True Immortal power encountered along the way. He had indeed been swayed by the suggestion made by the Dao Attainment Heavenly Venerable, Su Bai.

"Indeed, if used correctly, the power unleashed by these True Immortal scripts might be enough to shake the Immortal Ruins..." With this thought, the Heavenly Physician used his hand as a brush, conjuring several characters in the air. Although they were mere phantoms, the moment they appeared, a palpable power reverberated around them. The intensity of this vibration continued to increase as the Heavenly Physician approached the Heavenly Law Realm. This was the result of less than a year of the Heavenly Physician's comprehension, a testament to his terrifying talent.

As the Heavenly Law Realm came into view, the Heavenly Physician casually dismissed the True Immortal scripts he had comprehended. Then, he fully unleashed his aura, making a grand show of feeding the Heavenly Law Realm with world fragments. This attracted the attention of most of the Longevity Realm cultivators within the Heavenly Law Realm. Meanwhile, he, in his true form, silently split off a phantom and, along with the sealed Heavenly Demon, headed towards the direction of the [Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable].

It was unknown whether this Heavenly Venerable was absolutely confident in his own strength or simply too foolish. While other Longevity Realm cultivators in the Heavenly Law Realm had concealed their auras and floated about unpredictably, this Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable was unhidden and unrestrained. Thus, the Heavenly Physician easily infiltrated his vicinity. At this moment, he appeared to be in secluded cultivation, awakened by the Heavenly Physician's actions of feeding the Heavenly Law Realm. He looked up at the sky, a trace of hatred flashing in his eyes.

In front of the Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable, the phantom of the Heavenly Law Realm caught the Heavenly Physician's attention. Several locations were marked within the phantom, yet they were beyond the perception of the Great Venerable of All Laws. The Heavenly Physician's heart tensed. After careful observation, he suddenly understood. "So, these are remnants of the Xuanhuang Realm!" "This Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable, by achieving his Dao, has inadvertently helped the Xuanhuang Realm to eke out an existence, and thus, the residual Heavenly Dao consciousness of the Xuanhuang Realm has found him!" "Seeking death!" A killing intent surged within the Heavenly Physician. The Heavenly Law Realm was his homeland, carrying the past of himself and many loved ones. It could never be coveted or damaged by anyone!

"Heavenly Law, Constant Principles, Condense!" The Heavenly Physician no longer hesitated, unleashing his ultimate killing move. Within the Heavenly Law Realm, wind ceased, rain stopped, and all things, even the passage of heaven and earth, fell into stillness. The Longevity Realm cultivators, as embodiments of the principles of heaven and earth, were no exception! The Heavenly Physician appeared behind the Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable and slowly reached out, placing his hand on his opponent's head. In a sudden burst of ethereal light, a portion of the subdued Heavenly Demon was infused into the Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable!

On the Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable's face, similar to the Heavenly Physician's earlier state, countless countenances flashed and shifted. It seemed that halting the operation of the entire Heavenly Law Realm's constant principles was an immensely taxing feat even for the Heavenly Physician. After successfully implanting a portion of the Heavenly Demon into the Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable, the Heavenly Physician immediately restored the world's normal operation. In that brief moment, the Heavenly Physician's hair turned even whiter, and the light in his eyes gradually became somewhat clouded. As the Great Venerable of All Laws of the Heavenly Law Realm, the abnormalities on his person were also reflected in the Heavenly Law Realm. Thousands of miles turned barren, glaciers melted, and countless living beings withered and died. It seemed the entire world, after that brief "pause," had suffered a grave injury.

However, looking at the once contorted Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable, his shifting countenance finally calmed. Faced with the Heavenly Physician, the attacker, he displayed no hatred, even nodding in greeting. The Heavenly Physician finally exhaled a long sigh of relief. Because of the return of the Heavenly Demon's Dao and the nourishment of the newly added world fragment, the Heavenly Law Realm's lost vitality was quickly replenished.

The Heavenly Physician's successful possession of the Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable via the Heavenly Demon went undetected by anyone in the Heavenly Law Realm. To exercise caution, the Heavenly Physician inserted eighty-one golden needles into the Reverse Fusion Heavenly Venerable's body, completely severing the possibility of the Reverse Fusion's original consciousness awakening and the Heavenly Demon spiraling out of control. With one successful attempt, there would be others. Over the next thirty years, the Heavenly Physician used this method to gradually gain control over all the Longevity Realm cultivators in the Heavenly Law Realm, except for the [Unified Heart Heavenly Venerable].

As for Zhao Ruoxi, the Unified Heart Heavenly Venerable, her form had manifested in countless ways, permeating the entire Heavenly Law Realm. Cleaning and possessing her presented significant difficulties, and since she posed no immediate threat, the Heavenly Physician decided to leave her for the time being. After consolidating the Heavenly Law Realm under his sole control, the Heavenly Physician could finally dedicate himself entirely to his plan of saving the Heavenly Law Realm. Time flowed swiftly, and a century passed in the blink of an eye. The Heavenly Law Realm had devoured nearly a hundred world fragments meticulously selected by the Heavenly Physician, its overall size more than doubling. The continuous influx of vitality had allowed it to completely digest the Xuanhuang Realm. There were no longer any hidden dangers within the world.

The Heavenly Physician's strength also soared accordingly, faintly touching the limits of what this star field could accommodate, on the verge of breaking through yet facing an impassable barrier. This crucial step, however, remained elusive, causing even the Heavenly Physician's normally steadfast heart to feel a trace of vexation and despair. "Is this the so-called Supreme Realm?" the Heavenly Physician mused silently for a long time. After a prolonged silence, he let out a cold laugh. "Supreme..." "Alas, it is merely self-consolation for those unable to achieve immortality!" "The immortal path cannot be trodden, the immortal path cannot be trodden..." Feeling the constraints of being completely bound by some Great Dao law, the Heavenly Physician's mind suddenly recalled his experiences contemplating the High Wall over the years. "There seems to be some similarity between these two..." "Yet, there is an essential difference." With this thought, the Heavenly Physician's vision suddenly ascended rapidly. The vast Heavenly Law Realm appeared like a trinket in his palm. The High Wall on the frontier of the star sea was no longer distant, but within reach. With a single step, the Heavenly Physician vanished from his original position and reappeared a considerable distance forward in the miniature replica of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea!

This art of "shrinking the ground into an inch" was one of the Heavenly Physician's insights gained over the past century. Constantly traversing the star sea, accompanied by the forces of the High Wall and Immortal Ruins, although his realm had not significantly changed, the Heavenly Physician's strength had grown to an astonishing degree. What previously took over a year to traverse the star sea now took less than two days. Moreover, the Heavenly Physician had a premonition that his speed could continue to increase with his growing understanding of the star sea's momentum. Perhaps in the future, he could cross the star sea in the blink of an eye!

Arriving at the High Wall, the Heavenly Physician skillfully unleashed thousands of golden threads, which flowed like mercury, attempting to contact and perceive the invisible High Wall. This was something the Heavenly Physician had done countless times over the years. Despite always yielding no results, he continued this seemingly futile endeavor, for he had a subtle premonition that he would eventually discover something within the High Wall. As if in response to his unwavering patience, one day, the thousands of lines, which had been sweeping out like a golden waterfall, suddenly halted! The Heavenly Physician's body trembled slightly, and the light in his now completely clouded eyes suddenly erupted with a brilliant gleam. It was as if a crack had appeared in the boundless ocean; all the lines surged into it like seawater.

"What a pity, it's not a crack." "Merely a flaw." "There are even traces of artificiality..." After carefully savoring the sensation, the Heavenly Physician felt a pang of regret. "Perhaps it was created by some immensely powerful cultivator in the star sea back then." As his perception deepened, the Heavenly Physician's distracting thoughts vanished. He focused his entire being on comprehending this flaw in the High Wall. If the previous hundred years of exploration had prevented him from truly seeing the High Wall's face, then through this flaw, the Heavenly Physician could finally glimpse the true High Wall! *Creak... creak...* Upon witnessing some unimaginable sight, two streams of clear tears flowed uncontrollably from the Heavenly Physician's eyes. And his body, that of a Supreme Realm expert, could not withstand the pressure of unknown forces and began to stoop inch by inch.

Far away in the Star Sea, the Heavenly Law Realm's heaven and earth let out resounding booms. Cracks, as if cut by invisible blades, spread across the celestial canopy. At this critical juncture, forced to choose between further enlightenment and the life-or-death survival of the Heavenly Law Realm, the Heavenly Physician ultimately chose the latter. He retreated violently, instinctively disengaging from his state of enlightenment. The anomalies in the Heavenly Law Realm vanished instantly. Touching the tear tracks on his cheeks, the Heavenly Physician's eyes held a trace of confusion. He was horrified to discover that everything he had just seen and comprehended had completely dissipated the moment he broke contact with the High Wall. Moreover, a premonition surged within him: to retain this memory, he would need to reconnect with the High Wall before the physical sensations completely faded, to continue inscribing. "But the Heavenly Law Realm can no longer bear it; it has reached its limit..." A rare hint of hesitation and struggle appeared in the Heavenly Physician's eyes. Ultimately... the Heavenly Physician let out a long sigh. He did not approach the High Wall, allowing the profound enlightenment to completely fade. *Pfft!* Having gone against his own heart's desire for the Dao, the Heavenly Physician's spiritual heart suffered a grievous injury, and he spat out a mouthful of blood. He continuously inserted golden needles into important acupoints on his body. However, this could not suppress the injury originating from his soul. He spat out several more mouthfuls of blood. "A physician cannot heal himself..." Standing in the void for more than half a month, the Heavenly Physician finally recovered. He reluctantly wished to explore the flaw in the High Wall again, but ultimately, he had lost it forever. The High Wall now appeared no different than it did before. The Heavenly Physician stood rooted to the spot, his heart filled with a sense of loss. He knew he had missed his chance to uncover the secrets of the High Wall forever. However, the Heavenly Physician was still the Heavenly Physician. After another ten-odd days, he rallied his spirits. "My desire to prove myself as a True Immortal was only to save the Heavenly Law Realm." "If, for the sake of enlightenment, I were to allow the Heavenly Law Realm to be destroyed, that would never be my wish." "Moreover..." "Even if I cannot glimpse the secrets of the High Wall, I can still harness its power." With a thought, the Heavenly Physician wove thousands of golden threads before him, forming a long wall. However, the moment it took shape, all the golden threads disintegrated, scattering into countless golden lights! "The flaw in the High Wall has left its mark upon me." "From this day forward, the High Wall will no longer be invisible to my eyes." A sliver of enlightenment dawned upon the Heavenly Physician. "Perhaps..." "I can construct a High Wall outside the Heavenly Law Realm to isolate it from the Immortal Ruins' suction!" Having achieved enlightenment at the High Wall, the Heavenly Physician's strength advanced further. Over the next century, he spent his time weaving countless golden threads, encircling the Heavenly Law Realm. Miraculously, he managed to wrap it like a chrysalis, slowly dragging it out from the periphery of the Immortal Ruins! Seeing that the Heavenly Law Realm was truly about to escape the clutches of danger, this act of snatching food from the tiger's mouth finally drew the attention of the True Immortal who was contemplating the Immortal Ruins. A colossal figure suddenly appeared above the Heavenly Law Realm. It looked down at the Heavenly Physician blocking its path, and the tightly wrapped golden cocoon. Its expression was indifferent. The pressure emanating from the True Immortal caused the Heavenly Law Realm, even within its golden cocoon, to tremble violently, its mountains and rivers fracturing. Yet, the Heavenly Physician, facing this True Immortal, felt no fear for some unknown reason. Instead, a sense of doubt arose. "This..." "Is this a True Immortal?" The True Immortal phantom slowly extended a hand, and infinite suction surged forth from it. The entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea seemed to be drawn towards the True Immortal's palm, even light itself. However, it was as if a sturdy stake had firmly anchored the Heavenly Physician in place, rendering him immobile. The Heavenly Physician, dragging the Heavenly Law Realm, flew like a kite in a fierce gale, tossed about but never severed from the connection. The doubt in the Heavenly Physician's eyes deepened. Standing within the True Immortal's might, without resisting, he suddenly closed his eyes, as if recalling something.

Outside the Great Xuan Universal Sentient Beings Formation, Li Fan watched the rapidly rotating formation teetering on the brink of collapse with a slight sigh. "The Heavenly Physician's abilities are indeed extraordinary. And the downgraded immortal array is not a true immortal array. Moreover, even a complete immortal array might not be able to simulate the true might of an Immortal Ruins True Immortal." Li Fan surmised that the Heavenly Physician discovering a flaw was within expectations. "It matters not; I have already gleaned enough secrets." Li Fan then shifted his gaze to Mo Rubing, who was not far away. His performance was almost identical to the Heavenly Physician's when he touched the High Wall within the [Xuanhuang Beings] Great Array. No special aura emanated from him, but Mo Rubing seemed to have truly witnessed scenes beyond the High Wall, as if he had experienced instant enlightenment, tears streaming down his face. Fortunately, Mo Rubing was gradually emerging from his enlightened state, his eyes regaining clarity. "Let's go!" With a flick of his hand, several golden threads flew out, instantly wrapping around Mo Rubing. This divine ability was astonishingly similar to the one the Heavenly Physician had used within the Immortal Formation! Pulling Mo Rubing to his side, the phantom of the wooden sword was unsheathed. Moments later, the two had already left the Heavenly Physician's range of perception. Mo Rubing seemed to remain immersed in the afterglow of his enlightenment, his mind drifting distantly. Li Fan did not disturb him for the time being, continuing his journey back to the Xuanhuang Realm while organizing the spoils gained from trapping the Heavenly Physician with the [Xuanhuang Beings] Great Array. As the creator of this unprecedented immortal formation, Li Fan was not merely an observer. The [Ephemeral, Xuanhuang Beings] Great Array was like an illusion, and its foundation as an immortal formation, infused with a trace of Li Fan's profound meaning of [Transformation Between True and False], made it less like a mere illusion experienced by the Heavenly Physician. Rather, it was more akin to a possibility that had truly existed in the past – a possibility of the Heavenly Law Realm defeating the Xuanhuang Realm. However, this possibility only existed under the premise of the Immortal Formation's maintenance. Once the Immortal Formation was broken by the Heavenly Physician, everything would vanish. All beings within the Great Array, except for the Heavenly Physician, merged into a trace of Li Fan's will. This included Su Bai, Reverse Fusion, and so on. Even the so-called Heavenly Law Realm, Heavenly Demon, and High Wall were all composed of Li Fan's mixed intent. Therefore, Li Fan could experience the Heavenly Physician's various methods from an extremely close perspective. He could even sense the Heavenly Physician's thoughts and emotional fluctuations. This was the terrifying power of Immortal Formations! It was important to note that the Heavenly Physician had taught Li Fan the [Heavenly Physician Immortal Scripture] and the [Record of Mending Heaven], and could be considered Li Fan's semi-teacher. Li Fan was well aware of all the experiences the Heavenly Physician had gone through. Whether it was theoretical foundations or the materialization of divine abilities, after fully analyzing them, it was not difficult to replicate them. For the current Li Fan, it was not difficult! Even more so, with the integration of the transcendent [Transformation Between True and False], the myriad golden threads wielded by Li Fan were even more impressive than the original. He saw the myriad golden threads that seemed to bind Mo Rubing gradually disappear. In reality, they had been subtly implanted into Mo Rubing's body. However, they were currently in the "false" state, hidden, reserved for future use. Not only Mo Rubing was unaware of this, but perhaps no one in the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea could detect this seemingly insignificant yet extraordinary technique of Li Fan. When Li Fan needed it, the "false becoming true" transformation would be suddenly activated, and the myriad golden threads would transform from incorporeal to corporeal, erupting within Mo Rubing's body in an instant. "These golden threads, although externally appearing as golden threads, are in reality insights into the principles of heaven and earth, and the principles of the Great Dao." "Although my current strength is still slightly inferior to the Heavenly Physician's, in terms of comprehension in this area, I am by no means inferior to the Heavenly Physician!" In addition to this golden thread divine ability, Li Fan also learned the Heavenly Physician's method of sealing the Heavenly Demon. The eighty-one golden needles, although the technique differed from the [Soul Sealing and Realm Replacement] previously displayed by the Heavenly Physician, were of the same origin. Li Fan had already learned most of it. With further study, it would not be difficult to decipher it. Beyond these two, the Heavenly Physician's actions in saving the Heavenly Law Realm, as the Great Venerable of All Laws, also provided Li Fan with much inspiration. Especially the final move, condensing all constant principles of law and freezing the world's operational power. This gave Li Fan a nascent idea regarding the Heavenly Dao essence that would be harmonized in this lifetime. "The Heavenly Physician is indeed an inexhaustible treasure trove. It's a pity that the same immortal formation can probably no longer trap him." "I can still try again in the next life." "Using the [Xuanhuang Beings] as eyes, extracting all of the Heavenly Physician's knowledge and foundation." As they neared the Xuanhuang Realm, Mo Rubing finally completely regained consciousness. He was initially stunned for a moment, then upon realizing his current situation, he immediately wanted to return to the High Wall. Li Fan frowned and restrained him with myriad golden threads. Mo Rubing instinctively tried to break free but failed, his expression changing. He hadn't expected Li Fan to have such a trump card. "Brother Mo, calm down." "You have already achieved enlightenment of the High Wall twice. If you still cannot escape its temptation, you will likely be unable to escape it forever and will be perpetually lost within it!" Li Fan's icy words finally brought Mo Rubing back to his senses. His struggling movements slowly ceased. However, Li Fan did not remove the golden thread restraints. "Do you still feel the 'loss forever'?" Li Fan asked sternly. With Li Fan's comprehension, he had yet to gain any insight from that "flaw" in the High Wall. His current words were entirely based on the Heavenly Physician's enlightenment of the High Wall's flaw within the Immortal Formation. Mo Rubing's expression became somewhat subtle: "Loss forever. That phrase is truly fitting." He cupped his hands, expressing his gratitude for Li Fan's previous intervention, then sighed deeply: "Thanks to Daoist brother, I can now fully glimpse the secret of the High Wall's flaw." "However, all that I have comprehended..." Mo Rubing paused for a long time before slowly saying, "Is not something that I, at my current level, can see." "Hmm?" Li Fan raised his eyebrows. "I know it sounds convoluted and even somewhat incredible, but that is precisely the truth." "That is an enlightenment that does not exist within the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. Only by using the High Wall as a medium can we know and perceive it." "And after leaving the High Wall, even if I have 'remembered' and 'comprehended,' I ultimately cannot manifest this non-existent thing..." Mo Rubing's expression was somewhat dazed, and he explained to Li Fan what he had encountered, word by word, with great difficulty. Li Fan could somewhat understand Mo Rubing's explanation. It was like if Li Fan tried to explain the [Transformation Between True and False] to Mo Rubing. Without possessing [Returning to True], no matter how hard Mo Rubing tried, he could not grasp or comprehend even a fraction of it. He would simply regard Li Fan as a nonsensical liar. Because, in Mo Rubing's perception, the so-called [Transformation Between True and False] simply did not exist. "Touching the High Wall allows me to recall this enlightenment, but after leaving the High Wall, all the enlightenment is lost..." "This is not like the moon in the mirror or the flower in the water, completely useless. It's even worse, as at least the flower and moon can be seen." Li Fan deliberately expressed extreme disappointment. Mo Rubing pondered for a moment and then slightly shook his head: "That's not entirely true. Even if I cannot retain the enlightenment, these two times of meditation have allowed me to translate the form of the High Wall's existence into something I can understand." As he spoke, Mo Rubing lightly tapped his index finger, drawing a circle in the air before Li Fan. It enveloped Li Fan. In Li Fan's field of vision, Mo Rubing suddenly disappeared. Even the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea vanished from his observation range. Furthermore, his divine sense and the golden needle traces he had left behind all became ineffective! It was as if walls had been erected on all four sides of him, surrounding him completely, blocking his sight and senses. "Interesting." "A miniature High Wall." However, Mo Rubing's wall was clearly incomparable to the High Wall that encircled the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. Without even needing to use the [Nine Heavens Descending Dust Finger]. With a slight ascent and elevation, Li Fan casually took a step and crossed this obstacle! Mo Rubing remained in his original position, not surprised that Li Fan had escaped so easily. "My level of enlightenment is still insufficient." "If you give me more time, I'm afraid it wouldn't be so easy for you to escape." Mo Rubing said slowly. Li Fan frowned and said, "Brother Mo, your divine ability seems to be missing some crucial elements compared to the invisible High Wall..." "Precisely because of this lack, your divine ability's power is greatly reduced. If you could analyze this missing element, you could probably achieve the effect of 'drawing a cage and trapping yourself' at will!" Upon hearing this, a hint of unwillingness and longing flashed in Mo Rubing's eyes. Being so easily stirred emotionally was almost impossible for Mo Rubing, who cultivated the [Myriad Tribulations Indestructible Demonic Heart Immortal Art]. The current situation could only mean that the secret of the High Wall's flaw had thoroughly shaken his mental foundation. "I possess [Returning to True], so I have no need to worry about the 'loss forever' characteristic. However, I still haven't gained anything from that unfathomable entity. Is the gap in comprehension really that large? It seems I will have to return and continue using the myriad beings of the small world to help me comprehend the Dao. Although there may not be much time left in this life." Li Fan mused inwardly. Next, Li Fan inquired about Mo Rubing's future plans. "Are you still going to search for King Xuan Tian's whereabouts in the remaining areas of the Star Sea Crossing Formation?" "During the time you were enlightening yourself at the High Wall, I have searched the Xuanhuang Realm once more. Unlike the Sky Beast's Eye and Spirit Gathering Ascension, the other parts of the Star Sea Crossing Formation appear to be severely damaged. There are likely no conditions for King Xuan Tian to conceal himself..." Li Fan said slowly. Mo Rubing looked at the Xuanhuang Realm, not far away. When King Xuan Tian was mentioned again, the wavering expression on his face gradually faded, returning to that of the inscrutable Twelve Law Kings of the Xuan Tian Sect. Perhaps it was due to Li Fan's selfless obstruction earlier that trust was built. Mo Rubing hesitated for a moment, then slowly said, "I still want to go to one last place." "However, ten thousand years have passed, and the Xuanhuang Realm has undergone earth-shattering changes. It's difficult to distinguish the location immediately..." "That's easy." In an instant, a comparative map of the Xuanhuang Realm's past and present appeared before Mo Rubing. "Here." Mo Rubing carefully identified the location and finally chose a spot. Li Fan's expression immediately became somewhat subtle. "What's wrong?" Mo Rubing naturally noticed the change in Li Fan's expression. Li Fan shook his head slightly: "You'll know when you go." With a flash of the wooden sword phantom, Li Fan brought Mo Rubing to their destination. It was precisely the small mountain where the fishing pond was located, and the Taoist temple! In this lifetime, Li Fan had not utilized the fishing pond. He had only forcibly relocated Zhong Shen Tong and the disciple Liu Li from the temple. "This place was Brother Xuanyuan's homeland." "It was also his final place of ascension." "I didn't expect it to become so desolate now." Mo Rubing slowly walked into the Taoist temple, observing carefully, and lamented. "It's actually the last ascension site in the Xuanhuang Realm?" Li Fan was slightly surprised. "Yes. Brother Xuanyuan was extremely sentimental about this place back then. Whenever he couldn't be found elsewhere, he could always be found here. I don't know what remarkable things happened here or what he experienced." Mo Rubing walked slowly, as if searching for King Xuan Tian's aura. He walked all the way to the back courtyard of the Taoist temple. And saw that ordinary small pond, Mo Rubing's pupils suddenly contracted sharply. Then he rushed forward rapidly. "This..." "After ten thousand years, this place hasn't changed at all?!" Mo Rubing was shocked but also keenly sensed the extraordinary nature of this place. "You looked strange just now, that's why? Is it this place?" Mo Rubing suddenly turned his head and asked. Li Fan nodded slightly: "This small pond, I was unable to destroy it. Hence, I realized the peculiarity of this place." "However, I searched it thoroughly but could never find anything strange..." Mo Rubing heard this and looked at the fishing pond again. "The surrounding mountains have all changed drastically, yet only this pond water remains unchanged. There must be something hidden here..." "Strange, but Brother Xuanyuan never mentioned any secrets here back then." Having found the only clue, Mo Rubing was unwilling to let it go. He tried all sorts of methods, even personally diving into the water. But in the end, he gained nothing. It was as if this was truly just an ordinary small pond. The secret was right before his eyes, yet he could not perceive it. Mo Rubing's expression became somewhat gloomy. "This is King Xuan Tian's homeland? What kind of person was King Xuan Tian before his ascension?" Li Fan seized the opportunity to ask. "Brother Xuanyuan's early life was truly ordinary. So ordinary that he passed before me many times, and I never even lowered my head to look at him." "Back then, I was a direct descendant of the Nine Refinements Temple, while he was merely a cultivator at the Qi Refining stage." "However, no one knew that hidden beneath Brother Xuanyuan's unassuming appearance was an extraordinary talent. He rose to prominence overnight, not relying on sect resources, but solely on himself, becoming the foremost ascension expert of the Xuanhuang Realm at that time, and the last one..." Mo Rubing's expression was filled with infinite nostalgia. And Li Fan, listening to these words, fell into deep thought. Li Fan was certainly aware of the existence of the fishing pond. But he had no idea when the fishing pond had existed in the Xuanhuang Realm. After all, the fishing pond was implicitly a creation of an anonymous True Immortal, completely transcending the Xuanhuang Realm. Even in the historical records documenting the Xuanhuang Realm's history, there was no mention of the fishing pond. All along, Li Fan had subconsciously believed that the fishing pond suddenly appeared in the Xuanhuang Realm after the Star Sea catastrophe and the destruction of various realms. But now it seemed... "Could it be that King Xuan Tian's meteoric rise was due to this supreme treasure, the fishing pond?" A thought couldn't help but arise in Li Fan's mind.

Chapter 1367: The Former Residence of King Xuantian

“The Supreme Realm…”

“Is this the realm the Heavenly Physician now claims?”

Li Fan’s thoughts raced, and he again set up formations around the Heavenly Physician to delay him, while looking towards Mo Rubing not far away. His performance was almost identical to the Heavenly Physician's when he touched the High Wall within the [Xuanhuang Beings] Great Array. There were no special auras emanating from him, but Mo Rubing seemed to have truly witnessed scenes beyond the High Wall, as if he had experienced instant enlightenment, tears streaming down his face. Fortunately, Mo Rubing was gradually emerging from his enlightened state, his eyes regaining clarity.
