However, they were currently in the “false” state, hidden, reserved for future use. Not only Mo Rubing was unaware of this, but perhaps no one in the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea could detect this seemingly insignificant yet extraordinary technique of Li Fan. When Li Fan needed it, the “false becoming true” transformation would be suddenly activated, and the myriad golden threads would transform from incorporeal to corporeal, erupting within Mo Rubing’s body in an instant.

“These golden threads, although externally appearing as golden threads, are in reality insights into the principles of heaven and earth, and the principles of the Great Dao.”

“Although my current strength is still slightly inferior to the Heavenly Physician’s, in terms of comprehension in this area, I am by no means inferior to the Heavenly Physician!”

In addition to this golden thread divine ability, Li Fan also learned the Heavenly Physician’s method of sealing the Heavenly Demon. The eighty-one golden needles, although the technique differed from the [Soul Sealing and Realm Replacement] previously displayed by the Heavenly Physician, were of the same origin. Li Fan had already learned most of it. With further study, it would not be difficult to decipher it. Beyond these two, the Heavenly Physician’s actions in saving the Heavenly Law Realm, as the Great Venerable of All Laws, also provided Li Fan with much inspiration. Especially the final move, condensing all constant principles of law and freezing the world’s operational power. This gave Li Fan a nascent idea regarding the Heavenly Dao essence that would be harmonized in this lifetime.

“The Heavenly Physician is indeed an inexhaustible treasure trove. It’s a pity that the same immortal formation can probably no longer trap him.”

“I can still try again in the next life.”

“Using the [Xuanhuang Beings] as eyes, extracting all of the Heavenly Physician’s knowledge and foundation.”

As they neared the Xuanhuang Realm, Mo Rubing finally completely regained consciousness. He was initially stunned for a moment, then upon realizing his current situation, he immediately wanted to return to the High Wall. Li Fan frowned and restrained him with myriad golden threads. Mo Rubing instinctively tried to break free but failed, his expression changing. He hadn’t expected Li Fan to have such a trump card.

“Brother Mo, calm down.”

“You have already achieved enlightenment of the High Wall twice. If you still cannot escape its temptation, you will likely be unable to escape it forever and will be perpetually lost within it!”

Li Fan’s icy words finally brought Mo Rubing back to his senses. His struggling movements slowly ceased. However, Li Fan did not remove the golden thread restraints.

“Do you still feel the ‘loss forever’?” Li Fan asked sternly. With Li Fan’s comprehension, he had yet to gain any insight from that “flaw” in the High Wall. His current words were entirely based on the Heavenly Physician’s enlightenment of the High Wall’s flaw within the Immortal Formation.

Mo Rubing’s expression became somewhat subtle: “Loss forever. That phrase is truly fitting.” He cupped his hands, expressing his gratitude for Li Fan’s previous intervention, then sighed deeply: “Thanks to Daoist brother, I can now fully glimpse the secret of the High Wall’s flaw.”

“However, all that I have comprehended…” Mo Rubing paused for a long time before slowly saying, “Is not something that I, at my current level, can see.”

“Hmm?” Li Fan raised his eyebrows.

“I know it sounds convoluted and even somewhat incredible, but that is precisely the truth.”

“That is an enlightenment that does not exist within the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. Only by using the High Wall as a medium can we know and perceive it.”

“And after leaving the High Wall, even if I have ‘remembered’ and ‘comprehended,’ I ultimately cannot manifest this non-existent thing…” Mo Rubing’s expression was somewhat dazed, and he explained to Li Fan what he had encountered, word by word, with great difficulty.

Li Fan could somewhat understand Mo Rubing’s explanation. It was like if Li Fan tried to explain the [Transformation Between True and False] to Mo Rubing. Without possessing [Returning to True], no matter how hard Mo Rubing tried, he could not grasp or comprehend even a fraction of it. He would simply regard Li Fan as a nonsensical liar. Because, in Mo Rubing’s perception, the so-called [Transformation Between True and False] simply did not exist.

“Touching the High Wall allows me to recall this enlightenment, but after leaving the High Wall, all the enlightenment is lost…”

“This is not like the moon in the mirror or the flower in the water, completely useless. It’s even worse, as at least the flower and moon can be seen.” Li Fan deliberately expressed extreme disappointment.

Mo Rubing pondered for a moment and then slightly shook his head: “That’s not entirely true. Even if I cannot retain the enlightenment, these two times of meditation have allowed me to translate the form of the High Wall’s existence into something I can understand.”

As he spoke, Mo Rubing lightly tapped his index finger, drawing a circle in the air before Li Fan. It enveloped Li Fan. In Li Fan’s field of vision, Mo Rubing suddenly disappeared. Even the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea vanished from his observation range. Furthermore, his divine sense and the golden needle traces he had left behind all became ineffective! It was as if walls had been erected on all four sides of him, surrounding him completely, blocking his sight and senses.

“Interesting.”

“A miniature High Wall.”

However, Mo Rubing’s wall was clearly incomparable to the High Wall that encircled the Utmost Darkness Star Sea. Without even needing to use the [Nine Heavens Descending Dust Finger]. With a slight ascent and elevation, Li Fan casually took a step and crossed this obstacle! Mo Rubing remained in his original position, not surprised that Li Fan had escaped so easily.

“My level of enlightenment is still insufficient.”

“If you give me more time, I’m afraid it wouldn’t be so easy for you to escape.” Mo Rubing said slowly.

Li Fan frowned and said, “Brother Mo, your divine ability seems to be missing some crucial elements compared to the invisible High Wall…”

“Precisely because of this lack, your divine ability’s power is greatly reduced. If you could analyze this missing element, you could probably achieve the effect of ‘drawing a cage and trapping yourself’ at will!”

Upon hearing this, a hint of unwillingness and longing flashed in Mo Rubing’s eyes. Being so easily stirred emotionally was almost impossible for Mo Rubing, who cultivated the [Myriad Tribulations Indestructible Demonic Heart Immortal Art]. The current situation could only mean that the secret of the High Wall’s flaw had thoroughly shaken his mental foundation.

“I possess [Returning to True], so I have no need to worry about the ‘loss forever’ characteristic. However, I still haven’t gained anything from that unfathomable entity. Is the gap in comprehension really that large? It seems I will have to return and continue using the myriad beings of the small world to help me comprehend the Dao. Although there may not be much time left in this life.” Li Fan mused inwardly.

Next, Li Fan inquired about Mo Rubing’s future plans.

“Are you still going to search for King Xuan Tian’s whereabouts in the remaining areas of the Star Sea Crossing Formation?”

“During the time you were enlightening yourself at the High Wall, I have searched the Xuanhuang Realm once more. Unlike the Sky Beast’s Eye and Spirit Gathering Ascension, the other parts of the Star Sea Crossing Formation appear to be severely damaged. There are likely no conditions for King Xuan Tian to conceal himself…” Li Fan said slowly.

Mo Rubing looked at the Xuanhuang Realm, not far away. When King Xuan Tian was mentioned again, the wavering expression on his face gradually faded, returning to that of the inscrutable Twelve Law Kings of the Xuan Tian Sect. Perhaps it was due to Li Fan’s selfless obstruction earlier that trust was built. Mo Rubing hesitated for a moment, then slowly said, “I still want to go to one last place.”

“However, ten thousand years have passed, and the Xuanhuang Realm has undergone earth-shattering changes. It’s difficult to distinguish the location immediately…”

“That’s easy.”

In an instant, a comparative map of the Xuanhuang Realm’s past and present appeared before Mo Rubing.

“Here.”

Mo Rubing carefully identified the location and finally chose a spot. Li Fan’s expression immediately became somewhat subtle.

“What’s wrong?” Mo Rubing naturally noticed the change in Li Fan’s expression.

Li Fan shook his head slightly: “You’ll know when you go.”

With a flash of the wooden sword phantom, Li Fan brought Mo Rubing to their destination. It was precisely the small mountain where the fishing pond was located, and the Taoist temple! In this lifetime, Li Fan had not utilized the fishing pond. He had only forcibly relocated Zhong Shen Tong and the disciple Liu Li from the temple.

“This place was Brother Xuanyuan’s homeland.”

“It was also his final place of ascension.”

“I didn’t expect it to become so desolate now.”

Mo Rubing slowly walked into the Taoist temple, observing carefully, and lamented.

“It’s actually the last ascension site in the Xuanhuang Realm?” Li Fan was slightly surprised.

“Yes. Brother Xuanyuan was extremely sentimental about this place back then. Whenever he couldn’t be found elsewhere, he could always be found here. I don’t know what remarkable things happened here or what he experienced.” Mo Rubing walked slowly, as if searching for King Xuan Tian’s aura. He walked all the way to the back courtyard of the Taoist temple. And saw that ordinary small pond, Mo Rubing’s pupils suddenly contracted sharply. Then he rushed forward rapidly.

“This…”

“After ten thousand years, this place hasn’t changed at all?!” Mo Rubing was shocked but also keenly sensed the extraordinary nature of this place.

“You looked strange just now, that’s why? Is it this place?” Mo Rubing suddenly turned his head and asked.

Li Fan nodded slightly: “This small pond, I was unable to destroy it. Hence, I realized the peculiarity of this place.”

“However, I searched it thoroughly but could never find anything strange…”

Mo Rubing heard this and looked at the fishing pond again.

“The surrounding mountains have all changed drastically, yet only this pond water remains unchanged. There must be something hidden here…”

“Strange, but Brother Xuanyuan never mentioned any secrets here back then.”

Having found the only clue, Mo Rubing was unwilling to let it go. He tried all sorts of methods, even personally diving into the water. But in the end, he gained nothing. It was as if this was truly just an ordinary small pond. The secret was right before his eyes, yet he could not perceive it. Mo Rubing’s expression became somewhat gloomy.

“This is King Xuan Tian’s homeland? What kind of person was King Xuan Tian before his ascension?” Li Fan seized the opportunity to ask.

“Brother Xuanyuan’s early life was truly ordinary. So ordinary that he passed before me many times, and I never even lowered my head to look at him.”

“Back then, I was a direct descendant of the Nine Refinements Temple, while he was merely a cultivator at the Qi Refining stage.”

“However, no one knew that hidden beneath Brother Xuanyuan’s unassuming appearance was an extraordinary talent. He rose to prominence overnight, not relying on sect resources, but solely on himself, becoming the foremost ascension expert of the Xuanhuang Realm at that time, and the last one…”

Mo Rubing’s expression was filled with infinite nostalgia. And Li Fan, listening to these words, fell into deep thought. Li Fan was certainly aware of the existence of the fishing pond. But he had no idea when the fishing pond had existed in the Xuanhuang Realm. After all, the fishing pond was implicitly a creation of an anonymous True Immortal, completely transcending the Xuanhuang Realm. Even in the historical records documenting the Xuanhuang Realm’s history, there was no mention of the fishing pond. All along, Li Fan had subconsciously believed that the fishing pond suddenly appeared in the Xuanhuang Realm after the Star Sea catastrophe and the destruction of various realms. But now it seemed…

“Could it be that King Xuan Tian’s meteoric rise was due to this supreme treasure, the fishing pond?” A thought couldn’t help but arise in Li Fan’s mind.

Chapter 1368: Immortal Treasure Azure Nether Pearl

Heavenly King Xuan’s greatest trump card was actually the fishing pond?

This was not impossible. After all, Heavenly King Xuan had no foundation, yet was able to suppress the proud talents of his generation alone and ascend first… This truly couldn’t be simply described by “extraordinary talent.”

But if this guess were true… Li Fan’s heart couldn’t help but recall the stone tablet that sought to comprehend the Dao of Fishing but was instead lured away, and the Cat Treasure that appeared from the fishing pond, seemingly harmless, yet capable of devouring True Immortals.

“Could it be that Heavenly King Xuan’s fate was similar?”

Li Fan looked at the shallow pool before him, his apprehension rising unprecedentedly.

The scene then fell into a long silence. It wasn’t that Mo Rubing was dull-witted, but without a hint, wanting to connect this pond to the Dao of Fishing was truly difficult.

Although the secrets of the fishing pond were never discovered, Mo Rubing had already regarded it as his last hope, with no intention of leaving in the short term.

“Lingering here forever is not a solution.”

“Actually, I have another method that might help us inquire about Heavenly King Xuan’s whereabouts,” Li Fan suddenly broke the silence after a long while.

Mo Rubing’s head snapped up.

Li Fan deliberated for a moment and carefully said, “I have mastered part of the power of the True Immortal script ‘Manifest.’ The Manifest character can visualize and reveal the subtle connections between things.”

“Mm, from the residual memories of Dharma King Ji, I learned of the existence of the Azure Nether Pearl…”

As Li Fan spoke, he observed Mo Rubing’s reaction. When the Azure Nether Pearl was mentioned, Mo Rubing’s pupils truly contracted, his aura changed, and he involuntarily became defensive. However, perhaps it was due to their shared experiences that enough trust had accumulated between them. After a short while, Mo Rubing’s guard disappeared on its own.

Li Fan then continued, “If the memory I obtained is not wrong, the cultivation techniques practiced by the Twelve Dharma Kings back then were all subtly connected to that Azure Nether Pearl.”

“I wonder if, using the Manifest character, we can trace Heavenly King Xuan’s whereabouts based on this connection.”

“This method, after all, involves directly confronting the power of the True Immortal script, so there will certainly be some risk. Moreover, it only tracks the Azure Nether Pearl, the Supreme Treasure of the Xuan Tian Sect, not Heavenly King Xuan himself. To avoid Brother Mo’s suspicion, I did not proactively suggest it before.”

Li Fan looked at Mo Rubing, leaving the choice to him.

Mo Rubing did not answer directly but suddenly asked a seemingly unrelated question, “Fellow Daoist, what do you think of the expert who laid those golden threads at the breach of the High Wall? Who could they be?”

Li Fan did not conceal anything but answered truthfully, “When I trapped him using formations, I also took the opportunity to pry into his identity. He should be a Venerable from the Heavenly Law Realm, which has merged with the Xuanhuang Realm.”

He extended a finger, transmitting information related to the Heavenly Physician to Mo Rubing.

“Heavenly Law’s constant principles, acting on behalf of heaven?”

“And how can it compare to the unity of heaven and man for us cultivators? Even if it replaces heaven…”

“It’s just a bunch of unenlightened, low-class individuals. Although this person is strong now, it’s probably only due to these ten thousand years of accumulation.”

Mo Rubing shook his head, his tone filled with disdain. However, he continued to look at the fishing pond without answering.

Only after standing by the pond for a full seven days, still unable to discern its mysteries, did Mo Rubing finally shake his head slightly and then say with great solemnity, “We can give it a try.”

“The power of the True Immortal script is no trivial matter, and I have no guarantee that I can fully control the force. Moreover…”

“If it truly points to this pool of water, capable of swallowing a figure like Heavenly King Xuan, this pool absolutely contains immense risks. We must not be careless!”

“The safety of the Xuanhuang Realm now hinges on both of us. We cannot afford to be careless,” Li Fan reminded.

Mo Rubing seemed to agree with Li Fan’s viewpoint. By the fishing pond of this desolate mountain Taoist temple, they made ample preparations. Only then did they begin the test of the Manifest character.

“Back then, when Elder Brother Xuanyuan imparted techniques to me, he introduced that the cultivation methods of most of us Twelve Dharma Kings originated from True Immortals who ascended from the [Divine Witch Realm].”

“The cultivators of this realm resonate with the Great Dao with their souls, manipulate the Great Dao, and replace the Great Dao. Although their cultivation and outward manifestations are somewhat strange, they are the immortal techniques that most easily lead directly to the Great Dao. It is said that this Divine Witch Realm is one of the most ancient cultivation realms, and perhaps even the origin of human cultivators.”

“The Divine Witch people are almost indistinguishable from ordinary humans. Only their overall talent is much higher; the difficulty for their souls to resonate with the Great Dao is far less than ours.”

“Back then, when I started cultivating the [Myriad Tribulations Indestructible Demonic Heart Immortal Art], it truly took considerable effort. But according to Elder Brother Xuanyuan, for the Divine Witch people, cultivating it takes no effort.”

Li Fan’s eyes narrowed slightly as he listened to Mo Rubing’s description.

Mo Rubing suddenly changed the subject, “But even amongst such powerful True Immortals of the Divine Witch race, when the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation arrived, they were no different from ants. Their corpses rained down, and they even died unnaturally while desperately fleeing…”

“True Immortals are nothing to be feared! Come on!” Mo Rubing let out a low roar, and countless black hearts surged out from within him in a frenzy. They spun and howled around him, like a terrifying storm.

Li Fan glanced at the immortal formations and the phantom wooden sword beside him, ensuring that if anything unexpected happened, he could escape immediately. He then swept over the 400% charge progress on the True Return panel. Only then did he steadfastly write a “Manifest” character in the air and send it directly towards Mo Rubing.

Mo Rubing did not resist, allowing the power of the Manifest character technique to envelop his body. Streams of green smoke rose from the myriad black hearts. They first ascended straight up, then began to circle and roam endlessly after seemingly touching the limits of the sky. They seemed to be searching for a target. Mo Rubing’s true body writhed and contorted his face, as if a great force was constantly rubbing back and forth upon him.

“Brother Mo, hold on,” Li Fan said in a deep voice, unleashing several golden threads and inserting them into Mo Rubing’s body. Since it was a prearranged action, it did not elicit resistance from Mo Rubing. Pure spiritual energy and even soul power continuously poured in along the golden threads, helping Mo Rubing maintain his state under the pressure of the True Immortal script.

Above Mo Rubing’s head, the myriad green smoke gradually fused into one. Then, as if it had finally found its target, the green smoke surged, as if it had come alive. Like a green dragon soaring into the heavens, it suddenly swooped down. Looking at its flight path, it was heading directly for the fishing pond!

“It’s actually like this?” Li Fan’s heart sank heavily, and he subconsciously moved slightly away from the pond. However, what happened next was somewhat beyond his expectations. The thick green dragon, just as it was about to plunge into the fishing pond water, inexplicably paused slightly. Then it split into two streams. One stream plunged into the fishing pond, while the other stream surged back into the sky, flying towards the world outside the Xuanhuang Realm!

“This?” The sudden change left both men completely stunned. Mo Rubing reacted quickly, first following one stream of green smoke into the fishing pond. But as the green smoke entered the water, it vanished without a trace. Mo Rubing could not find any trace of the Azure Nether Pearl’s aura in the seemingly bottomless pond. For a moment, he felt somewhat dejected. As for Li Fan, he looked up at the place where the other stream of green smoke had disappeared.

“Brother Mo, what do you think? Could it be that the Azure Nether Pearl actually split into two?” Li Fan asked with a frown.

“Judging by the performance of the Manifest character, perhaps so. But what if the Manifest character not only points to the Azure Nether Pearl’s connection but also simultaneously points to Elder Brother Xuanyuan?”

“Since we cannot get any results from this pool of water for now, let’s go and investigate the place where the other stream of green smoke went,” Mo Rubing suddenly had a flash of inspiration after a period of silence. This was exactly what Li Fan wanted. Before having sufficient self-protection capabilities, Li Fan really did not want to deal with the fishing pond himself. Previously, there was a wonder in the fishing pond like the Cat Treasure, and now that it was confirmed that Heavenly King Xuan’s disappearance was related to the fishing pond, Li Fan was naturally even more cautious. The phantom of the wooden sword, carrying the two men, followed the green smoke. Although the green smoke traced its source rapidly, it was still slower than Li Fan’s supreme escape technique. Not long after, catching up to the green smoke, they could only wait behind it. Mo Rubing’s expression was not good, so Li Fan took the initiative to change the subject.

“Besides the Divine Witch Realm, did Heavenly King Xuan ever mention any other anecdotes about the Immortal Realm?”

“To be honest, even though the immortal path has been severed for ten thousand years, we cultivators are still filled with yearning and curiosity for the legendary [Immortal Realm].”

Li Fan’s words pulled Mo Rubing’s thoughts back to the past.

“Perhaps he truly went to the Immortal Realm, or perhaps Elder Brother Xuanyuan heard it from the Faceless Immortal. In any case, Elder Brother Xuanyuan really talked about some matters concerning the Immortal Realm in private. We could all tell that he was very concerned about completing the ascension process halfway and being forced to return from the Immortal Realm.” Mo Rubing chuckled lightly.

“It is said that the Immortal Realm is a beautiful sacred land with endless resources. After ascending to immortality, one no longer needs to worry about the needs of cultivation. How many resources one can collect depends entirely on personal strength and luck.”

“Brother he didn’t mention what these so-called resources were. I suppose they are not as simple as immortal spiritual power.”

“By the way, there’s another matter. Have you ever heard of the Ascension Thunder Tribulation?” Mo Rubing’s expression shifted as he asked.

“Ascension Thunder Tribulation? I have certainly heard of it. In the past, when the immortal path was not severed, ancient cultivators were said to be able to ascend to immortality only after passing the trial of the thunder tribulation,” Li Fan replied quickly.

Mo Rubing’s expression was somewhat strange, “Back then, I was only one step away from ascension. But after Elder Brother Xuanyuan left and returned, ascension became a mere illusion. In fact, I have had a significant emotional burden because of this and have always been regretful about missing the opportunity.”

“However, in private, when no one else was around, Elder Brother Xuanyuan once comforted me. The reason he was able to pass the tribulation and ascend back then was because the True Immortal presiding over the thunder tribulation at the immortal realm passage suddenly died due to the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation…”

“According to the originally estimated strength of the thunder tribulation, Elder Brother Xuanyuan would not have been able to pass it. In fact, the thunder tribulation was never intended to let any cultivator pass!” Li Fan was astonished by this remark.

“Therefore, Elder Brother Xuanyuan told me not to dwell on it too much. If my cultivation had been even slightly faster, the fate awaiting me would not have been ascension to immortality, but merely turning to ashes under the lightning bolts,” Mo Rubing said in a somber tone.

“Of course, I’m not sure if this is true or just something Elder Brother Xuanyuan said to comfort me. However, out of trust for Elder Brother Xuanyuan, he spoke casually, and I listened casually.”

“Hehehe…” Li Fan remained silent. The beautiful illusion he had of Heavenly King Xuan had been somewhat shattered. In the silence, the green smoke of the Manifest character technique finally reached its end. It was still beneath the High Wall. However, this time, it did not touch the High Wall. Instead, in an inconspicuous corner beneath the High Wall, it suddenly disappeared. Li Fan’s heart stirred, and he recognized the point where the green smoke had vanished. It was precisely one of the nodes beneath the High Wall leading into the ground fissure depression!

“Let’s go!” Mo Rubing’s expression became invigorated, and he plunged down into it.

Li Fan pondered for a moment, then followed. The same situation as before played out again, with the rapid descent of the [Potential] domain. Soon they arrived at the lowest point of the Star Sea. This place was filled with dormant energy, leaving Mo Rubing, a newcomer, stunned. But he did not forget the purpose of their journey. Tightly following the green smoke, they sped rapidly forward through the winding and twisting ground fissure depression. Li Fan had known before that these ditches and fissures covering the Star Sea were a vast maze. Venturing in rashly likely carried the risk of getting lost. But now that the green smoke was leading the way, and more importantly, the target of their pursuit might involve Heavenly King Xuan and the Azure Nether Pearl, Li Fan did not hesitate and followed to explore. They even spent more than dozens of times the usual time for traversing the Star Sea. Only after a long while did the green smoke finally stop. Li Fan looked at the place where the connection of the Manifest character technique had vanished, somewhat surprised. A complete green pearl was quietly floating there. The moment Li Fan saw this Azure Nether Pearl, he finally understood the true meaning of the character "Azure" in the resplendent azure sky. Mo Rubing looked at the Azure Nether Pearl, his body trembling slightly. At the same time, his eyes were filled with confusion. He didn't know why the immortal artifact that Elder Brother Xuanyuan relied on would be left alone here.

“It seems something is not right.”

“Why is the Azure Nether Pearl devoid of any spiritual essence?”

Having seen many incomplete immortal artifacts before, Li Fan keenly sensed the anomaly within the Azure Nether Pearl. Being reminded, Mo Rubing also reacted. He flew forward, intending to touch it. However, the Azure Nether Pearl instantly transformed into wisps of green as Mo Rubing approached. It shattered and dissipated without a trace.

“No!” All this effort had ultimately been in vain. Even with Mo Rubing’s composure, he was momentarily distraught. He tried to grasp the surrounding unseen green wisps, attempting to restore the Azure Nether Pearl. Li Fan, however, did not engage in such futile actions. Instead, he pondered, “The aura within this Azure Nether Pearl seems somewhat similar to the ground fissure depression of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea…”

“Similar?”

“I was previously astonished by the amount of energy accumulated in the ground fissures, which seemed beyond reasonable limits.”

“Now it seems, perhaps it is related to the Azure Nether Pearl.”

Chapter 1369: Eternal Obsession Rising

Li Fan surveyed his surroundings in secret.

After the Azure Nether Pearl shattered and dissipated, it felt as if a formless giant stone had fallen into a crevice and hollow.

Threads of ripples emanated from the endless, labyrinthine dark rivers within the Star Sea hollows.

A mysterious aura surged within them, bestowing a strange vitality upon this place.

It seemed that the complete dissipation of the Azure Nether Pearl had activated something.

Li Fan vaguely sensed that this crevice hollow had become different.

"It seems that for ten thousand years, the Azure Nether Pearl has been continuously releasing its energy to the outside. It was already nearing its limit, about to be completely drained."

"Our approach merely provided the final push," Li Fan sighed.

Mo Rubing also noticed this. His expression, which had become somewhat agitated due to excitement earlier, gradually calmed down.

He looked back at the entire crevice hollow and, in a daze, understood its purpose: to accumulate vitality, wait for the opportune moment to trigger a massive revival, and then guide the comprehensive resurgence of the Star Sea!

"Such intricate engineering could not have been naturally formed by the Star Sea. Not to mention the Azure Nether Pearl serving as the catalyst for vital energy supply..." Mo Rubing's thoughts raced.

"Could it be that this was Xuan Yuan's arrangement? But when exactly?"

"The Azure Nether Pearl, as Brother Xuan Yuan's most treasured possession, never left his side. Yet it ended up here... and Brother Xuan Yuan disappeared into that mysterious pond."

Mo Rubing's expression was filled with doubt and uncertainty.

"This matter is truly bizarre," Li Fan nodded. "Either, on the day King Xuan Tian was attacked, he didn't directly disappear but fell into a coma due to severe injuries. Only after waking up later did he make this arrangement for the crevice hollow. Perhaps that pond in the Xuanhuang Realm is connected to a crevice here."

"Or, King Xuan Tian had already handed over the Azure Nether Pearl to someone else before being attacked. And for all these years, this person has been acting on his behalf, carrying out various plans related to the revival of the Star Sea..."

"Impossible!" Before Li Fan could finish speaking, Mo Rubing instinctively interrupted him.

Li Fan gazed meaningfully at Mo Rubing, "Brother Mo, could you tell me, among the Twelve Law Kings back then, who was the one King Xuan Tian trusted the most?"

"No need to speak of treating everyone equally. Disparities in closeness are a principle of the Great Dao; even saints find it difficult to avoid."

Mo Rubing's face turned cold, and he wanted to speak but stopped.

Then, he actually closed his eyes, attempting to conceal his inner turmoil.

But in the end, Mo Rubing did not evade the question: "I think, if Brother Xuan Yuan truly had someone he trusted the most, it would definitely be Xing Wuque."

"Xing Wuque..."

Information about this Law King instantly appeared in Li Fan's mind.

Missing all four limbs, his facial features destroyed. Always wearing a bronze fang mask, he almost never communicated with others.

"In the Xuan Tian Sect, aside from Brother Xuan Yuan, no one knew Xing Wuque's true identity. Just as you said, there are differences in closeness. We Twelve Law Kings also formed small groups based on our relationships."

"Sun Xingwang and Sikong Lin were often seen together, speaking words others couldn't understand; Gongye Tianzong and Tianxingke would frequently converse, raising their cups and toasting; Luo Yichen, Nie Daniu, and Ji Yuzhen, the three ladies always had endless whispers for each other..."

"But Xing Wuque alone, always kept his distance from other Law Kings, never initiating contact with anyone in the sect. When he appeared, he was always alone. However, every task assigned to him was flawlessly executed with extreme efficiency," Mo Rubing said with a distant look.

"As if he were a machine that had shed its emotions and desires, no longer living for itself."

"It is precisely because of this that Brother Xuan Yuan might have trusted him the most."

"Moreover, when the incident occurred that day, Xing Wuque indeed seemed to be absent from the sect," Mo Rubing frowned.

Li Fan nodded slightly: "If it was indeed this Xing Wuque who took the Azure Nether Pearl back then, then he must have been busy running errands for King Xuan Yuan's mission all these years. Brother Mo, do you have a way to contact this Law King Xing?"

Mo Rubing shook his head: "Xing Wuque only ever had direct contact with Brother Xuan Yuan. However..."

As if suddenly recalling something, Mo Rubing looked again towards the place where the Azure Nether Pearl had just dissipated.

"I wonder if we can use the [Manifest] character technique again on the Azure Nether Pearl? We might be able to follow the trail..."

"The Azure Nether Pearl is an immortal artifact. True Immortal scripts are likely useless against it, especially since it has already dissipated," Li Fan pointed to the surroundings, where ripples were still continuously surging.

"Dissipation does not mean disappearance. Even among King Xuan Yuan's many treasures obtained from the Immortal Realm, the Azure Nether Pearl was among the most precious. How could it disappear so easily?"

"The Azure Nether Pearl has not vanished; it has transformed into vitality and exists within these dark rivers in a different, special form..." Mo Rubing said with certainty, regaining the style of one of the Twelve Law Kings of the Xuan Tian Sect. "Just directly use the [Manifest] character technique on this endless dark river of vitality!"

Li Fan re-sensitized the boundless dark river within the crevice, and gradually understood.

Gathering his spirits, he once again solemnly inscribed the character [Manifest] in the air. The moment the profoundly mysterious character took form, it dissolved into the dark river like ink.

The surging ripples, with their regular rhythm, were quickly disrupted.

It was as if another unrelated, completely independent fluctuation had appeared.

Li Fan and Mo Rubing followed the direction of the fluctuation's transmission, moving rapidly.

This time, they continuously delved deeper into the crevice, navigating a thousand twists and turns. It took more than thirty days before they finally reached their destination.

"Be careful, there seems to be the aura of a living person ahead!" Mo Rubing suddenly transmitted a warning.

Li Fan had already shielded himself with the phantom of his wooden sword, and slowly approached.

At the end of the dark river, a figure sat alone.

Its aura was erratic, and it wore a fang mask!

"Xing Wuque?" Seeing the familiar attire, Mo Rubing couldn't help but exclaim loudly.

However, after a slight moment of stunned silence, Li Fan felt a sense of strangeness welling up within him.

Xing Wuque had long since lost his hands and feet, yet this figure distinctly possessed all four limbs.

More importantly...

The clothing and attire he wore were extremely familiar to Li Fan.

It was exactly the same as Xu Ke, who had previously disappeared into the depths of the dark river!

"Is it Xu Ke?"

"Or Xing Wuque?"

"No wonder I sensed his aura was erratic before..." Li Fan pondered, not acting rashly.

After a moment of shock, Mo Rubing also discerned the difference between the person before them and his old comrade.

After careful observation for a while, he made a judgment: "It's similar but not identical. They seem to be in some miraculous state of fusion? Could it be that after all these years, Xing Wuque is also nearing the end of his lifespan and had to resort to such a method of preservation?"

Li Fan, however, saw that this fusion seemed to be led by Xu Ke. It was less a matter of Xing Wuque's preservation and more a matter of inheritance.

"As expected of a Son of Heavenly Destiny, to have encountered such an opportunity after being impacted by the reverberating Star Force and sent to this desperate place."

"If Mo Rubing's previous guess was correct, and Xing Wuque has been diligently carrying out the tasks assigned by King Xuan Yuan for ten thousand years..."

"Xu Ke also shouldered the responsibility of solely and eternally suppressing the malevolent intentions of the Xuanhuang Realm, as instructed by Mr. Bai in his dying moments."

"These two are quite similar in this regard. Perhaps this is why Xu Ke was able to inherit Xing Wuque's legacy?" Li Fan pondered inwardly.

Mo Rubing shook his head slightly: "This new body is far too weak to bear Xing Wuque's full strength. However, we can help!"

With that, Mo Rubing unleashed a demonic heart.

As it flew towards the target, the originally somewhat ferocious expression on the demonic heart slowly dissolved.

It transformed into a faceless entity, then completely melted into viscous gray solution.

In an instant, it permeated Xu Ke's body.

Moments later, Xu Ke's erratic aura began to stabilize.

"Billions of demonic hearts can not only harm and seize bodies but also suppress disasters and save lives. Truly worthy of being an Immortal technique of the Divine Witch race," Li Fan couldn't help but sigh as he witnessed this. He also spared no effort, unleashing dozens of golden needles.

Just as he had helped Mo Rubing before, he infused pure spiritual energy and soul power through the golden threads.

With the combined assistance of two powerful cultivators, Xu Ke's fusion with the bronze mask process accelerated a thousandfold!

What would have taken at least decades to complete the full inheritance absorption was now achieved in a short time.

Xu Ke's aura gradually stabilized.

Li Fan and Mo Rubing waited quietly.

Finally, two beams of bright light shone from the eyes of the mask.

Seeing the two before him, Xu Ke's body trembled.

"Sacred Master?!" he exclaimed subconsciously, his tone filled with astonishment.

His voice and tone had completely changed from Xu Ke's usual manner, but the content of his words clearly indicated the identity of the figure currently in front of them.

"Hmm?" Hearing a familiar voice call out an unfamiliar term, Mo Rubing was momentarily stunned, then finally reacted, looking at Li Fan.

Li Fan also wore a look of shock at this moment, asking with disbelief, "Xu Ke? How could it be you?!"

He acted as if he had completely failed to notice anything earlier.

Mo Rubing said coldly, "You are not Xing Wuque? What did you do to him?"

His eyes flashed with dangerous light, but it was only because Xu Ke was acquainted with Li Fan that he didn't act immediately.

"Senior Xing... he has already reached his limit and has passed away."

"By chance, I found this mask and passed his trial, thus barely inheriting his legacy," Xu Ke said with a hint of sadness.

Xu Ke elaborated on the entire sequence of events.

Just as Li Fan had speculated, Xing Wuque might have initially harbored thoughts of soul possession and rebirth, but upon sensing Xu Ke's life story, which bore a striking resemblance to his own, Xing Wuque ultimately chose to abandon that idea.

The fusion transformed into an inheritance.

"Senior's inheritance is too vast. Even if he willingly allowed me to absorb it, I would find it difficult to fully accept it all at once, and I would fall into a state of instability..."

"Fortunately, the two seniors intervened," Xu Ke bowed respectfully.

Hearing the voice of his former comrade speaking to him like this, Mo Rubing was momentarily unaccustomed.

Li Fan, however, directly inquired about the connection between Xing Wuque and the dark rivers in the Star Sea.

"Senior Xing's inheritance seems to have deliberately omitted memories related to this aspect."

"But through some fragmented memories, I can infer the general idea."

"These crevice dark rivers that span the entire Star Sea were painstakingly dug out by Senior Xing over the years using the power of the immortal artifact, the Azure Nether Pearl," Xu Ke stated, stunning both Li Fan and Mo Rubing.

"The crevice dark rivers wind throughout the entire Star Sea. It is truly difficult to imagine that such an undertaking could be accomplished by a single person. However, even with the memories intentionally erased by Senior, there is still a vast amount of residual memories about the pioneering of these dark rivers, which undoubtedly attests to his achievements," Xu Ke said sorrowfully.

"Ever since Senior Xing received the command from King Xuan Yuan back then, he has been holding the Azure Nether Pearl and carrying out this work."

"For ten thousand years, he has not rested for a single moment."

"Even with Senior's profound cultivation, propelling the immortal artifact Azure Nether Pearl is an immensely taxing task. Ten thousand years of unrelenting effort have finally pushed him to his limit..."

"With regret, he perished at the end of this crevice dark river," Xu Ke recounted everything with a sorrowful expression.

Li Fan remained silent.

Although it sounded preposterous, if Xing Wuque truly possessed the personality Mo Rubing had described...

It was not entirely impossible.

Mo Rubing was even more profoundly shaken, hesitating to speak several times.

He looked towards the end of the crevice dark rivers, "Xing Wuque... he did not complete the task assigned by Brother Xuan Yuan even until his death?"

Xu Ke nodded: "This is also what I must continue to do for the rest of my life. Since I have inherited Senior Xing's legacy, I must naturally help him complete his unfinished task."

His tone was calm, yet extremely resolute.

Upon hearing this, Mo Rubing's expression subtly changed, looking at Xu Ke with surprise.

"Absurd..."

"Setting aside the meaning of this endeavor, the Azure Nether Pearl, an immortal artifact, has been shattered. With your current cultivation, how can you possibly open new crevice dark rivers?"

Xu Ke remained unmoved: "Persisting in completing Senior Xing's ambition is its own meaning."

"As for the shattered immortal artifact..."

A radiant azure light suddenly emanated from Xu Ke's mask.

It was exactly the same as what Li Fan had seen on the Azure Nether Pearl itself before!

"During Senior's ten thousand years of pioneering, he had already transformed the act of opening crevice dark rivers into an innate instinct. Now that the inheritance has been passed to me, even without the immortal artifact, I can accomplish it!"

"It is merely a repetition ten thousand years later!"

Bathed in azure light, shooting forth from the mask.

Illuminating the path ahead, at the end of the dark river.

Under the joint witness of Mo Rubing and Li Fan, another new crevice was indeed opened by Xu Ke!

However, they only managed to advance less than ten feet before the azure light suddenly cut off.

Xu Ke also consequently collapsed to the ground, as if having been completely drained.

"With this pace, when will you ever finish?" Li Fan couldn't help but let out a cold snort.

"As long as there is progress with each attempt, there will come a day when it is completed," Xu Ke said with a difficult smile.

"Just as Senior Xing said, King Xuan Yuan's command must have its own significance."

Chapter 1370: Star Sea Ascension Domain

Xu Ke rested for a moment, his energy inexplicably replenished in a short period.

The green light from the mask reappeared, and he began the act of carving out crevices in the void once more.

"I have inherited Senior Xing Wuque's legacy, greatly increasing my lifespan limit. This is truly a debt of rebirth. With this damaged body, completing the excavation of the dark rivers should be sufficient."

"After all, Senior Xing Wuque had already advanced the dark rivers through the vast majority of the Star Sea before his death. All I need to do is add a few more bricks and mortar..."

Xu Ke babbled on, as if explaining to Li Fan and Mo Rubing, or perhaps more accurately, trying to convince himself.

His hands continued their work, the green light carving a path forward.

Fully concentrated, he worked tirelessly.

Li Fan paid no mind to whether Xu Ke was carving the dark rivers out of his own volition or due to the influence of Xing Wuque's inheritance. To him, there was no difference between the two.

Li Fan was more interested in the method Xu Ke was using to carve out the crevices in the void with the green light.

The crevices, while still within the Star Sea, were located at the lowest points of momentum.

Li Fan, with his Ascension Formation, could continuously elevate his own momentum. However, he had no effective means to deal with the descent of momentum.

Li Fan vaguely sensed that the high and low points of momentum were merely two sides of the same coin. To comprehend only one aspect would be incomplete.

If he could understand the method of carving out crevices, he could further his understanding of 'momentum.'

Xu Ke, while appearing to carve forward, was actually excavating and bombarding the Star Sea, creating low points of momentum that did not originally exist.

In essence, it was the same as the natural high platforms within the Great Wall of Remaining Realms, with the only difference being the level of momentum.

"It mainly relies on the green light emanating from that mask."

"This mask..." After observing it for a while, Li Fan understood.

He needed to use True Immortal flesh as an auxiliary material for his Ascension Formation.

Xing Wuque's mask, however, served a similar purpose to True Immortal flesh.

"Not only is it an immortal artifact, but it also possesses another extremely special power."

Li Fan stared at the green glow on Xu Ke's face, and for some reason, felt a sense of vague familiarity.

This familiarity flashed and disappeared. By the time he wished to trace and confirm it, he found no clues, as if it had been his own illusion all along.

But Li Fan would not easily give up such a lead.

Past sights flashed rapidly in his mind, constantly reappearing and being compared.

The more times he reincarnated, the richer and more complex his experiences became, and the greater the pressure he faced when recalling the past.

As time passed, the sense of familiarity in his heart was rapidly disappearing. To successfully find his target, Li Fan pushed the Dao Transformation Stone's operational efficiency to its maximum.

Faint beads of sweat dripped from his forehead, and fine cracks even appeared on the Dao Transformation Stone. Infinite soul power was channeled into it, repairing and replenishing it under Li Fan's self-directed control.

Perhaps it was Li Fan's good luck, or perhaps it was the help of pushing the Dao Transformation Stone's efficiency to its limit subconsciously.

Finally, just before that sudden sense of familiarity completely vanished.

Li Fan finally found its origin amidst countless past experiences.

"With the protection of the remnant remains left by the First Generation Great Heavenly Venerate, and using the detonation of those few immortal artifacts as power, there is a very high probability that you and I can traverse the High Wall!"

"We have already prepared for so long, why change our minds now?!"

Even after such a long time, Li Fan could still sense the endless resentment carried by the voice of the speaker.

It was precisely...

The scene that would appear in the illusionary trial of the Fallen Immortal Realm when making the same choice as the former Su Bai!

Fallen Immortal Realm, Illusionary reality blending reality.

Everything that occurred in the Fallen Immortal Realm was both illusory and real.

When fragmented consciousnesses of the Xuanhuang Heavenly Dao roared and questioned him,

In the illusion of the Fallen Immortal Realm, Li Fan, as 'Su Bai,' felt a trace of inexplicable emotion in that instant.

The remnant remains of the First Generation Great Heavenly Venerate...

Did indeed exist.

Moreover, the timeline recorded in the illusion suggested that the First Generation Great Heavenly Venerate's remnant remains were on Su Bai at that time.

Therefore, when experiencing it again in the illusion, Li Fan could sense its special aura through Su Bai's body.

When he first sensed it, Li Fan had not been able to form a cognitive understanding of it. Thus, for such a long time, he hadn't realized its existence, only having the Dao Transformation Stone silently record everything.

Returning to the present, when Li Fan carefully sensed Xing Wuque's mask,

That familiar aura finally awakened Li Fan's perception.

"Remnants of the First Generation Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate?"

Li Fan's first thought was indeed this.

But soon, he realized something was wrong.

"The similarity in aura is not because they are from the same person."

"Rather, their nature is of the same origin."

Feeling a slight regret in his heart, Li Fan soon pondered what this common origin might be.

Li Fan's anomaly naturally attracted Mo Rubing's attention.

"Fellow Daoist, have you also encountered Xing Wuque?"

"I have not seen him, but I am amazed that there are such people in this world..."

Li Fan paused slightly, finally stating, "Stubbornness" as his evaluation.

Mo Rubing gave a wry smile: "More than stubborn, it's simply foolish and idiotic. Let alone you, even I, as one of the Twelve Law Kings of the Xuan Tian Sect, could never have imagined he could achieve something like this."

Mo Rubing's tone suddenly became somewhat melancholic.

"Perhaps this is why Brother Xuanyuan entrusted this matter to him back then. If it were me, or any of the other Twelve Law Kings, we certainly couldn't have done it like Xing Wuque."

"It's not that we are less loyal than Xing Wuque. It's just that after Brother Xuanyuan disappeared, instead of going to search for him, he chose to remain in this depression and dark river, executing his mission day after day for ten thousand years..." Mo Rubing shook his head repeatedly.

"Xu Ke's temperament is indeed somewhat similar to Xing Wuque's. Now that he has inherited the mission and chosen to continue excavating the unfinished dark river, I cannot dissuade him. However, Daoist Brother Mo, do you know of any other deeper meanings behind these crevice dark rivers?" Li Fan mused about the common origin while intensely staring at Mo Rubing and questioning him.

"If it were merely to accumulate vitality for the Star Sea's revival, then there would be no need to cover the entire Star Sea. Even if it only covered half of the Star Sea, the goal could be achieved."

"Half versus the whole—the workload is incomparable. King Xuan Tian was a remarkable individual; he would never make such a mistake. Just as Xing Wuque said, King Xuan Tian's instructions must have had their own significance. What could that significance be?"

Mo Rubing squinted his eyes, his gaze sweeping across the crevice dark rivers.

He was stumped by Li Fan's question and could not answer for a moment.

Li Fan chuckled: "It couldn't be that King Xuan Tian made a mistake when assigning tasks to Xing Wuque, right?"

"That is absolutely impossible!" Mo Rubing flatly denied.

Furrowing his brows, he still could not figure it out.

When asked, Xu Ke only said that regarding King Xuan Tian's instructions, Xing Wuque had always followed them diligently without questioning why.

Mo Rubing was momentarily speechless.

"It should be... like how a formation only takes shape when it is completely laid out. Even if nine-tenths are completed, if the connection is not established, it is all useless."

"Yes, that's definitely it." After a long while, Mo Rubing finally offered a seemingly reasonable explanation.

Li Fan remained noncommittal: "To traverse the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea—what a grand undertaking. If such a large-scale formation were to erupt, let alone revive the Star Sea, it might even be capable of overturning the High Wall."

Although he said this on the surface, Li Fan actually did not agree with Mo Rubing's statement in his heart.

Li Fan believed that with his current formation mastery, he was not much inferior to King Xuan Tian.

These crevice dark rivers showed no trace of a formation at all; how could he fail to see that?

"However, even if it's not a formation, the principle might be the same."

"Only by reaching 'completion' can the conditions be met and activated."

Li Fan's thoughts condensed slightly.

This feeling of building a nine-story tower but failing within the last step, was it not akin to his own experience when using the Ascension Formation to ascend to the peak of momentum?

Unless the ultimate point of ascension to immortality was reached, no matter how high one ascended before, it was all meaningless.

Only after the final ascension process was completely finished would all previous efforts have meaning.

"Ascension."

"Ascension."

Li Fan was located at the lowest depression in the Star Sea, but his gaze seemed to have instantly leaped out of its confines.

The entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea, surrounded by the High Wall, appeared before him in a miniature form.

"Could it be that King Xuan Tian's ultimate goal was the same as my plan in this life?"

"I intend to push the Xuanhuang Realm to sublimate and evolve into an Immortal Domain."

"And King Xuan Tian..."

"Intended to directly sublimate the entire Star Sea?"

Li Fan himself found this sudden thought utterly absurd.

Only through personal experience could one truly understand the immense gap between mortals and immortals.

Let's carefully count the preparations Li Fan had made in this life to foster the birth of the Xuanhuang Immortal Domain.

The life force nourishing the myriad remaining realms, the explosive Star Force stored and echoed in the depressions.

The legacy of the Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate, Immortal Spiritual Energy.

The return of countless small worlds, all converging into one.

Even a complete Immortal Domain fragment, from the hand of an unknown True Immortal...

With such a multitude of factors, Li Fan dared not guarantee that the creation of the Xuanhuang Immortal Domain would be 100% successful.

The Star Sea, compared to the Xuanhuang Realm, was not even on the same scale.

If one were to truly attempt to sublimate the Star Sea into an Immortal Realm...

The required energy was simply unimaginable!

Even if Li Fan possessed the ultimate treasure 'Returning to True,' which could continuously collect all the resources within the current Star Sea,

Li Fan could not even see a glimmer of hope for success before his psychological lifespan was completely exhausted.

"Ultimately, it's just my own groundless fantasy."

"Unless..."

"King Xuan Tian saw something that I cannot yet see."

For some reason, Li Fan suddenly thought this.

"Brother Mo, are you staying here to accompany Xu Ke next?"

In the crevice hollow, after another long period of silence, it was finally Li Fan who broke the quiet.

Mo Rubing withdrew his gaze from Xu Ke's determined back, remaining silent for a long time.

"We have tried all possible methods."

"Although it is difficult to admit, at present, it seems that King Xuan Tian has most likely vanished into that mysterious pond."

"He no longer exists in the current Utmost Darkness Star Sea."

"Although King Xuan Tian is gone, I will never sit idly by. However, to save the Xuanhuang Realm from now on, it will completely depend on ourselves!" Li Fan sighed slightly.

Mo Rubing, however, remained optimistic: "Since Brother Xuanyuan made such a contingency plan, he would not have met with misfortune so easily. I think the key still lies in that peculiar pond."

"I must return to the Xuanhuang Realm to continue my research."

Li Fan nodded slightly, looking at Xu Ke once more.

"Regarding Xu Ke, you can rest assured. I will arrange for people to come here periodically to heal him, ensuring he is in the best possible condition to continue this endless excavation," Li Fan said in a deep voice.

"You also heard just now that Xu Ke addressed me as 'Sacred Master.' "

"It's just that I happened to save some young children in the process of saving the Xuanhuang Realm, and then casually taught them. I am truly unworthy of the title 'Sacred Master,' and I have made Brother Mo laugh." Li Fan said dismissively.

Mo Rubing nodded, not paying much attention to this matter.

At his urging, Li Fan first took him back to the Xuanhuang Realm.

Standing by the fishing pond, he began to study it carefully again. It seemed that although Xing Wuque had perished, the traces he left behind had given Mo Rubing great encouragement.

"King Xuan Tian is truly a charismatic person."

"Some worked tirelessly for him for ten thousand years, fighting to their last breath. Others remain blindly confident in him."

Li Fan snorted inwardly. He openly set up an immortal formation to protect the fishing pond.

Under the guise of preventing outsiders from disturbing Mo Rubing's enlightenment of the pond's mysteries.

In reality, the true purpose of the formation was to suppress Mo Rubing at a critical moment!

In this life, as the Xuanhuang Realm sublimated, nothing must be allowed to be fished out of the fishing pond!

As for Mo Rubing, it would likely be a while before he discovered the secret of the fishing pond.

Li Fan remained lost in thought, still pondering that commonality of nature.

A subconscious intuition told him that the similarity between Xing Wuque's mask and the First Generation Great Heavenly Venerate hid a great secret.

Li Fan returned to the small world of Great Xuan, looking at the myriad beings within the world, lost in thought.

He even put aside the work of fusing the Immortal Realm fragments for the time being.

Days turned into nights, and three months passed in the blink of an eye.

Li Fan still had no gains.

Just as he was about to shake his head and give up, his gaze suddenly fell upon the clouds and mist rising within the small world.

"Clouds, mist, rain, ice. They are all different forms of water."

"This is the so-called similarity of nature."

"And then..."

Li Fan's tightly furrowed brow suddenly relaxed.

"I shouldn't be looking for the similarities between the bronze mask and the First Generation Great Heavenly Venerate."

"Instead, I should be looking for the similarities between the First Generation Great Heavenly Venerate and the bronze mask."

"The function of the bronze mask is to carve out crevices—the low points of 'momentum'—the dark rivers. This is the opposite of Ascension, it's descending momentum."

"Therefore..."

Li Fan's thoughts instantly became clear.

"The First Generation Xuanhuang Great Heavenly Venerate was also like this."

"Descending momentum..."

"From Immortal, descending momentum to mortal!"

[Rebirth] [High School] [Campus] [Daily Life] [Light Entertainment]

Li Luo is a 35-year-old unemployed... flexibly employed individual.

After graduation, he wrote novels, filmed short dramas, played music, delivered food, sold street snacks, and even worked as a customer service representative for an online lingerie store.

And now, Li Luo has been reborn back to the summer when he was 15 years old.

In this life, what is most important?

Making money! Making money! Making money!

But with the middle school entrance exam looming, he should focus on his studies first.

Chapter 1371: Immortal Chess Fusion Opens

“The First Generation Profound Yellow Great Heavenly Venerate did not descend as an immortal…”

“But rather, this immortal became mortal?”

In an instant, Li Fan’s mind was greatly shaken.

An immortal descending to the mortal realm, and an immortal becoming mortal – these two appear similar but have fundamental differences.

An immortal descending to the mortal realm is still a True Immortal, merely bound by the limits of what the mortal realm can endure.

But once one becomes mortal…

The immortal is no longer an immortal!

Becoming a True Immortal is the goal that all mortal cultivators dream of. Yet, in the ancient Profound Yellow Realm, there was such a True Immortal who chose to degrade himself and descend to the mortal world.

“The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation!” Li Fan’s mind flashed with this name.

Aside from evading that terrifying calamity that later destroyed the Immortal Realm, Li Fan could not think of any other reason for such an action.

“When the First Generation Profound Yellow Great Heavenly Venerate descended to mortality, there was still a considerable amount of time before the great tribulation of the Immortal Realm.”

“Such foresight, such courage!”

“This is a true True Immortal descending to the mortal world!” Li Fan couldn't help but exclaim in his heart.

But then Li Fan suddenly had another thought: “However, it cannot be ruled out that he was forced to do so. After all, from the True Immortal memories I obtained before, it is known that the Immortal Realm also has a strict hierarchy.”

“If it were merely to evade the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation for himself, theoretically, he would never have taken on the position of Profound Yellow Heavenly Venerate again.”

“It is obvious that the First Generation’s descent was to cooperate with the Immortal Realm in some plan.”

“And the Profound Yellow Realm was one of the testing grounds for this.”

Connecting this with the indeterminate rings seen in the Immortal Formation earlier, the Nine Star Red Pearls, and the countless frozen corpses controlled by the watcher.

Li Fan vaguely pieced everything together.

“Perhaps, the purpose of the Immortal Realm creating the Profound Yellow as a trial ground was not just to seek refuge.”

“They were also attempting to find a solution to the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.”

“However, judging by the final outcome, they failed.”

“The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation raged and spread in the Immortal Realm at a faster pace than imagined. Countless True Immortals perished within it.”

“But the lower realm, Profound Yellow, remained safe and sound. This caused the will of some immortals to resist the disaster to waver.”

“Hence, the subsequent Immortal Domain Fragment plan…”

Squinting his eyes and pondering, a bigger question arose in Li Fan’s mind.

“Did that First Generation Profound Yellow Great Heavenly Venerate truly die?”

The remnants of True Immortals had been passed down and controlled by successive Profound Yellow Heavenly Venerates.

Then what about the First Generation himself?

Mortals are different. Since the First Generation could leave behind descendants, he should have completely transformed into mortal flesh.

Could such a figure, like countless mortals, have simply disappeared into the river of history due to the exhaustion of his lifespan?

Or did he change his identity, conceal his name, and secretly observe everything from the shadows?

“It now appears that the close connection between the Profound Yellow Realm and the Immortal Realm is definitely related to this First Generation Heavenly Venerate. A True Immortal who descended in status and was banished, serving as a bridge of communication between immortality and mortality, secretly monitoring everything that happened in the Profound Yellow Realm.”

“And this True Immortal was also regulated by the Immortal Realm, perhaps harboring dissatisfaction, thus faking his death and escaping.”

“The second Profound Yellow Heavenly Venerate was no longer an immortal becoming mortal, but a chosen being from the Profound Yellow Realm…”

“Either the cost of an immortal becoming mortal was too high and could not be sustained. Or even in the Immortal Realm, the Profound Yellow Realm plan was a top secret, and not too many True Immortals could participate. They simply couldn't find anyone to descend.”

“Or perhaps, both are true.”

Recalling the mysterious character he saw in the You Clan bloodline earlier, Li Fan mused, “For an immortal to become mortal, it is far more than simply descending in status.”

“It also involves the [Transformation Between Immortality and Mortality].”

“That is a power almost on par with [Creation]…”

His thoughts raced. In an instant, Li Fan roughly reconstructed the possible truth regarding the Immortal Realm and Profound Yellow. Most of this was inferred from the commonality Li Fan grasped in an instant between the First Generation Great Heavenly Venerate and Xing Wuque’s descent. However, being able to correspond with the clues investigated before was enough to explain the matter.

“The banished immortal who has been hidden in secret all along…”

“But in my previous life, when the High Wall collapsed and the Star Sea was in turmoil, he still did not show his traces.”

“It seems that at this point in time, even the banished immortal does not exist in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.”

“Of course, it is not necessarily that he has perished. It is highly possible that he has already jumped beyond the High Wall!”

The Utmost Darkness Star Sea, as Li Fan’s current base of operations, appears relatively safe on the surface, which somewhat reassures Li Fan.

“You Clan members, since they are descendants of the First Generation Profound Yellow Great Heavenly Venerate.”

“Then, does the character technique [Manifest] have the ability to activate the bloodline connection between them and track that banished immortal?”

A dangerous idea suddenly appeared in Li Fan’s mind, but he quickly suppressed it.

“Now is not the time for such futile actions. Perhaps in the future, when I have the strength to begin exploring beyond the High Wall, I will consider this matter.”

From the fragmented clues, Li Fan caught a glimpse of the tip of the iceberg of the past Immortal Realm. While it made him even more curious about the Immortal Realm, it also brought him immense wariness towards the Immortal Domain Fragments he had already collected but had not yet assembled.

“If there were indeed True Immortals in the past who regarded the mortal realm as a breeding ground for evasion, then this disassembled and sealed Immortal Domain could very well become their hiding place…” Li Fan murmured inwardly, hesitating whether to activate the Immortal Domain Fragments left by Sun Piaomiao.

After pondering for a long time, he finally made up his mind, suppressing his hesitation.

“Such a blind box will eventually be opened someday.”

“Better sooner than later.”

“With the method of de-escalating Immortal Formations, and with numerous Immortal Formations at my disposal, even if any accidents occur, I can ensure that I can calmly activate Returning to True.”

“Moreover, there is another place in the Star Sea that is specialized against Immortals…” Li Fan’s eyes flashed with a sharp light.

He summoned Liu Ruchen and the other descendants of the Medicine King Sect, carrying all the Immortal Domain Fragments. Under the shroud of the wooden sword phantom, he enveloped them and moved to the center of the Star Sea.

The phantom solidified, manifesting the scene of a clear sky and ordinary world during the day. He did not let the Medicine King Sect members perceive their predicament.

Only Li Fan, alone, could see the terrifying boundless dark energy not far away.

“The rate of spread is faster than expected.”

“Moreover, the outer edge of this dark energy region…” Li Fan observed for a while, comparing it to what he had seen before, and couldn’t help but frown slightly.

He had seen the precursor to the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation here more than once before, but from a great distance, he only felt a sense of crisis when he "witnessed" the dark energy.

But now, even if he shifted his gaze and did not look directly at the boundless dark energy.

Li Fan still felt an inexplicable sense of dread, emerging like a tide.

The sense of crisis lingered, and the Profound Yellow Immortal Heart Incantation could not dispel it.

Moreover, the longer he stayed, the stronger it accumulated.

Suppressing the instinct to flee, Li Fan savored this concrete feeling.

“It feels like a precarious wall crumbling, a great edifice about to collapse, and I am beneath this perilous wall, beneath this great edifice…”

Under intense crisis, Li Fan advanced instead of retreating. The wooden sword phantom reached the edge of the continuously churning and expanding sea of dark energy.

“Let’s begin,” Li Fan said calmly to Liu Ruchen and the others within the wooden sword phantom.

Unaware of their situation, the Medicine King Sect disciples looked at the floating light clusters ahead with dazed expressions.

Entangled by golden chains, a seven-colored chess piece, a white chess piece, and six gray chess pieces were all present.

“These are the Immortal Realm fragments left by our ancestor!” With trembling hearts, the Medicine King Sect members, under Li Fan's instruction, began the fusion of the Immortal Domain Fragments, about to unravel the ancient Immortal Realm secrets left by Sun Piaomiao.

With Liu Ruchen's [World-Saving Longevity Scripture]’s longevity and pure power as the guide, they first fused the six gray chess pieces, each sealed individually.

The process was surprisingly smooth. Similar to Li Fan’s previous fusion results, the six gray pieces merged to form a larger seven-colored chess piece.

Now, only two six-in-one seven-colored chess pieces remained on the field, along with the crucial white chess piece that had transformed from the Medicine King Cauldron.

The white chess piece seemed to be stimulated by the other two fused chess pieces, its edges constantly rippling with seven-colored light.

Although it was a size smaller than the seven-colored chess pieces, it served as the core.

The restraining golden chains were on the verge of breaking.

Li Fan’s figure retreated rapidly, simultaneously releasing the seal.

The eyes of the Medicine King Sect disciples were filled with fervor as they manipulated the two seven-colored chess pieces, guarding and delivering them to the side of the white chess piece.

In an instant, the light halo around the white chess piece’s edge expanded outwards by a circle.

It engulfed the two seven-colored chess pieces.

In the field, only the final chess piece remained.

*Hummm…* A low, almost imperceptible humming sound began to emanate from this chess piece.

Through layer upon layer of Immortal Formations, Li Fan meticulously observed this newly formed chess piece.

Strangely, all the chess pieces had been annexed, yet the expected Immortal Domain did not directly manifest.

However, Li Fan was very certain that the fusion was successful.

Because he sensed that the “weight” of the Immortal Domain not far away was continuously increasing.

The wooden sword phantom and the encompassing Immortal Formation were both on the verge of collapse. Under the influence of the Immortal Domain, they could shatter at any moment.

Just as Li Fan was about to inject more power, at least to maintain it until the true Immortal Domain appeared.

A peculiar protective power was released from the final white chess piece.

It directly enveloped the wooden sword phantom and the Immortal Formation.

It was as if they had entered another layer of space, and the pressure of the Immortal Domain’s power naturally disappeared. Li Fan, however, remained outside the scope of the Immortal Domain.

Using the wooden sword phantom as his eyes, he peered into the scene within the Immortal Domain. Strictly speaking, the wooden sword phantom had not truly entered the Immortal Domain; it was merely that the Immortal Domain had erected pillars of protection for them.

The Medicine King Sect disciples, still in shock, received the same treatment.

Like a folded piece of paper slowly unfolding, the light released by the chess piece representing the Immortal Domain grew brighter and brighter.

It even pushed back the continuous dark energy that was about to spread from not far away.

Li Fan retreated rapidly again, avoiding these rays of light from shining upon himself.

The radiance of the Immortal Domain, unlike ordinary light, did not continue to extend infinitely into the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

It expanded to a certain area and then stopped.

From a distance, it looked like a giant ball of light floating at the edge of the sea of dark energy.

This white light was too dazzling, even blinding the perception of the wooden sword phantom Li Fan had placed within it.

Li Fan vaguely saw countless blurry, shifting images within it.

Like people, not like people. Like scenery, not like scenery.

Just as Li Fan was anticipating the imminent appearance of the Immortal Domain.

The sea of dark energy, previously repelled by the Immortal Domain's radiance, suddenly became turbulent.

The dark tide surged, its expansion accelerating.

The rolling dark energy instantly reached the edge of the Immortal Domain’s light sphere.

And the Immortal Domain, which was about to manifest, as if sensing something extremely terrifying, suddenly retracted its radiance.

From a giant ball of light, it reverted back to the white-rimmed chess piece.

Then, to the stunned disbelief of the Medicine King Sect disciples, it transformed into a beam of white light and shot through the sky, rapidly fleeing.

In the eyes of the Medicine King Sect disciples, the sky was naturally the wooden sword phantom and the Immortal Formation defenses Li Fan had set up.

The means that could temporarily trap the Heavenly Physician were actually unable to obstruct this beam of white light even for a moment.

Just as the Immortal Domain chess piece was about to disappear into the Star Sea, a giant finger descended from the sky, breaking through space and firmly pressing down on it!

It was exactly Li Fan’s Nine Heavens Descending Dust Finger!

Perhaps sensing the aura of the Supreme Dao emanating from the Nine Heavens Descending Dust Finger, or perhaps because the threat from the dark energy had been removed.

In any case, after a slight tremor, the white light stopped struggling.

It also retracted all its aura fluctuations.

It floated silently in the air.

“This reaction… is a bit too strong.”

“It must be the appearance of the dark energy that stimulated some kind of obstruction.”

“The unfolding of the Immortal Domain has failed.” Li Fan understood after observing for a moment.

This temporary failure did not mean the Immortal Domain chess piece had lost its function. It was merely lying dormant for the time being.

However, from the moment it was about to unfold, Li Fan had already glimpsed some scenes within the Immortal Domain.

“It is basically certain that there are no living beings within this Immortal Domain.”

“The scenario I was worried about, with slumbering True Immortals lurking within, will not occur.”

“However, besides the most basic Immortal Realm laws, the most obvious thing within this Immortal Domain is…” Li Fan frowned, extending his hand as if gesturing.

“These floating light shadows…”

“Are True Immortal script characters?” Li Fan was somewhat uncertain.

From the fleeting scenes of the Immortal Domain he glimpsed earlier, Li Fan saw many moving black lines. Having deeply studied True Immortal script characters for a long time, Li Fan naturally recognized at a glance that those were the structures appearing in various True Immortal script characters.

“True Immortal script characters are, in essence, the materialization of laws.”

“And when materialized True Immortal script characters decompose and revert back into laws…”

“Is this the process of the chess piece unfolding into an Immortal Domain?” Li Fan suddenly understood.

An Immortal Domain chess piece could actually be seen as a superposition of countless True Immortal script characters!

At the same time, Li Fan’s heart stirred.

To be able to construct a complete Immortal Domain, the number of True Immortal script characters contained within this chess piece was likely beyond imagination!

“The True Immortal who created this chess piece in ancient times was no ordinary individual!”

Chapter 1372: Medicine King Stone Pill Secret

“Perhaps it was the work of that Master of Dao Inscription!”

“After all, each True Immortal inscription corresponds to a law of the Immortal Realm. And one who can pile and fuse so many characters so casually…”

Li Fan’s expression grew solemn as he levitated the Immortal Domain chess piece.

All the divine and sacred aura that had emanated from it disappeared with the cessation of its unfolding. The chess piece now felt like an ordinary object, resting silently in Li Fan’s palm.

He attempted to stimulate it again, but the Immortal Domain chess piece showed no reaction to external stimuli.

“Indeed, it still requires the Long Life Pure Essence of the Medicine King Sect.”

“Moreover, the unfolding of the Immortal Domain chess piece itself consumes a certain kind of energy. The recently failed unfolding process requires time to accumulate energy again.”

Li Fan toyed with the smooth, cold chess piece, contemplating inwardly.

Far away, in the center of the Star Sea. The sea of black energy, stirred by the aura of the Immortal Domain, had not subsided with the retreat of the Immortal Domain’s unfolding.

Instead, as if a “fast forward” button had been pressed, the rolling black energy continued to spread outwards irreversibly.

It seemed intent on swallowing the entire Star Sea in one go.

Li Fan’s brow furrowed. After a moment of thought, he employed the [Grand Preceptor's Divine Technique] at this location.

Due to the frequent use of the Profound Immortal Boat, the consciousness of the Star Sea had lost interest in responding to Li Fan’s communications.

However, from the limited sensory feedback…

The True Will of the Star Sea's origin seemed utterly oblivious to the encroaching tide of black energy flooding the Star Sea's center!

This blind indifference struck Li Fan with a sense of dread.

It was as if his body was being gnawed by countless black insects, yet the owner remained completely unaware.

Such a bizarre scenario could only indicate that the true nature of the black energy far surpassed the True Will of the Star Sea's origin.

And what Li Fan witnessed as “black energy” was merely its external manifestation.

“A precursor to the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation…”

“The time remaining for me is likely not much.”

A trace of apprehension flashed in Li Fan’s eyes. He gathered the Medicine King Sect disciples, who were still shrouded by the wooden sword phantom, and returned them to the Profound Yellow Realm.

“Senior, just now…” The Medicine King Sect Master, Liu Ruchen, hesitated to speak.

Having been completely enveloped by the illusion of the wooden sword phantom, the Medicine King Sect disciples were utterly unaware that they had, in a short span of time, traversed the center of the Star Sea.

From their perspective, the Immortal Chess was merely obstructed during its fusion, and ultimately shattered the sky before tearing through space and departing.

Li Fan’s expression was calm. “No need to worry, I have intercepted and reacquired the Immortal Domain Chess Piece…”

Liu Ruchen couldn't help but breathe a sigh of relief upon hearing this.
