Li Fan sighed slightly, “We were perhaps a bit too optimistic. The Immortal Domain Chess Piece left by Sun Piaomiao is not so easily brought back into the world. The backlash from the recent failed unfolding almost cost us our lives. Fortunately, I managed to block it.”

Although Liu Ruchen and the others could not see the rolling sea of black energy, they had all felt the sense of impending doom.

They all nodded in agreement, “Thank you, Senior, for your timely rescue.”

Li Fan waved his hand, “It was nothing! What matters now is how to successfully unfold the Immortal Domain Chess Piece. Junior Sun Piaomiao must have left behind some clues.”

“It is a pity that later generations did not attach importance to it, leading to the severance of crucial information.”

The disciples of the Medicine King Sect all displayed expressions of shame.

Ever since learning of the ancestor Mo Da Shen Tong’s grand plan, they had been constantly delving into the past, trying to find any overlooked clues related to Sun Piaomiao.

Hoping to uncover other valuable leads.

But too much time had passed. Aside from that travelogue, the Medicine King Sect ancestor only existed in the teachings passed down by word of mouth, yielding no effective results.

“Senior, I believe that if there truly is any hidden information we have failed to discover, it should exist within the Medicine King Sect’s ancestral grounds!” Liu Ruchen suddenly declared.

“Back then, I left in haste. To avoid detection by the Ten Sects, I only took the useful items from the sect. As for other things, they were simply left behind…”

Liu Ruchen’s suggestion was echoed by other Medicine King Sect members.

“The former Medicine King Sect grounds…” Li Fan mused for a moment, then, with the assistance of several of his reconciled disciples, instantly transported them to the destination.

On the desolate land, piles of rubble lay scattered. Weeds grew wild, making it impossible to discern that this place, ten thousand years ago, was the renowned Medicine King Sect.

However, Li Fan had previously obtained the precise location of the Medicine King Sect from Jiao Xiu.

“This is the Grand Hall… the Alchemy Pavilion, the Forging Mountain…”

After much identification, the Medicine King Sect members finally recognized remnants of their past within the surviving structures, their voices filled with nostalgia and regret.

“Although there isn't a single statue of our ancestor within the entire Medicine King Sect, I recall my master mentioning a place related to the ancestor…” Liu Ruchen frowned, trying to recall his memories.

Scanning his surroundings, attempting to jog his childhood recollections.

Li Fan, having previously scoured Liu Ruchen’s soul, instantly recalled the person in question, “Are you referring to the place where Sun Piaomiao used to refine medicine?”

“Ah, yes, yes!” Liu Ruchen exclaimed, nodding eagerly.

“When I first refined medicine back then, because I succeeded on my first try and achieved a high-grade result, I became quite smug. However, my master reprimanded me, stating that when Patriarch Piaomiao succeeded in his alchemy, celestial phenomena would descend, and the aroma of his pills would travel for ten thousand miles. Just a single breath of it could grant a weak effect; it was even rumored that pills could gain sentience and develop their own consciousness. The gap between my master and the ancestor was immeasurable. Upon hearing this, my arrogance instantly vanished…”

“The ancestor refined countless pills but left none behind, distributing them all to those in need in the world, thus embodying 'healing the world with an inverted pot and benefiting all living beings.'”

“But the place where the ancestor often refined medicine was respected by our descendants. Even after the ancestor disappeared, we did not occupy or utilize it. This custom, established over time, led to disciples forgetting the origin of the rule, only knowing it was a forbidden area of the sect…”

Liu Ruchen explained as he searched for the target.

“Ah, found it, it’s here.” Liu Ruchen’s aura surged, unearthing the buried ruins of a structure.

Even after ten thousand years, Li Fan could still faintly discern the past appearance of this structure.

It was revealed to be a colossal square stone.

“When the ancestor refined medicine, it is said he did not need an alchemy furnace. He used spiritual energy as fire and heaven and earth as a furnace. However, he liked to sit cross-legged on this large stone when refining pills.”

“Over time, this stone became imbued with an indelible scent of alchemy. Later, our Medicine King Sect built a structure around this stone to protect it.”

“However, all the successive Patriarchs had inspected it, and this stone was indeed just an ordinary rock.”

Liu Ruchen sniffed the air, his face beaming with joy, “You smell it? Even after ten thousand years, there’s still a faint fragrance.”

Li Fan enveloped the square giant stone with his divine sense, meticulously examining it. He, too, could smell the faint fragrance.

But this stone, unlike Sun Piaomiao’s other relics, was not concealed by any mysterious means.

It was truly just an ordinary stone.

Of course, the method of verification was simple.

A sword glow flickered from his fingertip, striking the square giant stone.

In an instant, the stone disintegrated into countless particles of dust.

Liu Ruchen, who had been speaking volubly, abruptly stopped.

However, facing Li Fan’s cold and indifferent expression, he dared not say more.

Watching the stone powder drift and settle in the air.

Li Fan, ever cautious, re-examined it. It was indeed just ordinary dust and fragments.

The faint fragrance also originated from these fragments themselves.

There was truly no anomaly detected.

“You guessed wrong, this stone holds no special properties. Let’s think of other possibilities.” Li Fan finally spoke, his tone indifferent.

Liu Ruchen nodded sheepishly.

The other elders also showed a hint of embarrassment, rejoining the search for other potential clues within the Medicine King Sect’s former grounds.

Except for one person.

This person’s attention, far from being diverted by Li Fan’s conclusion, seemed to grow more curious as he observed the scattered stone dust.

“Senior…” he began.

Li Fan looked at him with interest, and information about him surfaced in his mind.

One of the Medicine King Sect's Harmonized Dao cultivators, Ruan Tianxiao.

Unlike other elders who used spiritual plants for medicine, Ruan Tianxiao habitually used animal and demonic beast bodies, as well as human bodily tissues, for his concoctions.

While the effects were indeed extraordinary, the scent of blood and killing intent was too strong, and it was quite unconventional.

Therefore, Ruan Tianxiao’s “flesh pills” were not widely accepted.

“Feel free to speak.” Li Fan encouraged him.

“That ancestral square giant stone, after being shattered, actually resembles a pill.”

“In its stone form, it was still in the process of alchemy. Only upon crushing the stone did the pill finally become complete…” Ruan Tianxiao articulated his thoughts carefully.

“Elder Ruan, how can you speak such nonsense before Senior?”

“Indeed, according to your theory, why did the scent of alchemy weaken after the giant stone was shattered?”

“Where is the pill?” After observing for a while, the Harmonized Dao cultivators of the Medicine King Sect voiced their objections.

Ruan Tianxiao did not argue but smiled faintly, “To verify whether these fragments are truly pills…”

“One only needs to swallow them!”

“Senior, I am willing to test the medicine myself!”

The Medicine King Sect members fell silent instantly.

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, appraising Ruan Tianxiao. He extended his right hand, and a gust of invisible wind swept through,

Gathering all the giant stone fragments into a stone ball.

He tossed it in his hand, and Li Fan sensed it one last time, “It’s still stone.”

“Are you certain this is a pill?”

Ruan Tianxiao stared intently at the stone pill in Li Fan’s hand, nodding. “I have tested medicines on myself for many years. Over time, my body develops an inexplicable connection with beneficial pills.

“In my eyes, the fragrance from this stone pill surpasses that of any pill I have encountered in my life by thousands of times!”

Ruan Tianxiao stated with absolute certainty.

Li Fan, however, fell into deep thought.

He suddenly recalled Mo Rubing, who had been unable to uncover the mystery of the fishing pond despite numerous attempts.

Without the perspective of a fisherman, one could not perceive the secrets of the fishing pond.

Similarly, without the perspective of an alchemist, one could not discover the secret of this stone pill.

“Interesting.”

–

Feeling unwell, that’s all for today.

Recommending a new book by Gu Zhenren, already ten thousand words and well-developed.

Within the volcano, a mechanical immortal palace left by a wise ancient being awaits its successor.

The mother sacrificed her life to obtain the Immortal Palace Seal, leaving it to Ning Zhuo before her death.

My Buddha Heart Demonic Seal!

To save oneself is Buddhism, to save others is demonization.

With this seal, one can engrave heart imprints and command mechanical creations with minimal burden. Ordinary people find commanding them extremely taxing, but Ning Zhuo can command myriad things with ease.

Ning Zhuo: “Mother, I will definitely not fail your trust and will obtain that immortal palace!”

As the poem goes:

Immortal companions communicate spiritually, intricate craftsmanship achieves ultimate reason.

Opening the universe reveals new realms, where worldly wonders match the heavens.

Ancient bells transmit the Dharma, moonlit dances bring pure radiance.

True selves embody myriad forms, who in the human world can match?

Chapter 1373: Scripture of the Medicine King Who Refines the Dao

"The Stone Pill's concealment methods are surprisingly similar to those of the Fishing Pond. Perhaps Sun Piaomiao's strength and foundation are even greater than imagined."

As Li Fan mused in secret, the stone pill in his eyes instantly transformed.

Formations and pills originated from the same source.

Li Fan's mastery of formations had reached unparalleled heights, even touching upon the realm of Immortals. By extension, although he had not formally studied alchemy, he was far superior to ordinary alchemists.

Moreover, medicine and alchemy were intertwined, and Li Fan had deeply grasped the true teachings of Heavenly Physicians...

At this moment, with Ruan Tianxiao's reminder, Li Fan seemed to have transformed into an alchemist.

Heaven and Earth became his pill furnace, and the round stone in his hand truly transformed into a crystal-clear pill!

Instantly, the previously faint aroma of the pill became thousands of times more potent.

Saliva involuntarily flowed from his mouth, and Li Fan's throat surged with the urge to swallow this pill directly.

"It seems this Stone Pill is truly a gift left by Sun Piaomiao for his descendants..."

This thought flashed through Li Fan's mind, and he then threw the pill in his hand to Ruan Tianxiao.

"Then you shall try this medicine!" he said calmly, completely unaffected by the pill's allure.

Ruan Tianxiao trembled uncontrollably with excitement. Fearing Li Fan would change his mind, he immediately swallowed the Stone Pill.

The members of the Medicine King Sect, who had gradually regained their senses, all displayed expressions of deep regret.

After Ruan Tianxiao consumed the Stone Pill, his demeanor and temperament instantly changed, as if he had become a different person.

Standing with his hands behind his back, his eyes swept lightly over everyone present, his face filled with nostalgic reminiscence.

Though standing before them, he seemed not to occupy the same space as them, ethereal and otherworldly, like a celestial being descended from the heavens.

Such a pronounced change did not escape the notice of Li Fan and the others present.

However, their speculations were too extraordinary, and they suppressed them in their hearts, daring not to voice them.

"Sun, Piaomiao," Li Fan finally uttered these three words slowly.

Concurrently, the phantom of the wooden sword was quietly prepared, ready to flee at any moment.

Ruan Tianxiao, whose very essence had been altered by the Stone Pill, as if possessed by the sect ancestor Sun Piaomiao, after a brief moment of reminiscing, sat cross-legged in the air.

He began to expound.

"Indeed, a pill is a transformation of the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth; a medicine remedies the ailments of all things in the world. The Great Dao is formless, unchanging, and ceaselessly cycles. Through the pill, it integrates; through medicine, it manifests. Heaven and Earth themselves? Are but a single pill formula."

The very first sentence captivated everyone present.

Including Li Fan.

His vigilance did not lessen, and Li Fan frowned, meticulously memorizing every word Sun Piaomiao spoke.

"The Dao has life, the Dao has death. The Dao lives and dies, the Dao manifests and vanishes; like a pill is born, like a pill is formed."

"The moment the pill is formed, it is death disguised as life. It is the shadow of the Great Dao, the corpse of the Great Dao."

...

Ruan Tianxiao spoke at a leisurely pace, and before him, a phantom image of a pill furnace appeared.

Within the furnace, one could see the sun rising and setting, stars drifting in the sea of stars. One could see the birth and death of all things, the rise and fall of Heaven and Earth.

And as the light continuously extinguished and rekindled, the cycles displayed accelerated.

Finally, they converged into a single point.

It was like an infinite, dark void, or perhaps blindingly brilliant, or perhaps a fusion of both.

"Life and death are one, integrating with the Dao."

"Free from worldly constraints, my pill is complete."

Upon uttering these final words, the phantom pill furnace exploded and scattered.

A scorching storm, as if real, swept across.

Though merely an illusion, it caused Li Fan's beard and hair to flutter.

The onlookers all saw within it the rise and fall of starry seas and the Great Dao.

Like brilliant fireworks, gone in an instant.

The ethereal and transcendent aura emanating from Ruan Tianxiao also dissipated with the vanishing of the illusion.

"Uh..." Ruan Tianxiao awoke as if from a dream, letting out a groan of pain.

He pressed his forehead, seemingly enduring immense agony. Blood gushed from his seven orifices.

Li Fan even observed that Ruan Tianxiao's soul seemed to have been filled and ravaged by something, left with numerous cracks.

However, the mysterious energy absorbed from swallowing the Stone Pill nourished and helped it heal.

Otherwise, Ruan Tianxiao, with his mere Harmonized Dao cultivation, would likely have had his soul annihilated.

Seeing this, the members of the Medicine King Sect rushed forward to tend to him.

Li Fan's thoughts, however, remained fixated on the profound text that Sun Piaomiao had expounded through Ruan Tianxiao's body.

"Life and death are one, integrating with the Dao. Free from worldly constraints, my pill is complete." Li Fan repeatedly murmured the last sentence, a rare surge of excitement welling up in his heart.

"Marvelous, indescribably marvelous. This scripture of Sun Piaomiao, compared to the Heavenly Physician's discourse, is far superior."

"This passage..."

Li Fan frowned, about to name this passage, when a word naturally sprang into his mind.

It was the single choice that would inevitably arise in the minds of all living beings who heard this passage.

"The Scripture of Alchemy and Medicine King."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, savoring these five words while his heart grew exceptionally solemn.

"The Scripture of Alchemy and Medicine King is clearly Sun Piaomiao's fundamental esoteric legacy. Compared to it, that so-called Scripture of Worldly Longevity is simply like a child's primer, crude and vulgar."

"It is not merely a cultivation technique, but a strategic ideology that directly reaches the origin of the Great Dao. Like the Record of Mending Heaven, although it does not mention any specific cultivation methods, as long as one's comprehension is not too poor, they can all deduce suitable cultivation techniques and divine abilities for themselves."

With Li Fan's current experiences and accumulated knowledge, he was still constantly bombarded with inspiration and thoughts while comprehending the Scripture of Alchemy and Medicine King.

The subtlety and profoundness of this method were truly remarkable.

It was like being caught in a storm of thought, which only gradually subsided after three days and three nights.

Moreover, residual sparks of inspiration continued to flicker occasionally.

Li Fan recorded all the ideas that had emerged, preserving them.

Only then did he have the leisure to review everything that had just happened.

At the same time, unavoidable doubts arose in his heart.

"Is Sun Piaomiao still alive in this world?"

Although Ruan Tianxiao seemed possessed just now, seemingly a legacy left by Sun Piaomiao from an ancient era through the Stone Pill, Li Fan inexplicably felt as if Sun Piaomiao had truly descended through Ruan Tianxiao's body from some unknowable distant place at that very moment.

"The Scripture of Alchemy and Medicine King makes no mention of ascension, yet it vividly describes a power that transcends the mortal realm."

"I would rather believe that this was a new scripture created by the current Sun Piaomiao, with ten thousand years of accumulated knowledge, rather than something Sun Piaomiao had already comprehended back then..."

While Li Fan was in deep thought, the members of the Medicine King Sect, who were helping Ruan Tianxiao recover, excitedly discussed the Scripture of Alchemy and Medicine King.

"Alchemy involves refining Heaven and Earth, much like refining pills. My previous understanding of the Dao of Pills was truly too superficial!"

"I never imagined that our Medicine King Sect's true legacy would be so extraordinary. We have allowed it to be tarnished for thousands of years... truly a sin, a sin."

...

While everyone was engaged in heated discussion, Liu Ruchen quietly approached Li Fan.

"Senior, I believe I understand why the unfolding of the Immortal Domain Chess Piece encountered problems before."

"If we liken that process to alchemy, it's as if the alchemical fire was manipulated too intensely, too hastily, too impatiently. It requires gentle tempering with a slow flame, step by step." said Liu Ruchen with newfound confidence.

Li Fan did not expose him, merely nodding slightly.

"There's no rush. Sun Piaomiao's legacy is profound and extensive. Even I have benefited greatly; you should all take this opportunity to comprehend and digest it."

Liu Ruchen cupped his hands, about to rejoin the other elders in discussing the Scripture of Alchemy and Medicine King.

Before departing, Liu Ruchen hesitated, then whispered, "Senior, is Ancestor Piaomiao still alive?"

It seemed that Li Fan was not the only one who had experienced an illusion. Li Fan did not answer directly, but instead gave Liu Ruchen a meaningful smile.

Subsequently, the members of the Medicine King Sect, while exchanging their insights, scoured the former grounds of the Medicine King Sect inch by inch.

They attempted to find any other legacies left behind by Sun Piaomiao.

Alas, that Stone Pill seemed to be Sun Piaomiao's only remaining inheritance.

With nothing found, Li Fan, along with the Harmonized Dao elders of the Medicine King Sect, returned to the Da Qi small world.

They either entered secluded cultivation or began refining pills, eager to translate their insights into tangible gains.

"Alchemy..."

If these Harmonized Dao elders could achieve such enlightenment, how much more could Li Fan achieve?

He looked towards the Xuanhuang Realm, and the inspirations that had been suppressed and recorded earlier now erupted in full force.

"In this life, the process of sublimating the Xuanhuang Realm into an Immortal Domain, as I originally planned, can, in a sense, be considered alchemy."

"Adding ingredients, tempering with external forces, and then... the pill is formed."

Li Fan's eyes gleamed with excitement, and unprecedented understanding surged in like a tide.

"However, my final choice to integrate with the essence of the Xuanhuang Immortal Domain's heaven and earth was like 'buying a gem box and returning the gem.' I discarded the most precious pill after its formation."

"Instead, I merely licked its pill inscription and consumed its residue..."

Li Fan pondered, and as this thought emerged, an uncontrollable desire to swallow the future Xuanhuang Immortal Domain as a pill arose within him.

And it was uncontainable.

From the moment the thought appeared, it could no longer be suppressed.

His heart leaped with joy, urging Li Fan to act quickly.

Li Fan's mind instantly became alert. He closed his eyes, forcefully suppressing the budding impulse.

"The line of thought and the idea are indeed correct."

"Unfortunately..."

"This Xuanhuang Immortal Domain, this immortal pill, is not something just anyone can swallow."

"Even with my current capabilities, exhausting all my trump cards, I still might not be able to achieve it."

Li Fan was not blinded by the immense potential gain; he still had a clear understanding of his own strength.

"Even if swallowed, the Immortal Domain will inevitably lead to indigestion and explosion, resulting in death."

"Hmph, how could I be so foolish?"

Bit by bit, the Scripture of Alchemy and Medicine King flashed through Li Fan's mind again.

"Sun Piaomiao can be called the foremost alchemist in the world."

"But his limit was, after all, only to refine pills in one lifetime."

"As for me..."

The words of the Scripture of Alchemy and Medicine King instantly turned into starlight, swirling and tumbling as Li Fan absorbed them.

"With the aid of [Returning to True], I can refine pills in the second, third... life!"

"From this aspect, I possess an unparalleled advantage over anyone else in the world!"

"I am naturally destined to be the foremost alchemist!"

His gaze refocused on the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan's thoughts racing.

"Even if in this lifetime, I am destined not to directly consume the Xuanhuang Immortal Pill."

"But I can use the methods of alchemy to make the sublimation process of the Xuanhuang Realm more harmonious and smooth. The methods planned before can still be executed. However, compared to the current situation, they seem a bit too crude."

"Moreover..."

"The experience accumulated in this lifetime can be fully utilized in the next, and even subsequent lives."

"Alchemists in the world, to refine a good pill, rack their brains day and night. Once they start refining, there is no turning back. There are only two outcomes: success or failure."

"But I can continue to refine the same pill, until it reaches its theoretical peak."

In Li Fan's vision, a colossal purple-gold pill furnace suddenly appeared, enshrouding Heaven and Earth.

The majestic Xuanhuang Heaven and Earth, all beings and myriad things, all became a single pill within this purple-gold furnace!

"Now, all that remains is to wait for the right time to ignite the fire!"

Sensing it, in the small world, the number of beings covered by the Jun Tian ritual had met the requirements of the Profound Immortal Boat.

Li Fan, like lightning, streaked towards the edge of the Star Sea.

Not long after, he returned to the vicinity of the Profound Immortal Boat, deliberately releasing his aura.

"Hm? The aura on you..."

"It seems you've gained some new insights?"

Perhaps due to their shared participation in the Jun Tian ritual, Zhong Daogong and the other elders of the Immortal Boat were extremely perceptive to the subtle changes in Li Fan's aura.

Li Fan, unlike before, did not reveal everything.

He merely smiled in response.

"The goal of encompassing beings for the Jun Tian ritual has been achieved; we can initiate it at any time."

"When shall we draw upon the power of the Star Sea?"

"I've waited too long; I'm getting impatient."

Without suggesting entering the Immortal Boat, Li Fan went straight to the point.

After a brief silence, the elders of the Immortal Boat replied.

"We... still need to make some preparations."

"Seven days later, outside the Immortal Boat, we shall commence."

"Fellow Daoist might as well rest inside in the meantime."

Li Fan shook his head, refusing courteously, "No need, I shall wait here."

"Recently, while communicating with the Star Sea, I've gained new insights. Being inside the Immortal Boat would be detrimental rather than beneficial."

The Immortal Boat crew did not insist, and the atmosphere fell into an awkward silence.

Meanwhile, Li Fan stood in the Star Sea, closing his eyes in contemplation.

As if he were truly comprehending something.

Seven days later, the elders emerged one by one.

After exchanging nods with Li Fan, they began preparing the ritual in the void outside the Immortal Boat.

White paper flags were placed by them in a peculiar order.

Li Fan clearly saw that the flags were inscribed with over a dozen overlapping True Immortal script characters.

Li Fan was familiar with each True Immortal script character.

But the way they were fused and superimposed together seemed to impart a different meaning.

"Hm?"

Li Fan's heart stirred as he recalled the Immortal Domain Chess Piece, still sealed in the Great Xuan Realm.

It was also a superposition of True Immortal script characters, but the flags on the Immortal Boat were far simpler in comparison.

"But they should be sufficient to support the ritual."

Li Fan observed that each flag resembled a sharp needle,

Standing tall in the void, piercing fiercely into the Star Sea.

"Alas!"

With the ritual setup complete, the elders took their positions.

Zhong Daogong, leading them, flew into the center of the ritual.

He looked up and shouted.

Chapter 1374: The Heavenly Equal Stars

“As if the body becomes the universe, the intent roams the starry river. Supreme Emperor's Endless Form, Divine Roaming; Supreme Emperor's Endless Change, Divine Transformation; Supreme Emperor's Endless Void, Divine God…”

What Zhong Daogong began chanting like a poem was the [Supreme Emperor's Divine Technique] obtained by Master Yin from the black and white dual pearls, and later passed on by Li Fan to the Immortal Boat!

Previously, it was only a fragmented text. Now, this divine ability, specifically used to communicate with the consciousness of the Star Sea, had been perfected after research by all the elders of the Immortal Boat.

Combined with the power of True Immortal inscriptions, amplified by the ritual, its might had increased a hundredfold, a thousandfold!

Zhong Daogong led the chanting, and the elders of the Immortal Boat followed suit with their harmonies.

It was like a magnificent symphony, echoing within the Star Sea.

As the chanting voices changed, certain characters on the flags inscribed with fused True Immortal inscriptions would flicker in response.

It was as if a colossal entity composed of countless characters was breathing in and out!

Li Fan, witnessing this scene outside the ritual, suddenly understood the unique meaning he had felt before.

A single character, [Uniformity], hidden within the fused and superimposed True Immortal inscriptions at the scene, remained latent.

Only waiting…

Until the Star Sea consciousness was forcibly connected and descended. And then erupted unexpectedly!

The Jun Tian ritual, meticulously prepared by the Profound Immortal Boat, was, in essence, this simple and unpretentious.

But achieving it was far from easy.

Take the first step, forcing communication with the Star Sea consciousness. This alone far exceeded the capabilities of the [Supreme Emperor's Divine Technique]. Li Fan had also used this technique before, and relying on the accumulated goodwill of ten thousand years from the now-destroyed Taijia Realm, he had secured a promise from the Star Sea consciousness to help Xuanhuang sublimate and revive.

After that, the Star Sea never responded again.

But now, the Taijia Divine Technique, improved by the elders of the Immortal Boat, had directly opened the bridge between cultivators and the Star Sea. Forcing the true intent of the Star Sea source to cast its gaze this way!

The chanting grew louder, and Li Fan faintly sensed a massive vortex forming above the ritual.

Unlike the deathly silent Utmost Darkness Sea, within the vortex, light flickered, and life was boundless. Vague, incomprehensible roaring whispers also echoed.

The Star Sea space it occupied seemed to emit groans of unbearable strain.

And corresponding anomalies also emerged within Li Fan's body.

It was exactly the same as what happened before when he encountered the True Immortal's phantom after touching the immortal realm copper coin. Spiritual energy, body, and divine soul all boiled as if they would be vaporized at any moment!

“It’s just that before, when facing the True Immortal phantom, I could barely resist. But now…”

Li Fan took a deep breath and managed to suppress the anomaly within his body.

“Although the Star Sea's pressure is immense, it is ultimately not as powerful as a True Immortal.”

“Vast and magnificent, it is ultimately inferior to dimensional ascension and transformation!”

As numerous thoughts flashed through his mind, Zhong Daogong's voice suddenly echoed in Li Fan's ear, “Fellow Daoist, aren't you coming into the ritual yet!”

“Your contribution to the success of the Jun Tian ritual is immense. Now is the time to reap the fruits of your labor!”

It was not only Zhong Daogong's voice, but also the voices of Jian Daosheng, Nangong Lie, and all the other elders of the Immortal Boat, sounding in unison!

It sounded like an invitation, and also like a coercion.

“This is because the elders of the Immortal Boat have all come out, leaving the interior empty. They cannot leave me, a variable, outside, in case of unforeseen accidents?” Li Fan coldly snorted inwardly.

“Then I shall gratefully accept!” But he replied fearlessly and with a loud voice, flying into the ritual.

There was no need for him to find a suitable position himself.

The moment he entered the ritual, Li Fan felt countless flags around him constantly rotating and changing positions, "receiving" him into the ritual!

The chanting voices from all directions also forced him to subconsciously harmonize with them!

With everyone in their positions, the long-prepared Taijia ritual finally reached its climax. In the purple-gold swirling vortex, the previously roaring winds and thunder suddenly fell silent.

Even the vortex itself fell into absolute stillness.

The scene in the eyes of everyone within the ritual suddenly changed, as if they had leaped up and out of the Star Sea, gaining an audience with the Star Sea itself.

If the previous Taijia Divine Technique was merely indirect communication with the Star Sea through transmission. Then, at this moment, everyone had forcibly pried open the door between humans and the Star Sea, their eyes meeting!

A feeling of being completely seen through, which had not been felt for a long time, surged within Li Fan.

Even with his absolute confidence, his treasure of [Returning to True] would not be discovered by a mere Star Sea consciousness. Yet, Li Fan remained on extreme alert, already summoning the Returning to True interface, ready to activate it at any moment.

Just as Li Fan had predicted, even the black energy, which represented the precursor to the Tribulation of Annihilation of Dao, the Star Sea consciousness was like a blind man, unable to notice it. Let alone Returning to True.

The Star Sea consciousness did not focus particularly on Li Fan, but evenly distributed its anger upon every Immortal Boat elder in the ritual.

After all, being forcibly communicated with by ants was, in fact, a humiliation to the Star Sea consciousness. Now, the Star Sea consciousness was waiting to see what the "ants" before it wanted to express.

Only then would it unleash its thunderous wrath.

However…

The "ants" did not truly wish to communicate.

Ten thousand flags fluttered in the magnificent chanting, and as each flag unfurled, parts of it were revealed, forming a whole in an instant.

The character [Uniformity], hidden beneath myriad True Immortal inscriptions, finally revealed itself!

It was as if an invisible shackle had suddenly connected the grand Star Sea consciousness above the vortex with the "ants" in the ritual below.

At this moment, the "ants" were able to stand on the shoulders of the Star Sea, looking down upon all living beings.

Li Fan had previously transformed into a Canghai Bead, transformed into a small world's Heavenly Dao, and even connected his mind with the Xuanhuang Realm.

But none of these could compare to the delightful sensation of the present moment.

The vast Star Sea was no longer boundless; it was like a part of his own body, visible to the naked eye. The Star Sea was no longer dark and silent; with every inhalation and exhalation, one could feel the infinite vitality accumulated beneath the calmness.

Even the various laws constituting the Star Sea were no longer so difficult to comprehend. Like the hair and pores on his body, one could see them all with a mere downward glance.

With the slightest thought, one could use the eyes of the Star Sea to observe every corner of it.

At this moment, under the effect of the [Uniformity] character technique, everyone in the ritual had truly achieved the same state as the Star Sea, seeing what it saw and feeling what it felt.

Li Fan, like all the elders of the Immortal Boat, was uncontrollably immersed in this wondrous state. He even took the liberty to look at the center of the Star Sea.

Indeed, from the Star Sea's perspective, the central star field did not have any black energy.

Instead, it was filled with hidden vitality, waiting to be revived, a scene of great promise!

Li Fan naturally did not have the kindness to remind them. He seized this rare opportunity, trying his best to comprehend the Dao of the Star Sea.

At the same time, he felt a slight curiosity about the Star Sea's attitude.

Under normal circumstances, being plotted against by "ants" with the [Uniformity] character, the true intent of the Star Sea source should be furious.

Even if it couldn't break free from the influence of the [Uniformity] character for a moment, it should at least struggle symbolically.

But now, the Star Sea was terrifyingly calm.

It was not the calm before a storm, gathering strength.

It was a true and genuine lack of any angry emotion.

Why was this?

A doubt suddenly arose in Li Fan's mind.

Under the influence of the True Immortal inscription's power, the Star Sea consciousness was now connected with everyone in the Jun Tian ritual.

Therefore, Li Fan, without much effort, was able to glimpse its thoughts along the Star Sea's train of thought. "This is..."

"While we are peeking into the Star Sea, the Star Sea is also peeking into us?!" Li Fan was suddenly shocked.

In Li Fan's previous understanding, transcendents like the source of the Star Sea or True Immortals would absolutely not pay attention to mortal "ants." But the performance of the Utmost Darkness Star Sea now directly overturned Li Fan's cognition.

Not only did it not resist the Jun Tian act of "ants," but it even actively accepted it!

Just as Li Fan and the others were immersed in the Star Sea's perspective,

The Star Sea consciousness seemed to be extremely interested in the lives of these "ants."

The two sides were in a subtle balance, experiencing each other's lives.

However, due to the disparity in their magnitudes, this balance was destined not to last long.

The Star Sea remained unharmed.

But within the ritual, the cultivators underwent drastic changes.

Li Fan had previously turned himself into a Canghai Bead and witnessed the changes of the Yunhai Sea. Compared to the mountains and seas, a cultivator's entire life was like a fleeting moment. And compared to this Star Sea, the birth and death of worlds were but a blink of an eye.

Viewing everything from the Star Sea's perspective naturally meant enduring the time evolution of the Star Sea.

Even with the billions of beings in the Xuanhuang Small World as sacrifices, it only delayed things for a few fleeting moments.

Soon, old age enveloped the Immortal Boat members.

“Hold on! The power obtained from Uniform Star Sea is being infused! As long as we can absorb this power, we will no longer fear this level of aging!” The Immortal Boat members seemed to have anticipated this, and Zhong Daogong transmitted a reminder to everyone.

However, like Li Fan, they had not expected that the Star Sea would actually become interested in them, these transgressors.

It was not just them actively contacting the Star Sea's origin consciousness, but also the Star Sea itself actively contacting them.

The original plan was for the Star Sea to resist, and for them to delve deeper.

But now, both sides had taken a step forward.

This also resulted in the Star Sea's erosion upon them being nearly double what was estimated!

“Not good!”

The Immortal Boat members quickly discovered this change, looking at the white-stained hair and bodies of the people within the ritual with terrified expressions.

However, all the elders were resolute and decisive. After understanding their current situation and exchanging thoughts for only a moment, they reached a consensus.

“As things stand, the Jun Tian ritual must not stop. Abandoning it halfway would lead to even greater losses!”

“We must sacrifice some people to buy more time and wait for the Star Sea's power to be infused.”

After a brief silence, someone first chuckled, “This old man has lived long enough. Living for another ten or twenty years is just a waste. If I can help the Immortal Boat obtain the Star Sea’s creation, this old man can die without regret!”

Before he could finish speaking, and before others could respond, Gan Jingda's life force had already dissipated.

And the remaining members within the ritual felt a surge of life energy appear out of nowhere within their bodies.

“My old friend has passed away. My remaining in the world only adds to sorrow. It's better to return. It's better to return. The future of the Immortal Boat is entrusted to you all!”

“I am talentless and shallow, so I shall die first!”

“Everyone, you must succeed! I'm off!”

“I originally didn’t want to die. But after calculating, the remaining ones are all more valuable than me… There’s no other way. Who told me my luck in this life has always been poor.”

…

One by one, figures within the ritual voluntarily gave up their life force. Catalyzed by the power of time, they turned into dust and scattered with the wind.

One after another, the last dying words of the Immortal Boat elders echoed in everyone's ears.

Sensing the life force from their companions surging within them like bamboo shoots after a spring rain, the survivors were all deeply heartbroken and filled with sorrow.

But thanks to their sacrifice, just as the detrimental effects of existing on the same level as the Star Sea were about to completely consume them, the Jun Tian Star Sea's obtained power finally descended.

Tens of thousands of streams of light suddenly emerged from the purple-gold vortex.

They flowed into the cultivators still persisting in the ritual.

This was the true origin power of the Star Sea. While perhaps not superior to True Immortals in "quality," it was even superior to True Immortals in "quantity"!

It was a completely different sensation from facing a True Immortal.

The vast origin power of the Star Sea poured down.

Under the cleansing of this great power, the bodies of the surviving Immortal Boat elders gradually dissolved.

But their life force did not disappear; instead, it became even more vigorous.

They no longer aged, and their appearance was frozen at the moment before the infusion. They were merely enveloped by the purple-gold radiance, their true forms indistinguishable.

The Star Sea's mighty power continuously poured in, and their shadowy bodies grew in proportion.

Gradually, they transformed into giants standing tall and spanning across the Star Sea.

The sacrifices of their companions and the excitement of obtaining their achievements, coupled with emotions arising from various reasons, gradually subsided.

…

Li Fan personally witnessed the entire process of the birth of such peculiar beings.

As always cautious, Li Fan did not, like the Immortal Boat elders, directly absorb the Star Sea origin power bestowed from above. Instead, he used an immortal formation to isolate and preserve it. Combined with the power of [Transformation Between True and False] to seal it, it vanished into the Star Sea, undetectable even by the Star Sea consciousness.

Another ingredient was added to the cauldron for refining the Profound Yellow pill.

However, Li Fan did not feel much pleasant surprise. Instead, he looked at the star-light figures that appeared one after another, with great solemnity.

After completely achieving a Star-Light Body, they were automatically disconnected from the [Uniformity] character's connection. At this moment, only Li Fan remained in the entire ritual.

“Unable to communicate.”

“Even their subjective consciousness from before seems lost? No, it's still there! It’s just that the human emotional fluctuations have been suppressed to the extreme, making them more like ‘the Star Sea’.”

“So similar to the Heavenly Dao essence of the Xuanhuang Realm…”

Li Fan looked again at the gradually closing purple-gold vortex.

He vaguely sensed that the Star Sea's own power had not diminished despite this "uniform sharing."

“It's not that the [Uniformity] character has failed.”

“Rather…”

“Infinite, no matter how it is divided, remains infinite!”

Chapter 1375: First Glimpse Beyond the High Wall

"So the Star Sea consciousness reacted to the Immortal Boat elders' act of rebellion with 'Jun' not with great anger, but even actively accepted it..."

"Apart from the novelty of the mortal perspective to the Star Sea, which it found interesting to observe, the more important reason is that the Jun Tian Ritual actually had no impact on the Star Sea at all!"

"True infinity!"

As long as it wasn't infinite, no matter how large the quantity, when divided equally with even just one person, the result would inevitably be significantly reduced compared to the original. It was impossible to achieve the state where the Star Sea's consciousness was indifferent to its losses, just like the current situation.

"How can this be?" Li Fan was filled with bewilderment and shock.

The concept of "infinity" completely surpassed his cognition and understanding.

Although the Utmost Darkness Star Sea was vast and boundless, Li Fan could now traverse it with ease. This was a matter of quantity.

The Star Sea was ravaged by the power of True Immortal Character Scripts, order was destroyed, and vitality was hidden. This was a matter of quality.

Whether from the perspective of quantity or quality, this Star Sea did not seem to be related to "infinity."

But looking at the eighteen starlight giants, formed after the ritual ended and the purple-gold vortex closed, their power was vast and boundless, almost equivalent to this Star Sea itself. Li Fan could not help but believe in the "infinity" of the Star Sea's power.

He instantly recalled the secret heavenly information that Mo Rubing had mentioned hearing from King Xuan Tian.

"It is said that the Immortal Realm is a beautiful holy land with infinite resources."

Like a clap of thunder, this sentence echoed repeatedly in Li Fan's mind.

Before, Li Fan had somewhat believed that this was King Xuan Tian exaggerating or embellishing his words. But now, it seemed that King Xuan Tian was likely telling the truth!

If the Star Sea could achieve "infinity," how much more could the Immortal Realm, which stood above the Star Sea?

If one first accepted this established fact, then the next step was to figure out why.

Let's put aside the Immortal Realm for now.

Regarding this Utmost Darkness Star Sea, how was it connected to "infinity"?

With the purple-gold vortex completely closed, Li Fan's thoughts raced as he confronted the eighteen starlight giants.

"The High Wall only sealed the beings within our Star Sea, but it did not completely divide the Star Sea itself."

"The Utmost Darkness Star Sea within the High Wall and the Star Sea outside are actually still one entity. It's just that now, this sealed region has developed its own independent consciousness."

"This is one possibility."

"But... if that's the case."

Li Fan gazed at the starlight giants before him, evaluating their strength.

Perhaps it was due to their recent birth, they were still somewhat lost and standing in the Star Sea. They seemed to be contemplating their next course of action.

Their auras were gradually retracting.

Their blurred figures became clearer. Familiar human faces were slowly appearing.

Their starlight bodies also temporarily dimmed.

Finally, they turned light blue and transparent.

Within them, countless stars and worlds forming their skeletal structure and meridians could be faintly seen.

"These starlight giants are to the Star Sea what the Heavenly Dao Essence is to the Xuanhuang Realm."

"They have lost their cultivator characteristics, retaining only a trace of subjective consciousness, and have been completely assimilated by the Star Sea..."

"Perhaps they can be called Star Spirits."

Li Fan quietly set up an immortal formation around them, concealing his presence, and secretly observed these peculiar life forms.

"In the Xuanhuang Realm, although the Heavenly Dao Essences have different strengths due to their different heavenly duties, they are roughly between the Nascent Soul and Longevity stages."

"But these starlight spirits before me..."

"With the power of infinite Star Sea they can wield, they are enough to crush all cultivators who have not yet become True Immortals. The limit of the Star Sea is the Star Sea itself. They can be called 'Supreme'!" Li Fan recalled the memory of the Heavenly Physician glimpsed in the illusory formation earlier.

Although he believed these starlight spirits were on par with the Heavenly Physician as Supreme beings, Li Fan did not think they could fight the Heavenly Physician to a standstill.

"If a real fight were to break out, let alone the Heavenly Physician, even I have too many ways to deal with them!"

"But the outcome of the battle is ultimately meaningless!"

"The Star Sea is infinite. Therefore, these starlight spirits cannot be killed by ordinary means."

"Even the True Immortal Character Scripts that brought disaster to the Star Sea only temporarily made the Star Sea's vitality wither. On the timescale of the Star Sea, tens of thousands of years are merely a fleeting moment. Vitality will eventually be fully restored."

"Perhaps only the 'Calamity of Dao Annihilation' that caused the destruction of the Immortal Realm..."

Li Fan thought of the various strange phenomena that frequently occurred in the Star Sea in ancient times.

"One is all. If the Star Sea's power is truly infinite, then if the starlight spirits and Star Sea anomalies erupt with their full power, they can all be considered as the Star Sea itself!"

"An infinite number of Supreme beings, no wonder the cultivators in the world speculate that even True Immortals would retreat in the face of those terrifying anomalies."

Although True Immortals are transcendent beings, if there were an infinite number of Heavenly Physicians surrounding and attacking them, they might not be unable to injure or even capture them!

Li Fan's thoughts raced in an instant.

While contemplating, the eighteen starlight giants finally made their move.

Some of them looked towards the hidden Xuan Immortal Boat not far away, some looked towards the border of the Star Sea and the High Wall, and some gradually scanned the entire Star Sea.

"If the Star Sea consciousness wanted to revive itself before, it needed the cultivators' help. Then now, it can repair itself through the starlight spirits."

"Although the starlight spirits still retain the obsessions from their lives, they must now act according to the Star Sea's requirements."

……

Li Fan had not forgotten the reason why he had infiltrated the Immortal Boat in this life.

Besides coveting the many treasures hidden within the Immortal Boat, the more important reason was to use the Immortal Boat as a pawn to explore as far as possible towards the outside of the High Wall.

Now that all the elders of the Immortal Boat had transformed into starlight spirits, possessing the power to rival the Star Sea. It was enough to implement the plan of ramming the High Wall, which was similar to the original plan of the Shang Immortal Boat.

Seeing that these starlight spirits were about to be driven by the Star Sea's consciousness to travel to various parts of the Star Sea, how could Li Fan waste this excellent opportunity?

Tai Jia Divine Art, the perfected version deduced by the Immortal Boat, materialize!

In a short period, this divine ability to communicate with the Star Sea reappeared.

However, this time, Li Fan's target of communication was not the Star Sea's primordial will, but these eighteen starlight spirits!

Compared to the Star Sea itself, the starlight spirits, evolved from cultivators, were much easier to communicate with.

The moment the Tai Jia Divine Art's radiance appeared, it attracted the attention of the starlight spirits.

Li Fan's consciousness also instantly connected with theirs.

If these starlight spirits were still human, upon seeing Li Fan, who had participated in the ritual with them, and who had neither perished nor transformed into a starlight spirit, but was still alive and well, they would have surely erupted in rage and suspicion.

Let alone communication, direct confrontation would be normal.

But Li Fan, at this moment, felt no emotional fluctuations from these eighteen starlight spirits.

"Immortal Boat, outside the High Wall."

"Dear friends, sacrifice."

"Do not forget!"

Li Fan, having initially mastered the art of communicating with the Star Sea, spoke concisely.

As if awakening memories from their lives, the human faces of the starlight spirits instantly became much clearer.

Their movements, which had stopped, halted. They all looked at Li Fan, their eyes filled with hesitation. "Giving up halfway would be a waste!"

"With the Star Sea's power to assist, crossing the High Wall with the Immortal Boat is as easy as lifting a finger!"

Under Li Fan's persuasion, the original obsessions and ideas of the starlight spirits were slowly reviving.

Sensing the thoughts of the starlight spirits, Li Fan continued to instigate them.

"Even if the Star Sea can be revived, it will be millions of years from now. The elders have all become starlight spirits and cannot protect the Immortal Boat at all times. What will be the future of the Immortal Boat? Should they just watch them die like this?"

Zhong Daogong, transformed into a starlight spirit, was eventually persuaded.

Intermittent thoughts were transmitted.

Unlike communicating with cultivators, the starlight spirit Zhong Daogong stated the facts with no emotional fluctuation.

Over time, their original consciousness would only grow weaker. Eventually, they would become starlight spirits completely belonging to the Star Sea. Although they still possessed some subjective consciousness, they could not defy the Star Sea's will and act of their own accord.

But to mobilize the Star Sea's power to help the Immortal Boat cross the High Wall, perhaps the Star Sea consciousness would not object.

True Immortal Character Scripts were hated by the Star Sea consciousness. The starlight spirits could no longer use them.

To successfully cross the High Wall according to the plan, Li Fan's help was still needed to preside over it.

……

More and more starlight spirits temporarily regained their own consciousness.

They reached a consensus with Li Fan.

During this final period of remaining consciousness, the starlight spirit Zhong Daogong entrusted the Immortal Boat's top-secret plan to cross the High Wall entirely.

With the escort of the eighteen starlight giants, they dragged the Immortal Boat to the vicinity of the trace left by the Shang Immortal Boat when it crossed the High Wall.

"Time is running out; let's start quickly."

Li Fan nodded slightly and looked at the dozens of white papers that slowly floated out from the Immortal Boat.

These appeared blank, but faint traces could be seen on the paper, as if they had been written on countless times.

These were the painstaking efforts of the Immortal Boat elders over the years.

Through continuous imitation, comprehension, and discussion, they had restored all known True Immortal Character Scripts to their original state as much as possible.

"The abilities of these old foxes are truly not to be underestimated!"

"After receiving my guidance, they actually managed to advance the research of True Immortal Character Scripts so much in such a short time without anyone noticing!"

"The Immortal Boat of this life is far stronger than the one that perished in the Immortal Formation in the previous life!"

"Not only is its foundation rich, but its ability to study and progress is also terrifyingly strong." Li Fan looked at the familiar yet unfamiliar characters, his heart filled with alarm.

The inscriptions on the white paper were like molds forged by the Immortal Boat elders through countless trials. Li Fan did not need to familiarize himself with them or write them again; as long as he injected energy along the inscriptions, one True Immortal Character Script would spontaneously appear!

"This is probably the backup measure left by the Immortal Boat elders. With these True Immortal Character Script imprints, even if the entire Immortal Boat elders were wiped out, the Immortal Boat's inheritance would not be completely severed. Given enough time, it might not be impossible for them to return to their peak..."

Thinking this, Li Fan poured his Origin Energy Essence into all the character molds.

Only Li Fan, with his profound accumulation, could support such an action. The Five Elements Great Heavenly Cave Heaven and the Xuanhuang World Destruction Transformation made Li Fan alone equivalent to an entire cultivation world.

Any other normal cultivator would probably have their Origin Energy drained the moment they injected it into the True Immortal Character Scripts. Even a Supreme being of the Star Sea like the Heavenly Physician might not be able to support such an expenditure!

Li Fan's immense power within his body was all transformed into the driving force for the formation of True Immortal Character Scripts.

At this moment, the eighteen starlight giants began to take further action.

Letting out continuous roars, each taking turns, they elevated the momentum of the Immortal Boat, like steps, one after another, higher and higher!

It was not actual roaring sounds, but rather like some kind of fluctuation, like giant waves containing the power of "infinity."

Li Fan ascended, yet he still needed to use True Immortal flesh and blood as a medium, but these eighteen starlight giants actually relied solely on the infinite Star Sea origin power to continuously elevate the Immortal Boat's momentum!

And throughout this process, there was no fluctuation in the auras emanating from these starlight spirits. It was as if the burden of ascending was insignificant to them.

They still retained the memory of the Shang Immortal Boat's collision point, and after the starlight giants raised the Xuan Immortal Boat to a certain level of momentum, they stopped ascending further.

They continued to roar incessantly, maintaining the Immortal Boat's momentum.

At the same time, they were like hammers, continually striking at Li Fan's heart, urging him to proceed to the next step.

Li Fan, facing the Star Sea's might directly for the first time, felt a slight sense of awe and forcibly suppressed the surging blood in his body.

"It's a pity that after colliding with the High Wall, their fate is uncertain. Many treasures within the Immortal Boat will be destroyed along with this collision!"

Thinking this, his hands did not hesitate. Looking at the completed but still sealed True Immortal Character Script papers, he grabbed them all with a large hand.

He compressed them all into a "paper ball."

Then, he threw it towards the Immortal Boat surrounded by the eighteen starlight giants.

Chaos and terror, power at the True Immortal level, were contained within and flew towards the Xuan Immortal Boat.

"Explode!"

Li Fan roared in his heart, simultaneously retreating rapidly.

The True Immortal Character Script storm erupted beneath the Immortal Boat.

The power, capable of temporarily blowing away the Star Sea's vitality, caused the blue bodies of the eighteen starlight giants to flicker unstably. However, their actions did not falter in the slightest. The infinite Star Sea power continuously replenished them, and even when facing this True Immortal Character Script storm, the starlight spirits remained indestructible.

Under their control and guidance, the erupted True Immortal power did not directly destroy the Xuan Immortal Boat. Instead, it served as the final boost for the Immortal Boat's ascension.

This made the goal, which was originally impossible for beings within the Star Sea, possible at this very moment!

"True power that surpasses the mortal realm, comparable to True Immortals! Supreme power capable of crossing the High Wall!"

As one of the instigators, Li Fan, watching from afar as the storm erupted at the initial collision point of the High Wall, and the Xuan Immortal Boat rising vigorously above the storm.

He could not help but feel an uncontrollable surge of excitement.

After countless reincarnations, the time had finally come.

To have the possibility of glimpsing the world beyond the High Wall.

As early as when he helped the Xuan Immortal Boat rebuild its defensive system, Li Fan had secretly laid his own groundwork.

What the Immortal Boat saw would also be what he, Li Fan, saw!

Everything was ready.

The Immortal Boat was about to collide head-on with the High Wall.

And at this very moment…

The eighteen starlight giants, as if sensing something extremely terrifying,

The ones least likely to flee from battle, actually vanished in an instant.

However, the Xuan Immortal Boat continued to ram towards the invisible High Wall.

And it also vanished from this Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

Only Li Fan was left, his face filled with bewilderment.

He had witnessed the entire process of the Immortal Boat ramming the High Wall, yet he did not sense the slightest hint of danger.

And…

The means he had placed within the Immortal Boat had not functioned at all.

Chapter 1376: Ink Kills Heavenly Immortal Soul

Li Fan lingered at the border of the High Wall, unable to recover from the sudden upheaval for a long time.

The eighteen Star Spirits had detached themselves at the most critical moment when the Immortal Boat was about to traverse the High Wall…

It was certain that this was absolutely not the will of the Star Spirits themselves.

The Immortal Boat elders' concern and care for the Immortal Boat were unquestionable. They could even sacrifice their lives without hesitation for its continuation.

"It was the origin consciousness of the Star Sea that sensed something at that instant."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes and, with great caution, retreated a considerable distance away.

"The Star Sea consciousness acts according to its instincts and does not engage in empty posturing like humans. It seems something inexplicably terrifying truly descended just now."

"But I, who witnessed the entire process, was completely unaware."

This was what troubled him the most.

Li Fan couldn't help but recall a scene.

It was during a time before his transmigration, when he was strolling along a wooden walkway in a wetland park.

Walking there, he could see clearly through the transparent glass to the world below. The scene observed was completely different from the landscape above, offering a unique taste.

The fish underwater would gather and approach the glass wall.

The young ones, even when tourists stared at them through the glass, remained oblivious. They continued to play.

But the larger ones, which seemed to have lived for a long time, sensed danger long before any person approached. They flicked their tails and fled, disappearing into the depths of the water.

…

This scene was strikingly similar to what had just happened!

As past memories resurfaced, Li Fan belatedly felt a shiver of revulsion.

"My current strength is still that of a young fish unable to sense the existing danger."

"Perhaps only at the Star Sea level, or rather, at the pinnacle of the Star Sea, the Supreme Realm, are they akin to adult fish."

"But regardless of which it is, compared to those eyes silently watching from beyond the High Wall…"

At this thought, Li Fan's expression turned grim, and his wariness of the world beyond the High Wall grew increasingly intense.

"Beyond the High Wall… I wonder if the Xuan Immortal Boat, which risked its life just now, managed to break through the High Wall?"

Li Fan carefully recalled the senses he had left within the Immortal Boat at the moment of its disappearance.

After a long while, Li Fan's expression subtly changed. To verify his thoughts, he returned to the vicinity of the High Wall.

He differentiated a wisp of his divine sense and then, by manipulating it, sent it towards the intangible High Wall.

Li Fan's action was undoubtedly like an egg hitting a rock.

The moment it collided with the High Wall, his fragile divine sense vanished, repelled by the High Wall's power.

Li Fan's movements did not cease; he projected more strands of divine sense.

Finally, after tens of thousands of attempts, he vaguely sensed it.

"The disappearance after colliding with the High Wall is different from the disappearance just now within the Immortal Boat."

"When struck and destroyed by the High Wall, one could still faintly perceive the process of destruction. Even if this process were extremely brief, I would have to repeat it tens of thousands of times to even detect it. But it is ultimately unlike the instantaneous disappearance after leaving the High Wall."

"The Xuan Immortal Boat succeeded; it truly broke through the High Wall's blockade!"

Li Fan was deeply shaken.

"The combined efforts of eighteen Star Spirits, infinite Star Sea energy, plus the surge of power from the fusion of True Immortal scripts, indeed possessed the power to transcend in an instant."

The success of the Xuan Immortal Boat finally gave Li Fan a glimmer of hope for crossing the High Wall.

The methods from this lifetime could be replicated.

In that instant, Li Fan's emotions couldn't help but become somewhat agitated.

But soon, after thinking of the changes that occurred to the Xuan Immortal Boat after it crossed the High Wall, Li Fan's brief flicker of joy instantly vanished.

"Once traversed, the perception disappears. Even if it succeeds, to me, it's the same as not succeeding."

"Beyond the High Wall, there are clearly myriad dangers. Unknown forces even covet and hunt True Immortals. I absolutely cannot rashly enter beyond the Wall without knowing anything."

Placing his own safety first was Li Fan's most fundamental principle of action; he would never abandon it for temporary gain. Of course, accidents encountered during the execution of the principle were another matter.

"I must find a way to establish a connection, even if it's through the High Wall."

"Perhaps only by having a certain understanding of the High Wall's essence can this be achieved."

Li Fan couldn't help but turn his gaze towards the only known flaw in the High Wall.

Suddenly, Li Fan's heart stirred, and he approached a little closer.

Observing and sensing carefully in the direction where the Xuan Immortal Boat had disappeared.

Threads of golden light, like mercury spilling onto the ground, spread outwards. This was Li Fan's method, learned from the Heavenly Physician in the illusory formation, for peering into the High Wall.

After some time, Li Fan retracted the golden threads, his expression becoming somewhat subtle: "Even though the Xuan Immortal Boat has broken through the High Wall, I still cannot sense any so-called flaw in the High Wall."

"And yet, a single thought transmission from King Xuan Tian in ancient times could leave an everlasting mark on the High Wall?"

"Indeed, for non-corporeal forms, the High Wall's blockade is more than a hundred times weaker. To achieve communication perception between the inside and outside of the High Wall, perhaps we can start from this aspect."

Li Fan's current peak combat power was primarily concentrated in the Transformation Between True and False and several Immortal Formations. In terms of spirit and soul, it was not his forte.

"Without Worries, Dreamland Paradise." Li Fan suddenly thought of the Longevity Heavenly Venerate in the Xuanhuang Realm.

"I wonder what stage the spread of Paradise in the Star Sea has reached. Has it touched the border of the High Wall?"

The disciples of the Medicine King Sect and the beings of various small worlds continued their exploration of the dreamscape.

However, the boundless Dreamland Paradise was truly too vast. Every newcomer could only explore step by step.

Even the pioneers, the trio of Sun Erlang, had only just reached Dreamland Level 6. It was still too early to truly uncover the secrets of the dreamscape.

But Li Fan believed that even if there were no significant gains in this lifetime, with the experience gained, coupled with the unceasing exploration of countless beings, it would not be too long before the secrets of the dreamscape were fully revealed.

"Ultimately, it is my own strength that is too weak. Otherwise, why would I need to rely on 'Without Worries'?" Li Fan sighed inwardly.

"Perhaps, after I merge with the Tao, harmonizing with the Xuanhuang Immortal Soul in this lifetime, the situation will improve to some extent."

"However…" Li Fan's gaze once again turned towards the direction of the High Wall. "It is highly likely that when the Xuanhuang elevates to the Immortal Realm, the watchful eyes from beyond the High Wall will reappear. I must also prepare in advance to delay time as much as possible."

Fortunately, the incident in his previous life where the Cat Treasure captured an Immortal, causing the High Wall to collapse and the Star Sea to be in turmoil, provided Li Fan with a reference.

"This lifetime is a realm's sublimation into an Immortal Domain, which might cause even greater commotion. To be safe, I must complete the swallowing of the Immortal Soul before half the time of the previous life's anomaly occurs."

"Heaven and Earth Immortal Soul, although its name has changed, its essence has not. It is also born with heavenly duties."

"To achieve the fastest swallowing, the birth of the Heaven and Earth Soul must first be rapid."

Li Fan had been planning in the Xuanhuang Realm for a long time. Naturally, he was very familiar with all sorts of Heaven and Earth Souls. He could even summon the Heaven and Earth Soul out of thin air with the 'Erosion Transformation of Heaven and Earth'.

"Heaven and Earth Souls, from the moment they are stimulated by the will of Heaven and Earth to manifest their form, require varying amounts of time. In a hundred reincarnations, the fastest observed manifestation is…"

"Only [Ink Kill]!"

A glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

In that lifetime, Zhang Haobo, who had cleaved through the Crimson Flame with the Twenty-Eight Swords of Canopy Clouds, became the youngest Harmonized Dao Immortal Venerable in history. The moment he harmonized with the Tao, he tragically died under Ink Kill.

Almost the instant Crimson Flame was slain, Ink Kill was activated by the will of Heaven and Earth.

"Unlike other Heaven and Earth Souls, Ink Kill, as a part of the operations of Heaven and Earth, is likely in a constant state of readiness. It can be activated instantly. This might be a self-generated change after the Xuanhuang Realm was patched together with fragments from outside." Li Fan understood after a moment of thought.

"Ink Kill will likely undergo a transformation from a Heaven and Earth Soul to a Heaven and Earth Immortal Soul, simultaneously with the sublimation of the Xuanhuang Realm. Moreover, Ink Kill's actual combat power is among the strongest of all Heaven and Earth Souls."

"It is indeed the most suitable." Li Fan nodded slightly, his thoughts racing as he locked onto his target.

"The Immortal Boat matter is concluded; it's time to return and make thorough preparations for the final sublimation of the Xuanhuang." Sensing the Star Sea spiritual power sealed within his body, which he had obtained from the Star Sea, Li Fan's confidence in completing the plan increased by another notch.

Just as he was about to use his wooden sword to leave, an anomaly occurred at the edge of the High Wall.

It was not from the High Wall itself, but from the entrance leading to the trench depression.

A large amount of vital energy suddenly gushed out.

Like a fountain, it surged upwards, rushing towards the Star Sea.

A figure actually escaped from it, utilizing this surge of power.

Li Fan focused his gaze and saw it was Qiao Gong, who had been missing for a long time!

Qiao Gong had been affected by the reverberating Star Force storm and was trapped in the labyrinthine trench depression, his whereabouts unknown. Li Fan had been unable to contact him, only vaguely sensing that his aura was stable and he was not in mortal danger. He hadn't expected him to finally escape the labyrinth!

Qiao Gong seemed extremely excited about his escape, waving his hands and shouting loudly.

Li Fan extended his palm and directly drew him to his side.

The scene suddenly changed. Qiao Gong thought he had escaped one tiger's den only to fall into another, and his face turned pale.

Only when he saw Li Fan did he breathe a sigh of relief.

Clearing his throat, Qiao Gong solemnly bowed, "Greetings, Sacred Master."

Li Fan said calmly, "I haven't seen you for a long time. I did search for you below before, but that trench depression was winding and extensive, spreading throughout the entire Star Sea underground. I couldn't find you, so I gave up."

"Now it seems you've turned misfortune into fortune?"

Compared to before he went missing, Qiao Gong's spirit and energy had undergone a qualitative change. Clearly, he had gained some fortuitous encounter in that endless trench depression.

As soon as this was mentioned, a hint of pride appeared on Qiao Gong's face. "Sacred Master's discernment is indeed remarkable. I have indeed gained a small harvest."

"Initially, when I found myself lost in those winding dark rivers, I was somewhat panicked. But I soon discovered that vitality was abundant there, and even if I were trapped for a lifetime, there would be no danger to my life. So I relaxed."

"Sacred Master, you know me best. I'm used to staying in the laboratory and not going out. Being in the trench depression was merely a change of environment. Moreover, I still had Shangguan's puppet to vent my frustrations on, so I wouldn't be bored…" Qiao Gong rambled on.

Li Fan said sternly, "Get to the point."

Qiao Gong paused, let out a ha-ha, and continued, "After I adapted for a while, I started researching those endless dark rivers out of curiosity.

"Who knew I would actually stumble upon their secret!" Qiao Gong's tone became somewhat excited.

"Those underground rivers are too winding. At first, I tried to memorize them all, but because there were too many branches, I never succeeded."

"I didn't give up, though. During that period, my mind was filled with the shapes of the underground rivers."

"Then one day, after I broke Shangguan again, while repairing it, I inexplicably applied the flowing shapes of the trench dark rivers in my mind to Shangguan's puppet! What happened next was something I had never heard of before!" At this point, Qiao Gong licked his lips, a strange gleam in his eyes.

Li Fan knew that Qiao Gong's so-called Shangguan puppet was actually a memory backup of his master, Shangguan Tuo, an elder from the Heavenly Mechanism Realm, sealed within Qiao Gong.

However, according to the rules of the Heavenly Mechanism Realm, memory backups did not have the same status as the original owner and could only obey the commands of Heavenly Mechanism Realm cultivators.

Li Fan had always known about Qiao Gong's rather perverse hobby, but since Qiao Gong was just entertaining himself, Li Fan hadn't bothered with him.

But seeing Qiao Gong's expression now, Li Fan was also piqued with interest.

Qiao Gong seemed to savor the memory for a moment before saying word by word, "I never expected that after the repair, the Shangguan puppet, which should not have resisted at all, not only refused my command but also cursed me viciously…"

"The curses were so vile that they reminded me of unpleasant memories from a long time ago. I was a bit angry at the time and was a little heavy-handed, breaking it again."

"After a long time when I came to my senses, I suddenly realized that something unimaginable had happened!"

Li Fan pondered, "You mean, the shape of the trench dark river actually activated Shangguan's self-awareness?"

Qiao Gong shook his head frantically, "That was already a consciousness backup; it naturally had complete self-awareness. However, due to the restrictions of the ancient Heavenly Mechanism Realm's formation, it could only obey my commands completely."

"But after inscribing those shapes, it was different."

Qiao Gong licked his lips again, "The newly formed Shangguan was no longer a consciousness backup. According to the Heavenly Mechanism Realm's restrictions, it became Shangguan Tuo himself!"

"Shangguan Tuo has been dead for who knows how many years, so this is naturally impossible."

"But precisely because of the influence of that unknown shape, she was resurrected in a sense!"

"Moreover, all I inscribed was merely an insignificant part of the shape of the trench dark rivers. This is simply, simply…"

"Unimaginable!" Qiao Gong exclaimed.

Hearing Qiao Gong's narration, Li Fan suddenly understood the purpose of these trench dark rivers that permeated the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

They were not just reservoirs of vitality.

They were also a powerful divine ability.

A divine ability that could give the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, sealed by the High Wall, an independent self-awareness.

Chapter 1377: Life Forms Transform into Immortal Forms

Li Fan, who had previously been perplexed by how the Utmost Darkness Star Sea, sealed beneath the High Wall, had developed an independent consciousness, never imagined that the mystery would unravel so quickly.

"The crevice hollows were built by Xing Wuque under the King Xuan Tian's orders. For tens of thousands of years of diligent effort, they still haven't been fully constructed. Xu Ke needs to take over."

"Regardless of whether Xu Ke's persistence is his own will or influenced by Xing Wuque's inheritance, King Xuan Tian's plan required the 'completeness' condition to be met for the crevice hollows."

"I previously speculated that King Xuan Tian intended to elevate the entire Utmost Darkness Star Sea to the Immortal Realm. But now it seems..."

"Perhaps there was another motive beyond that."

Hermit Qiao continued his ceaseless narration, explaining how the crevice patterns transformed the decayed into the miraculous. With his hand as a brush, he drew the shapes he had memorized before Li Fan. At first glance, there was nothing extraordinary about them; they seemed like meaningless scribbles of a child.

Li Fan also recalled the route of the crevice depths he had traveled in his mind. He had followed the guidance of the [Manifest] character, delving deep to the very end of the crevice hollows. Therefore, the patterns he had recorded were far more detailed and precise than those of Hermit Qiao. Even so, after careful contemplation, Li Fan could not discern the profound mystery within these patterns.

"It seems to be a completely different system from what I've encountered and understood so far."

"Only through inscription can it manifest its effect?"

"Even a small part of it could spawn independent consciousness. But when all the patterns are complete, what kind of efficacy will it possess?" Li Fan frowned inwardly.

With a thought, a long sword, flowing like azure liquid, appeared in Li Fan's hand. This was one of the five treasures Li Fan had obtained from the Immortal Boat's secret repository, which he had claimed to have acquired to gain Master Da Qi's trust and facilitate the Jun Tian Ritual. The Immortal Boat's secret repository's second level yielded two items: the Yin-Yang Jade and the Three-Pronged Tree. The first level yielded three items: the Black Star Stone, the Strange Bronze Mirror, and the Liquid Long Sword. The Three-Pronged Tree inexplicably triggered a simulation within his [Returning to True], aiding Li Fan in deepening his understanding of the transformation between true and false. The Yin-Yang Jade was part of a plan that would soon transform into Yin and Yang energies to facilitate the Xuanhuang's sublimation. The Black Star Stone had already been integrated into the body of the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet. Only the Strange Bronze Mirror and the Liquid Long Sword remained idle.

The treasures Li Fan had casually selected from the Immortal Boat's secret repository were already so helpful to him, given his current strength that allowed him to roam the Star Sea at will. This demonstrated the immense richness of the Immortal Boat's secret repository. This was only from the first and second layers of the Hundred Question Immortal Records. It was hard to imagine what treasures lay stored in the third layer.

"It's a pity that in this lifetime, the entire boatload of treasures has already gone beyond the Wall. I can only wait to explore it in detail later."

"However, if I can successfully merge with the Immortal Soul of Heaven and Earth, facing the Immortal Boat again in the future will not require such a convoluted process as in this lifetime."

As his thoughts churned, Li Fan quietly inscribed the known patterns of the crevice hollows onto the liquid long sword before him. Although no energy fluctuations appeared, the liquid long sword suddenly began to boil! Li Fan narrowed his eyes, separating a wisp of his divine sense to carefully sense the changes in the liquid long sword.

"Kill! Kill! Kill! Kill! Kill! Kill! Kill!" The azure sword body slowly turned completely black. Within it, an ignorant, nascent consciousness emerged, endlessly repeating the word "kill" as if possessed. The crevice hollow patterns gradually faded into the interior of the liquid long sword. The sword then transformed from its flowing liquid form into a sharp, solid sword radiating a chilling aura. With a whoosh, it flew towards the nearest living target. It was like an ink brush drawing a straight line on white paper, with black ink spreading around it.
