"Kill!" The space was torn open, and a monstrous killing intent surged towards Li Fan's face. The entire Star Sea seemed to disappear from Li Fan's vision; all he saw, perceived, and felt was this lone sword in the air.

"Impressive." Li Fan praised softly. Two giant index fingers, piercing through space, descended from the heavens. They blocked in front of Li Fan, gently clamping the black sword body.

"Kill..." The black long sword still wanted to struggle, but how could it move? It could only rage impotently, letting out low roars. Hermit Qiao, stunned by this turn of events, abruptly halted his speech. The power he felt from the [Nine Heavens Descending Dust Finger] made Hermit Qiao tremble with fear and dare not look directly at Li Fan.

"It has indeed developed self-awareness. The previous liquid long sword was just a purely inanimate object, without any consciousness fluctuations."

"It's a pity that perhaps due to incomplete patterns, or from nothing to something, the consciousness born within this sword cannot yet be called complete intelligence." Li Fan had already gained a preliminary understanding of the efficacy of the crevice patterns. The [Nine Heavens Descending Dust Finger] then exerted a slight force. With a squeeze, the patterns inscribed on the sword body were instantly erased. The blackness receded, and the sword returned to its liquid form, the accompanying monstrous killing intent also vanishing.

"Wait for me for a moment." Li Fan put away the liquid long sword and instructed Hermit Qiao before disappearing from the spot. Having witnessed Li Fan's might, Hermit Qiao dared not disobey. He obediently stayed put, waiting. At the same time, his eyes darted around, recalling the patterns that had flashed across the liquid long sword's body just moments ago.

"The pattern's completeness that Sacred Master possesses is so much greater than mine. Unfortunately, the details of the shape are too complex. In that instant, I only remembered a little more than half."

"But it should be enough. Hehehe, I wonder what this will turn Shangguan into this time?" Hermit Qiao's mind was in turmoil.

The next moment, Li Fan's voice suddenly rang out in his ear. "You want to know the complete pattern too?"

"Of course," Hermit Qiao responded instinctively. But soon, he realized his mistake, his face turning ashen. He hastily shook his head frantically. "Hehehe, Sacred Master, you misunderstand. How could I dare to pry into such profound secret techniques in their entirety? What I have now is enough..."

Li Fan waved his hand, stopping Hermit Qiao's incessant chatter. At the same time, he projected a pattern into the other's sea of consciousness. "Since you are also interested, I don't mind passing on the [Form of Living Beings] to you," Li Fan said calmly. Hermit Qiao, however, remained silent, his eyes dazed, clearly immersed in the complex and wondrous patterns.

The so-called [Form of Living Beings] was not the original name of the crevice patterns. Li Fan had casually given it that name. Previously, Li Fan had returned to the depths of the crevice to try and obtain the complete patterns from Xu Ke. Xing Wuque, as the actual builder of the crevice, should have had relevant memories in his inheritance. Unfortunately, it was somewhat disappointing for Li Fan that Xing Wuque's inheritance was too vast. If all details were imparted, Xu Ke's soul would absolutely not be able to bear it. Therefore, in Xing Wuque's view, extraneous matters were discarded and not included in the inheritance. This included the memories of building the outer parts of the crevice that had already been completed. Fortunately, the uncompleted portion of the [Form of Living Beings] was within Xing Wuque's inheritance. After obtaining it from Xu Ke, Li Fan had also laid countless golden threads in the dark rivers of the crevice. With the vitality of the dark rivers, they continuously proliferated and evolved. Like mercury spreading across the ground, they began a comprehensive exploration of the crevice hollows.

The crevice hollows, although having countless branches and permeating the entire Star Sea, were not an insurmountable challenge for Li Fan. It was merely troublesome, not impossible to clarify. It was just that previously, Li Fan had lacked the motivation to do so. But now, knowing that the complete patterns might be a new and unknown powerful divine ability, Li Fan was motivated to explore them completely. "According to the current search progress of the golden threads in the crevice hollows, the exploration should be completed before the end of this lifetime."

"Hopefully, it will bring me some surprises." Sensing the [Form of Living Beings] continuously spreading outwards in his mind, Li Fan thought to himself. After returning to the crevice depths just now, Li Fan also learned the reason why Hermit Qiao had escaped. It was likely a chain reaction caused by the Xuan Immortal Boat traversing the High Wall. The moment the Immortal Boat crossed the High Wall, it attracted the attention of unknown existences beyond the High Wall. The Star Sea consciousness thus felt an extremely intense crisis. It was like a catalyst, igniting the vast vitality stored within the crevice hollows.

"The revival of the Star Sea has been expedited once again."

"The [Form of Living Beings], the consciousness of the Star Sea, the High Wall, the Immortal Realm..." Grasping Hermit Qiao, who was still in the process of enlightenment, Li Fan returned to the Xuanhuang Realm while deep in thought.

"Wonderful!" At this moment, Hermit Qiao finally awoke as if from a dream, shouting with surprise.

"Although I haven't glimpsed its entirety yet, I already have a premonition. With this [Form of Living Beings], I can modify Shangguan's thoughts according to my wishes, creating the Shangguan Tuo of my dreams, tailored just for me!"

"Shangguan, wait for me, wait for me..." Hermit Qiao's eyes had already become somewhat frenzied due to extreme joy. At this moment, the only thought in his mind was to immediately find a quiet, hidden place to craft a tailor-made Shangguan Tuo puppet.

"I heard you still have several combat memory data fragments of the Immortal Puppet [Ancestor] on you, Hermit Qiao?" Li Fan blocked his path at this opportune moment.

"Yes, yes. Sacred Master needs it? Feel free to take it!" Hermit Qiao, now gradually dominated by his own desires, did not bother to delve into how Li Fan knew about this secret. He directly threw a seven-colored light cluster to Li Fan.

Li Fan examined it and smiled slightly, clearing the path. Hermit Qiao scurried away, disappearing to an unknown location. Li Fan, holding the light cluster in one hand, arrived at the Heavenly Yang's secluded cultivation area. Ever since his battle with the Thousand-Eyed Desolate God on the Immortal Boat previously, Heavenly Yang had entered a state of secluded enlightenment. His aura fluctuated like the sea clouds, sometimes freely spreading outwards, sometimes rapidly retracting, completely concealing itself. Li Fan could even faintly sense the dread he had felt when facing the Thousand-Eyed Desolate God previously from Heavenly Yang.

"Star Spirit power, complete Immortal Realm foundation, remnants of a broken realm, convergence of True Immortal residual power..."

"In this lifetime, the means I have prepared are increasing, but for some reason, my inner unease is also growing day by day." Li Fan stood before the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet, his expression inscrutable. "My intuition has always been accurate. Countless experiences in reincarnation have verified this point."

"It seems that promoting the Xuanhuang's sublimation will inevitably encounter unforeseen crises..."

"I need a helper, even if it can only delay things for a moment." Li Fan slowly implanted the entire cluster of seven-colored light into the Heavenly Yang Immortal Puppet. The moment the light cluster approached, it seemed to sense a threat. The True Immortal flesh and blood on Heavenly Yang's body actually rose like living creatures, baring their fangs and claws. However, upon truly coming into contact with the combat memory of [Ancestor], the flesh and blood momentarily quieted down, then reacted even more violently, eagerly drawing the light cluster into Heavenly Yang's body.

A trace of ferocity flickered across Heavenly Yang's originally calm face. Two completely different auras simultaneously appeared on him. One was ancient, desolate, and malevolent. The other was righteous, majestic, and unmoving. One came from the Thousand-Eyed Desolate God, the other from the Immortal Puppet Ancestor. Both of these were beings that transcended the mortal realm. Although not comparable to True Immortals, they were not beings that ordinary cultivators could withstand. Logically, under the influence of these two completely opposing auras, even Supremes in the Star Sea should have their minds wavered and worn down by this fierce storm. But the core of the Immortal Puppet was the Eternal Remnant Thought! In the struggle of auras, Li Fan was forced to retreat slightly. But Heavenly Yang, at the center of the storm, stood unmoving amidst the wind and rain, becoming even more radiant and brilliant as if tempered by fire!

"Is this the Eternal Remnant Thought?" Li Fan, for the first time, truly witnessed what eternity meant. It was merely a mortal's遗物 (relic), yet it could stand firm in the face of Immortal-level power. This extreme contrast shook Li Fan's mind. He suddenly thought of another [Returning to True] Eternal Remnant Thought in the Xuanhuang Realm: the skull of Mr. Bai from the Divine Treasury Museum!

"It's been too long. After achieving the Immortal Soul, it's time to go and collect it." Although he now had few rivals within the Star Sea, he still felt constrained at times. "Only by merging with the Dao as the Immortal Soul, stepping into the Immortal Realm, even if only half-immortal, can I roam freely!" At this moment, Li Fan's resolve was more determined than ever. "The Heavenly Yang Immortal Soul is one reliance. Perhaps this sword can also serve."

Li Fan flashed to the center of the Great Xuan lecture platform. He took out the liquid long sword and placed it quietly in front of him. He circulated the spiritual energy within his body, inscribing all the known patterns of [Form of Living Beings] onto the sword body. Compared to the first attempt, the size of the [Living Beings] pattern was almost twice as large. The sword body did not transform into ink color but remained azure blue. Li Fan deliberately left large blank spaces in the unexplored areas for future refinement.

After the [Form of Living Beings] inscription was completed, a fluctuation that Li Fan could not currently comprehend descended and enveloped the liquid long sword. Dazzling light flashed, then slowly extinguished. A naked, delicate young Daoist boy slowly appeared before Li Fan. In the instant of his birth, the young Daoist boy showed a trace of confusion in his eyes. A moment later, he seemed to understand his own origin. "Thank you, Master, for giving me life," the young Daoist boy said crisply, bowing before Li Fan. "Today's update is early."

Chapter 1378: Autumn Waters Enter the Star Sea

The effect of the "Life Form Shape" was even more miraculous than Li Fan had anticipated.

Looking at the young Taoist boy kneeling before him, Li Fan tried to sense his specific life form.

"Bestowed life..." He savored these two words in his heart.

Li Fan's act of inscribing the Life Form Shape onto the liquid long sword had created an existence akin to a "tool spirit." And a natural strong connection existed between him and his creation.

The "Great Master" the Taoist boy mentioned was actually the master, the sovereign.

Li Fan vaguely felt that with a single thought, he could erase the Taoist boy's consciousness at will and return the liquid long sword to its original state.

Even if the Taoist boy's strength were to become immense, as long as he couldn't break free from the shackles of the Life Form Shape, he could not escape his fate as a creation.

"The Life Form Shape is indeed profound and unfathomable. The only regret is that it created a truly independent life with its own consciousness. I cannot fully perceive his thoughts."

"However, I can still manipulate him like a puppet."

In a flash, Li Fan understood the entire situation. He casually gestured with a finger, and a Taoist robe materialized, covering the boy's body.

"Thank you, Great Master, for the robe!" The Taoist boy respectfully bowed his head twice and then rose as instructed.

"Attack me with your full strength."

"This..." The young Taoist hesitated for a moment, but ultimately obeyed.

The young Taoist's figure vanished in an instant.

It was replaced by a torrential downpour from the sky.

Upon closer inspection, each drop of rain was a chillingly sharp sword.

The sword rain storm surrounded Li Fan, intending to tear him to shreds.

The newly born young Taoist was a complete blank slate, only able to faithfully execute Li Fan's commands.

Now, when he attacked, he showed no restraint whatsoever.

"Even with nascent intelligence, it could unleash so many pure and different sword intents. If it were a cultivator, they might need centuries of training to reach such a realm. Is this the innate advantage of a tool spirit's transformation?"

"Unfortunately, this liquid long sword is still within the category of a realm artifact. The limit of its power is only so much."

Li Fan did not dodge or evade, letting the sword rain pour down on him.

Each sword energy, though seemingly powerful, would explode with a dazzling golden light as if hitting something invisible just before touching Li Fan. Then, it would dissipate into nothingness.

The heavy rain did not even manage to wet Li Fan's clothes.

"Withdraw!"

Li Fan merely waved his sleeve. All the sword rain was gathered. He tapped his finger lightly, producing a crisp "ding" sound.

The young Taoist immediately revealed his original form, falling to the ground in a disheveled state.

"Thank you, Great Master, for showing mercy!"

"Great Master's divine power is boundless, invincible throughout the universe!"

The young Taoist hastily got up and instinctively knelt, praising Li Fan.

"It has transformed into a life form. However, its strength is far from being able to serve as my shield."

"It needs further strengthening." Li Fan narrowed his eyes and had the young Taoist revert to his original form.

After the Life Form Shape was inscribed, the surface of the liquid long sword seemed to ripple like living water, appearing even more agile.

Li Fan already had a plan in mind for how to strengthen this sword.

His strength lay entirely in immortal formations. The best method, naturally, was "Formation Refinement."

Origin Energy Essence surged, and Daoist golden patterns transformed into array units, all integrated into the liquid long sword.

The immortal array entered the sword, and the liquid long sword instantly seemed to boil, its surface shaking violently.

As a realm artifact, under normal circumstances, it should not have been able to withstand the majestic and transcendent power of the immortal array. However, Li Fan was currently inscribing the "Ephemeral, Xuanhuang Beings" Great Array, which incorporated all the immortal arrays he had mastered so far.

The array transformed and evolved, possessing the power of life and death, which was enough to protect and maintain the liquid long sword, preventing it from being destroyed.

Of course, Li Fan also vaguely sensed the effect of the "Life Form Shape" during the formation array process.

"The birth of intelligence has caused the liquid long sword itself to undergo a qualitative change. Otherwise, it might not have been able to withstand the initial impact before the immortal array inscription was completed."

Golden light flickered continuously. Seven days later, Li Fan finally completed the inscription of the Xuanhuang Beings Great Array.

What he had left within the liquid long sword at this moment was merely a rudimentary form, like basic array units of a precisely assembled mechanism. To activate the array and make it evolve, energy needed to be injected. If it relied solely on the liquid long sword itself, it would likely be drained and depleted within a short time.

As for Origin Energy Essence, Li Fan had no intention of letting this sword use it.

After all, with the Xuanhuang sublimation imminent, every additional point of Origin Energy Essence reserve increased Li Fan's chances of success.

If this creation, meant to be a shield, had to compete with him for resources…

Wouldn't that go against his original intention?

However, Li Fan did not intend to let this liquid long sword become a mere decorative piece that could only drive the immortal array for a short time. In fact, Li Fan already had a brilliant idea in mind.

"Energy. Infinite."

Li Fan looked up at the Star Sea, his eyes narrowing.

After some preparation, twenty days later.

In the empty Star Sea, a blue-robed young Taoist chanted unintelligibly.

What he chanted was the enhanced version of the Immortal Boat's Tai Jia Divine Art.

And Li Fan was hidden far away, secretly observing.

That's right, he intended to replicate the Immortal Boat's act of "Jun Xing Hai." However, this time, it was not Li Fan, but the liquid long sword!

Admittedly, based on past experiences, by performing "Jun Xing Hai," it was possible to be assimilated by the Star Sea.

To become a Star Spirit.

But the liquid long sword contained the "Life Form Shape"!

The Life Form Shape had even created the independent consciousness of this Utmost Darkness Star Sea. Its status must be above the Star Sea.

As long as the Life Form Shape remained unbroken, even if it transformed into a Star Spirit, its life and death would be within Li Fan's grasp.

"Star Spirits cannot defy the Star Sea's consciousness."

"Creations of the Life Form Shape cannot defy their creator's will."

"When these two contradict..."

"Let's see who is superior!"

The young Taoist's chanting continued endlessly, as if he had done it countless times, without the slightest hint of unfamiliarity. It was even more perfect than most of the Immortal Boat elders.

The learning ability of a tool spirit transformed into a human form was indeed far beyond ordinary people.

However, perhaps because he had already been forced to communicate with the Star Sea once through the Tai Jia Divine Art, the Star Sea consciousness seemed to have developed some "resistance." This time, it took almost twice as long as before to summon the Star Sea consciousness.

A purple-gold vortex, like a deep, mysterious eye, reappeared in the Star Sea.

The young Taoist did not hesitate in the slightest. His movements were like a flying dragon, and the "Jun" character script erupted vigorously.

The Star Sea's reaction was still to accept whatever came.

But compared to the Immortal Boat elders who had experienced thousands of years of storms, the young Taoist, who had only been born for less than a month and had almost no knowledge or experience, did not seem to arouse much interest from the Star Sea.

But no matter what, the "Jun" character was formed.

Infinite Star Sea energy then poured down from the void.

The young Taoist's body was tempered by starlight and gradually transformed into a starlight spirit, with blue starlight shining, and stars connected like bones and meridians.

Suddenly, as if impacted by the infinite power of the Star Sea, the Life Form Shape patterns hidden within the young Taoist's body inexplicably began to shine, appearing on his body surface.

It was just enough to serve as an external force of collision and excitation, and the Life Form Shape finally revealed its original radiance.

It was black, representing emptiness, but at the same time, it shone with all the brilliant colors of the world.

The outermost part of the pattern was covered with a faint white light, also representing emptiness.

This colorful black with fluorescent edges.

So dazzling and unforgettable, the color immediately overshadowed the blue of the Star Sea.

Within the purple-gold vortex, thunderous roars, amplified ten thousand times, suddenly erupted.

Even Li Fan, who was observing from afar, could feel the Star Sea's fury from the turbulent Star Sea vortex.

Anger notwithstanding.

But the Star Sea consciousness would not act rashly.

The thunder was loud, but the rain was light. The purple-gold vortex disappeared far faster than it had appeared.

The threat from the Star Sea vanished, and the Life Form Shape re-hidden within the body. Only the starlight spirit Taoist boy remained, standing blankly in the Star Sea.

"Success?"

Li Fan did not expect things to be easier than he had estimated. He calmed his mind and sensed the connection between himself and the young Taoist.

The sovereign power of the Life Form Shape still existed.

It had not disappeared due to the influence of the Star Sea's primordial will.

Li Fan thought with a move of his mind, and the young Taoist's figure, fluttering, arrived before him several times faster than before.

"Thank you, Great Master, for bestowing this good fortune!"

Li Fan calmly observed the young Taoist's new starlight body.

With the sovereign power of the Life Form Shape, Li Fan was able to see the internal details through the infinite starlight.

Each point of light resembled a passage.

Leading to an unknown mysterious place, which was the true source of infinite Star Sea power.

Perhaps because it was too vast and exceeded Li Fan's perceptual abilities, Li Fan could not sense any anomalies from it.

The Star Sea consciousness's restrictions had not disappeared, but were merely suppressed by the Life Form Shape, unable to affect the young Taoist for the time being.

Li Fan also vaguely sensed that as infinite Star Sea power continuously gushed out from the passage, under the tempering of the Star power, the myriad laws of the Star Sea were also slowly integrating into and transforming the young Taoist's sword body.

"Although it has not reached the level of an immortal artifact, it is still a Supreme sword."

"With infinite Star Sea power as its source, it is enough to drive the immortal array to its maximum load and operate continuously."

Li Fan reached out and grasped the long sword, which had returned to its liquid form.

It was no longer liquid. Brilliant starlight surged, as if it were the Star Sea itself.

In the flickering light, countless worlds seemed to be born and die within it.

Having personally forged such a sharp weapon, Li Fan could not help but feel a surge of emotion.

"I wonder if I can use this sword to mobilize the infinite power of the Star Sea?"

With a thought, a large amount of Star Sea power surged out from the sword.

But this primordial and pure Star Sea power was not the same as the spiritual energy cultivated by mortals.

After entering Li Fan's body, it could not be absorbed and utilized.

Instead, it rampaged within his body like a flood, wantonly causing destruction.

Li Fan frowned slightly, and had no choice but to force it out of his body.

"What a pity. However, there must be a cultivation method that can transform Star Sea power into my own use." Li Fan could not help but think of the Tai Jia Realm cultivators who had wielded the power of the Star Sea back then.

After a moment, Li Fan shook his head: "I might be getting confused. Even with the Star Sea's infinity, it is ultimately bound by the Life Form Shape."

"Pursuing quantity that cannot achieve qualitative change..."

"Ultimately leads to going astray."

"But being able to easily create a Supreme being like this is definitely a great thing for me right now."

If he had more than a dozen Supreme beings to protect him, even if they were just Supreme tool spirits, it would be enough for Li Fan to sweep through the Star Sea.

Thinking this, Li Fan was about to use the same method again.

However, what surprised Li Fan was that.

The Life Form Shape…

He could no longer inscribe it onto other objects!

Although he still remembered the patterns in his mind, he could not inscribe them when it mattered.

"So there is such a restriction."

After trying a few more times and confirming that the restriction was indeed real, Li Fan could not help but feel a pang of regret.

"I originally wanted to use the Life Form Shape to create an army of tool spirits. To unify the Star Sea and explore beyond the High Wall."

"After all, a creation that is completely under control is much easier to use than a cultivator."

"What a pity."

Li Fan sighed and shook his head, tossing the starlight long sword in his hand.

The young Taoist reverted to human form and stood before Li Fan with his head bowed.

Li Fan pondered: "The saying goes, 'Things are infinite in quantity and endless in time, their divisions are not constant.' Now that you have obtained the infinite power of the Star Sea, you are no longer bound by mortal shackles and have transcended the mundane."

"From now on, I shall call you..."

"【Qiu Shui】 (Autumn Water)!"

The young Taoist was initially stunned, not understanding how the words "infinite," "endless," and "constant" related to Qiu Shui.

But the Great Master's words were like commands.

The young Taoist no longer thought about it and happily kowtowed and bowed before Li Fan.

After accepting the name "Qiu Shui," the aura emanating from the young Taoist seemed to have undergone some mysterious change.

He seemed more like a naturally born creature.

As the creator, Li Fan instantly felt a sense of enlightenment.

If, one day, Qiu Shui could fully evolve into a true life form and escape his destiny as a creation.

Then Li Fan could begin again, inscribing the Life Form Shape to create a new one.

Li Fan savored it for a long time, his expression unreadable.

"Hmph."

"It's better to have pure creations."Chapter 1371

"Perhaps it was the 'Dao Inscriber Immortal' who made it!"

"After all, each True Immortal Character Script corresponds to an Immortal Realm law, and to be able to superimpose and fuse so many characters so effortlessly..."

Li Fan's expression turned grave as he levitated the Immortal Domain chess piece in front of him.

All the sacred aura had vanished after the unfolding process halted. The chess piece now felt like an ordinary object, lying quietly in Li Fan's hand.

He attempted to activate it again, but the Immortal Domain chess piece showed no reaction to external stimuli.

"As expected, it still requires the Medicine King Sect's Longevity Azure Energy."

"Furthermore, the unfolding of the Immortal Domain chess piece itself requires some form of energy. The previous failure, however, means it needs time for energies to accumulate again."

Li Fan toyed with the smooth, cold chess piece, pondering in his heart.

In the distance, at the center of the Star Sea, the sea of black energy, agitated by the aura of the Immortal Domain, did not subside with the halting of the Immortal Domain's unfolding. Instead, it seemed to have been put into overdrive, its black energy rolling and expanding uncontrollably, threatening to engulf the entire Star Sea.

Li Fan's brow furrowed as he contemplated for a moment before using the 'Great Annihilation Divine Technique' in this location.

Due to the frequent use of the Xuan Immortal Boat, the Star Sea consciousness had lost interest in responding to Li Fan's communications.

However, from his limited senses...

The Star Sea's origin intent seemed to be completely unaware of the rampant black energy flooding the Star Sea's center.

This acting blind was deeply unsettling for Li Fan.

It was as if his body were being gnawed by countless black insects, yet the owner remained oblivious.

Such a bizarre phenomenon could only mean that the true nature of the black energy far surpassed the Star Sea

Chapter 1379: Condensing the Eternal Remnant Thought

The little Taoist boy Qiu Shui let out a yelp, and his body instantly exploded into countless fragments.

But he did not simply fall in defeat. Instead, the countless fragments continued to rain down upon Tian Yang's head.

This move, which Qiu Shui had previously demonstrated before Li Fan, had been greatly enhanced after its sublimation.

Connected to the power of the infinite Star Sea, the torrential rain was relentless and unending.

Each drop of rain contained the maximum destructive power that the Qiu Shui Sword could unleash.

Boom boom boom boom!

Even with the combat consciousness of the Immortal Puppet Ancestor boosting him, allowing him to dodge most of the sword rain attacks through his shifting form, the sheer number of sword lights erupted instantly.

Countless points of light exploded violently on Tian Yang's immortal body.

The surrounding spatial field vibrated incessantly. The defense that could even isolate the power of True Immortal Character Scripts became precarious under the attack of an infinite number of Supreme Sword Qi.

But Tian Yang's expression remained as calm and detached as ever. It did not change in the slightest due to the gradually unfavorable situation.

On his forehead, a vertical eye suddenly appeared.

The third eye, emitting a faint golden light, was not an ordinary object, like an ancient Desolate God. Its gaze saw all the sword rain in the sky freeze.

Tian Yang let out an unconscious growl, his hands forming a void grip in front of his chest.

The countless sword rain transformed by Qiu Shui was instantly fused by Tian Yang. It transformed into a single sphere!

An invisible fire emerged from Tian Yang's palm.

It seemed as if it were about to completely incinerate the water sphere within!

Qiu Shui, appearing disheveled from the water sphere, hurriedly shouted towards Li Fan, "Great Master, save me!"

Li Fan only wanted to test Qiu Shui's actual combat power, not to destroy this hard-won Supreme assistant. With a thought, Tian Yang, who was about to make the final killing blow, paused slightly and finally stopped.

At the same time, Li Fan sensed that an extremely profound and inexplicable aura had disappeared from Tian Yang's body.

Tian Yang silently returned to Li Fan's side, while Qiu Shui hurriedly knelt and kowtowed, repeatedly calling out, "Great Master is merciful."

Although Qiu Shui lost to Tian Yang, Li Fan was quite satisfied with the strength he displayed during the battle.

Leaving aside everything else, the move of 'Heavenly Sword Rain' alone was something Li Fan himself could not resist, only evade.

And the reason Tian Yang won so easily was not only due to the insights gained from the Immortal Puppet Ancestor and the Thousand-Eyed Desolate God but also, crucially, the strand of invisible fire that Tian Yang finally displayed.

Judging from Qiu Shui's extreme fear, this invisible fire had the ability to truly threaten his survival.

This made Li Fan curious.

He had always known that the power of the invincible Star Sea could be wielded by Qiu Shui Sword, and even Li Fan himself could not destroy Qiu Shui Sword, only evade it. No other divine ability or spell could inflict actual damage on it. But this invisible fire could do what Li Fan could not...

Li Fan then inquired about it from Tian Yang.

Who knew that Tian Yang's answer was only two words: "Unknown."

Li Fan frowned slightly. After further communication, he finally understood. It turned out that this invisible fire was naturally unleashed by Tian Yang after entering a pure combat consciousness. As for its principle and how it was unleashed, Tian Yang knew nothing about it.

That pure combat consciousness originated from the inheritance of the Ancestor Puppet. Once activated, with a singular focus and a subtle connection to the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth, it launched relentless attacks on the target based on instinct.

"Instinct..."

Li Fan had a vague guess: "It must be related to that Eternal Remnant Thought."

"I never expected that this Eternal Remnant Thought could also be used as a divine ability to harm others. It is indeed worthy of being an existence that can resonate with the Great Dao."

Li Fan pondered carefully for a moment, feeling a slight regret.

Although he had already known that the Eternal Remnant Thought had a very high status, he had not yet found a way to comprehend and apply it, other than 'Returning to True' actively absorbing it.

"Speaking of which, the seeds planted in this life should be bearing fruit and ready for harvest."

After instructing Qiu Shui to continue seeking guidance from "Second Master" Tian Yang, Li Fan flashed and arrived within the Lecture Platform.

Li Fan gently waved his hand, and on the giant eye formed by the simulated Heavenly Dao, the figures of Kou Hong and Dao Xuanzi were projected.

In this life, when he sensed that the beliefs of these two "Sincere Dao Seekers" might be the seeds of an Eternal Remnant Thought, Li Fan had secretly made many arrangements.

He attempted to catalyze these seeds, or even the birth of a true Eternal Remnant Thought.

Thus, the brothers, whose paths had already been bumpy, who had fought to the death over a mere Core Formation technique in past reincarnations, had even more tragic experiences in this life.

Over the years, they had traveled far and wide in search of cultivation techniques beyond the Core Formation stage.

It could not be said that they had gained nothing.

But every time, after finding anything valuable in the ancient sect ruins, a Nascent Soul stage cultivator would suddenly descend from the sky. In front of them, they would snatch away their gains.

If it happened once or twice, Kou Hong and Dao Xuanzi could barely accept it.

But this had happened about ten times in a row.

The pent-up frustration in Kou Hong's chest could no longer be contained. Every time, he had to fight to the death with the Nascent Soul cultivators who snatched their gains, but he was always restrained by the still rational Dao Xuanzi.

But even a clay figurine has a temper. In the last incident, after this happened again, even Dao Xuanzi could not stand it. The brothers joined forces and launched a desperate attack on the suddenly appearing Nascent Soul cultivator.

The outcome was as expected.

The brothers were severely humiliated, but the other party did not take their lives. Instead, they directly revealed their identity and contemptuously ridiculed them, saying, "Two wastes, I will beat you every time I see you." Then they left.

After this, Kou Hong and Dao Xuanzi were truly dejected for a while.

But worthy of being Sincere Dao Seekers, they quickly recovered from the blow. In fact, they secretly vowed in their hearts to cultivate successfully and seek revenge on that Nascent Soul cultivator.

For this purpose, they even abandoned their long-held principles and their identity as rogue cultivators, choosing to join the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

From then on, they no longer needed to venture into the ancient sect ruins. They simply accepted commission tasks daily, slowly accumulating Alliance Contribution Points.

The brothers scrimped and saved, finally accumulating enough Contribution Points to exchange for a Core Formation technique.

The moment the cultivation technique's content flowed into their minds as golden light, Kou Hong and Dao Xuanzi both burst into tears.

Although they had managed to step into the Core Formation realm, they were still far from their goal of revenge.

The two brothers worked even harder, accepting commission tasks to earn Contribution Points.

But the price of Nascent Soul techniques had suddenly skyrocketed. It required tens of thousands of Contribution Points, leaving the two of them just staring blankly, completely unable to do anything. Especially if they wanted to succeed in revenge, the Nascent Soul technique they cultivated had to be powerful. Otherwise, even at the same Nascent Soul realm, they might not be a match for their great enemy.

The powerful Nascent Soul techniques they coveted cost almost over a hundred thousand points. The price was so high that it was almost despair-inducing.

At first, the two of them silently accumulated. But after a period of time, after calculating their income and expenses, they realized that it would take nearly fifty to sixty years to exchange for a Nascent Soul technique.

This was assuming no accidents occurred.

However, how could there be no accidents in this world?

To earn Contribution Points faster, they had to take on tasks that were somewhat dangerous. This meant that during the process of completing the tasks, they were likely to get injured. Without the power of a Grotto-Heaven to constantly reshape their bodies, healing injuries was an extremely costly matter.

Moreover, the two of them had notoriously bad luck.

During their missions, three out of ten times, they would encounter various accidents. Although they did not lose their lives, they were always seriously injured. After deducting the cost of healing, there was almost no surplus. If it weren't for the fact that these accidents were all due to natural disasters, beast rampages, and other events not involving cultivators, the two would have suspected that they had offended some great power who was toying with them.

It was bad enough that they earned little, but just accumulating a little each day, they could still see hope.

But somehow, their misfortunes somehow spread, becoming more and more exaggerated. Some even rumored that they had been cursed with an anomaly, and anyone who became involved with them would suffer misfortune.

Gradually, cultivators willing to accompany them on missions became extinct. More crucially, the task issuers, to avoid being implicated by the so-called curse, often specifically stated in task descriptions that Kou Hong and Dao Xuanzi were unable to accept the tasks.

Accumulating Contribution Points completely became a futile endeavor.

At this point, the brothers had still not given up on their ideals.

After some discussion, they returned to their old profession: exploring sect ruins.

Anyway, with the Heaven Profound Mirror responsible for recycling exploration materials, they didn't have to worry about exploration gains being unsellable.

It had to be said that after advancing to the Core Formation realm, their strength had greatly increased. Combined with years of experience exploring ruins, after several attempts, they had indeed reaped considerable rewards.

Kou Hong and Dao Xuanzi were overjoyed, thinking their luck had finally turned.

However, the two brothers were somewhat puzzled. The recycling prices given by the Heaven Profound Mirror were often much lower than the market price. After deducting the cost of various materials needed for each exploration, they actually didn't save much Contribution Points.

But compared to slowly earning through tasks before, it was still much better.

The two brothers were very optimistic.

Looking at their Contribution Point balance increasing little by little each day, they felt a faint sense of happiness.

Finally, after successfully exploring several small ruins without encountering any Nascent Soul cultivators intercepting them.

They were only one step away from finally purchasing their desired Nascent Soul technique.

The two decided to seize the moment while their luck was still good and go explore again.

As long as they didn't come back completely empty-handed, they would achieve their goal.

For this last exploration, the two were extremely cautious.

As if all the bad luck in their lives was finally being reversed at this moment.

Based on their previous exchange experience, this time the harvest should be at least worth 30,000 Contribution Points. The brothers had truly turned their fortunes around.

Kou Hong and Dao Xuanzi suppressed the joy in their hearts, maintaining calm expressions, and quickly rushed towards the nearest floating sky city.

At the same time, they were fantasizing about the days to come: soon, they would successfully exchange for the Nascent Soul technique, find a Nascent Soul Grotto-Heaven, advance to the Nascent Soul realm, achieve bloody revenge, and soar to new heights.

The journey was all smooth sailing. When they returned to the Heaven Profound Mirror and sold all the ancient items from the ruins, receiving a full 30,000 Contribution Points.

Kou Hong and Dao Xuanzi finally breathed a sigh of relief.

After weeping tears of joy, the two eagerly opened the cultivation technique exchange page, ready to make their purchase.

However, the next moment, the mechanical, cold voice of the Heaven Profound Mirror sounded like thunder in the ears of the two brothers.

"What do you mean, 'Insufficient Contribution Points'?" "We clearly each have over seventy thousand Contribution Points!" Kou Hong roared, his eyes turning blood red, his entire body trembling, fiercely digging his nails into his flesh, oblivious to the pain. He roared and questioned. "We have painstakingly accumulated these over the years through hard work and risking our lives. It's impossible that there aren't..." Dao Xuanzi, however, managed to maintain some semblance of calm, stating the two numbers and requesting the Heaven Profound Mirror to re-examine.

But the cold sweat constantly dripping from his forehead and his increasingly pale face ultimately revealed his inner panic.

There was no long silence, and soon the Heaven Profound Mirror's reply arrived.

"Verified, Kou Hong currently holds 234 Contribution Points, and Dao Xuanzi currently holds 264 Contribution Points."

"The source of the Contribution Points is detailed as follows."

"Besides this, there are no other records."

"Repeat..."

The cold voice echoed in the ears of the two brothers like a death sentence.

At this point, even Dao Xuanzi could no longer maintain his composure.

He stared blankly at the records displayed by the Heaven Profound Mirror.

He discovered that the Contribution Point data had returned to the very first day they joined the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

All the hard work and accumulated Contribution Points of countless days had turned into nothing?

Dao Xuanzi felt a wave of dizziness.

"Could it be that all of this was our hallucination?"

But then, Kou Hong's roar awakened him.

Their Core Formation realm strength was real.

And the 30,000 Contribution Points they had just obtained were also real.

If that were the case, how could the memories of these past few years be false?

"You swallowed our Contribution Points! Our hard-earned money!"

"Give it back!"

Dao Xuanzi's face also turned grim.

The Heaven Profound Mirror continued to repeat the same cold words.

The two finally completely broke down and actually attacked the Heaven Profound Mirror.

After several warnings yielded no results, the Heaven Profound Mirror directly expelled them.

The miserable state of Kou Hong and Dao Xuanzi naturally attracted the attention of the Myriad Immortals Alliance cultivators.

But no matter how they cried and complained, the Heaven Profound Mirror, which had never made a mistake, actually swallowed their accumulated Contribution Points...

Coupled with the notorious "two unlucky duo,"

Naturally, no one believed their words.

Kou Hong and Dao Xuanzi cried tears of blood, realizing that despite their pleas, the surrounding people remained indifferent.

Having recognized the reality, they finally stopped crying and struggling.

The memories of the past few years since joining the Myriad Immortals Alliance flashed through their minds. It was like a dream.

"Let's go," Kou Hong gritted his teeth and said.

Chapter 1380: Dark Secrets Hidden in the Underworld Prison

"The Myriad Immortals Alliance truly devours without spitting out bones!" The thought that his hard-earned seventy thousand contribution points had vanished in an instant made Kou Hong's eyes turn bloodshot, his heart gripped by piercing pain.

"Why did we get bewitched and choose to join the Myriad Immortals Alliance?" Even Dao Xuanzi, usually the calmer of the two, could no longer suppress his turmoil.

"Let's defect to the Five Elders Association! We must make the Myriad Immortals Alliance pay the price!"

Having reached a consensus, the two silently set off towards the Five Elders Association's territory after leaving the Immortal Alliance Sky City.

However, they forgot one crucial fact.

Although the Myriad Immortals Alliance officially stated that it did not restrict the personal freedom of its members, and the act of leaving the Myriad Immortals Alliance to join the Five Elders Association was not forbidden.

Everything obtained within the Immortal Alliance, however, had to be returned.

Thus, as soon as they showed signs of defecting, a Soul Transformation stage cultivator from the Enforcement Hall pursued them.

Sensing the powerful aura behind them, Kou Hong and Dao Xuanzi's expressions shifted slightly.

Even as they quickened their pace, the vast gap in cultivation between the "Heavenly Abyss" and their realm was not something that could be bridged. Soon, they were intercepted.

To add insult to injury, the cultivation techniques we painstakingly redeemed with our contribution points are also to be recalled?"

Now that you are clearly going to join the Five Elders Association, do you expect us to let you provide resources to our enemy? Letting you keep your dog lives is already the Immortal Alliance's mercy!"

The Soul Transformation stage protector raised his brow slightly, appearing somewhat surprised by the power the two could manifest.

In the firmament, a cave void phantom, resembling a black sun, suddenly materialized. The gap between the Golden Core stage and the Soul Transformation stage was simply too vast. Though Kou Hong and Dao Xuanzi had some luck, they were ultimately just ordinary beings in the world, without any fortuitous encounters to bridge such a disparity.

Just then, a resolute glint flashed in Dao Xuanzi's eyes.
