A rusty-looking long sword hovered before Dao Xuanzi, its tip pointing directly at the Myriad Immortals Alliance Soul Transformation stage protector. The Soul Transformation stage protector's eyes flashed with a hint of surprise. Countless specks of light erupted from Dao Xuanzi's body, resembling myriad stars twinkling for a moment before all converging towards the Dao Xuan Sword. The specks of light repaired the decaying long sword. At this moment, Dao Xuanzi and the Dao Xuan Sword became one! The peerless divine weapon from ancient times finally revealed its true form.

"Escape quickly!" Dao Xuanzi's voice echoed in Kou Hong's ear. Then, Kou Hong saw a dazzling sword light that seemed to cleave heaven and earth. Amidst a massive roar, the black circular cave void emitted a faint white light and disintegrated inch by inch. The Dao Xuan Sword, however, continued its momentum unimpeded. Taking advantage of its final moments of life, it flew towards the direction of the Myriad Immortals Alliance Sky City.

"Dao Xuanzi!" The cave void of the Soul Transformation stage cultivator was shattered, and Kou Hong regained his mobility. His eyes were filled with tears, his heart filled with grief. He knew that Dao Xuanzi had sacrificed his own life to save him. With the Soul Transformation stage protector dead, the Myriad Immortals Alliance would surely send stronger pursuers. Kou Hong knew he couldn't linger here. He wiped away his tears and galloped towards the Five Elders Association's territory. "Myriad Immortals Alliance..." Kou Hong gritted his teeth inwardly. "You wait!" "I will become stronger! I will take revenge!" The flames of vengeance burned fiercely in Kou Hong's eyes. As he was about to reach the border line... A ray of light suddenly descended from the horizon, passing straight through Kou Hong's body. "..." Kou Hong's mouth opened, wanting to say something, but ultimately could not utter a sound. His head flew off, blood gushing forth. It was only then that the ray of light revealed its true form: a flowing long sword. A young cultivator, clad in black Enforcement Hall robes, slowly materialized. "To fail to capture two mere Golden Core cultivators, what utter trash. They deserve to die!" The young cultivator spat dismissively, then ignored Kou Hong's corpse. "Strange, why has that long sword disappeared? And the inexplicable loss of contribution points... Perhaps it truly is a conspiracy by the Five Elders Association." Murmuring to himself, the young cultivator vanished. A long time later, Kou Hong's head, which had rolled to the ground, eyes wide open in disbelief, scattered into gravel dispersed by the wind. Only a dragon-shaped branch between his eyebrows remained. Li Fan's figure quietly appeared. With a wave of his hand, the dragon-shaped branch flew into his palm. Faintly, he could hear the endless, resentful roars emanating from within the branch. Li Fan frowned slightly, waiting and observing the reaction of the remnant. After a moment, he sighed faintly, "It doesn't seem to have as strong an appetite for devouring as I thought." "Alas, perhaps I was being too simplistic." "However, this wisp of remnant will crystallization is not entirely useless." Thinking this, Li Fan forcefully fed it to 'Returning to True'. The dragon-shaped branch in his hand slowly disappeared. At the same time, in Li Fan's mind, some blurry images flashed by rapidly. "This is..." Li Fan frowned. Undeniably, these flashing scenes were produced by 'Returning to True' after devouring Kou Hong's remnant will. Although Kou Hong's remnant will had not yet reached the condition to form an 'Eternal Remnant Will,' it was barely qualified to become food for 'Returning to True'. However, in the past, when 'Returning to True' devoured an Eternal Remnant Will, new functionalities would be born. What was the meaning of these fleeting images appearing this time after its meal? Like fleeting inspiration, these flashback scenes were difficult to capture even for Li Fan. Standing still, savoring them for a long time, Li Fan finally had some reaction. His expression became inscrutable: "It seems to be something that happened before this lifetime of mine." "What is the meaning of this?" Li Fan was somewhat bewildered, but an instinctive sense of unease welled up in his heart. However, no matter how he pondered, he could not determine the source of his unease. He could only suppress it in his heart for now. As if to calm himself, another sword, impossibly sharp, appeared in Li Fan's hand. It was Dao Xuanzi's sword, formed from his final desperate attack. The power, capable of killing a Soul Transformation cultivator, was naturally not something Li Fan paid much attention to. What Li Fan was truly interested in was the origin of this Dao Xuan Sword. He felt a trace of familiarity from this sword. Previously, Li Fan had absorbed the 'Rust Sword Dao Xuan,' which had become a "Heaven and Earth Anomaly." However, due to the absorption and erosion by heaven and earth, the Dao Xuan Sword had already greatly diverled from its original state. Therefore, even though Li Fan later experienced related events, he could not recall its origin. But in this lifetime, perhaps due to long-term nurturing and Dao Xuanzi's natural compatibility with the Dao Xuan Sword, despite only being in the Golden Core realm, he was able to restore the Dao Xuan Sword to its perfect original state. "So it's an heirloom of the Heavenly Sword Sect," Li Fan said with a sigh. With a casual flick of his finger, the Xuanhuang Sword Dao laws transformed into strands of luminous threads, infusing into the unstable, potentially shattering body of the Dao Xuan Sword. The sword body gradually stabilized. Li Fan then used the 'Array Refinement' technique to solidify it. Finally, this ancient Dao Xuan Sword was reborn, its power undiminished, perhaps even amplified. The Heavenly Sword Sect, once one of the Ten Great Immortal Sects, had long since shattered and departed, leaving only a pile of broken swords in the Sword Tomb ruins. "Heavenly Sword Sect..." Li Fan had also attempted to use the 'Manifest' character's connection ability on these remnant swords to investigate whether the Heavenly Sword Sect had successfully escaped back then. But unfortunately, under the 'Manifest' technique's shroud, although all the remnant swords extended light beams, they all pointed towards the wooden sword 'Heavenly Wonder' in the center of the Sword Tomb. Now, this resurrected Dao Xuan Sword gave Li Fan a new idea. Silently, he executed the 'Manifest' character script. Enveloping the reborn Dao Xuan Sword. Instantly, three rays of light shot out from the Dao Xuan Sword. The thickest one, like a dragon emerging from water, shot towards the sky before scattering outwards and dissipating into heaven and earth. Another ray flew towards Li Fan. The last ray, the most subtle one, drifted towards a certain location within the Xuanhuang Realm. "Hmm?" This immediately attracted Li Fan's attention. "Could it be that there are still descendants of the Heavenly Sword Sect within the Xuanhuang Realm?" Li Fan became interested. His figure floated, quickly following the ray of light. The 'Manifest' character script revealed the connections between all things. Only the caster, or someone deeply familiar with the True Immortal Character Script 'Manifest,' could see these connections. Therefore, he was not worried about this anomaly attracting others' attention. Li Fan followed the light ray, only to arrive at a place he had never considered before. The Myriad Immortals Alliance's Underworld Prison! He had once infiltrated it disguised. The restrictions of the Underworld Prison were utterly insignificant to Li Fan. Seeing the light ray rapidly descending towards the lowest level, Li Fan also entered the Underworld Prison. His expression became somewhat subtle. Because he saw that the light ray was precisely landing on the cultivator imprisoned at the deepest level of the Underworld Prison! "Strange..." Li Fan had long known that such a figure was imprisoned in the Myriad Immortals Alliance's Underworld Prison. And when he saw him before, he had vaguely felt a sense of familiarity. Now, connecting it with the performance of the Dao Xuan Sword under the 'Manifest' technique, Li Fan finally confirmed his previous guess. "A descendant of the Heavenly Sword Sect?" This imprisoned cultivator's eyebrows bore a striking resemblance to Situ Yao, the senior disciple of the Heavenly Sword Sect, from the past. However, this imprisoned cultivator had become skeletal, only showing a rough outline. Moreover, there were many people in the world who looked alike, so Li Fan could not be certain. But now, his judgment could be confirmed. "It seems I should trust my intuition." "A descendant of Situ Yao? Interesting. I recall that this senior disciple of the Heavenly Sword Sect seemed to have no descendants before the Heavenly Sword Sect departed." "Could it be..." Li Fan was greatly shaken in his heart. Just as he was about to rescue him and question him carefully, upon closer inspection, Li Fan discovered that the method used to imprison this descendant of the Heavenly Sword Sect appeared to be the work of the Heavenly Physician himself! If Li Fan hadn't secretly learned from the illusory formation in this lifetime, he wouldn't have recognized it! "Without specific unlocking methods, forcefully breaking it would undoubtedly attract the Heavenly Physician's attention." "The sublimation of the Xuanhuang in this lifetime has reached its critical final stage..." If it were before, Li Fan would definitely have waited for the next lifetime, when his strength had greatly increased, before proceeding. But precisely because Li Fan had glimpsed the Heavenly Physician's secrets in the illusory formation earlier, he did not give up directly. Instead, he attempted to try and decipher it. It was easier than he had imagined. It seemed the Heavenly Physician did not place too much importance on this individual. The seal placed upon him was not overly complex, mostly draining his spiritual energy and suppressing him. After considerable effort, Li Fan finally unsealed him. To avoid causing a commotion within the Myriad Immortals Alliance, he also set up an illusion, creating a false impression that the cultivator was still imprisoned. Li Fan, carrying the emaciated descendant of the Heavenly Sword Sect, quietly left the Myriad Immortals Alliance's Underworld Prison. Arriving at an open, unpopulated area, Li Fan was just about to speak when the golden light in his hand suddenly flashed. The person instantly broke free from Li Fan's restraint. Transforming into a beam of golden light, he fled towards the horizon. In the blink of an eye, he vanished from sight. This outcome greatly exceeded Li Fan's expectations. Instead of being surprised, he was delighted. Although the speed of the descendant of the Heavenly Sword Sect was not as fast as Li Fan's, how could he possibly outrun Li Fan? The phantom of the wooden sword unsheathed. In the next moment, Li Fan had already caught up. With a slap of his palm, he trapped him again. This time, no matter how the golden light twisted and turned, it could not escape. It was because Li Fan had already set up an immortal formation around them. "Hmm?!" The golden light stopped its futile attempts and revealed its form. In a short period, it had already recovered some vitality from its previously skeletal appearance. At least it still retained a human form, though it looked somewhat frail. "Thank you, senior, for saving my life," the person cautiously cupped his hands and said. "Why did you run?" Li Fan asked sternly. "I was imprisoned for too long... When I saw an opportunity, I couldn't help but flee," the other party explained with a wry smile. Li Fan, hearing this, had no interest in asking further. He pressed down with his left hand, intending to directly use the soul-searching technique on him. The person was struck as if by lightning. His already frail body trembled like a sieve. Countless images flooded into Li Fan's mind. However, Li Fan frowned deeply. The soul-searching proceeded smoothly, but... he found no information regarding the Heavenly Sword Sect in his memories.

Chapter 1381: Demonic Ink Killing

From the soul search, it was learned that the person before him was named Qin Zhuang.

He was originally the strongest in the Changyang Small World within the Profound Yellow Realm.

The Changyang Small World itself had no spiritual energy, only a peculiar Great Sun hanging across the sky, illuminating the world. Daytime occupied three-quarters of the day, and it was constantly lengthening, as if it intended to scorch and devour all living beings.

Qin Zhuang started as a mortal, continuously absorbing the energy of the Great Sun and developing his potential. It took him ninety-nine years to completely integrate the Great Sun in the sky into his own body.

From then on, Changyang had no sun and fell into a realm of eternal night.

Just as Qin Zhuang resolved to leave the small world, a mysterious figure approached him. Qin Zhuang, who prided himself on his world-destroying divine power, could not withstand even a few moves from the other party. Qin Zhuang was defeated miserably, but the other party spoke to him about the truth of the Profound Yellow Realm, mortals, and small worlds. And invited him to join the coalition army against the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

Qin Zhuang was convinced by the other party's demeanor and strength and readily agreed.

What followed was a vigorous and intense battle.

In this counter-offensive war of the small world, the Myriad Immortals Alliance was not as easy and dominant as their records suggested.

In fact, at the beginning, the Myriad Immortals Alliance retreated steadily, only able to cower within the central four prefectures, barely surviving.

Finally, it was the "Law Preacher" who sought help from the "Heavenly Venerate of Law Preaching," and countless golden threads rained down from outside the starry sky, completely defeating the coalition army.

The coalition army was defeated and scattered. Qin Zhuang, as one of the leaders of the coalition army, was eternally suppressed in the deepest part of the Dark Prison.

...

Li Fan carefully savored the memories of the person before him.

Seemingly without any flaws, all originating from imprints deep within the divine soul. However, Li Fan instinctively felt something was amiss.

It was not that this memory was fabricated. In fact, the Changyang Realm in its eternal night state did exist, and Li Fan had even visited it personally.

"It is the disharmony between the current body and this memory. It's like someone possessed it, a case of the cuckoo occupying the magpie's nest!" Li Fan, who had done similar things many times, instantly detected the peculiarity.

Although it was just an intuition, Li Fan believed his judgment.

"Since soul searching is useless, another method must be found."

Thinking this, Li Fan casually threw the 'Qin Zhuang', who was already weak from the soul search, to the ground.

Qin Zhuang appeared to be on the verge of death, but shortly after, he suddenly transformed into a golden light and flew towards the outside of the Profound Yellow Realm. This time, his speed was even several times faster than before. A trace of blood could be faintly seen within the golden light, indicating that Qin Zhuang was fighting desperately.

However, the outcome was the same.

With the flash of the wooden sword phantom, Li Fan picked him up again and threw him heavily back to the ground.

"Senior, spare my life, senior, spare my life..." Qin Zhuang finally showed fear, repeatedly begging for mercy.

"Situ Yao of the Heavenly Sword Sect, who is he to you?" Li Fan suddenly asked directly.

"Hmm? Junior does not understand what you are speaking of..." Qin Zhuang said blankly, cautiously.

But how could the fleeting change in Qin Zhuang's expression upon hearing the question escape Li Fan's eyes?

Having obtained the answer he wanted, Li Fan stopped wasting his breath. He pointed a finger at Qin Zhuang's forehead.

The Illusory Profound Formation enveloped Qin Zhuang.

Li Fan attempted to use the illusory formation to derive worlds and glimpse Qin Zhuang's true past.

However, this method, which had worked on the Heavenly Physician, was in vain this time!

Qin Zhuang's performance within the illusory formation perfectly matched the logic of the strongest expert in the Changyang Realm. The illusory formation's transformations derived dozens of possibilities, but the result was always the same.

This made Li Fan even doubt his own judgment.

As Qin Zhuang gradually awoke from the illusory formation, his eyes towards Li Fan held increasing fear.

He hesitated to speak.

However, it was precisely this fear that made Li Fan's doubts disappear. Instead, he became more certain that the other party must be hiding a great secret.

Li Fan clearly saw that Qin Zhuang's fear stemmed from his worry about his own secret being exposed.

If he were truly just Qin Zhuang from the small world, his fear after his entire life was exposed would be completely different from his current reaction.

"It seems that perhaps some kind of restriction or secret art protection from beyond the wall is preventing ordinary methods from prying into the secrets deep within his divine soul."

Li Fan understood and said meaningfully to Qin Zhuang, "It doesn't matter. Let me see how long you can hold on."

Li Fan was quite experienced in how to pry open a person's mouth.

He separated a simulated personality specifically for interrogation and torture. Then, Li Fan suppressed it within himself and treated it well.

"It's not that he doesn't want to speak, perhaps he truly cannot speak. Regardless, let's torture him for a while first." Li Fan narrowed his eyes, looking at Qin Zhuang, who was already suffering in hell and screaming, his expression indifferent.

"Beyond the high wall..." After a moment, he looked up at the sky, beyond the Profound Yellow Realm, and fell into deep thought.

From the various clues gathered in the past, it was known that since the beginning of the great tribulation, a group of refugees had left the Profound Yellow Realm, and some might have even successfully crossed the high wall and escaped to the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

"The Ten Great Immortal Sects, including the Heavenly Sword Sect, the Southern Underworld Sacred Beast Mountain's demonic beasts, the Shang Immortal Boat."

"These are only the known ones. The Star Sea is vast, and there are countless immortal cultivation worlds. Besides these, there must be other lucky ones."

"But Qin Zhuang is the only one who has gone and returned."

Li Fan naturally would not let him go easily.

The moment the Profound Immortal Boat broke through the High Wall, the actions of the Star Sea's origin true intent made Li Fan feel a profound sense of unease, making him unprecedentedly wary of the world beyond the High Wall.

"But most fear stems from the unknown. If I can gather some intelligence..."

"Let's see how much Qin Zhuang can endure."

Temporarily setting this matter aside, Li Fan began the final preparations before promoting the Profound Yellow's sublimation.

First, the practice of 'Hunting Ink Annihilation'.

Now, Li Fan had an eighty percent certainty of successfully promoting the Profound Yellow Realm to an Immortal Domain.

But how to eliminate the 'Heaven and Earth Soul Ink Annihilation' in the fastest time required further consideration.

Ink Annihilation was already the strongest of the Heaven and Earth Souls within the Profound Yellow Realm. After the Profound Yellow's sublimation, its power would undoubtedly increase.

"But no matter how it changes, its essence is still a Heaven and Earth Soul."

"As long as its attributes and weaknesses are known, a targeted strategy can be devised..."

Li Fan pondered for a moment and arrived at the Congyun Sea.

He separated a wisp of his divine sense and sent it towards the Myriad Immortals Island.

Concurrently, Hong Xi, the lord of Myriad Immortals Island and a cultivator of the Soul Transformation stage, suddenly felt something and looked up at the sky.

"Heaven and Earth Soul!"

A greedy intent arose in his heart.

Normally, given Hong Xi's cautious nature, he would have sought out a few fellow Daoists to plan together, or even invited a few Integrated Dao seniors to provide support.

But now...

"If the news leaks, attracting everyone's siege, who knows who will ultimately claim the Heaven and Earth Soul."

"I have been cultivating in seclusion for many years. A mere Heaven and Earth Soul... I alone will hunt it down."

A trace of arrogance appeared in Hong Xi's eyes.

Seven days later, believing he had made sufficient preparations, Hong Xi began hunting the Crimson Flame.

This Heaven and Earth Soul, capable of burning mountains and boiling seas, was truly just for show. It retreated steadily under his fierce attacks.

Hong Xi fought with increasing vigor, displaying all his learned skills with great satisfaction.

Finally, after a full day, he completely slew the Crimson Flame!

A new Integrated Dao Immortal Venerable was born above the Congyun Sea!

Hong Xi stood in the air, feeling the unprecedented power within his body, his heart surging with excitement.

He envisioned a beautiful future.

Suddenly, he felt a palpitation out of nowhere.

Then, cold sweat broke out, as if he had just walked back from the gates of hell.

Hong Xi abruptly turned his head, looking around.

The world was silent, the scenery was serene, yet nothing seemed to have happened.

Hong Xi was somewhat bewildered, but after much thought, he concluded that this was a normal phenomenon after integrating with the Dao.

He then dismissed it from his mind.

Little did he know, he had indeed narrowly escaped death.

If not for Li Fan intervening and stopping Ink Annihilation.

In the Great Profound Lecture Platform.

Li Fan looked at the ink-colored mass, still growing and expanding under the shroud of countless golden threads, a hint of solemnity flashing across his face.

"As expected of Ink Annihilation."

"It can even corrupt Origin Energy Essence, a near-Immortal power."

"And turn it into its own use!" Li Fan exclaimed in admiration after studying it for a while.

After Crimson Flame was slain, Ink Annihilation, which had been ordered to descend, was not destroyed by Li Fan.

Instead, it was trapped and studied.

Li Fan couldn't help but recall the Heavenly Physician's pointer in the illusory formation regarding the Great Five Elements Annihilation Sword.

"True annihilation does not exist within the self-circulation of the world. So-called extinction is merely a precursor to better rebirth. To touch upon true destruction, one must venture into the depths of the starry sky..."

But what Li Fan felt from Ink Annihilation now contradicted the Heavenly Physician's conclusion.

Li Fan had witnessed true annihilation and even personally brought it about.

Naturally, he knew what true destruction and void looked like.

It was almost exactly the same as what Ink Annihilation caused.

"Only with the addition of the Profound Yellow Realm's unique characteristics." Li Fan mused.

"Ink Annihilation's power of extinction is certainly not something that can originate from an ordinary immortal cultivation world."

"It is likely a mechanism that has existed in the Profound Yellow Realm since the beginning of its creation."

Li Fan extended one of his fingers into the layers of golden thread protection.

Instantly, the connection between his finger and his body was severed.

Even the ink-like substances, wriggling like countless insects, intended to further erode and encroach before the connection was severed.

Not only the body, but also the divine soul.

It was like peeling a potato, layer by layer, scraping away at his flesh and soul, before Li Fan could truly isolate himself from Ink Annihilation.

"Such strong offensive power!"

Li Fan frowned inwardly.

"And that feeling of the connection suddenly breaking..."

Li Fan was somewhat hesitant. After circulating the power within his body to replenish what was lost, he extended his index finger to test again.

Without a doubt, his index finger was instantly swallowed by Ink Annihilation.

Moreover, Li Fan keenly noticed that Ink Annihilation's movements this time were even faster than the previous one.

"The degree of erosion has also deepened considerably."

"Ink Annihilation is learning and improving."

After completing the 'potato peeling' repair for the second time, Li Fan finally stopped.

"My intuition was correct. The feeling of the connection disappearing when engulfed by Ink Annihilation is exactly the same as that from beyond the High Wall."

"What could this be?"

Li Fan's brow furrowed, full of doubts.

Unable to find an answer after much thought, Li Fan decided to first find Ink Annihilation's weakness.

"Theoretically speaking, the forces of life and destruction are mutually opposed."

"To deal with Ink Annihilation, one needs infinite vitality."

Li Fan's heart moved, and he arrived at the crevice hollows beneath the Star Sea.

He drew upon the power of vitality from within and infused it towards the sealed Ink Annihilation.

However, he did not expect that this vitality would serve as nourishment for Ink Annihilation.

The ink-colored mass suddenly collided, and the seal of countless golden threads became precarious in an instant.

Fortunately, outside the golden threads, there were still several layers of immortal formations providing protection.

Li Fan leisurely reinforced the golden threads and the blockade.

After a burst of impact, unable to break through the blockade, Ink Annihilation seemed to give up struggling after a while. It stopped expanding outwards.

Then, it retracted inwards.

The ink-colored mass grew denser, gradually becoming as deep and profound as the Utmost Darkness Star Sea.

A mysterious aura slowly emerged from Ink Annihilation.

Li Fan's pupils contracted: "This is..."

Within the void, shaped like a human figure with golden edges, Li Fan actually felt an aura similar to the black energy in the center of the Star Sea!

"Tribulation of Dao Annihilation?!"

Startled, Li Fan subconsciously doubled his protective measures.

At the same time, his thoughts raced: "I previously speculated that the Profound Yellow Realm might have been created by the Immortal Realm as a testing ground to find a solution to the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation."

"But I never figured out how to counter it."

"But if Ink Annihilation is a weakened version of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation..."

"The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, integrated into the Profound Yellow Realm's body, becomes part of the world's principles through the cycle of heaven and earth."

"Ink Annihilation acts, and all things in the world turn into nothingness. However, afterwards..."

Li Fan's eyes suddenly flashed with several images.

These were scenes from the past, after Ink Annihilation had annihilated the world, where vitality reappeared from the void of absolute extinction.

"Although Ink Annihilation's extinction is absolute, vitality can still be restored."

"This is the Profound Yellow Realm's self-evolving counteracting power."

A realization suddenly dawned upon Li Fan.

His gaze towards Ink Annihilation changed again.

"I was mistaken."

"Although Ink Annihilation's form of manifestation is extinction, its essence is still the Profound Yellow Realm's Heaven and Earth Soul."

"Since it is a Heaven and Earth Soul..."

Li Fan gently pointed towards the center of the ink-colored mass.

"Profound Yellow World Destruction Transformation!"

In an instant, not just one, but all the variations that the Profound Yellow Realm would instantly evolve when facing the crisis of annihilation.

They all descended upon the dense ink-colored mass simultaneously.

It was as if countless vortexes appeared at the same time, causing the ink-colored mass to churn and boil.

Under Li Fan's guidance, various transformations actually emerged from the void!

A magnificent array of colors, born from the ink-colored abyss.

Even Li Fan, the creator of this spectacle, had not anticipated this scene.

Watching Ink Annihilation's power being continuously transformed into other world-destroying variations, while Ink Annihilation itself was gradually weakened and died in this transformation.

Li Fan's expression was complex.

Only when the ink-colored mass was about to completely dissipate did Li Fan retract his divine ability and absorb the myriad Profound Yellow World Destruction Transformations into his body.

"Extinction is the parent of life."

"Life is the path to extinction..."

"Is this the contingency plan for the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation?"

Chapter 1382: The Death of Li Fan

Li Fan's thoughts churned, but his hands did not stop. He separated the myriad Profound Yellow World Destruction Transformations from the main body of Ink Annihilation. Each of these transformations could give rise to a Profound Yellow Nascent Soul stage cultivator of considerable strength.

"Although named World Destruction, they are in reality transformations of life."

"It would be best to collect them first. Even if the Profound Yellow Realm later sublimes into an Immortal Domain, as long as they are released simultaneously, they can still cause chaos in the Profound Yellow Realm in an instant!"

As Li Fan thought this, his golden threads moved rapidly, forming a seal to contain the numerous World Destruction Transformations and suppressing them within his body.

"As for Ink Annihilation…" Li Fan's expression turned solemn once more. The black shadow, originally reduced to a tiny ink spot, had inexplicably recovered completely in a short period after being given a moment to breathe. Unendingly, it continued to corrode everything around it.

"One is all. As expected of the weakened, preliminary version of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. If not completely eradicated, even a sliver remaining can quickly make a comeback!"

Li Fan recalled everything he had seen about Ink Annihilation in the past. Ink Annihilation rarely acted, but each time it did, it was earth-shattering, annihilating an entire province. Even the Myriad Immortals Alliance and the Five Elders Association, upon detecting Ink Annihilation's appearance, would choose to avoid it, allowing it to wreak havoc.

"Those five old turtles might have already sensed Ink Annihilation's extraordinary nature. It is by no means comparable to an ordinary Heaven and Earth Essence."

"Ink Annihilation's integration into the Profound Yellow Realm's laws of heaven and earth has caused the Profound Yellow Realm to develop a corresponding resistance. Even if it annihilates everything, life will eventually be reborn."

"If that's the case, doesn't it mean that after the Profound Yellow sublimes into an Immortal Domain, it will possess the power to resist the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation?" Li Fan's heart stirred.

"Presumably, this was the design of the True Immortals of the past. Of course, whether it succeeds or fails remains to be seen in this life."

Li Fan pondered extensively, experimenting multiple times to understand Ink Annihilation's various properties. He then brought it to the center of the Star Sea, near the sea of black energy. The surging black energy was devouring the Star Sea at a stable speed. The Star Sea consciousness remained oblivious, but Li Fan, however, frowned deeply at this increasingly alarming and continuous black energy. Even with the layers of golden thread seals, when Ink Annihilation sensed the presence of the black energy nearby, it instantly became more "lively." Originally coiled tightly, waiting for the opportune moment to break free, it now lunged left and right, desperately crashing against the golden threads, trying to escape.

"As expected!" A glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. After verifying that Ink Annihilation indeed had some connection to the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, and sensing that Ink Annihilation, sealed within the nearby sea of black energy, seemed to be drawing some form of energy, Li Fan dared not linger. He quickly departed. He brought Ink Annihilation back to the Profound Yellow Realm, to the Congyun Sea. He was still waiting for it to promote to the Heaven and Earth Immortal Essence and merge with the Dao, so naturally, he had no intention of killing it now.

Ink Annihilation broke free and searched the entire world but could not find its previous enemy who had sealed it. It could only vent its boundless rage upon Hong Xi and the Congyun Sea. Poor Hong Xi, who had just merged with the Dao and was returning to Myriad Immortals Island, receiving worship from the cultivators within, suddenly saw a mass of ink spreading from the sky. Then, it enveloped and swallowed everything. Although Ink Annihilation had only briefly touched the black energy, subtle changes had still occurred within it. Not only Li Fan but also the Profound Yellow Heaven and Earth seemed to have sensed this. Ink Annihilation's act of annihilation was not carried out completely. The Congyun Sea was being eroded down to its last thin layer of bedrock, but Ink Annihilation was forcibly recalled by the Heaven and Earth consciousness.

"Its actions are faster and more violent than before."

"And besides..." Li Fan flashed and arrived at the last remaining part of the Congyun Sea, observing it closely. Although Ink Annihilation had vanished, a corrosive force still remained. It was preventing the Profound Yellow Realm's vitality from rejuvenating.

"This conflicts with the Profound Yellow Realm's original intention. Ink Annihilation was specifically dispatched to annihilate everything, precisely for the subsequent complete integration. But now..." Li Fan extended his right index finger and pressed it onto the bedrock of the Congyun Sea.

"Sizzle..." A sound like being burned by fire, or corroded by strong acid, rang out. The power that destroyed everything actually began to devour Li Fan's body and divine soul along the contact point. It was exactly the same as when he had previously come into contact with Ink Annihilation.

"Its main body was recalled, yet some power still remains."

"This is almost impossible for a Heaven and Earth Essence. Yet now it has truly happened..."

"It's already showing signs of losing control before fully engaging." Breaking off a large piece of the last bedrock of the Congyun Sea to bring back for research, Li Fan's furrowed brow did not ease. Having perceived Ink Annihilation's possible true nature, the unease Li Fan felt from the self-simulated reincarnation in [Returning to True] had not diminished; instead, it had intensified. He temporarily set aside all his current affairs and, out of habit, went to the location where the Dissolution Mountain used to be. He sat in the center of the lecture platform, lost in thought.

"I must trust my intuition."

"This level of unease, even after so many reincarnations, has never occurred before."

"The source of the unease..."

"It should still be that time when [Returning to True] inexplicably initiated a simulation on its own."

"Sun Piaomiao's Three-Pronged Tree must involve the resonance of a certain Great Dao, or even the Great Dao itself, which is why [Returning to True] exhibited such peculiar changes after absorbing it."

"In reality, [Returning to True] initiating a reincarnation on its own is not terrifying. What is truly terrifying is that I retained no memories from it."

A shadow flashed across Li Fan's face. "Up until now, every simulation by [Returning to True] has been based on me as the main body. Every reincarnation was my personal experience."

"And now, [Returning to True] is still united with me, showing no signs of losing control."

"So there is only one possibility: in that simulation, I, due to some unforeseen circumstance..."

"Died."

A cold light flashed in Li Fan's eyes. His body stiffened for a moment, then he continued to ponder: "I didn't even have time to activate [Returning to True] before I died."

"It was [Returning to True] itself that reversed everything."

"Therefore, the experience of that life exists only within [Returning to True], not within my personal experiences."

"Only after absorbing Kou Hong's pseudo-Eternal Remnant Will did [Returning to True] spit out that memory."

As his thoughts flowed, and he deduced this result, Li Fan's unease in his heart suddenly lessened slightly. Although not completely gone, he had finally figured out the possible reason.

"I have already died once?" Li Fan felt an unprecedented chill in his heart.

"So those blurry memory fragments obtained from [Returning to True] were not from this life's experience. They occurred in the life where I died."

"I am now following the original trajectory, continuing to move forward."

"If I do not make a change..."

"It's a dead end!"

As if seeing the scene of his future demise, Li Fan's heart suddenly relaxed.

"Actually, to put it simply, after [Returning to True] absorbed the Three-Pronged Tree in this life, it initiated a simulation. In the simulation, I did not realize that there was a divergence. I still followed the original plan, executing the plan to promote the Profound Yellow Realm to an Immortal Domain and merge with the Heaven and Earth Immortal Essence."

"I didn't notice the hidden crisis, and even with thousands of preparations, I still died and failed."

Li Fan let out a long sigh.

"The Three-Pronged Tree is indeed a divine object. If not for this preemptive simulation, I would likely have followed the same fate as the failure."

"I wonder if [Returning to True] will be willing to absorb it again in the next life?"

Li Fan's thoughts quickly returned to the main issue. If what Li Fan speculated was true, then a life-or-death question now lay before Li Fan. What exactly was it that led to the death of Li Fan in the simulation? Currently, Li Fan possessed immortal formations, supreme escape techniques for protection, and the two great supreme guardians, Tian Yang and Qiu Shui. Even if the plan for merging with the Dao failed, it should not prevent him from having time to activate [Returning to True].

"In fact, there are very few things that can truly threaten me."

"Within the High Wall, True Immortals from the Immortal Ruins, the True Immortal corpses from the Profound Yellow Dark Sea seeking survival, and the black energy representing the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation."

"Beyond the High Wall, all unknown existences."

Thinking of this, Li Fan's thoughts paused, then a look of realization flashed across his face.

"And... the main material for promoting the Profound Yellow to an Immortal Domain, the fragment of the Immortal Domain left by Sun Piaomiao."

After much consideration, having ruled out all other possibilities, only these suspicious targets remained.

"The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, a terrifying tribulation specifically targeting the Immortal Realm. Although it doesn't appear to be fully descending now, only its endless black energy is revealed. But who knows, the moment I promote the Profound Yellow to an Immortal Domain, it might suddenly occur."

"Even countless True Immortals of the past could not escape it. If caught unprepared, I would likely also die without escaping." Li Fan first confirmed the biggest possibility for his failure.

"As for the two True Immortals in the Dark Sea and the Immortal Ruins, one dead and one alive. I should be able to delay them for a moment by using the Profound Yellow All Beings Formation."

"The forces beyond the High Wall... With the High Wall itself as cover, according to the experience of the previous life, I have enough time to deal with it. But it's not enough!"

"When the High Wall collapses and the Star Sea is in turmoil, I must stir up huge waves in the Star Sea to conceal the vision from external forces!" Li Fan instantly thought of the endless vitality within the trench depressions and the [Form of Living Beings].

"The descent of the forces beyond the Wall will inevitably pose an extreme threat to the Star Sea itself. Catalyzed by the Tai Jia Divine Art..."

"The infinite power of the Star Sea should be able to delay the forces beyond the Wall for a moment."

After some thought, Li Fan added a pile of tasks for himself.

"Finally, there is that Immortal Domain composed of numerous chess pieces."

"Although I have tried to fuse it before, and reached more than half of the process without sensing any True Immortals within, only a pure Immortal Domain world."

"But thinking about it now, it was still too hasty." Li Fan's expression became serious. "After all, they are True Immortals; concealing themselves from my perception would not be difficult."

"Without fully unfolding the Immortal Domain, how can I be sure it is truly safe?"

"It's just a waste of one reincarnation, twenty to thirty years of time." Li Fan thought, his heart already made up. No matter what, he must first fully unfold the Immortal Domain and confirm its safety within.

"The re-emergence of the Immortal Domain will, after all, shake the Star Sea."

"I must find a reliable place and prepare in advance."

"If there is truly a hidden True Immortal within, I will resolutely use [Returning to True]. In the next life, I will find other methods for anchoring the world's power."

"If there are no anomalies within, then it's even better..." Li Fan still wanted to minimize the impact of the Immortal Domain's unfolding.

"Using the lowliness of the trench depressions to offset the height of the Immortal Domain."

"The trench depressions, the lowest point of the Star Sea, should be an excellent location."

"Moreover, the trenches are intricate, and with the Form of Living Beings, it should be able to confuse potential enemies to some extent."

Li Fan then returned to the depths of the Star Sea. Without disturbing Xu Ke, who was still continuously excavating, he arrived at the very center of the mostly explored area, ensuring he would be as undisturbed by external factors as possible. Li Fan, with unprecedented seriousness, slowly laid down layer upon layer of immortal formations. Using all the means currently at his disposal, Li Fan resolutely restarted the unfolding of the Immortal Domain.

Hummm…

Within the immortal formations, a great wind seemed to arise, relentlessly impacting and ravaging. Li Fan's proud formations, like a dilapidated thatched hut, could not last long and were on the verge of collapse. Li Fan had no choice but to constantly replenish them with Origin Energy Essence, patching them up as much as possible to delay the process. With a focused expression, he stared intently at the blurred light and shadow in the center of the immortal formation.

Resembling a human, yet not. Resembling a scene, yet not. Just as seen before. However, the previous unfolding of the Immortal Realm was disturbed and interrupted by the black energy in the center of the Star Sea. This time, under Li Fan's will, it was able to continue!

Boundless light emanated from the Immortal Domain. Li Fan vaguely saw that those figures were clearly extremely profound characters. They scattered outwards, then melted into water, forming countless intersecting lines that held up the sky and the earth! Innumerable characters emerged from the boundless light. More and more horizontal and vertical lines intertwined, making the world brighter and more vibrant. The Immortal Domain was about to be born in the Utmost Darkness Star Sea! Li Fan could already feel the various changes occurring within the Star Sea. Including, but not limited to, the awakening of the True Immortal in the Immortal Ruins, the astonishment of the Heavenly Physician's teachings, and the shock of the Star Sea consciousness. But he had no time to care about them now. His gaze was fixed on the forming Immortal Domain. He wanted to determine if, besides the laws of the Immortal Realm, there were any other existences hidden within the Immortal Domain fragment left by Sun Piaomiao!

"The birth of the Immortal Domain is creating even more of a stir than I imagined!"

"It seems that even if there are no dangers within the Immortal Domain, I cannot stay here for long this lifetime."

"However, it's not a complete anticlimax, as I have avoided a fatal situation. In the next life, I will only need to follow the steps and repeat the process!" Li Fan's thoughts raced. And at this moment, as the Immortal Domain bloomed like a fruit from a flower, about to break through the trench depressions of the Star Sea and return to the normal Star Sea. Li Fan finally saw clearly the illusory figure that finally appeared within the Immortal Domain. An untitled monument standing between the heaven and earth of the Immortal Domain!
